javam mohayitvā ca mām tatra kṣaṇena antaradhīyata tatra ambudhara dhīreṇa bho śabdena anunādinā ayam bho aham iti prāha vākyam vākya viśāradaḥ śabda anusārī tu tatas tam deśam aham āvrajam tatra apaśyam tatas ca aham śrīmat haṃsa yutam saraḥ bho śabda śabda pratisṛṣṭena svareṇa aprativādinā viveśa devaḥ svām yonim mām idam ca abhyabhāṣata tatas ca prāviśam tatra saha tena mahātmanā dṛṣṭavān adbhutataram tasmin sarasi bhāsvatām agnīnām apraṇītānām iddhānām indhanaiḥ vinā dīptānām ājya siktānām sthāneṣu arciṣmatām sadā dīptiḥ teṣām anājyānām prāpta ājyānām iva abhavat aniddhānām iva satām iddhānām iva bhāsvatām atha aham vara dam devam na apaśyam tatra saṃgatam tatas saṃmoham āpannaḥ viṣādam agamam param apaśyam ca agnihotrāṇi śataśas atha sahasraśas vidhinā saṃpraṇītāni dhiṣṇyeṣu ājyavatām tadā a saṃmṛṣṭa saṃstṛ talāḥ ca eva vedīḥ kusuma saṃstṛtāḥ kuśa padma utpala āsaṅgān kalaśān ca hiraṇmayān agnihotrāṇi citrāṇi śataśas atha sahasraśas tāni ca atra samṛddhāni dṛṣṭavān asmi anekaśas manohṛdyatamaḥ ca atra surabhiḥ puṇya lakṣaṇaḥ teṣām tatra agnihotrāṇām īḍitānām sahasraśas candra aṃśu kāśa śubhrāṇām tuṣāra udbheda varcasām vimala vimala āditya bhāsānām sthaṇḍilāni sahasraśas dṛṣṭāni agni samīpeṣu dyutimanti mahanti ca eṣu ca agni samīpeṣu śuśrāva supada akṣarāḥ prabhāva antaritānām tu praspaṣṭa akṣara bhāṣiṇām ṛk ṛc yajuḥ sāma gānām ca madhurāḥ su svarāḥ giraḥ su saṃmṛṣṭa talaiḥ taiḥ tu bṛhadbhiḥ dīpta tejasaiḥ pāvakaiḥ pāvita ātmā aham abhavam laghu vikramaḥ tatas aham teṣu dhiṣṇyeṣu jvalamāneṣu yajvanām tam deśam praṇamitvā atha anveṣṭum upacakrame tāni aneka sahasrāṇi parīyan tu mahā javāt na antam teṣām prapaśyāmi khedaḥ ca sahasā bhavat śramam paramam āpannaḥ cintayāmi vicetanaḥ ṛk ṛc yajuḥ sāma nirghoṣaḥ śrūyate na ca dṛśyate na ca paśyāmi tam devam yena aham iha coditaḥ tatas cintayataḥ mahyam mohena āviṣṭa cetasaḥ mahān śabdaḥ prādurāsīt su bhṛśam me vyathā karaḥ atha aham sahasā tatra śṛṇomi vipula dhvanim apaśyam ca suparṇānām sahasrāṇi ayutāni ca dṛṣṭvā ātmānam parigatam saṃbhramam paramam gataḥ nārāyaṇāya śuddhāya śāśvatāya dhruvāya ca bhūta bhavya bhaveśāya śivāya śiva mūrtaye śivayoneḥ śiva ādyāya śiva pūjyatamāya ca viśvāya viśvadevāya viśveśāya mahātmane śuciśravāya mahate ṛtu saṃvatsarāya ca ṛk ṛc yajuḥ sāma vaktrāya atharvaśirase namaḥ hṛṣīkeśāya kṛṣṇāya druhiṇa urukramāya ca brahma udrekāya tārkṣyāya varāhāya ekaśṛṅgiṇe śipiviṣṭāya satyāya haraye atha śikhaṇḍine hutāya ūrdhvāya vakrāya raudra anīkāya sādhave garutmate trinetrāya sudhāmāya vṛṣāvṛṣe vṛṣāya vṛṣa rūpāya vibhave bhūrbhuvāya ca dīpta sṛṣṭāya yajñāya sthirāya sthavirāya ca acyutāya tuṣārāya vīrāya ca samāya ca jiṣṇave puruhūtāya vasiṣṭhāya varāya ca satyeśāya sureśāya haraye atha śikhaṇḍine kirīṭine sukeśāya vāsudevāya śuṣmiṇe bṛhadukthe suṣeṇāya yugme duṃdubhaye tathā bhāskarāya ca candrāya padmanābhāya bhūriṇe vaṣaṭkārāya svāhāya svadhāya nidhanāya ca śrī padma āyāja sadṛśe dharaṇe dhāraṇe pare viśvāya ca su viśvāya viśva rūpa dharāya ca keśavāya sukeśāya raśmikeśāya bhūriṇe hiraṇyagarbhāya namaḥ saumyāya vṛṣa rūpiṇe nārāyaṇa agra vapuṣe puruhūtāya vajriṇe śaraṇāya śaraṇyāya śakta iṣṭa śaraṇāya ca pāhi mām devadeveśa kaḥ api ajaḥ asi sanātanaḥ evam gataḥ asmi śaraṇam śaraṇyam brahma yoninam śṛṇomi ca giram divyām antardhāna gatām śivām apaśyam ca aham āyāntam nara nārāyaṇa āśrame yajataḥ tān ṛṣīn devān vadataḥ dhyāyataḥ munīn yuktān siddhān naiṣṭhikān ca japataḥ yajataḥ gṛhe puṣpa pūra parikṣiptam dhūpitam dīpitam hutam vanditam sikta saṃmṛṣṭam nara nārāyaṇa āśramam tat adbhutam aham dṛṣṭvā vismitaḥ asmi tadā anaghāḥ jagāma śirasā devam prayatena antarātmanā na adhyagaccham parām divyām tasya sarva bhava ātmanaḥ avocam tam adīna artham śreṣṭhānām śreṣṭham uttamam yat etat adbhutam deva mayā dṛṣṭam tvad āśrayam yadi jānāsi mām bhaktam yadi vā anugrahaḥ mayi śaṃsa sarvam aśeṣeṇa śrotavyam yadi ced mayā brūhi sarvam aśeṣeṇa tat āścaryam mahā mune kim tat ati adbhutam vṛttam teṣu agniṣu samantataḥ kāni tāni agnihotrāṇi keṣām śabdaḥ śrutaḥ mayā śṛṇvatām brahma satatam adṛśyāṇām mahātmanām etat me bhagavant kṛṣṇa brūhi sarvam aśeṣatas gṛṇanti agni samīpeṣu ke ca te brahmarāśayaḥ mad na deva na gandharvāḥ gandharva na piśācāḥ na rākṣasāḥ caturdhā aham vibhakta ātmā lokānām hita kāmyayā bhūta bhavya bhaviṣya ādiḥ anādiḥ viśvakṛttamaḥ pṛthivī pṛthivī vāyuḥ ākāśam apaḥ jyotiḥ ca pañcamam prakṛti aśubha sa kim cit śreyasā yuktaḥ śreṣṭha bhāvam vyavasyati yat svabhāva ātma tattva jñaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ upalakṣyate an ādi madhya nidhanaḥ saḥ antarātmā asmi śāśvataḥ yat tu me paramam guhyam rūpam sūkṣma artha darśibhiḥ gṛhyate sūkṣma bhāva jñaiḥ saḥ avibhāvyaḥ asmi śāśvataḥ mattaḥ mad jātāni bhūtāni mayā aharniśam yaḥ mām yathā vedayati tasya tasya asmi kāśyapa mām tu jñātum kṛtā buddhiḥ bhavatā pakṣi sattama śṛṇu yaḥ aham yatas ca aham yad arthaḥ ca aham udyataḥ agni kārya parāḥ nityam japa homa parāyaṇāḥ ātmani agnīn samādhāya niyatāḥ niyam indriyāḥ yajantaḥ japa yajñaiḥ mām mānasaiḥ ca su saṃyatāḥ agnīn abhyudyayuḥ śaśvat agniṣu eva abhisaṃsthitāḥ ananya ananya kāryāḥ śucayaḥ nityam agni parāyaṇāḥ yad evaṃbuddhayaḥ evaṃbuddhayaḥ dhīrāḥ te mām gacchanti tādṛśāḥ a kāma hata han saṃkalpāḥ jñāne nityam samāhitāḥ ātmani agnīn samādhāya nirāhārāḥ nirāśiṣaḥ viṣayeṣu nirārambhāḥ vimuktāḥ jñāna cakṣuṣaḥ an anya manasaḥ manas dhīrāḥ svabhāva niyama anvitāḥ tatra tatra agnayaḥ saṃnihitāḥ dīpyante sma nirindhanāḥ jñāna jñāna amala āśayāḥ tasmin ye ca candra aṃśu nirmalāḥ upāsīnāḥ gṛṇantaḥ agnim praspaṣṭa akṣara bhāṣiṇaḥ ākāṅkṣamāṇāḥ śucayaḥ teṣu agniṣu vihaṃgama ye ye mayā bhāvitātmānaḥ mayi eva abhiratāḥ sadā upāsate ca mām eva jyotiḥ bhūtāḥ nirāmayāḥ nirāhārāḥ hi aniṣpandāḥ candra aṃśu sadṛśa prabhāḥ nirmalāḥ nirahaṃkārāḥ nirālambāḥ lokānām dhāraṇa arthāya vidhānam vidadhāmi ca yathāvat tat aśeṣeṇa śrotum arhati me bhavān ekā mūrtiḥ nirguṇa ākhyā yogam paramam āsthitā dvitīyā sṛjate tāta bhūta grāmam carācaram sṛṣṭam saṃharate ca ekā jagat sthāvara jaṅgamam kṣapayan mohayan iva māyayā kṣipantī mohayantī ca ātma niṣṭhā sva māyayā caturthī me mahāmūrtiḥ jagat vṛddhim dadāti sā mayā sarvam idam vyāptam mayi sarvam pratiṣṭhitam yāni tāni agnihotrāṇi ye ca candra aṃśu rāśayaḥ gṛṇanti vedam satatam teṣu agniṣu vihaṃgama krameṇa mām samāyānti sukhinaḥ jñāna saṃyutāḥ teṣām aham tapaḥ dīptam tejaḥ samyak samāhitam śakyaḥ samāsādayitum aham vai jñānacakṣuṣā mām sthūladarśanam viddhi jagataḥ kāryakāraṇam mayā ca api caturdhā ātmā vibhaktaḥ prāṇiṣu sthitaḥ brahmaṇaḥ ca api saṃbhūtaḥ śivaḥ iti avadhāryatām śivāt skandaḥ saṃbabhūva etat sṛṣṭi catuṣṭayam tadā tadā aham dharma vṛddhi artham mūrtimān bhavitā āśuga yoginaḥ yoga yuktāḥ ca te mām paśyanti na anyathā vartamānaḥ ca teṣu evam nivṛttaḥ ca eva teṣu aham ye viduḥ jāta saṃkalpāḥ te mām paśyanti tādṛśāḥ kham kham vāyuḥ apaḥ jyotiḥ ca pṛthivī ca iti pañcamam vartamānam vṛt atītam ca pañcavargeṣu niścalam śabda sparśeṣu rūpeṣu rasa gandheṣu ca api aham rajaḥ tamobhyām āviṣṭā yeṣām buddhiḥ aniścitā draṣṭum vā veditum vā api na śakyā paramā gatiḥ sattva yuktā matiḥ yeṣām kevala ātma viniścitā ye yad yad agnihotra niyatāḥ japa yajña parāyaṇāḥ te mām upāsate śaśvat yān tān tvam dṛṣṭavān asi śāstra dṛṣṭa vidhāna jñāḥ asaktāḥ kva cit anyathā ye tu sāṃkhyam ca yogam ca jñātvā api adhṛta niścayāḥ tasmāt jñānena śuddhena prasanna ātmā ātma vid śuciḥ śuddha śuddha abhijana saṃpannāḥ śraddhā yuktena cetasā na vāyuḥ pavate tatra na tasmin jyotiṣām gatiḥ na ca apaḥ pṛthivī na eva na ākāśam na manogatiḥ sthūla darśanam etat me yat dṛṣṭam bhavata anagha etat sūkṣmasya ca dvāram kāryāṇām kāraṇam tu aham brahmaṇaḥ yat ahorātram saṃkhyāna jñaiḥ vibhāvyate mām yajñam āhuḥ yajña jñāḥ vedam veda vidaḥ janāḥ munayaḥ ca api mām eva japa yajñam pracakṣate vaktā mantā rasayitā ghrātā draṣṭā pradarśakaḥ boddhā bodhayitā ca aham gantā śrotā cit ātmakaḥ mām mad yaj svargam āyānti tathā ca āpnuvate mahat jñātvā mām eva ca edhante niḥsaṅgena antarātmanā mad tejaḥ tejaḥ dvijātīnām mama tejaḥ dvijātayaḥ prāṇa pālaḥ śarīre aham yoginām aham īśvaraḥ dharmam artham ca kāmam ca mokṣam ca eva ārjavam japam sa tadā aham tathārūpaḥ tvayā dṛṣṭaḥ sanātanaḥ nirārambha namaskārāḥ tathā sthūlaḥ aham evam vihaga tvayā dṛṣṭaḥ tathā anagha mā matiḥ tava gāt nāśam eṣā gatiḥ anuttamā etat evaṃvidham tasya mahimānam mahātmanaḥ acyutasya aprameyasya dṛṣṭavān asmi yat purā etat vaḥ sarvam ākhyātam ceṣṭitam tasya dhīmataḥ ṛṣayaḥ mayā mad anubhūtam pratyakṣam dṛṣṭvā ca adbhuta karmaṇaḥ aho śrāvitam ākhyānam bhavatā ati adbhutam mahat puṇyam yaśasyam āyuṣyam svargyam svastyayanam mahat etat jñānavatām jñeyam eṣā gatiḥ anuttamā yaḥ imām śrāvayet vidvān kathām parvasu parvasu sa tad lokān prāpnuyāt puṇyān devarṣibhiḥ abhiṣṭutān śrāddha kāle ca viprāṇām yaḥ imām śrāvayet śuciḥ na tatra rakṣasām bhāgaḥ na asurāṇām ca vidyate bhīṣmaḥ vaiśyaḥ tu dhana dhānya āḍhyaḥ śūdraḥ sukham avāpnuyāt svān eva ca āśramān jagmuḥ babhūvuḥ śānti tatparāḥ sthūla darśibhiḥ ākṛṣṭaḥ durjñeyaḥ hi akṛtātmabhiḥ eṣā śrutiḥ mahā rāja dharmyā dharma bhṛtām vara surāṇām brahmaṇā proktā vismitānām paraṃtapa mayā api eṣā kathā tāta kathitā mātuḥ antike tat agnihotra paramāḥ japa yajña parāyaṇāḥ santaḥ prayānti akṣara sāmya tām ārambha yajñān utsṛjya japa homa parāyaṇāḥ dhyāyantaḥ manasā viṣṇum gacchanti paramām gatim uvāca tvayā āpageya nāmāni śrutāni iha jagatpateḥ pitāmaha īśāya vibho nāmāni ācakṣva śambhave babhrave viśva māyāya mahābhāgyam ca tattvāt uvāca aśaktaḥ aham guṇān vaktum mahādevasya dhīmataḥ brahma viṣṇu sureśānām sraṣṭā yaḥ prabhuḥ eva ca brahma ādayaḥ piśāca antāḥ yam hi devāḥ upāsate prakṛtīnām para tvena puruṣasya ca yaḥ paraḥ prakṛtim puruṣam ca eva kṣobhayitvā sva tejasā brahmāṇam asṛjat tasmāt devadevaḥ prajāpatiḥ kaḥ hi śaktaḥ guṇān vaktum devadevasya dhīmataḥ kaḥ hi śaktaḥ bhavam jñātum madvidhaḥ parameśvaram ṛte nārāyaṇāt putra śaṅkha cakra gadā dharāt eṣa vidvān yadu śreṣṭhaḥ viṣṇuḥ parama durjayaḥ divya cakṣūḥ mahā tejāḥ vīkṣyate yoga cakṣuṣā rudra bhaktyā tu kṛṣṇena jagant vyāptam mahātmanā tam prasādya tadā devam badaryām kila bhārata prāptavān eva rāja indra suvarṇākṣāt maheśvarāt pūrṇam varṣa sahasram tu taptavan eṣa mādhavaḥ prasādya vara dam devam carācara gurum śivam yuge yuge tu kṛṣṇena toṣitaḥ vai maheśvaraḥ bhaktyā paramayā rājan prītaḥ ca eva mahātmanaḥ aiśvaryam yādṛśam tasya jagadyoneḥ mahātmanaḥ tat ayam dṛṣṭavan sākṣāt putra arthe hariḥ acyutaḥ yasmāt parataram ca eva na anyam paśyāmi bhārata vyākhyātum devadevasya śaktaḥ nāmāni aśeṣatas eṣa śaktaḥ mahā bāhuḥ vaktum bhagavantaḥ guṇān uvāca vibhūtim ca eva kārtsnyena satyām māheśvarīm nṛpa evam uktvā tadā bhīṣmaḥ vāsudevam mahā yaśāḥ bhava māhātmya saṃyuktam idam āha pitāmahaḥ dhyānena atha japaiḥ kāryā svadharmam ucitā sadā deve nārāyaṇe bhaktaḥ śaṃkaram sādhu pūjaya vāsudevam mahātmānam idam vacanam abravīt uvāca śivāya viśvarūpāya yat mām pṛcchat yudhiṣṭhiraḥ nāmnām sahasram devasya taṇḍinā brahma yoninā ṛṣayaḥ suvratāḥ dāntāḥ śṛṇvantu gadataḥ tava uvāca na gatiḥ karmaṇām śakyā vettum īśasya tattva hiraṇyagarbha pramukhāḥ devāḥ sa indrāḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ na viduḥ yasya nidhanam ādim vā sūkṣma darśinaḥ sa katham nara mātreṇa śakyaḥ jñātum satām gatiḥ bhavatām kīrtayiṣyāmi vrateśāya yathātatham uvāca evam uktvā tu bhagavant guṇān tasya mahātmanaḥ upaspṛśya śuciḥ bhūtvā kathayām āsa dhīmataḥ uvāca śuśrūṣadhvam brāhmaṇa indrāḥ tvam ca tāta yudhiṣṭhira tvam ca āpageya nāmāni niśāmaya jagatpateḥ yat avāptam ca me pūrvam sāmba hetoḥ su duṣkaram yathā ca bhagavant dṛṣṭaḥ mayā pūrvam samādhinā śambare nihate pūrvam raukmiṇeyena dhīmatā atīte dvādaśe varṣe jāmbavatī abravīt hi mām pradyumna cārudeṣṇa ādīn rukmiṇyāḥ vīkṣya putrakān putra arthinī mām upetya vākyam āha yudhiṣṭhira śūram balavatām śreṣṭham kānta rūpam akalmaṣam tvayā dvādaśa varṣāṇi vāyu bhūtena śuṣyatā ārādhya paśubhartāram rukmiṇyāḥ janitāḥ sutāḥ cārudeṣṇaḥ sucāruḥ ca cāruveṣaḥ yaśodharaḥ cāruśravāḥ cāruyaśāḥ pradyumnaḥ śaṃbhuḥ eva ca yathā te janitāḥ putrāḥ rukmiṇyāḥ cāru vikramāḥ anujānīhi mām rājñi kariṣye vacanam te sā ca mām abravīt gaccha vijayāya śivāya ca brahmā śivaḥ kāśyapaḥ ca nadyaḥ devāḥ manonugāḥ kṣetra oṣadhyaḥ yajñavāhāt chandāṃsi ṛṣi gaṇāḥ dharā samudrāḥ dakṣiṇā stobhāḥ ṛkṣāṇi pitaraḥ grahāḥ manvantarāṇi gāvaḥ ca candramāḥ savitā hariḥ sāvitrī brahma vidyā ca ṛtavaḥ vatsarāḥ kṣapāḥ kṣaṇāḥ lavāḥ muhūrtāḥ ca nimeṣāḥ yuga paryayāḥ evam kṛta svastyayanaḥ tayā aham tām abhyanujñāya kapīndra putrīm pituḥ samīpe nara sattamasya mātuḥ ca rājñaḥ ca tathā āhukasya tam artham āvedya yat abravīt mām vidyādhara indrasya sutā bhṛśa ārtā tān abhyanujñāya tadā ati duḥkhāt gadam tathā eva atibalam ca rāmam atha ūcatuḥ prīti yutau tadānīm prāpya anujñām guru janāt aham tārkṣyam acintayam prāpya anujñām guru mukhāt ājamīḍha tārkṣyam tadā manasā cintayitvā kṛtvā praṇāmam śirasā bhavāya tatas abhyagām prāk udīcīm su ramyām tatas mayā hi anusṛṣṭaḥ khaga indraḥ sthitaḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ bhava bhāva bhāvitaḥ nivedya mātuḥ ca pituḥ samīpe tathā abhyanujñāya gurūn ca sarvān mahā balam tārkṣyam acintayam vai saḥ aham himavantaḥ pārśvam prāpya tārkṣyam vyasarjayam kṣetram ca tapasām śreṣṭham paśyāmi āśramam uttamam badarī kunda punnāgaiḥ aśoka āmra atimuktakaiḥ puṣpa gulma latā ākīrṇam kadala ṣaṇḍa śobhitam nānā śakuni saṃbhojyaiḥ phalaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ alaṃkṛtam yathāsthāna vinikṣiptaiḥ bhūṣitam vana rājibhiḥ viśālaiḥ ca agni śaraṇaiḥ yathāsthāna āhitāgnibhiḥ ruru vāraṇa śārdūla siṃha dvīpi samākulam kuraṅga barhiṇa ākīrṇam mārjāra bhujaga āvṛtam pūgaiḥ ca mṛga jātīnām mahiṣa ṛkṣa niṣevitam prahṛṣṭa nānāvidha pakṣi sevitam mahīruhāṇām ca vanaiḥ vicitraiḥ nānā puṣpa rajaḥ miśraḥ gaja dāna adhivāsitaḥ dhārā ninādaiḥ vihaga praṇādaiḥ śubhaiḥ tathā bṛṃhitaiḥ kuñjarāṇām gītaiḥ tathā kiṃnarāṇām udāraiḥ śubhaiḥ svanaiḥ sāmagānām ca vīra viśālaiḥ ca agni śaraṇaiḥ bhūṣitam kuśa saṃvṛtam vibhūṣitam puṇya pavitra toyayā sadā ca juṣṭam nṛpa jahnukanyayā mahātmabhiḥ dharma bhṛtām variṣṭhaiḥ mahā ṛṣibhiḥ bhūṣitam agni kalpaiḥ dhūma aśanaiḥ ūṣmapaiḥ kṣīrapaiḥ ca nānā vṛndaiḥ veda ṣaḍaṅga pāragaiḥ gocāriṇaḥ atha aśmakuṭṭāḥ dantolūkhalinaḥ tathā marīcipāḥ phenapāḥ ca tathā eva mṛgacāriṇaḥ aśvattha phala bhakṣāḥ ca tathā hi udaka śāyinaḥ cīra carma ambara dharāḥ tathā valkala dhāriṇaḥ su duḥkhāt niyamān tān tān vahataḥ su tapaḥ nvitān su pūjitam deva gaṇaiḥ mahātmabhiḥ śiva ādibhiḥ bhārata puṇya karmabhiḥ rarāja tat ca āśrama maṇḍalam sadā divi iva rājan ravi maṇḍalam yathā krīḍanti sarpaiḥ nakulāḥ mṛgaiḥ vyāghrāḥ ca mitra vat prabhāvāt dīpta tapasaḥ saṃnikarṣa guṇa anvitāḥ tatra āśrama pade śreṣṭhe sarva bhūta manorame sevite dvija śārdūlaiḥ veda vedāṅga pāragaiḥ nānā niyama vikhyātaiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ ca mahātmabhiḥ praviśan eva ca apaśyam jaṭā cīra dharam prabhum tejasā tapasā ca eva dīpyamānam yathā analam śiṣya madhya gatam śāntam yuvānam brāhmaṇa ṛṣabham śirasā vandamānam mām upamanyuḥ abhāṣata svāgatam puṇḍarīkākṣa sa phalāni tapāṃsi naḥ yat pūjyaḥ pūjayasi naḥ draṣṭavyaḥ draṣṭum icchasi manuṣya tā anuvṛttyā tvām jñātvā tiṣṭhāma sarvagam tam aham prāñjaliḥ bhūtvā mṛga pakṣiṣu atha agniṣu tatas mām bhagavān āha sāmnā parama valgunā lapsyase tanayam kṛṣṇaḥ ātma tulyam asaṃśayam tapaḥ su mahat āsthāya toṣaya īśānam īśvaram iha devaḥ sa patnīkaḥ samākrīḍati adhokṣaja iha eva devatā śreṣṭham devāḥ sa ṛṣi gaṇāḥ purā toṣayitvā śubhān kāmān prāpnuvan te janārdana tejasām tapasām ca eva nidhiḥ sa bhagavant iha śubha aśubha anvitān bhāvān visṛjan saṃkṣipan api tena sarva amara aiśvaryam śarvāt prāptam sama arbudam viṣṇoḥ cakram ca tat ghoram vajram ākhaṇḍalasya ca śīrṇam purā bhavat tāta grahasya aṅgeṣu keśava utpāditam vṛṣāṅkena dīpta jvalana saṃnibham sudarśanam tadā tasya loke nāma pratiṣṭhitam tat jīrṇam abhavat tāta grahasya aṅgeṣu keśava ardyamānāḥ ca vibudhāḥ graheṇa su balīyasā śiva datta varān jaghnuḥ asura indrān surāḥ bhṛśam śatam varṣa sahasrāṇām sarva loka īśvaraḥ abhavat mama eva anucaraḥ nityam bhavitāsi iti ca abravīt kuśadvīpam ca sa dadau rājyena bhagavant ajaḥ tathā śatamukhaḥ nāma dhātrā sṛṣṭaḥ mahā asuraḥ yena varṣa śatam sāgram ātma māṃsaiḥ hutaḥ analaḥ tam prāh bhagavant tuṣ kim karomi iti śaṃkara balam ca daivata śreṣṭha śāśvatam saṃprayaccha me svāyaṃbhuvaḥ kratuḥ ca api putra artham abhavat purā āviśya yogena ātmānam trīṇi varṣa śatāni api yoga īśvaram deva gītam vettha kṛṣṇa na saṃśayaḥ yājñavalkyaḥ iti khyātaḥ ṛṣiḥ parama dhārmikaḥ ārādhya sa mahādevam prāptavan jñānam uttamam vedavyāsaḥ ca yoga ātmā parāśara sutaḥ muniḥ saḥ api śaṃkaram ārādhya prāptavan atulam yaśaḥ vālakhilyāḥ maghavatā avajñātāḥ purā kila tān ca api daivata śreṣṭhaḥ prāha prītaḥ jagatpatiḥ suparṇam soma hartāram tapasā utpādayiṣyatha atreḥ bhāryā sutam dattam somam durvāsasam prabhoḥ mahādevasya roṣāt ca apaḥ naṣṭāḥ purā abhavan tāḥ ca sapta kapālena devaiḥ anyāḥ pravartitāḥ atreḥ bhāryā api bhartāram saṃtyajya brahma vādinī na aham tasya muneḥ bhūyas vaśagā syām katham cana nirāhārā bhayāt atreḥ trīṇi varṣa śatāni api aśeta musaleṣu eva prasāda artham bhavasya sā vinā bhartrā ca rudreṇa bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ vaṃśe te eva nāmnā tu khyātim yāsyati ca īpsitām śākalyaḥ saṃśita ātmā vai nava varṣa śatāni api ārādhayām āsa bhavam manaḥ yajñena keśava tam ca āha bhagavān tuṣṭaḥ granthakāraḥ bhaviṣyasi akṣayam ca kulam te astu mahā ṛṣibhiḥ alaṃkṛtam sāvarṇiḥ ca api vikhyātaḥ ṛṣiḥ āsīt kṛte yuge iha tena tapaḥ taptam ṣaṣṭim varṣa śatāni atha tad āha bhagavant rudraḥ sākṣāt tuṣ asmi te anagha śakreṇa tu purā devaḥ vārāṇasyām janārdana ārādhitaḥ abhūt bhaktena digvāsāḥ bhasma guṇṭhanaḥ ārādhya sa mahādevam deva rājyam avāptavān nāradena tu bhaktyā asau bhavaḥ ārādhitaḥ purā śākalyaḥ grantha kartā ca sāvarṇiḥ ca tathā bhavat bāṇaḥ skanda sama tvam ca kāmaḥ darpa vimokṣaṇam mayā api ca yathā dṛṣṭaḥ devadevaḥ purā vibhuḥ sākṣāt paśupatiḥ tāta tat ca api śṛṇu mādhava ārādhitaḥ mahā tejāḥ tat ca api śṛṇu vistaram mahādevaḥ mayā prabhuḥ yat avāptam ca me pūrvam devadevāt maheśvarāt purā kṛta yuge tāta ṛṣiḥ āsīt mahā yaśāḥ vyāghrapādaḥ iti khyātaḥ veda vedāṅga pāragaḥ āgaccham āśramam krīḍan munīnām bhāvitātmanām tatra api ca mayā dṛṣṭā duhyamānā payasvinī lakṣitam ca mayā kṣīram svādutaḥ hi amṛta upamam dīyatām dīyatām kṣīram mama mātar iti īritam tatas piṣṭam samāloḍya toyena saha mādhava āvayoḥ kṣīram iti eva pāna artham upanīyate atha gavyam payaḥ tāta kadā cit prāśitam mayā pitrā aham yajña kāle hi nītaḥ jñāti kulam mahat tatra sā kṣarate devī divyā gauḥ sura nandinī tasya aham tat payaḥ pītvā rasena hi amṛta upamam jñātvā kṣīra guṇān ca eva upalabhya hi saṃbhavam tatas piṣṭa rasam tāta na me prītim udāvahat tatas aham abruvam bālyāt jananīm ātmanaḥ tadā abhāvāt ca eva dugdhasya duḥkhitā jananī tadā tatas mām abravīt mātā duḥkha śoka samanvitā kutas kṣīrodanam vatsa munīnām bhāvitātmanām vane nivasatām nityam kanda mūla phala āśinām āsthitānām nadīm divyām vālakhilyaiḥ niṣevitām kutas kṣīram vana sthānām munīnām giri vāsinām pāvanānām vana āśānām vana āśrama nivāsinām grāmya āhāra nivṛttānām āraṇya phala bhojinām nadī gahvara śaileṣu tīrtheṣu vividheṣu ca tapasā japya nityānām śivaḥ naḥ paramā gatiḥ a prasādya virūpākṣam vara dam sthāṇum avyayam kutas kṣīrodanam vatsa sukhāni vasanāni ca sarva kāraṇa bhūtaḥ ayam dhātā rudraḥ trilocanaḥ aṣṭa bāhuḥ jaṭī nāga bhūṣaṇaḥ candraśekharaḥ nāga upavītī sa gaṇaḥ nīlakaṇṭhaḥ umāpatiḥ su daṃṣṭraḥ su smitaḥ nāga kuṇḍalaḥ bhasma bhāsitaḥ sarva kāma pradaḥ bhaktyā pūjitaḥ puṣpa mūlakaiḥ bhaktyā pratyakṣatām nītaḥ sarva kāma pradaḥ haraḥ jananyāḥ tat vacaḥ śrutvā tadā prabhṛti śatru han prāñjaliḥ praṇataḥ bhūtvā idam ambām acodayam kutra vā vasate devaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ vā katham ca saḥ tuṣyate vā katham śarvaḥ rūpam vā tasya kīdṛśam evam uktā tadā kṛṣṇa mātā mama suta vatsalā mūrdhani āghrāya govinda sa bāṣpa ākula locanā pramārjantī ca gātrāṇi mama vai madhusūdana ambā durādhṛṣyaḥ ca durgrāhyaḥ durdṛśyaḥ hi akṛtātmabhiḥ yasya rūpāṇi anekāni pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ sthānāni ca vicitrāṇi prasādāḥ ca api anekaśas kṛtavān yāni rūpāṇi devadevaḥ purā kila krīḍate ca yathā śarvaḥ prasīdati yathā ca vai hṛdisthaḥ sarva bhūtānām viśva rūpaḥ maheśvaraḥ bhaktānām anukampā artham darśanam ca yathāśrutam munīnām bruvatām divyām īśāna caritām kathām kṛtavān yāni rūpāṇi kathitāni divaukasaiḥ anugraha artham viprāṇām śṛṇu vatsa samāsatas tāni te kīrtayiṣyāmi yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi brahma viṣṇu sura indrāṇām rudra āditya aśvinām api viśveṣām api devānām vapuḥ dhārayate bhavaḥ narāṇām deva nārīṇām tathā preta piśācayoḥ kirāta śabarāṇām ca jalajānām anekaśas karoti bhagavān rūpam āṭavya śabarāṇi api kūrmaḥ matsyaḥ tathā śaṅkhaḥ pravāla aṅkura bhūṣaṇaḥ yakṣa rākṣasa sarpāṇām daitya dānavayoḥ api vyāghra siṃha mṛgāṇām ca tarakṣu ṛkṣa patatriṇām ulūka śva śṛgālānām rūpāṇi kurute api ca haṃsa kāka mayūrāṇām kṛkalāsaka sārasām rūpāṇi ca balākānām gṛdhra cakrāṅgayoḥ api go rūpī ca mahādevaḥ hasti aśva uṣṭra khara ākṛtiḥ chāga śārdūla rūpaḥ ca aneka mṛga rūpadhṛk aṇḍajānām ca divyānām vapuḥ dhārayate bhavaḥ daṇḍī chatrī ca kuṇḍī ca dvijānām dhāraṇaḥ tathā aneka pāṇi pārśvaḥ ca aneka gaṇa saṃvṛtaḥ ṛṣi gandharva rūpaḥ ca siddha cāraṇa rūpadhṛk bhasma pāṇḍura gātraḥ ca candra ardha kṛta bhūṣaṇaḥ aneka rāva saṃghuṣṭaḥ ca aneka stuti saṃstutaḥ sarva bhūta antakaḥ sarvaḥ sarva loka pratiṣṭhitaḥ cakrī śūlī gadā pāṇiḥ musalī khaḍga paṭṭiśī bhūdharaḥ nāgamauñjī ca nāga kuṇḍala kuṇḍalī nāga yajña upavītī ca nāga carma uttaracchadaḥ vādayati api vādyāni vicitrāṇi gaṇaiḥ vṛtaḥ unmatta matta rūpam ca bhāṣate ca api susvaraḥ dadāti pratigṛhṇāti yuñjate dhyāyate api ca vedī madhye tathā yūpe goṣṭha madhye hutāśane dṛśyate dṛśyate ca api bālaḥ vṛddhaḥ yuvā tathā krīḍate ṛṣi kanyābhiḥ ṛṣi patnībhiḥ eva ca ūrdhva keśaḥ mahā śephaḥ nagnaḥ vikṛta locanaḥ gauraḥ śyāmaḥ tathā kṛṣṇaḥ pāṇḍuraḥ dhūma lohitaḥ arūpasya ādi arūpasya atirūpa ādi arūpiṇaḥ hṛdi prāṇaḥ manaḥ jīvaḥ yoga ātmā yoga saṃjñitaḥ dhyānam tat paramātmā ca bhāva grāhyaḥ maheśvaraḥ jananyāḥ tat vacaḥ śrutvā tadā prabhṛti śatru han tatas aham tapaḥ āsthāya toṣayām āsa śaṃkaram divyam varṣa sahasram tu pādāṅguṣṭha agra viṣṭhitaḥ ekam varṣa śatam ca eva phala āhāraḥ tadā abhavam dvitīyam śīrṇa parṇa āśī tṛtīyam ca ambu bhojanaḥ śatāni sapta ca eva aham vāyubhakṣaḥ tadā abhavam evam varṣa sahasram tu divyam ārādhitaḥ mayā tatas prītaḥ mahādevaḥ sarva loka īśvaraḥ prabhuḥ eka bhaktaḥ iti jñātvā jijñāsām kurute tadā śakra rūpam sa kṛtvā tu sarvaiḥ deva gaṇaiḥ vṛtaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ tadā bhūtvā vajrapāṇiḥ mahā yaśāḥ sudhā avadātam rakta akṣam stabdha karṇam mada utkaṭam āveṣṭita karam raudram catur daṃṣṭram mahā gajam samāsthā ca bhagavant dīp sva tejas ājagāma kirīṭī tu hāra keyūra bhūṣitaḥ pāṇḍureṇa ātapatreṇa dhriyamāṇena mūrdhani śakrasya tu vacaḥ śrutvā na aham prīta manāḥ abhavam abruvam ca tadā kṛṣṇa devarājam idam vacaḥ na aham tvattaḥ varam kāṅkṣe na anyasmāt api daivatāt satyam kauśika saṃsārāt mā mama astu vinirvṛtiḥ adya maheśvara baddhā kathā mama anyā priyā śrotum paśupati vacana bhavāmi sadyas kṛmiḥ atha vā taruḥ api aneka śākhaḥ yeṣām na kṣaṇam api rucitaḥ hara caraṇa smaraṇa vicchedaḥ divasam divasa ardham vā muhūrtam vā kṣaṇam lavam api kīṭaḥ pataṃgaḥ vā bhaveyam śaṃkara ājñayā śvā api maheśvara vacanāt bhavāmi sa hi naḥ paraḥ kāmaḥ na nāka pṛṣṭham na ca deva rājyam na sarva kāmān akhilān vṛṇomi harasya dāsa tvam aham vṛṇomi yāvat śaśāṅka śakala amala baddha mauliḥ na prīyate paśupatiḥ bhagavant mama īśaḥ tāvat jarā maraṇa janma śata abhighātaiḥ duḥkhāni deha vihitāni samudvahāmi divasakara śaśāṅka vahni dīptam tribhuvana sāram apāram ādyam ekam dhik teṣām dhik teṣām punar api dhik astu dhik teṣām uvāca kaḥ punar tava hetuḥ vai īśe kāraṇa kāraṇe yena devāt ṛte anyasmāt prasādam na abhikāṅkṣasi ātmānam paramam yasmāt varam tasmāt vṛṇīmahe abījāt bīja saṃbhūtam varam tasmāt vṛṇīmahe yam jñātvā na anuśocanti varam tasmāt vṛṇīmahe bhūta bhāvana bhāva jñam sarva bhūta abhibhāvanam sarvagam sarva dam devam pūjayāmi puraṃdara yam upāsanti tattva jñāḥ varam tasmāt vṛṇīmahe sarva bhūta gurum devam varam tasmāt vṛṇīmahe yaḥ pūrvam asṛjat devam brahmāṇam loka bhāvanam aṇḍam ākāśam āpūrya varam tasmāt vṛṇīmahe agniḥ apaḥ anilaḥ pṛthvī kham buddhiḥ ca manaḥ mahān sraṣṭā ca eṣām bhavet yaḥ anyaḥ brūhi kaḥ parameśvarāt manaḥ matiḥ ahaṃkāraḥ tanmātrāṇi indriyāṇi ca brūhi ca eṣām bhavet śakra kaḥ anyaḥ asti paramaḥ śivāt sraṣṭāram bhuvanasya iha vadanti iha pitāmaham ārādhya sa tu deveśam aśnute mahatīm śriyam vidyate vai mahādevāt brūhi kaḥ parameśvarāt kaḥ anyaḥ śaknoti deveśāt ṛte saṃpāditum sutān diś kāla sūrya tejāṃsi graha vāyu indu tārakāḥ kim ca atra bahubhiḥ sūktaiḥ hetuvādaiḥ puraṃdara sahasranayanam dṛṣṭvā tvām eva sura sattama cetana acetana ādyeṣu śakra viddhi maheśvarāt bhuva ādyeṣu mahā anteṣu loka aloka antareṣu ca dvīpa sthāneṣu meroḥ ca vibhaveṣu antareṣu ca yadi devāḥ surāḥ śakra paśyanti anyām bhava ākṛtim kim na gacchanti śaraṇam marditāḥ ca asuraiḥ surāḥ abhighāteṣu devānām sa yakṣa uraga rakṣasām vara dāna avaghātāya brūhi kaḥ anyaḥ maheśvarāt kasya ca ardhe sthitā kāntā anaṅgaḥ kena nirjitaḥ brūhi indra paramam sthānam kasya devaiḥ praśasyate śmaśāne kasya krīḍā artham nṛtye vā kaḥ abhibhāṣyate kasya aiśvaryam samānam vā bhūtaiḥ kaḥ vā api krīḍate kasya tulya balāḥ deva gaṇāḥ aiśvarya darpitāḥ kasmāt oṣadhi saṃpattiḥ kaḥ vā dhārayate vasu prakāmam krīḍate kaḥ vā trailokye sacarācare jñāna siddhi kriyā yogaiḥ sevyamānaḥ ca yogibhiḥ ṛṣi gandharva siddhaiḥ ca vihitam kāraṇam param karma yajña kriyā yogaiḥ sevyamānaḥ sura asuraiḥ nityam karma phalaiḥ hīnam tam aham kāraṇam vade sthūlam sūkṣmam anaupamyam agrāhyam guṇa gocaram guṇa hīnam guṇa adhyakṣam param māheśvaram padam viśveśam kāraṇa gurum loka aloka anta kāraṇam bhūta a bhūta bhaviṣyat ca janakam sarva kāraṇam akṣara akṣaram avyaktam vidyā avidye kṛta akṛte dharma adharmau yatas śakra tam aham kāraṇam vade devadevena rudreṇa sṛṣṭi saṃhāra hetunā mātrā pūrvam mama ākhyātam kāraṇam loka kāraṇam na asti ca īśāt param śakra tam prapadya yadi icchasi na anyam kāma sahasra kalpita dhiyaḥ śaṃsanti īśāt param kāma arthī varayāmi saṃyata manāḥ mokṣāya śarvam śivam hetubhiḥ vā kim anyaiḥ te īśaḥ kāraṇa kāraṇam yasya brahmā ca viṣṇuḥ ca tvam ca api saha daivataiḥ arcayadhvam sadā liṅgam tasmāt śreṣṭhatamaḥ hi saḥ na padma aṅkāḥ na cakra aṅkāḥ na vajra aṅkāḥ yatas prajāḥ liṅgāṅkā ca bhagāṅkā ca tasmāt māheśvarī prajā devyāḥ kāraṇa rūpa bhāva janitāḥ sarvāḥ bhaga aṅkāḥ striyaḥ liṅgena api harasya sarva puruṣāḥ pratyakṣa cihnīkṛtāḥ yaḥ anyat kāraṇam īśvarāt pravadate devyā ca yat na aṅkitam puṃliṅgam sarvam īśānam strī liṅgam viddhi ca api umām dvābhyām tanubhyām vyāptam hi carācaram idam jagat tasmāt varam aham kāṅkṣe nidhanam vā api kauśika gaccha vā tiṣṭha vā śakra yatheṣṭam balasūdana kāmam eṣa varaḥ mama astu śāpaḥ vā api maheśvarāt na ca anyām devatām kāṅkṣe sarva kāma phalāni api atha apaśyam kṣaṇena eva tam eva airāvatam punar haṃsa kunda indu sadṛśam mṛṇāla kumuda prabham vṛṣa rūpa dharam sākṣāt kṣīrodam iva sāgaram kṛṣṇa puccham mahā kāyam madhu piṅgala locanam vajra sāra mayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ niṣṭapta kanaka prabhaiḥ jāmbūnadena dāmnā ca sarvatas samalaṃkṛtam rakta akṣam su mahā nāsam su karṇam su kaṭi taṭam su pārśvam vipula skandham surūpam cāru darśanam kakudam tasya ca ābhāti skandham āpūrya viṣṭhitam tuṣāragiri kūṭa ābham sita abhra śikhara upamam śobhata mahādevaḥ paurṇamāsyām iva uḍurāj kirīṭam ca jaṭā bhāraḥ sarpa ādi ābharaṇāni ca vajra ādi śūla mātaṃga gambhīra smitam āgatam sahasram iva sūryāṇām sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati īśvaraḥ su mahā tejāḥ saṃvartakaḥ iva analaḥ tejasā tu tadā vyāpte durnirīkṣye samantataḥ praśāntam ca kṣaṇena eva devadevasya māyayā atha apaśyam sthitam sthāṇum bhagavantam maheśvaram sahita cāru sarva aṅga pārvatī parameśvaram nīlakaṇṭha mahātmānam asakta tejasām nidhim aṣṭādaśa bhujam sthāṇum sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitam śukla ambara dharam devam śukla mālya anulepanam śukla dhvajam anādhṛṣyam śukla yajña upavītinam vṛtam pāriṣadaiḥ divyaiḥ ātma tulya parākramaiḥ bāla indu mukuṭam pāṇḍum śarad candram iva uditam jātarūpa mayaiḥ padmaiḥ grathitā ratna bhūṣitā mayā dṛṣṭāni govinda bhavasya amita tejasaḥ sapta śīrṣaḥ mahā kāyaḥ tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭraḥ viṣa ulbaṇaḥ jyā veṣṭita mahā grīvaḥ sthitaḥ puruṣa vigrahaḥ śaraḥ ca sūrya saṃkāśaḥ kāla anala sama dyutiḥ sahasra bhuja jihvā āsyaḥ bhīṣaṇaḥ nāga vigrahaḥ śaṅkha śūla asibhiḥ ca eva paṭṭasaiḥ rūpavān sthitaḥ rāma niḥkṣatriya karaḥ paraśuḥ śaṃkara ājñayā yat tat astram mahā ghoram divyam pāśupatam mahat sa sphuliṅgam mahā kāyam visṛjantam iva analam eka pādam mahā daṃṣṭram sahasra śirasā udaram brāhmāt nārāyaṇāt aindrāt āgneyāt api vāruṇāt yat viśiṣṭam mahā bāho sarva śastra vighātanam yena tat tripuram dagdhvā kṣaṇāt bhasmīkṛtam purā śūlam ca yauvana aśva ghnam lavaṇasya kare sthitam evam dṛṣṭvā mahādevam jānubhyām avanīm gataḥ maheśvara bhuja utsṛṣṭam nimeṣa ardhāt na saṃśayaḥ tat aham dṛṣṭavān tāta āścarya adbhutam uttamam yat tat śūlam iti khyātam sarva lokeṣu śūlinaḥ dārayet yat mahīm kṛtsnām śoṣayet vā mahā udadhim saṃharet vā jagat kṛtsnam visṛṣṭam śūlapāṇinā yauvanāśvaḥ hataḥ yena māṃdhātā sa balaḥ purā cakravartī mahā tejāḥ triloka vijayī nṛpaḥ mahā balaḥ mahā vīryaḥ śakra tulya parākramaḥ tat śūlam ati tīkṣṇa agram su bhīmam loma harṣaṇam tri śikhām bhrukuṭim kṛtvā tarjamānam iva sthitam vidhūmam sa arciṣam kṛṣṇam kālasūryam iva uditam paraśuḥ tīkṣṇa dhāraḥ ca dattaḥ rāmasya yaḥ purā paramam tīkṣṇa sāreṇa śastram tasya api yat purā mahādevena tuṣṭena kṣatriyāṇām kṣayaṃkaraḥ tris sapta kṛtvas pṛthivī yena niḥkṣatriyā kṛtā jāmadagnyena govinda rāmeṇa akliṣṭa karmaṇā dīpta dhāraḥ su raudra āsyaḥ sarpa kaṇṭha agra veṣṭay asaṃkhyeyāni ca astrāṇi tasya divyāni dhīmataḥ prādhānyataḥ mayā etāni kīrtitāni te anagha vāma pārśva gataḥ ca eva tathā nārāyaṇaḥ sthitaḥ vainateyam samāsthāya śaṅkha cakra gadā dharaḥ skandaḥ mayūram āsthāya sthitaḥ devyāḥ samīpatas śaktim kaṇṭhe samādāya dvitīyaḥ iva pāvakaḥ śūlam viṣṭabhya tiṣṭhantam dvitīyam iva śaṃkaram svāyambhuva ādyāḥ manavaḥ bhṛgu ādyāḥ ṛṣayaḥ tathā śakra ādyāḥ devatāḥ ca eva sarve eva samabhyayuḥ sarva bhūta gaṇāḥ ca eva mātaraḥ vividhāḥ sthitāḥ tad abhivāday mahātmānam parivārya samantataḥ jagat mūrtim mahā liṅgam tad madhye sphīta rūpiṇam jyeṣṭhasāmnā ca deveśam jagau nārāyaṇaḥ tadā gṛ śakraḥ param brahma śatarudrīyam uttamam brahmā nārāyaṇaḥ ca eva devarājaḥ ca kauśikaḥ teṣām madhya gam devaḥ rarāja bhagavat śivaḥ śarad ghana vinirmuktaḥ pariviṣṭaḥ iva aṃśumant ayutāni ca candra arkān apaśyam divi keśava śakrāya śakra rūpāya śakra veṣa dharāya ca namaḥ te vajrahastāya piṅgalāya aruṇāya ca pinākapāṇaye nityam khaḍga śūla dharāya ca namaḥ te kṛṣṇa vāsāya kṛṣṇa kuñcita mūrdhaje kṛṣṇājina uttarīyāya kṛṣṇāṣṭam irata ca śukla varṇāya śuklāya śukla ambara dharāya ca namaḥ astu pīta varṇāya pīta ambara dharāya ca namaḥ astu ucchrita chatrāya kirīṭa vara dhāriṇe ardha hāra ardha keyūra ardha kuṇḍala karṇine namaḥ padma ardha mālāya utpalaiḥ miśritāya ca saumya rūpāya mukhyāya saumya daṃṣṭra vibhūṣaṇe namaḥ śyāmāya gaurāya ardha pīta ardha pāṇḍure nārī nara śarīrāya strīpuṃsāya namaḥ astu te namaḥ astu gaṇa gītāya gaṇa vṛnda ratāya ca gaṇa anuyāta mārgāya gaṇa nitya vratāya ca namaḥ śveta abhra varṇāya saṃdhyā rāga prabhāya ca an uddiṣṭa abhidhānāya svarūpāya namaḥ astu te maṇi bhūṣita mūrdhāya namaḥ candra ardha bhūṣiṇe vicitra maṇi mūrdhāya kusuma aṣṭa dharāya ca bhūcarāya bhuvanāya anantāya śivāya ca sarpa kaṇṭha upahārāya vicitra ābharaṇāya ca strīpuṃsāya napuṃsāya namaḥ sāṃkhyāya yogine namaḥ sarva ārti nāśāya namaḥ śoka harāya ca bīja kṣetra adhipālāya sraṣṭārāya namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ sura asura īśāya viśveśāya namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ kāñcana mālāya giri mālāya vai namaḥ namaḥ surāri mālāya caṇḍavegāya vai namaḥ namaḥ strī rūpa dhārāya sarva rūpa dharāya ca namaḥ kāma aṅga nāśāya kāla daṇḍa dharāya ca namaḥ skanda viśākhāya brahmadaṇḍāya vai namaḥ namaḥ bhavāya śarvāya viśvarūpāya vai namaḥ īśānāya bhagaghnāya namaḥ astu andhakaghātine namaḥ viśvāya māyāya cintya acintyāya vai namaḥ tvam brahmā sarva devānām rudrāṇām nīlalohitaḥ ātmā ca sarva bhūtānām sāṃkhye puruṣaḥ ucyase ṛṣabhaḥ tvam pavitrāṇām yogin niṣkalaḥ śivaḥ āśramāṇām gṛhasthaḥ tvam īśvarāṇām mahā īśvaraḥ kuberaḥ sarva yakṣa kratūnām viṣṇuḥ ucyase parvatānām mahat meruḥ nakṣatrāṇām ca candramas vasiṣṭhaḥ tvam ṛṣīṇām ca grahānām sūryaḥ ucyase āraṇyānām paśūnām ca siṃhaḥ tvam parameśvaraḥ grāmyāṇām go vṛṣaḥ ca asi bhagavān loka pūjitaḥ ādityānām bhavān viṣṇuḥ vasūnām ca eva pāvakaḥ pakṣiṇām vainateyaḥ ca anantaḥ bhujageṣu ca sāmavedaḥ ca vedānām yajuṣām śatarudriyam sanatkumāraḥ sāṃkhyānām kapilaḥ hi asi śakraḥ asi marutām deva pitṝṇām dharma rāj asi brahma lokaḥ ca lokānām gatīnām mokṣaḥ ucyase kṣīroda sāgara ca śaila himavant giri varṇānām brāhmaṇaḥ ca asi viprāṇām dīkṣitaḥ dvijaḥ ādiḥ tvam asi lokānām saṃhartā kālaḥ eva ca yad ca aparādham kṛ ajñānāt parameśvara mohitaḥ ca asmi deveśa tubhyam rūpa viparyayāt tena na arghyam mayā dattam pādyam ca api sureśvara evam stu aham īśānam pādyam arghyam ca bhaktitaḥ kṛta añjali puṭaḥ bhūtvā sarvam tasmai nyavedayam tatas śīta ambu saṃyuktā divya gandha samanvitā puṣpa vṛṣṭiḥ śubhā tāta papāta mama mūrdhani vavau ca mārutaḥ puṇyaḥ śuci gandhaḥ sukha āvahaḥ tatas prītaḥ mahādevaḥ sa patnīkaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ abravīt tridaśān tatra harṣayan iva mām tadā paśyadhvam tridaśāḥ sarve upamanyoḥ mahātmanaḥ mayi bhaktim parām divyām eka bhāvāt avasthitām evam uktāḥ tatas kṛṣṇa surāḥ te śūlapāṇinā ūcuḥ prāñjalayaḥ sarve namaskṛtvā vṛṣadhvajam āha mām bhagavant īśaḥ prahas iva śaṃkaraḥ dṛḍha bhaktaḥ asi viprarṣe mayā jijñāsitaḥ hi asi tasmāt sarvān dadāmi adya kāmān tava yathā īpśitān harṣāt aśrūṇi avartanta loma harṣaḥ ca jāyate abruvam ca tadā devam harṣa gadgadayā girā jānubhyām avanim gam praṇamya ca punar punar yat mad sākṣāt mahādevaḥ prasannaḥ tiṣṭhate agratas tam aham dṛṣṭavan devam kaḥ anyaḥ dhanyataraḥ mayā evam dhyā vidvas para tattvam sanātana ṣaḍviṃśakam iti khyātam yat parātparam akṣaram sarva tattva vidhāna jñaḥ pradhāna puruṣa īśvaraḥ yaḥ asṛjat dakṣiṇāt aṅgāt brahmāṇam loka saṃbhavam vāma pārśvāt tathā viṣṇum loka rakṣā artham īśvaraḥ yuga ante ca eva saṃprāpte rudram aṅgāt sṛjat prabhuḥ kālaḥ bhūtvā mahā tejāḥ saṃvartakaḥ iva analaḥ eṣa devaḥ mahādevaḥ jagat sṛṣṭvā carācaram kalpa ante ca eva sarveṣām smṛtim ākṣipya tiṣṭhati abravam tam aham bhūyas praṇamya śirasā bhavam tam tvām praṇamya śirasā prasādya prārthaye prabho bhaktiḥ bhavatu me nityam śāśvatā tvayi śaṃkara atī anāgata ca eva vartamāna ca yad vibhu kṣīrodanam ca bhuñjīyām akṣayam saha bāndhavaiḥ āśrame ca sadā mahyam sāṃnidhyam param astu te evam uktaḥ sa mām prāha bhagavān loka pūjitaḥ maheśvaraḥ mahā tejāḥ carācara guruḥ prabhuḥ yaśasvī tejasā yuktaḥ divya jñāna samanvitaḥ ṛṣīṇām abhigamyaḥ ca mad prasādāt bhaviṣyasi śīlavān guṇa saṃpannaḥ sarvajñaḥ priya darśanaḥ tatra te bhavitā kāmam sāṃnidhyam payasaḥ nidheḥ tatra tatra eva sāṃnidhyam kariṣyati na saṃśayaḥ akṣayāḥ bāndhavāḥ ca eva kulam gotram ca te sadā bhaviṣyati dvijaśreṣṭha mayi bhaktiḥ ca śāśvatā sāṃnidhyam āśrame nityam kariṣyāmi dvijottama tiṣṭha vatsa yathākāmam na utkaṇṭhām kartum arhasi smṛtaḥ smṛtaḥ ca te vipra sadā dāsyāmi darśanam mama īśānaḥ varam dattvā tatra eva antaradhīyata evam dṛṣṭaḥ mayā kṛṣṇa devadevaḥ samādhinā tat avāptam ca me sarvam yat uktam tena dhīmatā pratyakṣam ca eva te kṛṣṇa paśya siddhān vyavasthitān ṛṣīn vidyādharān yakṣān gandharva apsarasaḥ tathā paśya vṛkṣān manaḥ ramyān sadā puṣpa phala anvitān paśya vṛkṣa latā gulmān sarva puṣpa phala pradān prasādāt devadevasya īśvarasya mahātmanaḥ uvāca vismayam paramam gatvā abruvam tam mahā munim api tāvat mama api evam dadyāt sa bhagavant śivaḥ darśanam muni śārdūla prasādam ca api śaṃkaraḥ drakṣyase puṇḍarīkākṣa mahādevam na saṃśayaḥ acireṇa eva kālena yathā dṛṣṭaḥ mayā anagha ṣaṣṭhe māsi mahādevam drakṣyase puruṣottama ṣoḍaśa aṣṭau varān ca api prāpsyasi tvam maheśvarāt sa patnīkāt yadu śreṣṭha satyam etat bravīmi te atīta anāgatam ca eva vartamānam ca nityaśas viditam mama mahā bāho prasādāt tasya dhīmataḥ etān sahasraśas ca anyān samanudhyātavan haraḥ tvādṛśena hi devānām ślāghanīyaḥ samāgamaḥ brahmaṇyena anṛśaṃsena śraddadhānena ca api uta uvāca drakṣye ditija saṃghānām mardanam tridaśeśvaram evam kathayataḥ tasya mahādeva āśritām kathām dine aṣṭame ca vipreṇa dīkṣitaḥ aham yathāvidhi daṇḍī muṇḍī kuśī cīrī ghṛta aktaḥ mekhalī tathā māsam ekam phala āhāraḥ dvitīyam salila aśanaḥ tṛtīyam ca caturtham ca pañcamam ca anila aśanaḥ eka pādena tiṣṭhan ca ūrdhvabāhuḥ atandritaḥ tasya madhya gatam ca api tejasaḥ pāṇḍu nandana indrāyudha pinaddha aṅgam vidyut mālā gavākṣakam nīla śaila caya prakhyam balākā bhūṣitam ghanam tapasā tejasā kāntyā dīptayā saha bhāryayā rarāja bhagavant tatra devyā saha maheśvaraḥ apaśyam deva saṃghānām gatim ārti haram haram kirīṭinam gadinam śūla pāṇim vyāghra ajinam jaṭilam daṇḍa pāṇim pinākinam vajriṇam tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭram śubha aṅgadam vyāla yajñopavītam divyām mālām urasā aneka varṇām samudvahantam gulpha deśa avalambām candram yathā pariviṣṭam sa saṃdhyam varṣā atyaye tadvat apaśyam enam maheśvaram nandi vināyaka ādyaiḥ pramathānām gaṇaiḥ ca eva samantāt parivāritam śaradi iva su duṣprekṣyam pariviṣṭam divākaram ekādaśa tathā ca enam rudrāṇām vṛṣavāhanam ekādaśāḥ gatāḥ ca eva rudrāḥ ca enam sukha āvaham ādityāḥ vasavaḥ sādhyāḥ viśvedevāḥ tathā aśvinaḥ śatakratu ca bhagavant viṣṇuḥ ca aditi nandanau yogi īśvarāḥ su bahavaḥ yoga dam pitaram gurum pṛthivī ca antarikṣam ca nakṣatrāṇi grahāḥ tathā māsa ardha māsāḥ ṛtavaḥ rātryaḥ saṃvatsarāḥ kṣaṇāḥ muhūrtāḥ ca nimeṣāḥ ca tathā eva yuga paryayāḥ divyāḥ rājan namasyanti vidyāḥ sarvāḥ diśaḥ tathā marīciḥ aṅgirāḥ atriḥ pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ bhṛguḥ dakṣaḥ kaśyapaḥ ca vasiṣṭhaḥ kāśyaḥ eva ca chandāṃsi dīkṣāḥ yajñāḥ ca dakṣiṇāḥ pāvakaḥ haviḥ yajña upagāni dravyāṇi mūrtimanti yudhiṣṭhira prajānām patayaḥ sarve saritaḥ pannagāḥ nagāḥ devānām mātaraḥ sarvāḥ deva patnyaḥ sa kanyakāḥ sahasrāṇi munīnām ca ayutāni arbudāni ca namasyanti prabhum śāntam parvatāḥ sāgarāḥ diśaḥ vṛkṣa oṣadhyaḥ ca rāja indra dhātavaḥ vividhāḥ tathā vidyādharāḥ dānavāḥ ca guhyakāḥ rākṣasāḥ tathā sarvāṇi ca eva bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca purastāt viṣṭhitaḥ śarvaḥ mama āsīt tridaśeśvaraḥ purastāt viṣṭhitam dṛṣṭvā mama īśānam ca bhārata īkṣitum ca mahādevam na me śaktiḥ abhūt tadā tatas mām abravīt devaḥ paśya kṛṣṇa vadasva ca tvayā hi ārādhitaḥ ca aham śataśas atha sahasraśas śirasā vandite deve devī prītā umā bhavat tatas aham astuvam sthāṇum stutam brahma ādibhiḥ suraiḥ tatas astuvam devadevam devīm ca śubha lakṣaṇām yoga īśvarāḥ su bahavaḥ maheśam bahudhā astuvan mahābhūtāni chandāṃsi prajānām patayaḥ makhāḥ saritaḥ sāgarāḥ nāgāḥ gandharva apsarasaḥ tathā vidyādharāḥ ca gītena vādya nṛtta ādinā arcayan īkṣitum ca mahādevam na mama śaktiḥ abhūt tadā dṛṣṭvā devam tathā devīm astuvam saṃstutam suraiḥ dhātā tvaṣṭā vidhātā ca tvam prabhuḥ sarvatomukhaḥ tvattaḥ jātāni bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca tvam ādiḥ sarva bhūtānām saṃhāraḥ ca tvam eva hi tvayā sṛṣṭam idam kṛtsnam trailokyam sacarācaram ye ca indriya arthāḥ ca manaḥ ca kṛtsnam ye vāyavaḥ sapta tathā eva ca agniḥ ye vā divi sthāḥ devatāḥ ca api puṃsām tasmāt param tvām ṛṣayaḥ vadanti vedāḥ yajñāḥ ca somaḥ ca dakṣiṇā pāvakaḥ haviḥ yajña upagam ca yat kim cit bhagavant tat asaṃśayam iṣṭam dattam adhītam ca vratāni niyamāḥ ca ye hrīḥ kīrtiḥ śrīḥ dyutiḥ tuṣṭiḥ siddhiḥ ca eva tvad arpaṇā kṛtiḥ vikāraḥ pralayaḥ pradhānam prabhavaḥ avyayaḥ manasaḥ paramā yoniḥ svabhāvaḥ ca api śāśvataḥ avyaktaḥ pāvana vibho sahasrāṃśo hiraṇmayaḥ ādiḥ guṇānām sarveṣām bhavān vai jīvana āśrayaḥ mahān ātmā matiḥ brahmā viśvaḥ śaṃbhuḥ svayambhoḥ buddhiḥ prajñā upalabdhiḥ ca saṃvid khyātiḥ dhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥ paryāya vācakaiḥ śabdaiḥ mahant ātmā vibhāvyase tvām buddhvā brāhmaṇaḥ vidvān na pramoham nigacchati hṛdayam sarva bhūtānām kṣetrajñaḥ tvam ṛṣiṣṭutaḥ sarvatas pāṇi pādaḥ tvam sarvatas akṣi śiraḥ mukhaḥ sarvatas śrutimān loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhasi phalam tvam asi tigmāṃśo nimeṣa ādiṣu karmasu tvam vai prabhā arciḥ puruṣaḥ sarvasya hṛdi saṃsthitaḥ aṇimā laghimā prāptiḥ īśānaḥ jyotiḥ avyayaḥ tvayi buddhiḥ matiḥ lokāḥ prapannāḥ saṃśritāḥ ca ye dhyāninaḥ nitya yogāḥ ca satya saṃdhāḥ jita indriyāḥ yaḥ tvām dhruvam vedayate guhā āśayam prabhum purāṇam puruṣam viśva rūpam hiraṇmayam buddhimatām parām gatim sa buddhimān buddhim atītya tiṣṭhati viditvā sapta sūkṣmāṇi ṣaṣ aṅgam tvām ca mūrtyāḥ carācaram jagat sarvam siṃhanādam atha akarot sa vipra saṃghāḥ ca sura asurāḥ ca nāgāḥ piśācāḥ pitaraḥ vayāṃsi rakṣaḥ gaṇāḥ bhūta gaṇāḥ ca sarve mahā ṛṣayaḥ ca eva tathā praṇemuḥ mama mūrdhni ca divyānām kusumānām sugandhinām nirīkṣ bhagavant devīm umā mām ca jagat hitaḥ śatakratum ca abhivīkṣya svayam mām āha śaṃkaraḥ vidmaḥ kṛṣṇa parām bhaktim asmāsu tava śatru han kriyatām ātmanaḥ śreyaḥ prītiḥ hi paramā tvayi vṛṇīṣva aṣṭau varān kṛṣṇa dātāsmi te sattama brūhi yādavaśārdūla yān icchasi su durlabhān uvāca mūrdhnā praṇamya tu bhavam devam īśānam avyayam dharme dṛḍha tvam yudhi śatru ghātam yaśaḥ tathā agryam paramam balam ca yoga priya tvam tava saṃnikarṣam vṛṇe sutānām ca śatam śatāni evam astu iti tat vākyam mayā uktaḥ prāha śaṃkaraḥ tatas mām jagataḥ mātā dharaṇī sarva pāvanī uvāca umā praṇihitā śarvāṇī tapasām nidhiḥ mattaḥ api aṣṭau varān iṣṭān gṛhāṇa tvam dadāmi te praṇamya śirasā tā ca mayā uktā pāṇḍu nandana dvijeṣu akopam pitṛtaḥ prasādam śatam sutānām upabhogam param ca kule prītim mātṛtas ca prasādam śama prāptim pravṛṇe ca api dākṣyam evam bhaviṣyati amara prabhāva na aham mṛṣā jātu vade kadā cit bhāryā sahasrāṇi ca ṣoḍaśa eva tāsu priya tvam ca tathā akṣaya tvam prītim ca agrya bāndhavānām sakāśāt dadāmi te vapuṣaḥ kāmya tām ca gṛhe ca tubhyam prītimatām śatāni uvāca antarhitaḥ kṣaṇe tasmin sa gaṇaḥ bhīmapūrvaja etat ati adbhutam sarvam brāhmaṇāya ati tejase na asti śarva samaḥ dāne na asti śarva samaḥ raṇe na asti śarva samaḥ devaḥ na asti śarva samā gatiḥ ṛṣiḥ āsīt kṛte tāta taṇḍiḥ iti eva viśrutaḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi tena devaḥ samādhinā ārādhitaḥ abhūt bhaktena tasya udarkam niśāmaya sa dṛṣṭavan mahādevam astauṣīt ca stavaiḥ vibhum yam paṭhanti sadā sāṃkhyāḥ cintayanti ca yoginaḥ param pradhānam puruṣam adhiṣṭhātāram īśvaram utpattau ca vināśe ca kāraṇam yam viduḥ budhāḥ deva asura munīnām ca param yasmāt na vidyate ajam tam aham īśānam an ādi nidhanam prabhum yoginām parama ānandam akṣaram mokṣa saṃjñitam durvijñeyam asaṃkhyeyam duṣprāpam akṛtātmabhiḥ param purāṇam puruṣam parebhyaḥ paratas param yaḥ prāṇavantam ātmānam jyotiḥ jīva sthitam manaḥ tam devam darśana ākāṅkṣī bahūn varṣa gaṇān ṛṣiḥ tapasi ugre sthitaḥ bhūtvā dṛṣṭvā tuṣṭāva ca īśvaram pavitrāṇām pavitraḥ tvam gatiḥ gatimatām vara ati ugram tejasām tejaḥ tapasām paramam tapaḥ viśvāvasu hiraṇyākṣa puruhūta namaskṛta jātī maraṇa bhīrūṇām yatīnām yatatām vibho nirvāṇa da sahasrāṃśo namaḥ te astu sukha āśraya brahmā śatakratuḥ viṣṇuḥ viśvedevāḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ kāla ākhyaḥ puruṣa ākhyaḥ ca brahma ākhyaḥ ca tvam eva hi tanavaḥ te smṛtāḥ tisraḥ purāṇa jñaiḥ sura ṛṣibhiḥ vidvasaḥ yānti nirmuktāḥ param bhāvam anāmayam dvāram tvam svarga mokṣāṇām ākṣeptā tvam dadāsi ca brahmā viṣṇuḥ ca rudraḥ ca skanda indrau savitā yamaḥ varuṇa indū manuḥ dhātā vidhātā tvam dhaneśvaraḥ bhūḥ vāyuḥ jyotiḥ apaḥ ca vāc buddhiḥ tvam matiḥ manaḥ indriyāṇi indriya arthāḥ ca tad param prakṛtyāḥ dhruvam yā gatiḥ sāṃkhya yogānām sa bhavān na atra saṃśayaḥ nūnam adya kṛtārthāḥ sma nūnam prāptāḥ satām gatim yām gatim prāpnuvanti iha jñāna nirmala buddhayaḥ aho mūḍhāḥ sma su ciram imam kālam acetasaḥ yat na vidmaḥ param devam śāśvatam yam viduḥ budhāḥ saḥ ayam āsāditaḥ sākṣāt bahubhiḥ janmabhiḥ mayā bhakta anugraha kṛt devaḥ yam jñātvā amṛtam aśnute deva asura manuṣyāṇām yat ca guhyam sanātanam sarva ātmā sarva darśī ca sarva gaḥ sarva veditā prāṇa kṛt prāṇabhṛt prāṇī prāṇa daḥ prāṇinām gatiḥ deha kṛt deha bhṛt dehī deha bhuj dehinām gatiḥ adhyātma gati niṣṭhānām dhyāninām ātma vedinām a punarmāra kāmānām yā gatiḥ saḥ ayam īśvaraḥ ayam ca sarva bhūtānām śubha aśubha gati pradaḥ ayam ca siddhi kāmānām ṛṣīṇām siddhi daḥ prabhuḥ ayam ca mokṣa kāmānām dvijānām mokṣa daḥ prabhuḥ asmin ca pralayam yāti ayam ekaḥ sanātanaḥ ayam sa satya kāmānām satya lokaḥ paraḥ satām apavargaḥ ca muktānām kaivalyam ca ātma vādinām ayam brahma ādibhiḥ siddhaiḥ guhāyām gopitaḥ prabhuḥ deva asura manuṣyāṇām na prakāśaḥ bhavet iti teṣām eva ātmanā ātmānam darśayati eṣa hṛcchayaḥ yam jñātvā na punarjanma maraṇam ca api vidyate yam labdhvā paramam lābham manyate na adhikam punar prāṇa sūkṣmām parām prāptim āgacchati akṣaya āvahām yam sāṃkhyāḥ guṇa tattva jñāḥ sāṃkhya śāstra viśāradāḥ sūkṣma jñāna ratāḥ pūrvam jñātvā mucyanti bandhanaiḥ prāṇāyāma pare nityam yam viśanti japanti ca ayam sa deva yānānām ādityaḥ dvāram ucyate ayam ca pitṛ yānānām candramāḥ dvāram ucyate eṣa kāla gatiḥ citrā saṃvatsara yuga ādiṣu bhāva abhāvau tadātve ca ayane dakṣiṇa uttare evam prajāpatiḥ pūrvam ārādhya bahu stavaiḥ sāmabhiḥ yam ca gāyanti sāmagāḥ śuddha buddhayaḥ ṛtam satyam param brahma stuvanti ātharvaṇāḥ dvijāḥ yajñasya paramā yoniḥ patiḥ ca ayam paraḥ smṛ rātri ahar śrotra nayanaḥ pakṣa māsa śiraḥ bhujaḥ mṛtyuḥ yamaḥ hutāśaḥ ca kālaḥ saṃhāra vegavān kālasya paramā yoniḥ kālaḥ ca ayam sanātanaḥ pradhānam mahat avyaktam viśeṣa antam sa vaikṛtam eṣā gatiḥ viraktānām eṣa bhāvaḥ paraḥ satām śāstra vedāṅga vidvasām etat dhyānam param padam iyam tā paramā kāṣṭhā iyam sā paramā kalā iyam tad parama siddhiḥ iyam sā paramā gatiḥ iyam sā paramā śāntiḥ iyam sā nirvṛtiḥ para yam prāpya kṛtakṛtyāḥ smaḥ iti amanyanta vedhasaḥ iyam tuṣṭiḥ iyam siddhiḥ iyam śrutiḥ iyam smṛtiḥ adhyātma gati niṣṭhānām viduṣām prāptiḥ avyayā yajatām yajña kāmānām yajñaiḥ vipula dakṣiṇaiḥ tapyatām yā gatiḥ deva vairāje sā gatiḥ bhavān karma nyāsa kṛtānām ca viraktānām tatas tatas a punarmāra kāmānām vairāgye vartatām pare vikṛtīnām layānām ca sā gatiḥ tvam sanātana jñāna vijñāna niṣṭhānām nirupākhyā nirañjanā veda śāstra purāṇa uktāḥ pañca etāḥ gatayaḥ smṛtāḥ iti taṇḍiḥ tapaḥ yogāt tuṣṭāva īśānam avyayam evam stutaḥ mahādevaḥ taṇḍinā brahma vādinā brahmā śatakratuḥ viṣṇuḥ viśvedevāḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ na viduḥ tvām iti tatas tuṣṭaḥ provāca tam śivaḥ akṣayaḥ ca avyayaḥ ca eva bhavitā duḥkha varjitaḥ yaśasvī tejasā yuktaḥ divya jñāna samanvitaḥ ṛṣīṇām abhigamyaḥ ca sūtra kartā sutaḥ tava mad prasādāt dvijaśreṣṭha bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ kam vā kāmam dadāmi adya brūhi yat vatsa kāṅkṣase prāñjaliḥ saḥ uvāca idam tvayi bhaktiḥ dṛḍhā astu me evam dattvā varam devaḥ vandyamānaḥ surarṣibhiḥ ṛṣiḥ āśramam āgamya mama etat proktavan iha yāni ca prathitāni ādau taṇḍiḥ ākhyātavān mama nāmāni mānava śreṣṭha tāni tvam śṛṇu siddhaye daśa nāma sahasrāṇi vedeṣu āha pitāmahaḥ śarvasya śāstreṣu tathā daśa nāma śatāni vai guhyāni imā nāmāni taṇḍiḥ bhagavataḥ acyuta deva prasādāt deveśa purā prāha mahātmane uvāca tatas sa prayataḥ bhūtvā mama tāta yudhiṣṭhira prāñjaliḥ prāha viprarṣiḥ nāma saṃhāram āditas sarva lokeṣu vikhyātaiḥ sthāṇum stoṣyāmi nāmabhiḥ ṛṣiṇā taṇḍinā bhaktyā kṛtaiḥ deva kṛtātmanā vakṣye yadu kula śreṣṭha śṛṇuṣva avahitaḥ mama na śakyam vistarāt kṛtsnam vaktum śarvasya kena cid yuktena api vibhūtīnām api varṣa śataiḥ api kaḥ tasya śaknuyāt vaktum guṇān kārtsnyena mādhava kim tu devasya mahataḥ saṃkṣipta artha pada akṣaram a prāpya iha tatas anujñām na śakyaḥ stotum īśvaraḥ nāmnām kam cit samuddeśam vakṣye hi avyakta yoneḥ śṛṇu nāma samuddeśam yat uktam padmayoninā daśa nāma sahasrāṇi yāni āha prapitāmahaḥ gireḥ sāram yathā hema puṣpāt sāram yathā madhu ghṛtāt sāram yathā maṇḍaḥ tathā etat sāram uddhṛtam śāntikam pauṣṭikam ca eva rakṣaḥ ghnam pāvanam mahat idam bhaktāya dātavyam śraddadhāna āstikāya ca na aśraddadhāna rūpāya nāstikāya ajitātmane yaḥ ca abhyasūyate devam bhūtātmānam pinākinam sa kṛṣṇa narakam yāti saha pūrvaiḥ saha anugaiḥ idam jñātvā anta kāle api gacchet hi paramām gatim pavitram maṅgalam puṇyam kalyāṇam idam uttamam nigadiṣye mahā bāho stavānām uttamam stavam idam brahmā purā kṛtvā sarva loka pitāmahaḥ sarva stavānām divyānām rāja tve samakalpayat tadā makaraḥ kāla pūjitaḥ sa gaṇaḥ gaṇa kāraḥ ca bhūtabhāvana sārathiḥ bhasma śāyī bhasma goptā bhasma bhūtaḥ taruḥ gaṇaḥ agaṇaḥ ca eva lopaḥ ca mahātmā sarva pūjitaḥ śaṅkuḥ triśaṅkuḥ saṃpannaḥ śuciḥ bhūta bāndhavaḥ tumbavīṇī mahākopaḥ ūrdhvaretāḥ jaleśayaḥ ugraḥ vaṃśa karaḥ vaṃśaḥ vaṃśa nādaḥ hi aninditaḥ sarva aṅga rūpaḥ māyāvī suhṛdaḥ hi anilaḥ analaḥ sa yajñāriḥ sa kāmāriḥ mahā daṃṣṭraḥ mahā āyudhaḥ māyāvī sarva kāma kṛt mantavyaḥ bāhuḥ tu aninditaḥ śarvaḥ śaṃkaraḥ śaṃkaraḥ adhanaḥ amara īśaḥ mahādevaḥ viśvadevaḥ surāri hā ajaikapād ca kāpālī triśaṅkuḥ ajitaḥ śivaḥ dhātā śakraḥ ca viṣṇuḥ ca mitraḥ tvaṣṭā dhruvaḥ dharaḥ prabhāvaḥ sarvagaḥ vāyuḥ aryamā savitā raviḥ udagraḥ ca vidhātā ca māndhātā bhūtabhāvanaḥ ratitīrthaḥ ca vāgmī ca sarva kāma guṇa āvahaḥ balavān ca upaśāntaḥ ca purāṇaḥ puṇya cañcurī kurukartā kāla rūpī kuru bhūtaḥ maheśvaraḥ sarva āśayaḥ darbha śāyin sarveṣām prāṇinām patiḥ kailāsa śikhara āvāsī himavat giri saṃśrayaḥ kūla hārī kūla kartā bahu vidyaḥ bahu pradaḥ sāragrīvaḥ mahājatruḥ alolaḥ ca mahauṣadhaḥ prāṇeśaḥ bandhakī vṛkṣaḥ nakulaḥ ca adrikaḥ tathā hrasvagrīvaḥ mahājānuḥ alolaḥ ca mahauṣadhī siddhārtha kārī siddhārthaḥ chandovyākaraṇa uttaraḥ siṃhanādaḥ siṃhadaṃṣṭraḥ siṃhagaḥ siṃha vāhanaḥ prabhāva ātmā jagatkālaḥ tālaḥ loka hitaḥ taruḥ sāraṅgaḥ nava cakra aṅgaḥ ketumālī sabhāvanaḥ vāhitā sarva bhūtānām nilayaḥ ca vibhuḥ bhavaḥ vasu bhṛt sarva bhūta ātmā niścalaḥ suviduḥ budhaḥ asuhṛd sarva bhūtānām niścalaḥ cala vid budhaḥ amoghaḥ saṃyataḥ hi aśvaḥ bhojanaḥ prāṇa dhāraṇaḥ dhṛtimān matimān dakṣaḥ satkṛtaḥ ca yuga adhipaḥ hiraṇyabāhuḥ ca tathā guhāpālaḥ praveśinām pratiṣṭhāyī mahāharṣaḥ jita kāmaḥ jita indriyaḥ mahā gītaḥ mahā nṛttaḥ hi apsaraḥ gaṇa sevitaḥ āvedanīyaḥ āveśaḥ sarva gandha sukha āvahaḥ toraṇaḥ tāraṇaḥ vāyuḥ paridhāvati ca ekatas saṃyogaḥ vardhanaḥ vṛddhaḥ mahāvṛddhaḥ gaṇādhipaḥ nityaḥ ātma sahāyaḥ ca deva asura patiḥ patiḥ āṣāḍhaḥ ca suṣāḍhaḥ ca dhruvaḥ harihaṇaḥ haraḥ vapuḥ āvartamānebhyaḥ vasu śreṣṭhaḥ mahā pathaḥ śirohārī vimarṣaḥ ca sarva lakṣaṇa bhūṣitaḥ akṣaḥ ca ratha yogī ca sarva yogī mahā balaḥ samāmnāyaḥ asamāmnāyaḥ tīrthadevaḥ mahā rathaḥ nirjīvaḥ jīvanaḥ mantraḥ śubha akṣaḥ bahu karkaśaḥ ratna prabhūtaḥ rakta aṅgaḥ mahā arṇava nipāna vid ārohaṇaḥ nirohaḥ ca śailahārī mahā tapāḥ nyāya nirvāpaṇaḥ pādaḥ paṇḍitaḥ hi acala upamaḥ bahu mālaḥ mahāmālaḥ sumālaḥ bahulocanaḥ vistāraḥ lavaṇaḥ kūpaḥ kusumaḥ sa phala udaya vṛṣabhaḥ vṛṣabhāṅka aṅgaḥ maṇibilvaḥ jaṭādharaḥ nivedanaḥ sudhā jātaḥ sugandhāraḥ mahā dhanūḥ śirodharaḥ abhimarśanaḥ sarva lakṣaṇa bhūṣitaḥ girāvāsaḥ visargaḥ ca sarva lakṣaṇa lakṣa vid gandhamālī ca bhagavat utthānaḥ sarva karmaṇām taraḥ tālī karaḥ tālī ūrdhva saṃhananaḥ vahaḥ muṇḍaḥ virūpaḥ vikṛtaḥ daṇḍi muṇḍaḥ vikurvaṇaḥ sahasra bāhuḥ sarva aṅgaḥ śaraṇyaḥ sarva loka kṛt pavitram trimadhuḥ mantraḥ kaniṣṭhaḥ kṛṣṇa piṅgalaḥ brahmadaṇḍa vinirmātā śataghnī ananta rūpaḥ na eka ātmā tigma tejāḥ svayambhoḥ ūrdhva ga ātmā paśupatiḥ vāta raṃhāḥ manaḥ javaḥ karṇikāra mahā sragvī nīlamauliḥ pinākadhṛk umāpatiḥ umākāntaḥ jāhnavīdhṛk umādhavaḥ mahāprasādaḥ damanaḥ śatru hā śvetapiṅgalaḥ prīta ātmā prayata ātmā ca saṃyata ātmā pradhāna dhṛk sarvapārśva sutaḥ tārkṣyaḥ dharma sādhāraṇaḥ varaḥ carācara ātmā sūkṣmātmā suvṛṣaḥ govṛṣa īśvaraḥ sādhya ṛṣiḥ vasuḥ ādityaḥ vivasvān savitā mṛḍaḥ ṛtuḥ saṃvatsaraḥ māsaḥ pakṣaḥ saṃkhyā samāpanaḥ kalā kāṣṭhā lavaḥ mātrā muhūrtaḥ ahar kṣapāḥ kṣaṇāḥ viśvakṣetram prajā bījam liṅgam ādyaḥ tu aninditaḥ sat asat vyaktam avyaktam pitā mātā pitāmahaḥ svargadvāram prajādvāram mokṣadvāram triviṣṭapam nirvāṇam hlādanam ca eva brahma lokaḥ parā gatiḥ deva asura vinirmātā deva asura parāyaṇaḥ deva asura mahāmātraḥ deva asura gaṇa āśrayaḥ deva asura gaṇa adhyakṣaḥ deva asura gaṇa agraṇī īḍyaḥ hastī sura vyāghraḥ deva siṃhaḥ nara ṛṣabhaḥ vibudha agra varaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarva deva uttama uttamaḥ prayuktaḥ śobhanaḥ vajraḥ īśānaḥ prabhuḥ avyayaḥ guruḥ kāntaḥ nijaḥ sargaḥ pavitraḥ sarva vāhanaḥ śṛṅgī śṛṅgapriyaḥ babhruḥ rājarājaḥ nirāmayaḥ abhirāmaḥ sura gaṇaḥ virāmaḥ sarva sādhanaḥ lalāṭa akṣaḥ viśva dehaḥ hariṇaḥ brahmavarcasaḥ sthāvarāṇām patiḥ ca eva niyama indriya vardhanaḥ siddhārthaḥ sarva bhūta arthaḥ acintyaḥ satya vrataḥ śuciḥ vrata adhipaḥ param brahma muktānām parama gatiḥ vimuktaḥ mukta tejāḥ ca śrīmān śrīvardhanaḥ jagant yam na brahma ādayaḥ devāḥ viduḥ yam na mahā ṛṣayaḥ japata bahubhiḥ īritam viśeṣyam namaḥ śivāya iti sadā pradānam bhagavant iti tatas abhyanujñām prāpya eva stutaḥ matimatām varaḥ śivam ebhiḥ stu devam nāmabhiḥ puṣṭi vardhanaiḥ nitya yuktaḥ śuciḥ bhūtvā prāpnoti ātmānam ātmanā stūyamānaḥ mahādevaḥ prīyate ca ātma nāmabhiḥ bhakta anukampī bhagavān ātma saṃsthān karoti tān tathā eva ca manuṣyeṣu ye manuṣyāḥ pradhānatas āstikāḥ śraddadhānāḥ ca bahubhiḥ janmabhiḥ stavaiḥ bhaktyā hi ananyam īśānam param devam sanātanam karmaṇā manasā vācā bhāvena amita tejasaḥ svapantaḥ jāgramāṇāḥ ca vrajan upaviśan tathā unmiṣan nimiṣan ca eva cintayantaḥ punar punar jāgrataḥ ca svapantaḥ ca vrajantaḥ pathini saṃsthitāḥ śṛṇvantaḥ śrāvayantaḥ ca kathayantaḥ ca te bhavam janma koṭi sahasreṣu nānā saṃsāra yoniṣu etat deveṣu duṣprāpam manuṣyeṣu na labhyate yad yā para siddhi tad bhāva gam cetas ye sarva bhāva upagatāḥ para tvena abhavan narāḥ manuṣyāṇām mahādevāt anyatra api tapaḥ balāt kṛttivāsāḥ stu kṛṣṇa taṇḍinā śuddha buddhinā idam puṇyam pavitram ca sarvadā pāpa nāśanam yoga dam mokṣa dam ca eva svarga dam toṣa dam tathā yā gatiḥ sāṃkhya yogānām vrajanti etām gatim tadā brahmā provāca śakrāya śakraḥ provāca mṛtyave mṛtyuḥ provāca rudrāṇām rudrebhyaḥ taṇḍim āgamat mahatā tapasā prāptaḥ taṇḍinā brahmasadmani taṇḍi pravac śukra gautama ah bhārgava nārāyaṇāya sādhyāya manuḥ iṣ dhīmate yamāya prāh bhagavat sādhyaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ acyutaḥ mārkaṇḍeyāya vārṣṇeya nāciketaḥ abhyabhāṣata mārkaṇḍeyāt mayā prāptam niyamena janārdana na tasya vighnam kurvanti dānavāḥ yakṣa rākṣasāḥ piśācāḥ yātudhānāḥ ca guhyakāḥ bhujagāḥ api yaḥ paṭheta śuciḥ bhūtvā brahmacārī jita indriyaḥ uvāca mahā yogī tatas prāha kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ muniḥ paṭhasva putra bhadram te prīyatām te maheśvaraḥ labdhavan asmi tān kāmān aham vai pāṇḍu nandana tathā tvam api śarvāt hi sarvān kāmān avāpsyasi kapilaḥ ca tatas prāha sāṃkhya ṛṣiḥ deva saṃmataḥ mayā janmāni anekāni śaktyā ca ārādhitaḥ bhavaḥ prītaḥ ca bhagavant jñānam dadau mama bhava antakam catur śīrṣaḥ tatas prāha śakrasya dayitaḥ sakhiḥ ālambāyanaḥ iti eva viśrutaḥ karuṇā ātmakaḥ mayā gokarṇam āsādya tapaḥ taptvā śatam samāḥ a yoni jānām dāntānām dharma jñānām su varcasām ajarāṇām aduḥkhānām śata varṣa sahasriṇām labdham putra śatam śarvāt purā pāṇḍu nṛpa ātmaja vālmīkiḥ ca api bhagavat yudhiṣṭhiram abhāṣata uktaḥ kṣaṇena ca āviṣṭaḥ tena adharmeṇa bhārata saḥ aham īśānam anagham astauṣam śaraṇam gataḥ muktaḥ ca asmi avaśaḥ pāpāt tatas duḥkha vināśanaḥ jāmadagnyaḥ ca kaunteyam āha dharma bhṛtām varaḥ pitṛ vipra vadhena aham ārtaḥ vai pāṇḍava agraja śuciḥ bhūtvā mahādevam gatavan śaraṇam nṛpa nāmabhiḥ ca astuvam devam tatas tuṣṭaḥ abhavat bhavaḥ āha mām bhagavant evam śikhaṇḍī śiva vigrahaḥ yat avāptam ca mama sarvam prasādāt tasya dhīmataḥ brāhmaṇaḥ aham bhavāni iti mayā ca ārādhitaḥ bhavaḥ tad prasādāt mayā prāptam brāhmaṇyam durlabham mahat asitaḥ devalaḥ ca eva prāha pāṇḍu sutam nṛpam tat me dharmam yaśaḥ ca agryam āyuḥ ca eva adadat bhavaḥ ṛṣiḥ gṛtsamadaḥ nāma śakrasya dayitaḥ sakhā prāha ājamīḍham bhagavān bṛhaspati sama dyutiḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ nāma bhagavān cākṣuṣasya manoḥ sutaḥ vartamāne abravīt vākyam sāmni hi uccārite mayā a yajña vāhinam pāpam akārṣīḥ tvam su durmate evam uktvā mahā krodhāt prāha ruṣṭaḥ punar vacaḥ prajñayā rahitaḥ duḥkhī nityam bhītaḥ vanecaraḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi daśa aṣṭau ca śatāni ca naṣṭa pānīya yavase mṛgaiḥ anyaiḥ ca varjite bhavitā tvam mṛgaḥ krūraḥ mahā duḥkha samanvitaḥ tatas mām śaraṇam prāptam prāha yogī maheśvaraḥ ajaraḥ ca amaraḥ ca eva bhavitā duḥkha varjitaḥ param dhātā vidhātā ca sukha duḥkhe ca sarvadā acintyaḥ eṣa bhagavān karmaṇā manasā girā na me tāta vidyayā paṇḍitaḥ samaḥ suvarṇākṣaḥ mahādevaḥ tapasā toṣitaḥ mayā tatas atha bhagavān āha prītaḥ mām vai yudhiṣṭhira annāt priyataraḥ kṛṣṇa mad prasādāt bhaviṣyasi evam sahasraśas ca ātmā mahādevaḥ varam dadau maṇimanthe atha śaile vai purā saṃrādhitaḥ mayā varṣa ayuta sahasrāṇām sahasra śatam eva ca tatas mām bhagavān prītaḥ idam vacanam abravīt varam vṛṇīṣva bhadram te yaḥ te manasi vartate jaigīṣavyaḥ tathā prāha jagaddhātā maheśvaraḥ uvāca mama aṣṭaguṇam aiśvaryam dattam bhagavatā purā yatnena alpena balinā vārāṇasyām yudhiṣṭhira parāśaraḥ ca āha muniḥ purā mama ca toṣitaḥ uvāca catuḥṣaṣṭi aṅgam adadāt kāla jñānam mama adbhutam sarasvatyāḥ taṭe tuṣṭaḥ manaḥ yajñena pāṇḍava tulyam mama sahasram tu sutānām brahma vādinām uvāca prasādya aham purā śarvam manasā acintayam nṛpa mahā tapāḥ mahā tejāḥ mahā yogī mahā yaśāḥ vedavyāsaḥ śriyāvāsaḥ brahmaṇyaḥ karuṇā ātmakaḥ tat abhijñāya mām āha śaṃkaraḥ tripura ardanaḥ pitṛ kanyā vasoḥ putrī śāpāt dāśa gṛha vaditā tasyām viṣṇukṛtā nāma vidyayā śodhakaḥ satām iti matvā hṛdi matam prāha mām sura sattamaḥ vedānām ca sa vai vyastā kuru vaṃśa karaḥ tathā yudhiṣṭhira mahā yogī vīryavān akṣayaḥ avyayaḥ māṇḍavyaḥ ca āha deveśa bhaktaḥ loka hite bhave uvāca acauraḥ caura śaṅkāyām śūle bhinnaḥ hi aham yadā mokṣam prāpsyasi śūlāt ca jīviṣyasi sama arbudam rujā śūla kṛtā ca eva na te vipra bhaviṣyati pādāt caturthāt saṃbhūtaḥ ātmā yasmāt mune tava evam uktvā tu bhagavān vareṇyaḥ vṛṣavāhanaḥ maheśvaraḥ mahā rāja kṛttivāsāḥ mahā dyutiḥ uvāca viśvāmitra abhyanujñātaḥ hi aham pitaram āgataḥ abravīt mām tatas mātā duḥkhitā rudatī bhṛśam kauśikena abhyanujñātam putram veda vibhūṣitam na tāta taruṇam dāntam pitā tvām paśyate anagha śrutvā jananyāḥ vacanam nirāśaḥ guru darśane niyata ātmā mahādevam apaśyam saḥ abravīt ca mām pitā mātā ca te tvam ca putra mṛtyu vivarjitāḥ bhaviṣyatha viśa kṣipram draṣṭāsi pitaram kṣaye anujñātaḥ bhagavatā gṛham gatvā yudhiṣṭhira apaśyam pitaram tāta iṣṭim kṛtvā viniḥsṛtam upaspṛśya gṛhītvā idhmam kuśān ca śaraṇāt gurūn tān visṛjya ca mām prāha pitā sa asra āvila īkṣaṇaḥ praṇamantam pariṣvajya mūrdhani ca āghrāya pāṇḍava diṣṭyā dṛṣṭaḥ asi mama putra kṛtavidyaḥ iha āgataḥ uvāca proktāni munibhiḥ śrutvā āsa pāṇḍavaḥ tatas kṛṣṇaḥ abravīt vākyam punar matimatām varaḥ yudhiṣṭhiram dharma nityam puruhūtam iva īśvaraḥ aśubhaiḥ pāpa karmāṇaḥ ye narāḥ kaluṣīkṛtāḥ īśānam na prapadyante tamaḥ rājasa vṛttayaḥ īśvaram saṃprapadyante dvijāḥ bhāvita bhāvanāḥ sadṛśaḥ araṇya vāsīnām munīnām bhāvitātmanām brahma tvam keśava tvam vā śakra tvam vā suraiḥ saha manasā api śivam tāta ye prapadyanti mānavāḥ yajet devam virūpākṣam na sa pāpena lipyate sarva lakṣaṇa hīnaḥ api yuktaḥ vā sarva pātakaiḥ sarvam tudati tat pāpam bhāvayan śivam ātmanā kīṭa pakṣi pataṃgānām tiryañcām api keśava na te saṃsāra vaśa gāḥ iti mama niścitā matiḥ tatas kṛṣṇaḥ abravīt vākyam dharmaputram yudhiṣṭhiram dhātā aryamā śukra bṛhaspatī ca rudrāḥ sa sādhyāḥ varuṇaḥ vitta gopaḥ brahmā śakraḥ mārutaḥ brahma satyam vedāḥ yajñāḥ dakṣiṇāḥ veda vāhāḥ somaḥ yaṣṭā yat ca havyam haviḥ ca rakṣā dīkṣā niyamāḥ ye ca ke cit svāhā vaṣaṭ brāhmaṇāḥ saurabheyāḥ dharmam cakram kālacakram caram ca agryā buddhiḥ manasā darśane ca sparśe siddhiḥ karmaṇām yā ca siddhiḥ gaṇāḥ devānām ūṣmapāḥ somapāḥ ca lekhāḥ suyāmāḥ tuṣitāḥ brahmakāyāḥ ābhāsvarāḥ gandhapāḥ dṛṣṭipāḥ ca śuddhāḥ ca nirvāṇa ratāḥ ca devāḥ sparśāśanāḥ darśapāḥ ājyapāḥ ca cintā gatāḥ ye ca deveṣu mukhyāḥ ye ca api anye devatāḥ ca ājamīḍha suparṇa gandharva piśāca dānavāḥ yakṣāḥ tathā pannagāḥ cāraṇāḥ ca sūkṣmam sthūlam mṛdu yat ca api a sūkṣmam sukham duḥkham sukha duḥkha antaram ca sāṃkhyam yogam yat pareṣām param ca śarvāt jātam viddhi yat kīrtitam me tad saṃbhūtāḥ bhūta kṛtaḥ vareṇyāḥ sarve devāḥ bhuvanasya asya gopāḥ āviśya imām dharaṇīm ye abhyarakṣan purātanīm tasya devasya sṛṣṭim vicinvantam manasā toṣṭuvīmi kim cit tattvam prāṇa hetoḥ nataḥ asmi dadātu devaḥ sa varān iha iṣṭān abhiṣṭutaḥ naḥ prabhuḥ avyayaḥ sadā imam stavam saṃniyamya indriyāṇi śuciḥ bhūtvā yaḥ puruṣaḥ paṭheta vedān kṛtsnān brāhmaṇaḥ prāpnuyāt ca jayet rājā pṛthivīm ca api kṛtsnām vaiśyaḥ lābham prāpnuyāt naipuṇam ca śūdraḥ gatim pretya tathā sukham ca stava rājam imam kṛtvā rudrāya dadhire manaḥ sarva doṣa apaham puṇyam pavitram ca yaśasvinam yāvanti asya śarīreṣu romakūpāṇi bhārata tāvat varṣa sahasrāṇi svarge vasati mānavaḥ uvāca pāṇigrahaṇa kāle tu strīṇām etat katham smṛtam ārṣaḥ eṣa bhavet dharmaḥ prājāpatyaḥ atha vā āsuraḥ svarge mṛtānām bhavati sahadharmaḥ pitāmaha nānā karma phala upetāḥ nānā karma nivāsinaḥ nānā niraya niṣṭhā antāḥ mānuṣāḥ bahavaḥ yadā anṛtāḥ striyaḥ iti evam sūtrakāraḥ vyavasyati yadā anṛtāḥ striyaḥ tāta sahadharmaḥ kutas smṛtaḥ anṛtāḥ striyaḥ iti evam vedeṣu api hi paṭhyate dharmaḥ ayam paurvikī saṃjñā upacāraḥ kriyā vidhiḥ niḥsaṃdeham idam sarvam pitāmaha yathā śrutiḥ uvāca atra api udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam aṣṭāvakrasya saṃvādam diśayā saha bhārata niveṣṭu kāmaḥ tu purā aṣṭāvakraḥ mahā tapāḥ ṛṣeḥ atha vadānyasya kanyām vavre mahātmanaḥ suprabhām nāma vai nāmnā rūpeṇa apratimām bhuvi guṇa prabarhām śīlena sādhvīm cāritra śobhanām sā tasya dṛṣṭvā eva manaḥ jahāra śubha locanā vana rājī yathā citrā vasante kusuma ācitā ṛṣiḥ tam āha deyā me sutā tubhyam śṛṇuṣva me an anya strī janaḥ prājñaḥ hi a pravāsī priyaṃvadaḥ surūpaḥ saṃmataḥ vīraḥ śīlavān bhoga bhuj śuciḥ dāra anumata yajñaḥ ca sunakṣatrām atha udvahet gaccha tāvat diśam puṇyām uttarām drakṣyase tatas uvāca tathā idānīm mayā kāryam yathā vakṣyati mām bhavān uvāca rudrasya āyatanam dṛṣṭvā siddha cāraṇa sevitam prahṛṣṭaiḥ pārṣadaiḥ juṣṭam nṛtyadbhiḥ vividha ānanaiḥ divya aṅgarāgaiḥ paiśācaiḥ vanyaiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ tathā pāṇitāla sa tālaiḥ ca śamyātālaiḥ samaiḥ tathā saṃprahṛṣṭaiḥ pranṛtyadbhiḥ śarvaḥ tatra niṣevyate iṣṭam kila girau sthānam tat divyam anuśuśruma nityam saṃnihitaḥ devaḥ tathā pāriṣadāḥ śubhāḥ tatra devyā tapaḥ taptam śaṃkara artham su duścaram atas tat iṣṭam devasya tathā umāyāḥ iti śrutiḥ ṛtavaḥ kālarātriḥ ca ye divyāḥ ye ca mānuṣāḥ tapasvinīm mahābhāgām vṛddhām dīkṣām anuṣṭhitām draṣṭavyā sā tvayā tatra saṃpūjyā ca eva yatnatas tām dṛṣṭvā vinivṛttaḥ tvam tatas pāṇim grahīṣyasi yadi eṣa samayaḥ satyaḥ sādhyatām tatra gamyatām uvāca tathā astu sādhayiṣyāmi tatra yāsyāmi asaṃśayam uvāca himavantam giri śreṣṭham siddha cāraṇa sevitam sa gatvā dvija śārdūlaḥ himavantam mahā girim abhyagacchat nadīm puṇyām bāhudām dharma dāyinīm aśoke vimale tīrthe snātvā tarpya ca devatāḥ tatas rātrau vyatītāyām prātar utthāya sa dvijaḥ snātvā prāduścakāra agnim hutvā ca eva vidhānāt rudrāṇī kūpam āsādya hrade tatra samāśvasat saḥ apaśyat kāñcana dvāram dīpyamānam iva śriyā mandākinīm ca nalinīm dhanadasya mahātmanaḥ sa tān pratyarcayām āsa rākṣasān bhīma vikramān nivedayata mām kṣipram dhanadāya iti ca abravīt asau vaiśravaṇaḥ rājā svayam āyāti te antikam paśya enam tvam mahābhāgam jvalantam iva tejasā vidhivat kuśalam pṛṣṭvā tatas brahmarṣim abravīt sukham prāptaḥ bhavān kaccit kim vā mattaḥ cikīrṣasi brūhi sarvam kariṣyāmi yat mām tvam vakṣyasi dvija satkṛtaḥ kṛta kāryaḥ ca bhavān yāsyati avighnataḥ prāviśat bhavanam svam vai gṛhītvā tam dvijottamam niṣeduḥ tatra kauberāḥ yakṣa gandharva rākṣasāḥ tatas teṣām niṣaṇṇānām dhanadaḥ vākyam abravīt bhavat chandam samājñāya nṛtyeran apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ ātithyam paramam kāryam śuśrūṣā bhavataḥ tathā atha urvarā miśrakeśī rambhā ca eva urvaśī tathā alambusā ghṛtācī ca citrā citrāṅgadā ruciḥ manoharā sukeśī ca sumukhī hāsinī prabhā vidyutā praśamā dāntā vidyotā ratiḥ eva ca etāḥ ca anyāḥ ca vai bahvyaḥ pranṛtta apsarasaḥ śubhāḥ avādayan ca gandharvāḥ vādyāni vividhāni ca hāryaḥ ayam viṣayaḥ brahman gāndharvaḥ nāma nāmataḥ sarvam ājñāpyatām āśu paravantaḥ vayam tvayi atha vaiśravaṇam prītaḥ bhagavān pratyabhāṣata arcitaḥ asmi yathānyāyam gamiṣyāmi dhaneśvara niyogāt adya yāsyāmi vṛddhimān ṛddhimān bhava kailāse śaṃkara āvāsam abhivīkṣya praṇamya ca gaurīśam śaṃkaram dāntam śaraṇa āgata vatsalam gaṅgā dharam gopati gam gaṇa āvṛtam akalmaṣam kailāsam mandaram haimam sarvān anucacāra ha tān atītya mahā śailān kairātam sthānam uttamam pradakṣiṇam tatas cakre prayataḥ śirasā naman dharaṇīm avatīrya atha pūta ātmā asau tadā bhavat sa tam pradakṣiṇam kṛtvā tris śailam ca uttarā mukhaḥ tatas aparam vana uddeśam ramaṇīyam apaśyata śailān ca vividha ākārān kāñcanān ratna bhūṣitān maṇi bhūmau niviṣṭāḥ ca puṣkariṇyaḥ tathā eva ca bhṛśam tasya manaḥ reme mahā ṛṣeḥ bhāvitātmanaḥ dadarśa adbhuta saṃkāśam dhanadasya gṛhāt varam mahāntaḥ yatra vividhāḥ prāsādāḥ parvata upamāḥ vimānāni ca ramyāṇi ratnāni vividhāni ca mandāra puṣpaiḥ saṃkīrṇā tathā mandākinī nadī svayaṃprabhāḥ ca maṇayaḥ vajraiḥ bhūmiḥ ca bhūṣitā muktā jāla parikṣiptaiḥ maṇi ratna vibhūṣitaiḥ ramyaiḥ sarvatas saṃvṛtam śubhaiḥ atha kanyā parivṛtāḥ gṛhāt tasmāt viniḥsṛtāḥ nānā rūpāḥ sapta vibho kanyāḥ sarvāḥ manoharāḥ yām yām apaśyat kanyām sa sā sā tasya manaḥ aharat na aśaknuvat dhārayitum manaḥ atha asya avasīdati sa ca tāsām surūpāṇām tasya eva bhavanasya ca kautūhala samāviṣṭaḥ praviveśa gṛham dvijaḥ tatra apaśyat jarā yuktām araja umbara dhāriṇīm vṛddhām paryaṅkam āsīnām sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitām uvāca sarvāḥ svān ālayān yāntu ekā mām upatiṣṭhatu su prajñātā su praśāntā śeṣāḥ gacchantu chandataḥ tatas pradakṣiṇīkṛtya kanyāḥ tāḥ tam ṛṣim tadā nirākrāman gṛhāt tasmāt sā vṛddhā atha vyatiṣṭhata atha tām saṃviśan prāha śayane bhāsvare tadā saṃlāpāt tena vipreṇa tathā sā tatra bhāṣitā atha sā vepamāna aṅgī nimittam śīta jam tadā svāgatam svāgatena astu bhagavant tām abhāṣata sā upāgūhat bhujābhyām tu ṛṣim prītyā nara ṛṣabha nirvikāram ṛṣim ca api kāṣṭha kuḍya upamam tadā duḥkhitā prekṣya saṃjalpam akārṣīt ṛṣiṇā saha brahman na kāmakāraḥ asti strīṇām puruṣatas dhṛtiḥ kāmena mohitā ca aham tvām bhajatīm bhajasva mām prahṛṣṭaḥ bhava viprarṣe samāgaccha mayā saha upagūha ca mām vipra kāma ārtā aham bhṛśam tvayi prārthitam darśanāt eva bhajamānām bhajasva mām sarvān kāmān vidhāsyāmi ramasva sahitaḥ mayā tvad vaśā mama bhaviṣyāmi raṃsyase ca mayā saha sarvān kāmān upāśnānaḥ ye divyāḥ ye ca mānuṣāḥ na atas param hi nārīṇām kāryam kim cana vidyate uvāca dūṣitam dharma śāstreṣu para dāra abhimarśanam punar ca pātakam dṛṣṭam vipra kṣetre viśeṣataḥ bhadre niveṣṭu kāmam mām viddhi satyena vai śape prāyaścittam mahat atas dāra grahaṇa pūrvakam bījam na śudhyate voḍhuḥ asya ca akṛta niṣkṛteḥ mātṛtaḥ pitṛtaḥ śuddhaḥ jñeyaḥ putraḥ yathārthataḥ viṣayeṣu anabhijñaḥ aham dharma artham kila saṃtatiḥ evam lokān gamiṣyāmi putraiḥ iti na saṃśayaḥ bhadre dharmam vijānīṣva jñātvā ca uparamasva ha priyāḥ strīṇām yathā kāmaḥ rati śīlāḥ hi yoṣitaḥ sahasra ekā yatā nārī prāpnoti iha kadā cana līlāyatyaḥ kulam ghnanti kūlāni iva sarit varāḥ doṣān ca mandān mandāsu prajāpatiḥ abhāṣata uvāca tatas saḥ ṛṣiḥ ekāgraḥ tām striyam pratyabhāṣata āsyatām ruciram chandaḥ kim vā kāryam bravīhi me sā strī provāca bhagavan drakṣyase deśa kālataḥ vasa tāvat mahā prājña kṛtakṛtyaḥ gamiṣyasi vatsye aham yāvat utsāhaḥ bhavatyā na atra saṃśayaḥ atha ṛṣiḥ abhisaṃprekṣya striyam tām jarayā anvitām cintām paramakām bheje saṃtaptaḥ iva ca abhavat na aramat tatra tatra asya dṛṣṭiḥ rūpa parājitā devatā iyam gṛhasya asya śāpāt nūnam virūpitā asyāḥ ca kāraṇam vettum na yuktam sahasā mayā vyagamat tat ahar śeṣam manasā vyākulena tu rūpam saṃdhyā abhra saṃyuktam kim upasthāpyatām te saḥ uvāca tadā tām striyam snāna udakam iha ānaya upāsiṣye tatas saṃdhyām vāgyataḥ niyata indriyaḥ uvāca tailam divyam upādāya snāna śāṭīm upānayat anujñātā ca muninā sā strī tena mahātmanā atha asya tailena aṅgāni sarvāṇi eva abhyamṛkṣayat śanais ca utsāditaḥ tatra snāna śālām upāgamat bhadrāsanam tatas citram ṛṣiḥ anvāviśat navam atha upaviṣṭaḥ ca yadā tasmin bhadrāsane tadā snāpayām āsa śanakais tam ṛṣim sukha hasta vat vyatītām rajanīm kṛtsnām na ajānāt sa mahā vrataḥ pūrvasyām diśi sūryam ca saḥ apaśyat uditam divi atha upāsya sahasrāṃśum kim karomi iti uvāca tām sā ca amṛta rasa prakhyam ṛṣeḥ annam upāharat vyagamat ca api ahar śeṣam tatas saṃdhyā agamat punar atha ardharātre sā strī tu śayanam tat upāgamat uvāca uvāca sā tadā tena vipreṇa tathā dhṛtyā nivartitā uvāca na asti svatantra tā strīṇām asvatantrāḥ hi yoṣitaḥ uvāca haranti doṣa jātāni naram jātam yathecchakam prabhavāmi sadā dhṛtyā bhadre svam śayanam vraja bhūmau nipatamānāyāḥ śaraṇam bhava me anagha yadi vā doṣa jātam tvam para dāreṣu paśyasi ātmānam sparśayāmi adya pāṇim gṛhṇīṣva mama dvija svatantrām mām vijānīhi yaḥ adharmaḥ saḥ astu vai mayi uvāca kaumāram brahmacaryam me kanyā eva asmi na saṃśayaḥ kuru mā vimatim vipra śraddhām vijahi mā mama uvāca aṣṭāvakraḥ atha sa muniḥ cintayām āsa vismitaḥ jijñāsā iyam ṛṣeḥ tasya vighnaḥ satyam nu kim bhavet āścarya parama hi idam kim nu śreyaḥ hi me bhavet kim tu asyāḥ paramam rūpam jīrṇam āsīt katham punar uvāca uvāca aṣṭāvakraḥ anvapṛcchat tām rūpam vikuruṣe katham na ca anṛtam te vaktavyam brūhi brāhmaṇa kāmyayā dyāvāpṛthivī mātrā eṣā kāmyā brāhmaṇa sattama śṛṇuṣva avahitaḥ sarvam yat idam satya vikrama uttarām mām diśam viddhi dṛṣṭam strī cāpalam ca te jijñāsā iyam prayuktā me sthirīkartum tava anagha sthavirāṇām api strīṇām bādhate maithuna jvaraḥ vidvān su śīlaḥ puruṣaḥ sa dāraḥ sukham aśnute tuṣṭaḥ pitāmahaḥ te adya tathā devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ sa tvam yena ca kāryeṇa saṃprāptaḥ bhagavān iha nikṛtiḥ strī bhoga parā priya vāda apravāsanāt tava upadeśam kartum vai tat ca sarvam kṛtam mayā kṣemī gamiṣyasi gṛhān śramaḥ ca na bhaviṣyati kanyām prāpsyasi tām vipra putriṇī ca bhaviṣyati kāmyayā pṛṣṭavan tvam mām tatas vyāhṛtam uttaram an atikramaṇīyā eṣā kṛtsnaiḥ lokaiḥ tribhiḥ sadā yāvat bravīmi viprarṣe aṣṭāvakra yathātatham ṛṣiṇā prasāditā ca asmi tava hetoḥ dvijarṣabha tasya saṃmānana artham me tvayi vākyam prabhāṣitam śrutvā tu vacanam tasyāḥ sa vipraḥ prāñjaliḥ sthitaḥ anujñātaḥ tayā ca api sva gṛham punar āvrajat gṛham āgamya viśrāntaḥ sva janam pratipūjya ca pṛṣṭaḥ ca tena vipreṇa dṛṣṭam tu etat nidarśanam prāha vipram tadā vipraḥ su prītena antarātmanā tayā ca aham anujñātaḥ bhavān ca api prakīrtitaḥ śrāvitaḥ ca api tat vākyam gṛham abhyāgataḥ prabho tam uvāca tatas vipraḥ pratigṛhṇīṣva me sutām uvāca aṣṭāvakraḥ tathā iti uktvā pratigṛhya ca tām prabho kanyām parama dharma ātmā prītimān ca abhavat tadā kanyām tām pratigṛhya eva bhāryām parama śobhanām yudhiṣṭhiraḥ vaiśya yonyām samutpannāḥ śūdra yonyām tathā eva ca brahmarṣayaḥ iti proktāḥ purāṇāḥ dvijasattamāḥ bhīṣmaḥ īśanti ātmanaḥ iti etat gatiḥ ca eṣām na sajjate brahma bhūyāṃsaḥ iti eva ṛṣayaḥ śruti coditāḥ nindyāḥ na ca ete rāja indra pramāṇam hi pramāṇinām evam mahātmabhiḥ tāta tapaḥ jñāna samanvitaiḥ pravartitāni kāryāṇi pramāṇāni eva sattama bhāryāḥ catasraḥ rāja indra brāhmaṇasya svadharmataḥ brāhmaṇī kṣatriyā vaiśyā śūdrā ca bharata ṛṣabha rājñām tu kṣatriyā vaiśyā śūdrā ca bharata ṛṣabha vaiśyasya vaiśyā vihitā śūdrā ca bharata ṛṣabha śūdrasya ekā smṛtā bhāryā pratilome tu saṃkaraḥ śūdrāyāḥ tu nara śreṣṭha catvāraḥ patayaḥ smṛtāḥ varṇa uttamāyāḥ tu patiḥ savarṇaḥ tu ekaḥ eva saḥ dvau kṣatriyāyāḥ vihitau brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ tathā vaiśyāyāḥ tu nara śreṣṭha vihitāḥ patayaḥ trayaḥ savarṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ ca eva brāhmaṇaḥ ca viśām pate evam vidhim anusmṛtya tatas te ṛṣibhiḥ purā utpāditāḥ mahātmānaḥ putrāḥ brahmarṣayaḥ purā purāṇābhyām ṛṣibhyām tu mitreṇa varuṇena ca kakṣīvān ārṣṭiṣeṇaḥ ca puruṣaḥ kakṣaḥ eva ca māmateyasya vai putrāḥ gautamasya ātmajāḥ smṛtāḥ vatsapriyaḥ ca bhagavān sthūlaraśmiḥ tathā akṣaṇiḥ kapiṃjalādaḥ brahmarṣiḥ caṇḍālyām udapadyata vainateyaḥ tathā pakṣī turyāyām ca vasiṣṭhāt adṛśyantyāḥ pitā vaiśyaḥ nāmnā citramukhaḥ purā vaiśyaḥ citramukhaḥ kanyām vasiṣṭha tanayasya vai śubhām prādāt yatas jātaḥ brahmarṣiḥ tu parāśaraḥ tathā eva dāśa kanyāyām satyavatyām mahān ṛṣiḥ parāśarāt prasūtaḥ ca vyāsaḥ yoga mayaḥ muniḥ vibhaṇḍakasya mṛgyām ca tapaḥ yoga ātmakaḥ muniḥ ṛśyaśṛṅgaḥ samutpannaḥ brahmacārī mahā yaśāḥ śāṅgaryām ca mandapālasya catvāraḥ brahma vādinaḥ jātāḥ brahmarṣayaḥ puṇyāḥ yaiḥ stutaḥ havyavāhanaḥ droṇaḥ ca stambamitraḥ ca śārisṛkvaḥ ca buddhimān jaritāriḥ ca vikhyātāḥ catvāraḥ sūrya saṃnibhāḥ mahā ṛṣeḥ kālavṛkṣasya śakuntyām eva jajñivān hiraṇyahastaḥ bhagavān mahā ṛṣiḥ kāñcana prabhaḥ pāvakāt tāta saṃbhūtāḥ manasā ca mahā ṛṣayaḥ savarṇaḥ ca api rājarṣiḥ savarṇāyām ajāyata mṛṇmayyām bharata śreṣṭhaḥ ādityena vivasvatā śāṇḍilyaḥ ca agneḥ jātaḥ kāśyapasya ātmajaḥ prabhuḥ śaradvantaḥ śarastambāt kṛpaḥ ca kṛpayā saha reṇuḥ ca reṇukā ca eva rāma mātā yaśasvinī yamunāyām samudbhūtaḥ somakena mahātmanā arkadattaḥ mahān ṛṣiḥ prathitaḥ pṛthivī tale dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca saṃbhūtaḥ vedyām kṛṣṇā ca bhārata vyāghra yonyām tatas jātāḥ vasiṣṭhasya mahātmanaḥ ekonaviṃśatiḥ putrāḥ khyātāḥ vyāghrapada ādayaḥ mandhaḥ ca bādalomaḥ ca jābāliḥ ca mahān ṛṣiḥ ete ca anye ca vikhyātāḥ pṛthivyām gotra tām gatāḥ viśvakāśasya rājarṣeḥ aikṣvākoḥ tu mahātmanaḥ bālāśvaḥ nāma putraḥ abhūt śikhām bhittvā viniḥsṛtaḥ māndhātā ca eva rājarṣiḥ yuvanāśvena dhīmatā gaurikaḥ ca api rājarṣiḥ cakravartī mahā yaśāḥ bāhudāyām samutpannaḥ nadyām rājñā subāhunā bhūmeḥ ca putraḥ narakaḥ saṃvartaḥ ca eva puṣkalaḥ adbhiḥ ca eva mahā tejāḥ ṛṣiḥ gārgyaḥ hi ajāyata ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ rājanyāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ tathā prabhāvena abhisaṃbhūtāḥ mahā ṛṣīṇām mahātmanām na asādhyam tapasā teṣām vidyayā ātma guṇaiḥ paraiḥ dharmam praṇayatā rājan tam nibodha yudhiṣṭhira ṛṣīṇām ca nadīnām ca sādhūnām ca mahātmanām prabhavaḥ na adhigantavyaḥ strīṇām duścaritasya ca tat na atra cintā kartavyā mahā ṛṣīṇām samudbhave yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bhīṣmaḥ atra api udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam nāradena purā gītam mārkaṇḍeyāya pṛcchate āraṇeyam āraṇeya ca raibhyam ca etān atra āgatān purā dṛṣṭvā pūrvam samāsīnān mārkaṇḍeyaḥ abhyagacchata ṛṣayaḥ tu munim dṛṣṭvā samutthāya unmukhāḥ sthitāḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ ayam samāgamaḥ sadbhiḥ yatnena āsāditaḥ mayā atra prāpsyāmi dharmāṇām ācārasya ca niścayam ṛṣibhiḥ nāradaḥ proktaḥ brūhi yatra asya saṃśayaḥ dharma dharma tattva jña tvam hi chettāsi saṃśayān ṛṣibhyaḥ anumatam vākyam niyogāt nāradaḥ abravīt sarva dharma artha tattva jñam mārkaṇḍeyam tatas abravīt mārkaṇḍeyaḥ tat aham kathayiṣyāmi brūhi tvam su mahā tapas nāradaḥ āsīt dharmaḥ purā vipra catuṣpādaḥ kṛte yuge tatas tretā yugam nāma pravṛttam dharma dūṣaṇam tasmin vyatīte saṃprāptam tṛtīyam dvāparam yugam caturtham nandikam nāma dharma pādau aśeṣatas tatas prabhṛti jāyante kṣīṇa prajñā āyuṣaḥ narāḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ kṣīṇa prāṇa dhanāḥ loke dharma ācāra bahiṣkṛtāḥ nāradaḥ pratigṛhṇanti tat devāḥ dātuḥ nyāyāt prayacchataḥ sattva yuktam ca dātā ca sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt mārkaṇḍeyaḥ nāradaḥ mantra hīnam apanyāyam teṣām dattam kva gacchati asurān gacchate dattam rakṣāṃsi kṣatriyaiḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ vaiśyaiḥ pretāni vai dattam śūdraiḥ bhūtāni gacchati atha varṇa avare jātāḥ cāturvarṇya apadeśinaḥ nāradaḥ varṇa avarāṇām bhūtānām havya kavya pradātṛṇām yātudhānāḥ piśācāḥ ca bhūtāḥ ye ca api nairṛtāḥ teṣām sā vihitā vṛttiḥ pitṛ daivata nirgatā teṣām sarva pradātṝṇām havya kavyam samāhitāḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ śrutam varṇa avare dattam havyam kavyam ca nārada nāradaḥ saṃprayoge ca putrāṇām kanyānām ca bravīhi me kanyā pradānam putrāṇām strīṇām saṃyogam eva ca ānupūrvyāt mayā samyak ucyamānam nibodha me jāta mātrā tu dātavyā kanyakā sadṛśe vare avadhyātaḥ sa kanyāyāḥ bandhuḥ prāpnoti bhrūṇa hām dūṣitā pāṇi mātreṇa mṛte bhartri dārikā saṃskāram labhate nārī dvitīye sā punar patau mārkaṇḍeyaḥ a dūṣyā sā prasūtīṣu prajānām dārakarmaṇi yā tu kanyā prasūyeta garbhiṇī yā tu vā bhavet atha dārakriyām bhūyas sā bhajet ṛṣi sattama nāradaḥ tasmāt kurvanti vai bhāvam kumāryaḥ tāḥ na kanyakāḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ gṛhṇīyāt tām catur bhāgam viśuddhām sarjanāt punar katham kanyāsu yad jan bandhūnām dūṣay sadā nāradaḥ kanyāyāḥ tu pituḥ putrāḥ kānīnāḥ havya kavya dāḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ antarvatnyāḥ tu yaḥ pāṇim gṛhṇīyāt sa sahoḍha jaḥ atha yena āhitaḥ garbhaḥ kanyāyām tatra nārada nāradaḥ dharma ācāreṣu te nityam dūṣakāḥ kṛta śodhanāḥ bījam ca naśyate teṣām mogha ceṣṭāḥ bhavanti te mārkaṇḍeyaḥ atha kā cit bhavet kanyā krītā dattā hṛtā api vā nāradaḥ krītā dattā hṛtā ca eva yā kanyā pāṇi varjitā kaumārī nāma sā bhāryā prasavet aurasān sutān mārkaṇḍeyaḥ nāradaḥ nityam nivasate lakṣmīḥ kanyakāsu pratiṣṭhitā śobhanā śubha yogyā ca pūjyā maṅgala karmasu tathā kanyā mahā lakṣmī sarva lokasya maṅgalam evam kanyā parā lakṣmī ratiḥ toṣaḥ ca dehinām mahā kulānām cāritram vṛttena nikaṣa upalam ānayitvā svakāt varṇāt kanyakām yaḥ bhajet naraḥ dātāram havya kavyānām putrakam sā prasūyate sādhvī kulam vardhayati sādhvī puṣṭiḥ gṛhe parā mārkaṇḍeyaḥ sādhvī lakṣmī ratiḥ sākṣāt pratiṣṭhā saṃtatiḥ tathā śrutam bahuvidham vṛttam kanyakānām mahāmate icchāmi yoṣitām śrotum dharma adharmam parigrahe nāradaḥ aṣṭau bhāryā āgama dharmya narāṇām dārakarmaṇi sādhvī pāṇi gṛhītā yā kaumārī pāṇi varjitā mārkaṇḍeyaḥ trayaḥ tri bhāryā āgama jñātāḥ yatra dharmaḥ na naśyati nāradaḥ pañca anyāḥ paścimāḥ brūhi bhāryāḥ tāsām ca ye sutāḥ sagotra bhāryā krītā ca para bhāryā ca kāritā gata gam ca yā bhāryā āśramāt āhṛtā ca yā ete etad bhāryāgamāḥ pañca punar bhāryāḥ bhū yāḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ etāḥ bhāryāḥ nṛṇām gamyāḥ tad putrāḥ havya kavya dāḥ śrutāḥ bhāryāḥ ca putrāḥ ca vistareṇa mahā mune nāradaḥ āśrama sthāḥ katham nāryaḥ na duṣyanti iti brūhi me āśrama sthāsu nārīṣu bāndhava tvam praṇaśyati naṣṭa vaṃśyāḥ bhavanti etāḥ bandhūnām atha bhartṛṇām para dārāḥ mukta doṣāḥ tāḥ nāryaḥ āśrama saṃsthitāḥ svayam īśāḥ sva dehānām kāmyāḥ tad gata mānasāḥ evam nāryaḥ na duṣyanti narāṇām tad prasūtiṣu mārkaṇḍeyaḥ parasya bhāryā yā pūrvam mṛte bhartari yā punar nāradaḥ a sūtāḥ vā prasūtāḥ vā gṛhasthānām para striyaḥ parāmṛṣṭā iti tāḥ varjyāḥ dharma ācāreṣu dūṣitāḥ na ca āsām havya kavyāni pratigṛhṇanti devatāḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ para kṣetreṣu yaḥ bījam cāpalyāt visṛjet naraḥ nāradaḥ svayam vṛttaḥ tat bījam na vinaśyati garbha ādīnām ca bahubhiḥ tāḥ ca tyājyāḥ sameṣu api mārkaṇḍeyaḥ nāradaḥ te ca jātāḥ para kṣetre dehinām pretya ca iha ca dattāni havya kavyāni nāśayanti atha dātṛṇām mārkaṇḍeyaḥ kasya tad garh putrāḥ pitṝṇām havya kavya dāḥ nāradaḥ na rakṣati hi yaḥ dārān para dārān ca gacchati garhitāḥ te narāḥ nityam dharma ācāra bahiṣkṛtāḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ kuṇḍaḥ bhoktā ca bhojī ca kutsitāḥ pitṛ daivataiḥ nāradaḥ yātudhānāḥ piśācāḥ ca pratigṛhṇanti taiḥ hutam havyam kavyam ca taiḥ dattam ye ca bhūtāḥ niśācarāḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ atha te rākṣasāḥ prītāḥ kim prayacchanti dātṛṇām nāradaḥ kim vā dharma phalam teṣām bhavet tat ṛṣi sattama na dattam naśyate kim cit sarva bhūteṣu dātṛṇām mārkaṇḍeyaḥ pretya ca iha ca tām puṣṭim upāśnanti pradāyinaḥ atha golaka kuṇḍābhyām saṃtatiḥ yā bhaviṣyati nāradaḥ sādhvī jātāḥ sutāḥ teṣām tām vṛttim anutiṣṭhatām prīṇanti pitṛdaivatyam havya kavya samāhitāḥ evam golaka kuṇḍābhyām ye ca varṇa apadeśinaḥ havyam kavyam ca śuddhānām pratigṛhṇanti devatāḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ śrutam narāṇām cāpalyam para strīṣu prajāyatām nāradaḥ pramadānām tu cāpalye doṣam icchāmi veditum eka varṇe api doṣam tu gamanam pūrvakālikam dhātā ca samanujñātaḥ viṣṇunā tat tathā karot bhaga liṅge liṅga sarva prājña pūrvam eva prajāpatiḥ sasarja tābhyām saṃyogam anujñātaḥ cakāra saḥ tena ca eva prasādena sarvān lokān upāśnute tasmāt tu puruṣe doṣaḥ hi adhikaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ vinā garbham savarṇeṣu na tyājyāḥ gamanāt striyaḥ prāyaścittam yathānyāyam daṇḍam kuryāt sa paṇḍitaḥ śvabhiḥ vā daśanam snānam savana tritayam niśi maryādā sthāpitā pūrvam iti tīrtha antaram gate tat yoṣitām tu dīrgha āyaḥ na asti doṣaḥ vyatikrame rakṣyāḥ ca eva anya saṃvādaiḥ anya gehāt vimokṣaṇaiḥ āsām śuddhau viśeṣeṇa karmaṇām phalam aśnute na etāḥ vācyāḥ na vai vadhyāḥ na kleśyāḥ śubham icchatā viṣṇu viṣṇu prasādāt iti eva bhagaḥ tīrtha antaram gataḥ māsi māsi rajaḥ tāsām duṣkṛtāni apakarṣati striyaḥ toṣa karāḥ nṝṇām striyaḥ tuṣṭi pradāḥ sadā mārkaṇḍeyaḥ śrutam balam prabhāvaḥ ca yoṣitām muni sattama nāradaḥ bahu bhāryāsu saktasya nārī bhogeṣu dehinaḥ ṛtau vimucyamānasya sāṃnidhye bhrūṇa hā smṛtaḥ vṛddhām vandhyām su vratām ca mṛta apatyām apuṣpiṇīm ṛtu kāleṣu nārīṇām bhrūṇahatyām pramuñcati mārkaṇḍeyaḥ veśa nārīṣu vai jātāḥ parapreṣyāsu vā sutāḥ nāradaḥ paṇya strīṣu prasūtāḥ ye yasya strī tasya te sutāḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ krayāt ca kṛtrimāḥ putrāḥ pradānāt ca eva datrimāḥ nāradaḥ tīrtha bhūtāsu nārīṣu jñāyate yaḥ abhigacchati mārkaṇḍeyaḥ ṛtau tasya bhavet garbhaḥ yam vā nārī na śaṅkate narāṇām tyajatām bhāryām kāma krodhāt guṇa anvitām nāradaḥ aprasūtām prasūtām vā teṣām pṛcchāmi niṣkṛtim apāpām tyajamānasya sādhvīm matvā evam āditas ātma vaṃśaḥ svadharmaḥ vā tyajataḥ niṣkṛtiḥ na tu yaḥ naraḥ tyajate bhāryām puṣpiṇīm a prasūtikām sa naṣṭa vaṃśaḥ pitṛbhiḥ yuktaḥ tyajyeta daivataiḥ bhāryām apatya saṃjātām prasūtām putra pautriṇīm putra dāra parityāgī na saṃprāpnoti niṣkṛtim evam hi bhāryām tyajatām narāṇām na asti niṣkṛtiḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ kīdṛśīm
