eva tejasā atīva puṇyāḥ te bhāgāḥ salilasya ca tejasā manasaḥ ca pṛthivyāḥ ca puṇya tīrthāḥ tathā apare ubhayayoḥ eva yaḥ snātaḥ sa siddhim śīghram āpnuyāt yathā balam kriyā hīnam kriyā vā bala varjitā evam śarīra śaucena tīrtha śaucena ca anvitaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ sarveṣām upavāsānām yat śreyaḥ su mahat phalam bhīṣmaḥ śṛṇu rājan yathā gītam svayam eva svayambhunā yat kṛtvā nirvṛtaḥ bhūyāt puruṣaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ dvādaśyām mārgaśīrṣe tu ahorātreṇa keśavam arcya aśvamedham āpnoti duṣkṛtam ca asya naśyati tathā eva pauṣa māse tu pūjya nārāyaṇa iti ca ahorātreṇa dvādaśyām māgha māse tu mādhavam ahorātreṇa dvādaśyām caitre viṣṇuḥ iti smaran vaiśākha māse dvādaśyām pūjayan madhusūdanam ahorātreṇa dvādaśyām jyeṣṭhe māsi trivikramam āṣāḍhe māsi dvādaśyām vāmana iti ca pūjayet ahorātreṇa dvādaśyām śrāvaṇe māsi śrīdharam pañcayajñān avāpnoti vimāna sthaḥ sa modate tathā bhādrapade māsi hṛṣīkeśa iti pūjayan sautrāmaṇim avāpnoti pūta ātmā bhavate ca hi dvādaśyām āśvine māsi padmanābha iti ca arcayan go sahasra phalam puṇyam prāpnuyāt na atra saṃśayaḥ dvādaśyām kārttike māsi pūjya dāmodara iti ca gavām yajñam avāpnoti pumān strī vā na saṃśayaḥ abhyarcya puṇḍarīkākṣam evam saṃvatsaram tu yaḥ atas param na upavāsaḥ bhavati iti viniścayaḥ uvāca bhagavant viṣṇuḥ svayam eva purātanam vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ śara talpa gatam bhīṣmam vṛddham kuru pitāmaham upagamya mahā prājñaḥ paryapṛcchat yudhiṣṭhiraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ jñānam rūpam ca saubhāgyam priya tvam ca katham bhavet bhīṣmaḥ mārgaśīrṣasya māsasya candre mūlena saṃyute pādau mūlena rāja indra jaṅghāyām atha rohiṇīm aśvinyām sakthinī ca eva ūrū ca āṣāḍhayoḥ tathā guhyam tu phālgunī vidyāt kṛttikā kaṭikāḥ tathā nābhim bhādrapade vidyāt revatyām akṣi maṇḍalam pṛṣṭham eva dhaniṣṭhāsu anurādhā uttarāḥ tathā bāhubhyām tu viśākhāsu hastau hasteṣu nirdiśet punarvasu aṅguliḥ rājan āśleṣāsu nakhāḥ tathā grīvā jyeṣṭhā ca rāja indra śravaṇena tu karṇayoḥ mukham puṣyeṇa rāja indra danta uṣṭhau svātiḥ ucyate hastam śatabhiṣām ca eva maghām ca eva atha nāsikām netre mṛgaśiraḥ vidyāt lalāṭam mitram eva tu bharaṇyām tu śiraḥ vidyāt keśān ārdrām narādhipa samāpte tu ghṛtam dadyāt brāhmaṇe vedapārage subhagaḥ darśanīyaḥ ca jñānī bhogī ca jāyate jāyate paripūrṇa aṅgaḥ paurṇamāsyām iva uḍurāj uvāca pitāmaha mahā bāho sarva śāstra viśārada śrotum icchāmi martyānām saṃsāra vidhim uttamam mṛtam śarīram utsṛjya kāṣṭha loṣṭa samam janāḥ uvāca asau āyāti bhagavān bṛhaspatiḥ udāra dhīḥ uvāca tayoḥ saṃvadatoḥ evam pārtha gāṅgeyayoḥ tadā ājagāma viśuddha ātmā bhagavān sa bṛhaspatiḥ tatas rājā samutthāya dhṛtarāṣṭra purogamaḥ pūjām anupamām cakre sarve te ca sabhāsadaḥ uvāca martyasya kaḥ sahāyaḥ vai pitā mātā sutaḥ guruḥ mṛtam śarīram utsṛjya kāṣṭha loṣṭa samam janāḥ asahāyaḥ pitā mātā tathā bhrātā sutaḥ guruḥ mṛtam śarīram utsṛjya kāṣṭha loṣṭa samam janāḥ muhūrtam upatiṣṭhanti tatas yānti parāṅmukhāḥ tasmāt dharmaḥ sahāya arthe sevitavyaḥ sadā nṛbhiḥ tasmāt nyāya āgataiḥ arthaiḥ dharmam seveta paṇḍitaḥ dharmaḥ ekaḥ manuṣyāṇām sahāyaḥ pāralaukikaḥ lobhāt mohāt anukrośāt bhayāt vā api a bahu śrutaḥ naraḥ karoti akāryāṇi para arthe lobha mohitaḥ dharmaḥ ca arthaḥ ca kāmaḥ ca tritayam jīvite phalam uvāca śarīra vicayam jñātum buddhiḥ tu mama jāyate mṛtam śarīra rahitam sūkṣmam avyakta tām gatam pṛthivī vāyuḥ ākāśam apaḥ jyotiḥ ca pañcamam prāṇinām iha sarveṣām sākṣi bhūtāni ca aniśam tvac asthi māṃsam śukram ca śoṇitam ca mahāmate devatāḥ pañcabhūta sthāḥ kim bhūyas śrotum icchasi uvāca annam aśnanti ye devāḥ śarīra sthāḥ nareśvara pṛthivī vāyuḥ ākāśam apaḥ jyotiḥ manaḥ tathā tatas tṛpteṣu rāja indra teṣu bhūteṣu pañcasu manaḥ ṣaṣṭheṣu śuddha ātman retaḥ saṃpadyate mahat tatas garbhaḥ saṃbhavati strī puṃsoḥ pārtha saṃgame etat te sarvam ākhyātam kim bhūyas śrotum icchasi uvāca ākhyātam etat bhavatā garbhaḥ saṃjāyate yathā devatāḥ pañcabhūta sthāḥ kim bhūyas śrotum icchasi uvāca bhoga vaśyam karma vaśyam yātanā vaśyam iti api etat trayāṇām āsādya karmataḥ saḥ aśnute phalam jīvaḥ dharma samāyuktaḥ śīghram retaḥ tvam āgataḥ strīṇām puṣpam samāsādya sūte kālena bhārata duḥkham saṃsāra cakram ca naraḥ kleśam ca vindati jīvaḥ moha samāyuktaḥ tat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu iha sthānāni puṇyāni deva tulyāni bhū tale kharaḥ jīvati varṣāṇi daśan pañca ca bhārata kharaḥ mṛtaḥ balīvardaḥ sapta varṣāṇi jīvati balīvardaḥ mṛtaḥ ca api jāyate brahmarākṣasaḥ brahmarakṣaḥ tu trīn māsān tatas jāyati brāhmaṇaḥ tatra jīvati varṣāṇi daśan pañca ca bhārata gardabhaḥ pañca varṣāṇi pañca varṣāṇi sūkaraḥ kukkuṭaḥ pañca varṣāṇi pañca varṣāṇi jambukaḥ śvā varṣam ekam bhavati tatas jāyati mānavaḥ upādhyāyasya yaḥ pāpam śiṣyaḥ kuryāt abuddhimān sa jīvaḥ iha saṃsārān trīn āpnoti na saṃśayaḥ prāk śvā bhavati rāja indra tatas kravyād tatas kharaḥ tatas pretaḥ parikliṣṭaḥ paścāt jāyati brāhmaṇaḥ manasā api guroḥ bhāryām yaḥ śiṣyaḥ yāti pāpa kṛt saḥ adhamān yāti saṃsārān adharmeṇa iha cetasā śva yonau tu sa saṃbhūtaḥ trīṇi varṣāṇi jīvati kṛmi bhāvam anuprāptaḥ varṣam ekam sa jīvati yadi putra samam śiṣyam guruḥ hanyāt akāraṇe ātmanaḥ kāmakāreṇa saḥ api haṃsaḥ prajāyate saḥ api rājan mṛtaḥ jantuḥ pūrvam jāyati gardabhaḥ gardabha tvam tu saṃprāpya daśa varṣāṇi jīvati saṃvatsaram tu kumbhīraḥ tatas jāyati mānavaḥ putrasya mātā pitarau yasya ruṣṭau ubhau api kharaḥ jīvati māsān tu daśa śvā ca caturdaśa biḍālaḥ sapta māsān tu tatas jāyati mānavaḥ mātā pitaram ākruśya sārikaḥ saṃprajāyate tāḍayitvā tu tau eva jāyate kacchapaḥ nṛpa kacchapaḥ daśa varṣāṇi trīṇi varṣāṇi śalyakaḥ vyālaḥ bhūtvā tu ṣaṭ māsān tatas jāyati mānuṣaḥ bhartṛ piṇḍam upāśnan yaḥ rāja dviṣṭāni sevate vānaraḥ daśa varṣāṇi trīṇi varṣāṇi mūṣakaḥ śvā bhūtvā ca atha ṣaṭ māsān tatas jāyati mānuṣaḥ tatas śvā ca api bhavati tatas bhavati mānuṣaḥ nyāsa apahartā tu naraḥ yamasya viṣayam gataḥ saṃsārāṇām śatam gatvā kṛmi yonau prajāyate tatra jīv varṣa daśan pañca ca bhārata duṣkṛtasya kṣayam gatvā tatas jāyati mānuṣaḥ asūyakaḥ naraḥ ca api mṛtaḥ jāyati śārṅgakaḥ asūyakaḥ kutsitaḥ ca caṇḍālaḥ duḥkham aśnute viśvāsa hartā tu naraḥ mīnaḥ jāyati durmatiḥ bhūtvā mīnaḥ aṣṭa varṣāṇi mṛgaḥ jāyati bhārata mṛgaḥ tu caturaḥ māsān tatas chāgaḥ prajāyate chāgaḥ tu nidhanam prāpya pūrṇe saṃvatsare tatas kīṭaḥ saṃjāyate jantuḥ tatas jāyati mānuṣaḥ dhānyān yavān tilān māṣān kulatthān sarṣapān caṇān kalāyān atha mudgān ca godhūmān atasīḥ tathā sa jāyate mahā rāja mūṣakaḥ nirapatrapaḥ mūṣakaḥ jāyate paścāt sūkaraḥ jāyate tatas tatas pre mahat rāja punar jan sūkara śvā tatas jāyate mūḍhaḥ karmaṇā tena pārthiva śvā bhūtvā pañca varṣāṇi tatas jāyati mānuṣaḥ paradāra abhimarśam tu kṛtvā jāyati vai vṛkaḥ śvā sṛgālaḥ tatas gṛdhraḥ vyālaḥ kaṅkaḥ bakaḥ tathā sakhī bhāryām guroḥ bhāryām rāja bhāryām tathā eva ca pradharṣayitvā kāmāt yaḥ mṛtaḥ jāyati sūkaraḥ śvā biḍālaḥ kukkuṭaḥ ca jāyeta api pipīlikāḥ sūkaraḥ pañca varṣāṇi pañca varṣāṇi śvāvidhaḥ vilāḷaḥ pañca varṣāṇi pañca varṣāṇi kukkuṭaḥ pipīlakaḥ tu ṣaṭ māsān kīṭaḥ syāt māsam eva ca etān āsādya saṃsārān kṛmi yonau prajāyate tatra jīvati māsān tu kṛmi yonau trayodaśa tatas adharma kṣayam kṛtvā punar jāyati mānuṣaḥ mohāt karoti yaḥ vighnam sa mṛtaḥ jāyate kṛmiḥ śvā bhūtvā sapta janmāni tatas jāyati mānavaḥ dvija grāma ādhipatyam hi kṛtvā brahma sva bhakṣakaḥ śvāna yoni śatam prāpya caṇḍālaḥ puṣkalaḥ tatas varṣāt pañcadaśāt pūrvam kramāt bhavati mānuṣaḥ kṛmi jīvati varṣāṇi daśan pañca ca bhārata adharmasya kṣayam kṛtvā tatas jāyati mānuṣaḥ pūrvam dattvā tu yaḥ kanyām dvitīye saṃprayacchati tatra jīvati varṣāṇi trayodaśa yudhiṣṭhira adharma saṃkṣaye yuktaḥ tatas jāyati mānuṣaḥ deva kāryam upākṛtya pitṛ kāryam atha api ca vāyasaḥ daśa varṣāṇi tatas jāyati kukkuṭaḥ jāyate lavakaḥ ca api māsam tasmāt tu mānuṣaḥ jyeṣṭham pitṛ samam ca api bhrātaram yaḥ avamanyate krauñcaḥ jīvati māsān tu daśa dvau sapta pañca ca vṛṣalaḥ brāhmaṇīm gatvā kṛmi yonau prajāyate tatra apatyam samutpādya tatas jāyati mūṣakaḥ kṛtaghnaḥ tu mṛtaḥ rājan yamasya viṣayam gam paṭṭisam mudgaram śūlam agni kumbham ca dāruṇam asipattravanam ghoram vālukām kūṭaśālmalīm etāḥ ca anyāḥ ca bahvīḥ sa yamasya viṣayam gataḥ anyāḥ ca yātanāḥ prāpya kṛmi yonau prajāyate saṃsāra cakram āsādya kṛmi yonau prajāyate kṛmiḥ bhavati varṣāṇi daśa pañca ca bhārata saṃsārān ca bahūn gatvā tatas tiryak prajāyate mṛtaḥ duḥkham anuprāpya bahu varṣa gaṇān iha aśastram puruṣam hatvā sa śastraḥ puruṣa adhamaḥ artha arthī yadi vā vairī sa mṛtaḥ jāyate kharaḥ mṛgaḥ bhūtvā tatas śastraiḥ vadhyate bhṛśa dāruṇam māse caturthe saṃprāpte śvāpadaḥ saṃprajāyate śvāpadaḥ daśa varṣāṇi dvīpī varṣāṇi pañca ca adharmasya kṣayam kṛtvā tatas jāyati mānuṣaḥ bahūn kleśān samāsādya saṃsārān ca eva viṃśatim tatas paścāt mahā rāja kṛmi yonau prajāyate kṛmiḥ viṃśati varṣāṇi bhūtvā jāyati mānuṣaḥ bhojanam corayitvā tu makṣikā jāyate naraḥ makṣikā saṃgha vaśagaḥ bahūn māsān bhavati uta tatas pāpa kṣayam kṛ mānuṣa tvam avāpnute vādyam hṛtvā tu puruṣaḥ maśakaḥ saṃprajāyate tathā piṇyāka saṃmiśram aśanam corayet naraḥ sa jāyate babhru samaḥ dāruṇaḥ mūṣakaḥ naraḥ daśan vai mānuṣān nityam pāpa ātmā sa viśām pate ghṛtam hṛtvā tu durbuddhiḥ kākamadguḥ prajāyate matsya māṃsam atho hṛtvā kākaḥ jāyati durmatiḥ lavaṇam corayitvā tu cīrīvākaḥ prajāyate dadhi hṛtvā bakaḥ ca api plavaḥ matsyān a saṃskṛtān corayitvā payaḥ ca api balākā saṃprajāyate hṛtvā paiṣṭam apūpam ca kumbholūkaḥ prajāyate phalam vā mūlakam hṛtvā apūpam vā pipīlikaḥ phalāni vānaraḥ hṛtvā apūpam hṛtvā pipīlikaḥ corayitvā tu niṣpāvam jāyate hala golakaḥ kāṃsyam hṛtvā tu durbuddhiḥ hārītaḥ jāyate naraḥ rājatam bhājanam hṛtvā kapotaḥ saṃprajāyate hṛtvā tu kāñcanam bhāṇḍam kṛmi yonau prajāyate kauśikam tu tatas hṛtvā naraḥ jāyati vartakaḥ aṃśukam corayitvā tu śukaḥ jāyati mānavaḥ corayitvā dukūlam tu mṛtaḥ haṃsaḥ prajāyate krauñcaḥ kārpāsikam hṛtvā mṛtaḥ jāyati mānavaḥ sarpaḥ kārpāsakam hṛtvā kṣaumam hṛtvā śaśaḥ bhavet chāgaḥ ca api āvikam hṛtvā kūrmaḥ carma apahārakaḥ corayitvā naraḥ paṭṭam tu āvikam vā api bhārata kṣaumam ca vastram ādāya śaśaḥ jantuḥ prajāyate varṇān hṛtvā tu puruṣaḥ mṛtaḥ jāyati barhiṇa hṛtvā raktāni vastrāṇi jāyate jīvajīvakaḥ varṇaka ādīn tathā gandhān corayitvā tu mānavaḥ tatra jīvati varṣāṇi tatas daśa ca pañca ca adharmasya kṣayam gatvā tatas jāyati mānuṣaḥ viśvāsa tu nikṣip yad nihnu mānava matsya yonim anuprāpya mṛtaḥ jāyati mānuṣaḥ mānuṣa tvam anuprāpya kṣīṇa āyuḥ upapadyate pāpāni tu naraḥ kṛtvā tiryak jāyati bhārata na ca ātmanaḥ pramāṇam te dharmam jānanti kim cana ye pāpāni narāḥ kṛtvā nirasyanti vrataiḥ sadā a saṃvāsāḥ prajāyante mlecchāḥ ca api na saṃśaya narāḥ pāpa samācārāḥ lobha moha samanvitāḥ eteṣām eva jantūnām patnī tvam upayānti tāḥ para sva haraṇa doṣa sarva eva prakīrtay aparasmin kathā yoge bhūyas śroṣyasi bhārata etat mayā mahā rāja brahmaṇaḥ vadataḥ purā sura ṛṣīṇām śrutam madhye pṛṣṭaḥ ca api yathātatham uvāca kṛtvā karmāṇi pāpāni katham yānti śubhām gatim karmaṇā ca kṛtena iha kena yānti śubhām gatim kṛtvā pāpāni karmāṇi adharma vaśam āgataḥ mohāt adharmam yaḥ kṛtvā punar samanutapyate tathā tathā śarīram tu tena adharmeṇa mucyate yadi vyāharate rājan viprāṇām dharma vādinām a dattvā api pradānāni vividhāni samāhitaḥ pradānāni tu vakṣyāmi yāni dattvā yudhiṣṭhira naraḥ kṛtvā api akāryāṇi tadā dharmeṇa yujyate sarveṣām eva dānānām annam śreṣṭham udāhṛtam prāṇāḥ hi annam manuṣyāṇām tasmāt jantuḥ ca jāyate anne pratiṣṭhitāḥ lokāḥ tasmāt annam prakāśate annam eva praśaṃsanti deva ṛṣi pitṛ mānavāḥ svādhyāya samupetebhyaḥ prahṛṣṭena antarātmanā yasya hi annam upāśnanti brāhmaṇānām śatāḥ daśa brāhmaṇānām sahasrāṇi daśa bhojya nara ṛṣabha bhaikṣeṇa annam samāhṛtya vipraḥ veda puraskṛtaḥ suvarṇa dānāt pāpāni naśyanti su bahūni api dattvā vṛtti karīm bhūmim pātakena api mucyate pārāyaṇaiḥ ca vedānām mucyate pātakaiḥ dvijaḥ gāyatryāḥ ca eva lakṣeṇa go sahasrasya tarpaṇāt veda artham jñāpayitvā tu śuddhān viprān yathārthāt sarva ātithyam param hi eṣām tasmāt annam param smṛtam a hiṃsan brāhmaṇam nityam nyāyena paripālya ca tena apohati dharma ātmā duṣkṛtam karma pāṇḍava ṣaṣ bhāga pariśuddham ca kṛṣeḥ bhāgam upārjitam avāpya prāṇa saṃdeham kārkaśyena samārjitam annam dattvā dvijātibhyaḥ śūdraḥ pāpāt pramucyate śūdra annam na eva bhoktavyam vipraiḥ dharma parāyaṇaiḥ satām panthānam āśritya sarva pāpāt pramucyate dāna kṛdbhiḥ kṛtaḥ panthāḥ yena yānti manīṣiṇaḥ te sma prāṇasya dātāraḥ tebhyaḥ dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ sarva avastham manuṣyeṇa nyāyena annam upārjitam kāryam pātra gatam nityam annam hi paramā gatiḥ yatet brāhmaṇa pūrvam hi bhoktum annam gṛhī sadā avandhyam divasam kuryāt anna dānena mānavaḥ bhojayitvā daśa śatam naraḥ veda vidām nṛpa nyāya vid dharma viduṣām itihāsa vidām tathā na yāti narakam ghoram saṃsārān ca na sevate rūpavān kīrtimān ca eva dhanavān ca upapadyate mūlam etat hi dharmāṇām pradānasya ca bhārata uvāca tapaḥ atha guru śuśrūṣā kim śreyaḥ puruṣam prati sarvāṇi etāni dharmasya pṛthak dvārāṇi sarvaśas śṛṇu saṃkīrtyamānāni ṣaḍ eva bharata ṛṣabha ahiṃsā apāśrayam dharmam yaḥ sādhayati vai naraḥ trīn doṣān sarva bhūteṣu nidhāya puruṣaḥ sadā ahiṃsakāni bhūtāni daṇḍena vinihanti yaḥ ātma upamaḥ ca bhūteṣu yaḥ vai bhavati pūruṣaḥ sarva bhūta ātma bhūtasya sarva bhūtāni paśyataḥ eṣa saṃkṣepataḥ dharmaḥ kāmāt anyaḥ pravartate eṣā eva te astu upamā jīva loke yathā dharmaḥ naipuṇena upadiṣṭaḥ uvāca divam ācakrame dhīmān paśyatām eva naḥ tadā uvāca tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā śara talpe pitāmaham ṛṣayaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ devāḥ praśaṃsanti mahāmate ahiṃsā lakṣaṇam dharmam veda prāmāṇya darśanāt karmaṇā manujaḥ kurvan hiṃsām pārthiva sattama uvāca caturvidhā iyam nirdiṣṭā ahiṃsā brahma vādibhiḥ yathā sarvaḥ catuṣpādaḥ tribhiḥ pādaiḥ na tiṣṭhati yathā nāga pade anyāni padāni pada gāminām sarvāṇi eva apidhīyante pada jātāni kauñjare evam lokeṣu ahiṃsā tu nirdiṣṭā dharmāt parā pūrvam tu manasā tyaktvā tathā vācā atha karmaṇā tri kāraṇam tu nirdiṣṭam śrūyate brahma vādibhiḥ manaḥ vāci tathā āsvāde doṣāḥ hi eṣu pratiṣṭhitāḥ hiṃsām tu na upayuñjīta tathā hiṃsā caturvidhā kāye manasi vākye ca doṣāḥ hi ete prakīrtitāḥ na bhakṣayanti atas māṃsam tapaḥ yuktāḥ manīṣiṇaḥ doṣān tu bhakṣaṇe rājan māṃsasya iha nibodha me putra māṃsa upamam jānan khādate yaḥ vicetanaḥ māṃsam moha samāviṣṭaḥ puruṣaḥ saḥ adhamaḥ smṛtaḥ mātā pitṛ samāyoge putra tvam jāyate yathā hiṃsām kṛtvā avaśaḥ pāpaḥ bhūyiṣṭham jāyate tathā rasam ca prati jihvāyāḥ prajñānam jāyate tathā tathā śāstreṣu niyatam rāgaḥ hi āsvāditāt bhavet a saṃskṛtāḥ saṃskṛtāḥ ca lavaṇa a lavaṇāḥ tathā prajñāyante yathā bhāvāḥ tathā cittam nirudhyate bherī śaṅkha mṛdaṅga ādyān tantrī śabdān ca puṣkalān niṣeviṣyanti vai mandāḥ māṃsa bhakṣāḥ katham narāḥ pareṣām dhana dhānyānām hiṃsakāḥ stāvakāḥ tathā praśaṃsakāḥ ca māṃsasya nityam svarge bahiṣkṛtāḥ rasam gṛddhyā abhibhūtāḥ vai praśaṃsanti phala arthinaḥ praśaṃsā hi eva māṃsasya doṣa karma phala anvitā bhasma viṣṭhā kṛmiḥ vā api niṣṭhā yasya īdṛśī dhruvā sa kāyaḥ para pīḍābhiḥ katham dhāryaḥ vipaścitā jīvitam hi parityajya bahavaḥ sādhavaḥ janāḥ sva māṃsaiḥ para māṃsāni paripālya divam gatāḥ evam eṣā mahā rāja caturbhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ vṛtā ahiṃsā tava nirdiṣṭā sarva dharma artha saṃhitā uvāca śrāddheṣu ca bhavān āha pitṝn āmiṣa kāṅkṣiṇaḥ māṃsaiḥ bahuvidhaiḥ proktaḥ tvayā śrāddha vidhiḥ purā jātaḥ naḥ saṃśayaḥ dharme māṃsasya parivarjane doṣaḥ bhakṣayataḥ kaḥ syāt kaḥ ca a bhakṣayataḥ guṇaḥ hatvā bhakṣayataḥ vā api pareṇa upahṛ vā hanyāt vā yaḥ parasya arthe krītvā vā bhakṣayet naraḥ niścayena cikīrṣāmi dharmam etam sanātanam uvāca māṃsasya bhakṣaṇe rājan yaḥ adharmaḥ kuru puṃgava tam me śṛṇu yathātattvam yaḥ ca asya vidhiḥ uttamaḥ rūpam avyaṅga tām āyuḥ buddhim sattvam balam smṛtim prāptu kāmaiḥ naraiḥ hiṃsā varjitā vai kṛtātmabhiḥ ṛṣīṇām atra saṃvādaḥ bahuśas kuru puṃgava babhūva teṣām tu matam yat tat śṛṇu yudhiṣṭhira a māṃsa bhakṣaṇam rājan praśaṃsanti manīṣiṇaḥ tam mitram sarva bhūtānām manuḥ svāyambhuvaḥ abravīt adhṛṣyaḥ sarva bhūtānām viśvāsyaḥ sarva jantuṣu sādhūnām saṃmataḥ nityam bhavet māṃsasya varjanāt nāradaḥ prāha dharma ātmā niyatam saḥ avasīdati a viśvāsyaḥ avasīdet saḥ iti ha uvāca nāradaḥ madhu māṃsa nivṛttyā iti prāha evam sa bṛhaspatiḥ māsi māsi aśvamedhena yaḥ yajeta śatam samāḥ yaḥ bhakṣayitvā māṃsāni paścāt api nivartate cartum vratam idam śreṣṭham sarva prāṇi abhaya pradam sarva bhūteṣu yaḥ vidvān dadāti abhaya dakṣiṇām dātā bhavati loke sa prāṇānām na atra saṃśayaḥ evam vai paramam dharmam praśaṃsanti manīṣiṇaḥ prāṇāḥ yathā ātmanaḥ abhīṣṭāḥ bhūtānām api te tathā vikīrṇa kaṇṭakena api tṛṇa praspandane bhayam mṛtyutaḥ bhayam asti iti viduṣām bhūtim icchatām kim punar hanyamānānām tarasā jīvita arthinām arogāṇām apāpānām pāpaiḥ māṃsa upajīvibhiḥ mṛtyutaḥ bhayam asti iti śaṅkāyām duḥkham uttaram ahiṃsā paramaḥ dharmaḥ tathā ahiṃsā param tapaḥ na hi māṃsam tṛṇāt kāṣṭhāt upalāt vā api jāyate hatvā jantum tatas māṃsam tasmāt doṣaḥ asya bhakṣaṇe svāhā svadhā amṛta bhujaḥ devāḥ satya ārjava priyāḥ kravyādān rākṣasān viddhi jihma anṛta parāyaṇān rākṣasa indra bhayāt muktāḥ sarva bhūta parāyaṇāḥ kāntāreṣu atha ghoreṣu durgeṣu gahaneṣu ca rātrau ahani saṃdhyāsu catvareṣu sabhāsu ca udyateṣu ca śastreṣu mṛga vyāla bhayeṣu ca śaraṇyaḥ sarva bhūtānām viśvāsyaḥ sarva jantuṣu ghātakaḥ khādaka arthāya tam ghātayati vai naraḥ khādaka artham atas hiṃsā mṛga ādīnām pravartate yasmāt grasati ca eva āyuḥ hiṃsakānām mahā dyute tasmāt vivarjayet māṃsam yaḥ icchet bhūtim ātmanaḥ trātāram na adhigacchanti raudrāḥ prāṇi vihiṃsakāḥ udvejanīyāḥ bhūtānām yathā vyāla mṛgāḥ tathā saṃsargāt vā atha pāpānām adharma ruci tā nṛṇām māṃsasya a bhakṣaṇam prāhuḥ niyatāḥ parama ṛṣayaḥ idam tu khalu kaunteya śrutam āsīt purā mayā mārkaṇḍeyasya vadataḥ ye doṣāḥ māṃsa bhakṣaṇe bhīṣmaḥ mārkaṇḍeyena yat ca uktam śṛṇu mama paramam vacaḥ yudhiṣṭhira mahā bāho ye doṣāḥ māṃsa bhakṣaṇe yaḥ hi khādati māṃsāni prāṇinām jīvita arthinām hatānām vā mṛtānām vā yathā hantā tathā eva saḥ a khādan anumodan ca bhāva doṣeṇa mānavaḥ adhṛṣyaḥ sarva bhūtānām āyuṣmān nīrujaḥ sukhī bhavati a bhakṣayan māṃsam dayāvān prāṇinām iha hiraṇya dānaiḥ go dānaiḥ bhūmi dānaiḥ ca sarvaśas māṃsasya a bhakṣaṇe dharmaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ syāt iti śrutiḥ a prokṣitam vṛthāmāṃsam vidhi hīnam na bhakṣayet bhakṣayan nirayam yāti naraḥ na asti atra saṃśayaḥ prokṣita abhyukṣitam māṃsam tathā brāhmaṇa kāmyayā khādakasya kṛte jantum yaḥ hanyāt puruṣa adhamaḥ hanyāt jantum sa vai naraka bhāj naraḥ bhakṣayitvā tu yaḥ māṃsam paścāt api nivartate āhartā ca anumantā ca viśastā kraya vikrayī saṃskartā ca upabhoktā ca ghātakāḥ sarve eva te purāṇam ṛṣibhiḥ juṣṭam vedeṣu pariniścitam yathā uktam rāja śārdūla na tu tat mokṣa kāṅkṣiṇām haviḥ yat saṃskṛtam mantraiḥ prokṣita abhyukṣitam śuci veda uktena pramāṇena pitṝṇām prakriyāsu ca atas anyathā vṛthāmāṃsam abhakṣyam manuḥ abravīt vidhinā hi narāḥ pūrvam māṃsam rājan a bhakṣayan sa varjayeta māṃsāni prāṇinām iha sarvaśas śrūyate hi purākalpe nṛṇām vrīhi mayaḥ paśuḥ yena ayajanta yajvānaḥ puṇya loka parāyaṇāḥ ṛṣibhiḥ saṃśayam pṛṣṭaḥ vasuḥ cedi patiḥ purā ākāśāt medinīm prāptaḥ tatas sa pṛthivīpatiḥ prajānām hita kāmena tu agastyena mahātmanā āraṇyāḥ sarva daivatyāḥ prokṣitāḥ tapasā mṛgāḥ kṛtaḥ hi manasaḥ yajñaḥ tena devāḥ ca tarpitāḥ kriyāḥ hi evam na hīyante pitṛ daivata saṃśritāḥ prīyante pitaraḥ ca eva nyāyatas māṃsa tarpitāḥ idam tu śṛṇu rāja indra kīrtyamānam mayā anagha a bhakṣaṇe sarva sukham māṃsasya manuja adhipa yaḥ tu varṣa śatam pūrṇam tapaḥ tapyet su dāruṇam kaumude tu viśeṣeṇa śukla pakṣe narādhipa caturaḥ vārṣikān māsān yaḥ māṃsam parivarjayet catvāri bhadrāṇi āpnoti kīrtim āyuḥ yaśaḥ balam atha vā māsam api ekam sarva māṃsāni a bhakṣayan atītya sarva duḥkhāni sukhī jīvet nirāmayaḥ ye varjayanti māṃsāni māsaśas pakṣaśas api vā teṣām hiṃsā nivṛttānām brahma lokaḥ vidhīyate māṃsam tu kaumudam pakṣam varjitam pārtha rājbhiḥ sarva bhūta ātma bhūtaiḥ taiḥ vijñāta artha parāvaraiḥ nābhāgena ambarīṣeṇa gayena ca mahātmanā āyuṣā ca anaraṇyena dilīpa raghu pūrubhiḥ kārtavīrya aniruddhābhyām nahuṣeṇa yayātinā nṛgeṇa viṣvagaśvena tathā eva śaśabindunā yuvanāśvena ca tathā śibinā auśīnareṇa ca satyam vadata mā asatyam satyam dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ etaiḥ ca anyaiḥ ca rāja indra kṛpeṇa bharatena ca duḥṣantena karūṣeṇa rāma alarka nalaiḥ tathā virūpākṣeṇa kurūṣeṇa nṛga alarka naraiḥ tathā virūpāśvena niminā janakena ca dhīmatā ikṣvākuṇā śaṃbhunā ca śvetena sagareṇa ca etaiḥ ca anyaiḥ ca rāja indra purā māṃsam na bhakṣitam śāradam kaumudam māsam tatas te svargam āpnuvan brahma loke ca tiṣṭhanti jvalamānāḥ śriyā anvitāḥ upāsyamānāḥ gandharvaiḥ strī sahasra samanvitāḥ tat etat uttamam dharmam ahiṃsā lakṣaṇam śubham ye caranti mahātmānaḥ nāka pṛṣṭhe vasanti te madhu māṃsam ca ye nityam varjayanti iha dhārmikāḥ viśiṣṭa tām jñātiṣu ca labhante na atra saṃśayaḥ imam dharmam a māṃsa ādam yaḥ caret śrāvayeta vā paṭhet vā yaḥ idam rājan śṛṇuyāt vā api abhīkṣṇaśas a māṃsa bhakṣaṇa vidhim pavitram ṛṣi pūjitam ahiṃsraḥ dāna śīlaḥ ca madhu māṃsa vivarjitaḥ buddhimān vai kuruśreṣṭha prāpnuyāt ca mahat yaśaḥ uvāca ime vai mānavāḥ loke bhṛśam māṃsasya gṛddhinaḥ visṛjya bhakṣān vividhān yathā rakṣaḥ gaṇāḥ tathā na apūpān vividha ākārān śākāni vividhāni ca ṣāḍavān rasayogān ca tathā icchanti yathā āmiṣam na manye rasataḥ kim cit māṃsataḥ asti iha kim cana tat icchāmi guṇān śrotum māṃsasya a bhakṣaṇe api vā bhakṣaṇe ca eva ye doṣāḥ tān ca eva puruṣa ṛṣabha yathā etat yādṛśam ca etat guṇāḥ ye ca asya varjane uvāca kṣata kṣīṇa abhitaptānām grāmyadharma ratāḥ ca ye adhvanā karśitānām ca na māṃsāt vidyate param sadyas vardhayati prāṇān puṣṭim agryām dadāti ca nāśaḥ bhakṣaṇa doṣasya dānam eva satām matam kṣudhitānām dvijānām ca sarveṣām ca eva jīvanam dattvā bhavati pūta ātmā śraddhayā lobha varjitaḥ śikṣayanti na yācante darśayantaḥ sva mūrtibhiḥ dāna ādyaiḥ su śuciḥ māṃsam punar na eva sa bhakṣayet na bhakṣaḥ abhyadhikaḥ kaḥ cit māṃsāt asti paraṃtapa ye bhavanti manuṣyāṇām tān me nigadataḥ śṛṇu na asti kṣudrataraḥ tasmāt na nṛśaṃsataraḥ naraḥ tasmāt dayām naraḥ kuryāt yathā ātmani tathā pare śukrāt ca tāta saṃbhūtiḥ māṃsasya iha na saṃśayaḥ yajña arthe paśavaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ iti api śrūyate śrutiḥ atas anyathā pravṛttānām rākṣasaḥ vidhiḥ ucyate kṣatriyāṇām tu yaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ vidhiḥ tam api mama śṛṇu vīryeṇa upārjitam māṃsam yathā khādan na duṣyati āraṇyāḥ sarva daivatyāḥ prokṣitāḥ sarvaśas mṛgāḥ rakṣaṇa arthāya bhūtānām hiṃsrān hanyāt mṛgān punar sama tām upasaṃgamya rūpam hanyāt na vā nṛpa rājarṣayaḥ sarve mṛgayām yānti bhārata dayāvatām ime lokāḥ pare ca api tapasvinām abhayam tasya bhūtāni dadati iti anuśuśrumaḥ kṣatam ca skhalitam ca eva patitam kliṣṭam āhatam sarva bhūtāni rakṣanti sameṣu viṣameṣu ca na enam vyāla mṛgāḥ ghnanti na piśācāḥ na rākṣasāḥ prāṇa dānāt param dānam na bhūtam na bhaviṣyati aniṣṭam sarva bhūtānām maraṇam nāma bhārata mṛtyu kāle hi bhūtānām sadyas jāyati vepathuḥ jāti janma jarā duḥkhe nityam saṃsāra sāgare garbha vāseṣu pacyante kṣāra amla kaṭukaiḥ rasaiḥ mūtra śleṣma purīṣāṇām sparśaiḥ ca bhṛśa dāruṇaiḥ jātāḥ ca api avaśāḥ tatra bhid punar punar pāṭyamānāḥ ca dṛśyante vivaśāḥ māṃsa gṛddhinaḥ kumbhīpāke ca pacyante tām tām yonim upāgatāḥ ākramya māryamāṇāḥ ca bhrāmyante vai punar punar tasmāt prāṇiṣu sarveṣu dayāvān ātmavān bhavet sarva māṃsāni yaḥ rājan yāvajjīvam na bhakṣayet svarge sa vipulam sthānam prāpnuyāt na atra saṃśayaḥ ye bhakṣayanti māṃsāni bhūtānām jīvita eṣiṇām ākroṣṭā ākruśyate rājan dveṣṭā dveṣya tvam āpnute ahiṃsā paramaḥ dharmaḥ tathā ahiṃsā paraḥ damaḥ ahiṃsā paramam dānam ahiṃsā paramam tapaḥ ahiṃsā paramaḥ yajñaḥ tathā ahiṃsā param balam ahiṃsā parama mitra ahiṃsā paramam sukham ahiṃsā parama satyam ahiṃsā paramam śrutam sarva yajñeṣu vā dānam sarva tīrtheṣu ca āplutam ahiṃsraḥ sarva bhūtānām yathā mātā yathā pitā agastyena purā rājan māṃsa bhakṣam tu jāṅgale etat phalam ahiṃsāyāḥ bhūyas ca kuru puṃgava na hi śakyāḥ guṇāḥ vaktum iha varṣa śataiḥ api uvāca akāmāḥ ca sa kāmāḥ ca hatāḥ ye asmin mahā āhave kām yonim pratipannāḥ te tat me brūhi pitāmaha duḥkham prāṇa parityāgaḥ puruṣāṇām mahā mṛdhe jānāmi tattvam dharma jña prāṇatyāgam su duṣkaram samṛddhe vā asamṛddhe vā śubhe vā yadi vā aśubhe kāraṇam tatra me brūhi sarvajñaḥ hi asi mama mataḥ uvāca samṛddhe vā asamṛddhe vā śubhe vā yadi vā aśubhe saṃsāre asmin samājātāḥ prāṇinaḥ pṛthivīpate niratāḥ yena bhāvena tatra me śṛṇu kāraṇam atra te vartayiṣyāmi purāvṛttam idam nṛpa dvaipāyanasya saṃvādam kīṭasya ca yudhiṣṭhira brahma bhūtaḥ caran vipraḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ purā dadarśa kīṭam dhāvantam śīghram śakaṭa vartmani gati jñaḥ sarva bhūtānām ruta jñaḥ ca śarīriṇām sarvajñaḥ sarvatas dṛṣṭvā kīṭam vacanam abravīt uvāca śakaṭasya asya mahataḥ ghoṣam śrutvā bhayam mama āgatam vai mahābuddhe svanaḥ eṣa hi dāruṇaḥ śrūyate na sa mām hanyāt iti tasmāt apākrame śvasatām ca śṛṇomi evam go putrāṇām pracodyatām vahatām su mahā bhāram saṃnikarṣe svanam prabho nṛṇām ca saṃvāhayatām śrūyate vividhaḥ svanaḥ soḍhum asmadvidhena eṣa na śakyaḥ kīṭa yoninā tasmāt apakramāmi eṣa bhayāt asmāt su dāruṇāt duḥkham hi mṛtyuḥ bhūtānām jīvitam ca su durlabham atas bhītaḥ palāyāmi gaccheyam na asukham sukhāt uvāca iti uktaḥ sa tu tam prāha kutas kīṭa sukham tava śabdam sparśam rasam gandham bhogān ca uccāvacān bahūn na abhijānāsi kīṭa tvam śreyaḥ maraṇam eva te uvāca cetayāmi mahā prājña tasmāt icchāmi jīvitum iha api viṣayaḥ sarvaḥ yathādeham pravartitaḥ mānuṣāḥ tiryagāḥ ca eva pṛthak bhogāḥ viśeṣataḥ aham āsam manuṣyaḥ vai śūdraḥ bahu dhanaḥ purā a brahmaṇyaḥ nṛśaṃsaḥ ca kadaryaḥ vṛddhi jīvanaḥ vāc tīkṣṇaḥ nikṛti prajñaḥ moṣṭā viśvasya sarvaśas bhṛtya atithi janaḥ ca api gṛhe paryuṣitaḥ mayā mātsaryāt svādu kāmena nṛśaṃsena bubhūṣatā deva artham pitṛ yajña artham annam śraddhā kṛtam mayā guptam śaraṇam āśritya bhayeṣu śaraṇa āgatāḥ akasmāt naḥ bhayāt tyaktāḥ na ca trātā abhaya eṣiṇaḥ tyaktvā akasmāt niśāyām ca na dattam abhayam mayā dhanam dhānyam priyān dārān yānam vāsaḥ tathā adbhutam śriyam dṛṣṭvā manuṣyāṇām asūyāmi nirarthakam īrṣyuḥ para sukham dṛṣṭvā ātatāyī abubhūṣakaḥ trivarga hantā ca anyeṣām ātma kāma anuvartakaḥ nṛśaṃsa guṇa bhūyiṣṭham purā karma kṛtam mayā tena eṣā kṛmi tā prāptā bhayasya jananī sadā śubhānām api jānāmi kṛtānām karmaṇām phalam mātā ca pūjitā vṛddhā brāhmaṇaḥ ca arcitaḥ mayā sakṛt jāti guṇa upetaḥ saṃgatyā gṛham āgataḥ atithiḥ pūjitaḥ brahman tena mām na ajahāt smṛtiḥ karmaṇā tena ca eva aham sukha āśām iha lakṣaye uvāca aham hi darśanāt eva tārayāmi tapaḥ balāt jānāmi pāpaiḥ sva kṛtaiḥ gatam tvām kīṭa kīṭa tām karma bhūmi kṛtam devāḥ bhuñjate tiryagāḥ ca ye dharmāt api manuṣyeṣu kāmaḥ arthaḥ ca yathā guṇaiḥ vāc buddhi pāṇi pādaiḥ ca api upetasya vipaścitaḥ kim hīyate manuṣyasya mandasya api hi jīvataḥ jīvan hi kurute pūjām vipra agryaḥ śaśi sūryayoḥ bruvan api kathām puṇyām tatra kīṭa tvam eṣyasi guṇa bhūtāni bhūtāni tatra tvam upabhokṣyase śakaṭa vrajaḥ ca su mahān āgataḥ ca yadṛcchayā cakra ākrameṇa bhinnaḥ ca kīṭaḥ prāṇān mumoca ha saṃbhūtaḥ kṣatriya kule prasādāt amita ojasaḥ tam ṛṣim draṣṭum agamat sarvāsu anyāsu yoniṣu dadarśa ca mahā rāja saṃprāptam rāja putra tām śvāvidh godhā varāhāṇām tathā eva mṛga pakṣiṇām śvapāka vaiśya śūdrāṇām kṣatriyāṇām ca yoniṣu etāsu eva krameṇa eva yoniṣu āsa sva karmaṇā sa kīṭa iti evam ābhāṣya ṛṣiṇā satya vādinā pratismṛtya atha jagrāha pādau mūrdhnā kṛtāñjaliḥ paryāyeṇa tatas prāpya kṣātram sthānam anuttamam uvāca idam tat atulam sthānam īpsitam daśabhiḥ guṇaiḥ yat aham prāpya kīṭa tvam āgataḥ rāja putra tām vahanti mām atibalāḥ kuñjarāḥ hema mālinaḥ syandaneṣu ca kāmbojāḥ yuktāḥ parama vājinaḥ uṣṭra aśvatara yuktāni yānāni ca vahanti mām sa bāndhavaḥ saha amātyaḥ ca aśnāmi piśita odanam gṛheṣu su nivāseṣu sukheṣu śayaneṣu ca parārdhyeṣu mahābhāga svapāmi iha su pūjitaḥ sarveṣu apararātreṣu sūta māgadha bandinaḥ stuvanti mām yathā devam mahā indram priya vādinaḥ yat aham kīṭa tām prāpya saṃprāptaḥ rāja putra tām namaḥ te astu mahā prājña kim karomi praśādhi mām uvāca adya te kīṭa tām prāpya smṛtiḥ jātā a jugupsitā śūdreṇa artha pradhānena nṛśaṃseṇa ātatāyinā mama te darśanam prāptam tat ca eva su kṛtam purā itas tvam rāja putra tvāt brāhmaṇyam samavāpsyasi go brāhmaṇa kṛte prāṇān hutvā ātmīyān raṇa ajire rāja putra sukham prāpya ṛtūn ca eva āpta dakṣiṇān tiryagyonyāḥ śūdra tām abhyupaiti śūdraḥ vaiśya tvam kṣatriya tvam ca vaiśyaḥ vṛtta ślāghī kṣatriyaḥ brāhmaṇa tvam svargam puṇyam brāhmaṇaḥ sādhu vṛttaḥ uvāca tyaktvā sa kīṭa tām rājñ cacāra vipulam tapaḥ tasya dharma artha vidvasaḥ dṛṣṭvā tat vipulam tapaḥ ājagāma dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ tadā uvāca kṣātram ca eva vratam kīṭa bhūtānām paripālanam kṣātram ca eva vratam dhyāyan tatas vipra tvam eṣyasi pāhi sarvāḥ prajāḥ samyak śubha aśubha vid ātmavān śubhaiḥ saṃvibhajan kāmaiḥ aśubhānām ca pāvanaiḥ kṣātrīm tanum samutsṛjya tatas vipra tvam eṣyasi uvāca mahā ṛṣeḥ vacanam śrutvā prajāḥ dharmeṇa pālya ca acireṇa eva kālena kīṭaḥ pārthiva sattama tatas tam brāhmaṇam dṛṣṭvā punar eva mahat yaśāḥ ājagāma mahā prājñaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ tadā uvāca bho bho vipra ṛṣabha śrīmat mā vyathiṣṭhāḥ katham cana pālanāt ca viśiṣṭānām su yuddha maraṇena ca śiṣṭa saṃsevanāt ca eva sa gatim paramām gataḥ tatas sa para rāṣṭreṇa rājānam pīḍitāḥ prajāḥ ājagāma tatas prājñaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ tadā pārāśaryam mahā prājñam upayāntam dayā param ajñāna timira ādityam nityam vyāsam namāmi aham iti uktvā patitam padbhyām prītyā prāha mahā muniḥ brāhmaṇān pūjayasva iha japa satya parāyaṇaḥ śubha kṛt śubha yonīṣu pāpa kṛt pāpa yoniṣu tasmāt mṛtyu bhayāt kīṭa mā vyathiṣṭhāḥ katham cana uvāca dharma mūlām śriyam prāpya pāpmā naṣṭaḥ iha adya me uvāca bhagavat vacanāt kīṭaḥ brāhmaṇyam prāpya durlabham akarot pṛthivīm rājan yajña yūpa śata aṅkitām avāpa ca param kīṭaḥ pārtha brahma sanātanam te api yasmāt svabhāvena hatāḥ kṣatriya puṃgavāḥ saṃprāptāḥ te gatim puṇyām tasmāt mā śoca putraka uvāca vidyā tapaḥ ca dānam ca kim eteṣām viśiṣyate pṛcchāmi tvā satām śreṣṭha tat me brūhi pitāmaha uvāca atra api udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam maitreyasya ca saṃvādam kṛṣṇadvaipāyanasya ca kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ rājan ajñāta caritam caran vārāṇasyām upātiṣṭhat maitreyam svairiṇī kule tam upasthitam āsīnam jñātvā sa muni sattamam pratiṣṭhamānaḥ asmayata prītaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ mahā manāḥ tam utsmayantam saṃprekṣya maitreyaḥ kṛṣṇam abravīt kāraṇam brūhi dharma ātman yaḥ asmayiṣṭhāḥ kutas ca te ātmanaḥ ca tapaḥ bhāgyam mahā bhāgyam tathā eva ca pṛthak ācarataḥ tāta pṛthak ātmani ca ātmanoḥ alpa antaram aham manye viśiṣṭam api vā tvayā uvāca aticcheda ativādābhyām smayaḥ ayam samupāgataḥ trīṇi eva tu padāni āhuḥ puruṣasya uttamam vratam idānīm ca eva naḥ kṛtyam purastāt ca param smṛ alpaḥ api tādṛśaḥ dāyaḥ bhavati uta mahā phalaḥ tṛṣitāya ca yat dattam hṛdayena anasūyatā tṛṣitaḥ tṛṣitāya tvam dattvā etat aśanam mama ajaiṣīḥ mahataḥ lokān mahā yajñaiḥ iva abhibho adhikam mārjanāt tāta tathā eva api anulepanāt yāni imā uttamāni iha veda uktāni praśaṃsasi teṣām śreṣṭhatamam dānam iti me na asti saṃśayaḥ dāna kṛdbhiḥ kṛ panthāḥ yena yānti manīṣiṇaḥ te hi prāṇasya dātāraḥ teṣu dharmaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ yathā vedāḥ su adhītāḥ ca yathā ca indriya saṃyamaḥ śrīmantam āpnuvanti arthāḥ dānam yajñaḥ tathā sukham sukhāt eva param duḥkham duḥkhāt anyat param sukham dṛśyate hi mahā prājña niyatam vai svabhāvāt trividhāni iha vṛttāni narasya ahuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ yajña dāna tapaḥ śīlāḥ narāḥ vai puṇya karmiṇaḥ ye abhidruhyanti bhūtāni te vai pāpa kṛtaḥ janāḥ nityam ca akṛpaṇaḥ bhuṅkte sva janaiḥ dehi yācitaḥ bhāgya kṣayeṇa kṣīyante na upabhogena saṃcayāḥ uvāca atyantam śrīmati kule jātaḥ prājñaḥ bahu śrutaḥ asaṃśayam mahā prājña yathā eva āttha tathā eva tat anujñātaḥ tu bhavatā kim cit brūyām aham vibho uvāca brūhi tāvat mahā prājña śuśrūṣe vacanam tava vidyā tapobhyām hi bhavān bhāvitātmā na saṃśayaḥ bhavataḥ bhāvitātma tvāt dāyaḥ ayam su mahān mama bhūyas buddhyā anupaśyāmi su samṛddha tapāḥ iva tapaḥ śrutam ca yoniḥ ca api etat brāhmaṇya kāraṇam na hi śrutavatām kim cit adhikam brāhmaṇāt ṛte andham syāt tamaḥ eva idam na prajñāyeta kim cana cāturvarṇyam na varteta dharma adharmau ṛta anṛte a saṃskārāt kṣatra vaiśyau naśyete brāhmaṇāt ṛte śūdraḥ naśyati a śuśrūṣuḥ āśramāṇām yathārhāt yathā hi su kṛte kṣetre phalam vindati mānavaḥ evam dattvā śrutavati phalam dātā samaśnute brāhmaṇaḥ ced na vidyeta śruta vṛtta upasaṃhitaḥ pratigrahītā dānasya mogham syāt dhaninām dhanam sa ca annāt jāyate tasmāt sūkṣmaḥ eva vyatikramaḥ yaḥ tārayati vai vidvān pitṝn devān samādṛtān yat eva dadataḥ puṇyam tat eva pratigṛhṇataḥ yatra vai brāhmaṇāḥ santi śruta vṛtta upasaṃhitāḥ tatra dāna phalam puṇyam iha ca amutra ca aśnute ye yoni śuddhāḥ satatam tapasi abhiratāḥ bhṛśam dāna adhyayana saṃpannāḥ te vai pūjyatamāḥ sadā te hi svargasya netāraḥ yajña vāhāḥ sanātanāḥ uvāca diṣṭyā evam tvam vijānāsi diṣṭyā te buddhiḥ īdṛśī lokaḥ hi ayam guṇān eva bhūyiṣṭham sma praśaṃsati rūpa māna vayaḥ māna śrī mānāḥ ca api asaṃśayam diṣṭyā na abhibhavanti tvām daivaḥ te ayam anugrahaḥ yat te bhṛśataram dānāt vartayiṣyāmi tat śṛṇu yāni iha āgama śāstrāṇi yāḥ ca kāḥ cit pravṛttayaḥ aham dānam praśaṃsāmi bhavān api tapaḥ śrute tat tat bahuguṇam dānam śraddhayā sva guṇaiḥ api duranvayam duṣpradhṛṣyam durāpam duratikramam surāpaḥ a saṃmata ādāyī bhrūṇa hā guru talpa gaḥ sarva vidyaḥ tu cakṣuṣmān api yādṛśa tādṛśaḥ tapasvinau ca tau āhuḥ tābhyām kāryam sadā namaḥ dāna pradāḥ sukham pretya prāpnuvanti iha ca śriyam pūjitāḥ pūjayanti etān mānitāḥ mānayanti ca prāpsyase tu anna pānāni yāni dāsyasi kāni cit medhāvī asi kule jātaḥ śrutavān a nṛśaṃsavān etat gṛhāṇa prathamam praśastam gṛhamedhinām yaḥ bhartā vāśitā tuṣṭaḥ bhartuḥ tuṣṭā ca vāśitā brāhmaṇaḥ sa mahābhāga taret saṃsāra sāgarāt vidyayā gam moha tāraṇāya hariḥ smṛ tad bhaktāḥ na vinaśyanti hi aṣṭa akṣara parāyaṇāḥ praṇava upāsana parāḥ parama artha parāḥ tu iha etaiḥ pāvaya ca ātmānam tam praṇamya atha maitreyaḥ kṛtvā ca abhipradakṣiṇam bhīṣmaḥ svasti prāpnotu bhagavān iti uvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ uvāca sat strīṇām samudācāram sarva dharma bhṛtām vara uvāca sarvajñām sarva dharma jñām deva loke manasvinīm kaikeyī sumanā nāma śāṇḍilīm paryapṛcchata kena vṛttena kalyāṇi samācāreṇa kena vā vidhūya sarva pāpāni deva lokam tvam āgatā hutāśana śikhā iva tvam jvalamānā sva tejasā sutā tārādhipasya iva prabhayā divam āgatā arajāṃsi ca vastrāṇi dhārayantī gata klamā vimāna sthā śubhe bhāsi sahasraguṇam ojasā iti pṛṣṭā sumanayā madhuram cāru hāsinī śāṇḍilī nibhṛtam vākyam sumanām idam abravīt na aham kāṣāya vasanā na api valkala dhāriṇī na ca muṇḍā na jaṭilā bhūtvā deva tvam āgatā ahitāni ca vākyāni sarvāṇi paruṣāṇi ca devatānām pitṝṇām ca brāhmaṇānām ca pūjana apramattā sadā yuktā śvaśrū śvaśura vartinī advāre na ca tiṣṭhāmi ciram na kathayāmi ca asat vā hasitam kim cit ahitam vā api karmaṇā kārya arthe nirgatam ca api bhartāram gṛham āgatam āsanena upasaṃyojya pūjayāmi samāhitā kuṭumba arthe samānītam yat kim cit kāryam eva tu agni saṃrakṣaṇa parā gṛha śuddhim ca kāraye pātrāṇām dhana dhānyānām śayana āsana vastunām kumārān pālaye nityam kumārīḥ pariśikṣaye ātma priyāṇi hitvā api garbha saṃrakṣaṇe ratā bālānām varjaye nityam śāpam kopam pratāpanam a vikṣiptāni dhānyāni na anna vikṣepaṇam gṛhe samudgamya ca śuddhā aham bhikṣām dadyām dvijātiṣu pravāsam yadi me bhartā yāti kāryeṇa kena cit añjanam rocanām ca eva snānam mālya anulepanam ātureṣu api kāryeṣu tena tuṣyati me manaḥ na āyāsayāmi bhartāram kuṭumba arthe ca sarvadā gupta guhyā sadā ca asmi su saṃmṛṣṭa niveśanā imam dharma patham nārī pālayantī samāhitā arundhatī iva nārīṇām svarga loke mahīyate uvāca etat ākhyāya sā devī sumanāyai tapasvinī pati dharmam mahābhāgā jagāma adarśanam tadā yaḥ ca idam pāṇḍava ākhyānam paṭhet parvaṇi parvaṇi yudhiṣṭhiraḥ yat jñeyam paramam kṛtyam anuṣṭheyam mahātmabhiḥ bhīṣmaḥ sāram me sarva śāstrāṇām vaktum arhasi anugrahāt śrūyatām idam atyantam gūḍham saṃsāra mocanam śrotavyam ca tvayā samyak jñātavyam ca viśām pate puṇḍarīkaḥ purā vipraḥ puṇya tīrthe japa anvitaḥ nāradaḥ ca abravīt enam brahmanā uktam mahātmanā śṛṇuṣva avahitaḥ tāta jñāna yogam anuttamam aprabhūtam prabhūta artham veda śāstra artha sārakam yaḥ paraḥ prakṛtyāḥ proktaḥ puruṣaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ narāt jātāni tattvāni nārāṇi iti tatas viduḥ tāni eva ca ayanam tasya tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ nārāyaṇāt jagat sarvam sarga kāle prajāyate nārāyaṇaḥ param brahma tattvam nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ parāt api paraḥ ca asau tasmāt na asti parāt param vāsudevam tathā viṣṇum ātmānam ca tathā viduḥ saṃjñā bhedaiḥ saḥ eva ekaḥ sarva śāstra abhisaṃskṛtaḥ āloḍya sarva śāstrāṇi vicārya ca punar punar idam ekam su niṣpannam dhyeyaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ sadā tasmāt tvam gahanān sarvān tyaktvā śāstra artha vistarān an anya cetāḥ dhyāyasva nārāyaṇam ajam vibhum muhūrtam api yaḥ dhyāyet nārāyaṇam atandritaḥ namaḥ nārāyaṇāya iti yaḥ veda brahma śāśvatam śravaṇāt mananāt ca eva gīti stuti arcana ādibhiḥ ārādhyam sarvadā brahma puruṣeṇa hita eṣiṇā lipyate na sa pāpena nārāyaṇa parāyaṇaḥ punāti sakalam lokam sahasrāṃśuḥ iva uditaḥ keśava ārādhanam hitvā na eva yāti parām gatim svapne api puṇḍarīkākṣam śaṅkha cakra gadā dharam tam dṛṣṭvā devadeveśam prāṇamat sambhrama anvitaḥ atha kālena mahatā tathā pratyakṣatām gataḥ gataḥ saṃpūjitaḥ sarvaiḥ sa yogi nilayaḥ hariḥ sa guṇam aguṇam ādyam sthūlam atyanta sūkṣmam uvāca sāmnā vā api pradāne vā jyāyaḥ kim bhavataḥ matam uvāca sāmnā prasādyate kaḥ cit dānena ca tathā aparaḥ puruṣaḥ prakṛtim jñātvā tayoḥ ekataram bhajet guṇān tu śṛṇu me rājan sāntvasya bharata ṛṣabha dāruṇāni api bhūtāni sāntvena ārādhayet yathā atra api udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam gṛhītvā rakṣasā muktaḥ dvijātiḥ kānane yathā gṛhītaḥ kṛcchram āpannaḥ rakṣasā bhakṣayiṣyatā sa buddhi śruta saṃpannaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā atīva bhīṣaṇam rakṣaḥ tu vācā saṃpūjya praśnam papraccha tam dvijam mokṣyase brūhi me praśnam kena asmi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ ābhiḥ gāthābhiḥ avyagraḥ praśnam pratijagāda ha viṣayān atulān bhuṅkṣe tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ nūnam mitrāṇi te rakṣaḥ sādhu upacaritāni api sva doṣāt aparajyante tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ dhana aiśvarya adhikāḥ stabdhāḥ tvad guṇaiḥ parama avarāḥ avajānanti nūnam tvām tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ guṇavān viguṇān anyān nūnam paśyasi satkṛ prājñaḥ aprājñān vinīta ātmā tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ avṛttyā kliśyamānaḥ api vṛtti upāyān vigarhayan māhātmyāt vyathase nūnam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ saṃpīḍya ātmānam ārya tvāt tvayā kaḥ cit upaskṛtaḥ jitam tvām manyate sādho tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ kliśyamānān vimārgeṣu kāma krodha āvṛta ātmanaḥ manye nu dhyāyasi janān tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ prājñaiḥ saṃbhāvitaḥ nūnam na prājñaiḥ upasaṃhitaḥ hrīmān amarṣī durvṛttaiḥ tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ nūnam mitra mukhaḥ śatruḥ kaḥ cit ārya vat ācaran vañcayitvā gataḥ tvām vai tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ prakāśa artha gatiḥ nūnam rahasya kuśalaḥ kṛtī tad jñaiḥ na pūjyase nūnam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ nūnam śaktyā samārambhān vihitān su mahā udayān vipanna arthān vijānāsi tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ eka dravya niviṣṭena tulya artha śruta saṃpadā paribhūtaḥ asi nūnam tvam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ guṇāḥ te na virājante tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ mahat prārthayase nūnam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ tapaḥ praṇihita ātmānam manye tvā araṇya kāṅkṣiṇam bandhu vargaḥ na gṛhṇāti tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ iṣṭa bhāryasya te nūnam prātiveśyaḥ mahādhanaḥ yuvā su lalitaḥ kāmī tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ su durvinītaḥ putraḥ vā jāmātā vā pramārjakaḥ dārāḥ vā pratikūlāḥ te tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ bhrātaraḥ atīva viṣamāḥ pitā vā kṣudh kṣataḥ mṛtaḥ mātā jyeṣṭhaḥ guruḥ vā api tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ vā hataḥ gauḥ vā brahma svam vā hṛtam purā deva svam vā adhikam kāle tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ hṛta dāraḥ atha vṛddhaḥ vā loke dviṣṭaḥ atha vā naraiḥ a vijñātena vā vṛddhaḥ tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ vārddhakya artham dhanam dṛṣṭvā svā śrīḥ vā api paraiḥ hṛtā vṛttiḥ vā durjana apekṣā tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ saṃpad kāle na te dharmaḥ kṣīṇaḥ tāta suhṛd bruvaiḥ asaṃnyāsam atas tatra tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ na bhāti kāle abhihitam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ dṛḍha pūrva śrutam mūrkham kupitam hṛdaya priyam anunetum na śaknoṣi tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ nūnam āsaṃjayitvā te kṛtye kasmin cit īpsite kaḥ cit arthayate atyartham tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ parokṣa vādibhiḥ mithyā doṣaḥ te saṃpradarśitaḥ nūnam tvā sva guṇa apekṣam pūjayānam suhṛd dhruvam mayā arthaḥ iti jānāti tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ vivaktum prāpti śaithilyāt tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ nānā buddhi rucīn loke manuṣyān nūnam icchasi grahītum sva guṇaiḥ sarvān tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ alam arthayase hīnān tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ yaśaḥ prārthayase nūnam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ kṛtam anyaiḥ apahṛtam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ nūnam ātma kṛtam doṣam a paśyan kim cit ātmani akāraṇe abhiśastaḥ asi tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ suhṛdām apramattānām a pramokṣya artha hāni jam duḥkham artha guṇaiḥ hīnam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ sādhūn gṛhasthān dṛṣṭvā ca tathā asādhūn vanecarān muktān ca āvasathe saktān tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ na pratiṣṭhati te nūnam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ dattān akuśalaiḥ arthān manīṣī saṃjijīviṣuḥ prāpya vartayase nūnam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ pāpān vivardhataḥ dṛṣṭvā kalyāṇān ca avasīdataḥ dhruvam mṛgayase yogyam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ paraspara viruddhānām priyam nūnam cikīrṣasi suhṛdām avirodhena tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ śrotriyān ca vikarma sthān prājñān ca api ajita indriyān manye anudhyāyasi janan tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ evam saṃpūjitam rakṣaḥ vipram tam pratyapūjayat yudhiṣṭhiraḥ dānānām uttamam yat ca deyam yat ca yathā yathā vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ mānyān pūjyān ca gāṅgeya rahasyam vaktum arhasi evam pṛṣṭaḥ narendreṇa pāṇḍavena yaśasvinā bhīṣmaḥ dharmāṇām paramam guhyam bhīṣmaḥ provāca pārthivam śṛṇuṣva avahitaḥ rājan dharma guhyāni bhārata yathā hi bhagavān vyāsaḥ purā kathitavān mayi deva guhyam idam rājan yamena akliṣṭa karmaṇā ṛṣayaḥ pramathāḥ śrīḥ ca citraguptaḥ diśām gajāḥ ṛṣi dharmaḥ smṛtaḥ yatra sa rahasyaḥ mahā phalaḥ yaḥ ca etat evam jānīyāt jñātvā vā kurute anagha sa doṣaḥ doṣavān ca iha taiḥ guṇaiḥ saha yujyate daśa sūnā samam cakram daśa cakra samaḥ dhvajaḥ daśa dhvaja samā veśyā daśa veśyā samaḥ nṛpaḥ trivarga sahitam śāstram pavitram puṇya lakṣaṇam dharma vyākaraṇam puṇyam rahasya śravaṇam mahat pitṝṇām yatra guhyāni procyante śrāddha karmaṇi devatānām ca sarveṣām rahasyam kathyate akhilam ṛṣi dharmaḥ smṛtaḥ yatra sa rahasyaḥ mahā phalaḥ ye paṭhanti sadā martyāḥ yeṣām ca eva upatiṣṭhati śrutvā ca phalam ācaṣṭe svayam nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ gavām phalam tīrtha phalam yajñānām ca eva yat phalam śrotāraḥ śraddadhānāḥ ca yeṣām śuddham ca mānasam teṣām vyaktam jitāḥ lokāḥ śraddadhānena sādhunā yau tau kāma guṇa upetau aśvinau bhiṣajām varau ājñayā aham tayoḥ prāptaḥ sa narān pitṛ devatān kimartham ca trayaḥ piṇḍāḥ pravibhaktāḥ pṛthak pṛthak śraddadhānena dūtena bhāṣitam dharma saṃhitam pūrva sthāḥ tridaśāḥ sarve pitaraḥ pūjya khecaram svāgatam te astu bhadram te śrūyatām khecara uttama gūḍha arthaḥ paramaḥ praśnaḥ bhavatā samudīritaḥ śrāddham dattvā ca bhuktvā ca puruṣaḥ yaḥ striyam vrajet pravibhāgam tu piṇḍānām pravakṣyāmi anupūrvaśas piṇḍaḥ hi adhastāt gacchan tu apaḥ āviśya bhāvayet piṇḍam tu madhyamam tatra patnī tu ekā samaśnute piṇḍaḥ tṛtīyaḥ yaḥ teṣām tam dadyāt jātavedasi pitaraḥ tasya tuṣyanti prahṛṣṭa manasaḥ sadā dūtaḥ prajāḥ vivardhate ca asya akṣayam ca upatiṣṭhati ānupūrvyeṇa piṇḍānām pravibhāgaḥ pṛthak pṛthak pitṝṇām triṣu sarveṣām niruktam kathitam tvayā kam vā prīṇayate devam katham tārayate pitṝn etat icchāmi aham śrotum piṇḍeṣu triṣu yā gatiḥ phalam vṛttim ca mārgam ca yaḥ ca enam pratipadyate su mahān eṣa praśnaḥ vai yaḥ tvayā samudīritaḥ rahasyam adbhutam ca api pṛṣṭāḥ sma gaganecara te api evam na abhijānanti pitṛ kārya viniścayam trayāṇām api piṇḍānām śrutvā bhagavataḥ gatim deva dūtena yaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ śrāddhasya vidhi niścayaḥ gatiḥ trayāṇām piṇḍānām śṛṇuṣva avahitaḥ mama apaḥ gacchati yaḥ hi atra śaśinam hi eṣa prīṇayet śaśī prīṇayate devān pitṝn ca eva mahāmate bhuṅkte tu patnī yam ca eṣām anujñātā tu madhyamam pitaraḥ tena tṛpyanti prītāḥ kāmān diśanti ca etat te kathitam sarvam triṣu piṇḍeṣu yā gatiḥ śucinā tu sadā śrāddham bhoktavyam khecara uttama ye mayā kathitāḥ doṣāḥ te tathā syuḥ na ca anyathā tasmāt snātaḥ śuciḥ kṣāntaḥ śrāddham bhuñjīta vai dvijaḥ tatas vidyutprabhaḥ nāma ṛṣiḥ āha mahā tapāḥ āditya tejasā tasya tulyam rūpam prakāśate kīṭān pipīlikān sarpān meṣān sa mṛga pakṣiṇaḥ kilbiṣam su bahu prāptāḥ kim svid eṣām pratikriyā tatas deva gaṇāḥ sarve ṛṣayaḥ ca tapodhanāḥ śakraḥ pitaraḥ ca mahābhāgāḥ pūjayanti sma tam munim kurukṣetram gayām gaṅgām prabhāsam puṣkarāṇi ca tathā mucyati pāpena rāhuṇā candramāḥ yathā spṛśate yaḥ gavām pṛṣṭham vāladhim ca namasyati ghṛṣṭaḥ vaṭa kaṣāyeṇa anuliptaḥ priyaṅguṇā kṣīreṇa ṣaṣṭikān bhuktvā sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate śrūyatām ca aparam guhyam rahasyam ṛṣi cintitam śrutam me bhāṣamāṇasya sthāṇoḥ sthāne bṛhaspateḥ parvata ārohaṇam kṛtvā ekapādaḥ vibhāvasum nirīkṣeta nirāhāraḥ ūrdhva bāhuḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ grīṣma kāle atha vā śīte evam pāpam apohati tatas pāpāt pramuktasya dyutiḥ bhavati śāśvatā dharma guhyam tu bhagavat mānuṣāṇām sukha āvaham bṛhaspatiḥ sa rahasyāḥ ca ye doṣāḥ tān yathāvat udīraya bāla vatsām ca ye dhenum duhanti kṣīra kāraṇāt teṣām doṣān pravakṣyāmi tān nibodha śacīpate bhānumant anilaḥ ca eva havyavāhaḥ ca vāsava lokānām mātaraḥ ca eva gāvaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ svayambhunā lokān tārayitum śaktāḥ martyeṣu eteṣu devatāḥ varṣāṇi ṣaḍaśītim tu durvṛttāḥ kula pāṃsanāḥ striyaḥ sarvāḥ ca durvṛttāḥ pratimehanti yāḥ ravim agni kāryeṣu vai teṣām havyam na aśnāti pāvakaḥ kṣīram tu bāla vatsānām ye pibanti iha mānavāḥ na teṣām kṣīrapāḥ ke cit jāyante kula vardhanāḥ prajā kṣayeṇa yujyante kula vaṃśa kṣayeṇa ca evam etat purā dṛṣṭam kula vṛddhaiḥ dvijātibhiḥ tasmāt varjyāni varjyāni kāryam kāryam ca nityaśas tatas sarve mahābhāgāḥ devatāḥ sa marut gaṇāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca mahābhāgāḥ pṛcchanti sma pitṝn tatas ānṛṇyam vā katham martyāḥ gaccheyuḥ kena karmaṇā etat icchāmahe śrotum param kautūhalam hi naḥ nyāyataḥ vai mahābhāgāḥ saṃśayaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ śrūyatām yena tuṣyāmaḥ martyānām sādhu karmaṇām nīla ṣaṇḍa pramokṣeṇa amāvāsyām tila udakaiḥ varṣāsu dīpakaiḥ ca eva pitṝṇām anṛṇaḥ bhavet akṣayam nirvyalīkam ca dānam etat mahā phalam mama paritoṣaḥ ca akṣayaḥ parikīrtyate śraddadhānāḥ ca ye martyāḥ āhariṣyanti saṃtatim durgāt te tārayiṣyanti narakāt prapitāmahān pitṝṇām bhāṣitam śrutvā hṛṣṭa romā tapodhanaḥ vṛddhagārgyaḥ mahā tejāḥ tān evam vākyam abravīt ke guṇāḥ nīla ṣaṇḍasya pramuktasya tapodhanāḥ nīlaṣaṇḍasya lāṅgūlam toyam abhyuddharet yadi ṣaṣṭim varṣa sahasrāṇi pitaraḥ tena tarpitāḥ yaḥ tu śṛṅga gatam paṅkam kūlāt uddhṛtya tiṣṭhati varṣāsu dīpa dānena śaśi vat śobhate naraḥ kṛtam bhavati taiḥ śrāddham sa rahasyam yathārthavat hṛṣṭa puṣṭa manāḥ teṣām prajā bhavati nityadā śraddadhānaḥ tu yaḥ kuryāt pitṝṇām anṛṇaḥ bhavet evam eṣa samuddiṣṭaḥ śrāddha kāla kramaḥ tathā bhīṣmaḥ iti pṛṣṭaḥ surendreṇa provāca hariḥ avyayaḥ brāhmaṇānām parīvādaḥ mama vidveṣaṇam mahat brāhmaṇaiḥ pūjitaiḥ nityam pūjitaḥ aham na saṃśayaḥ nitya abhivādyāḥ vipra indrāḥ bhuktvā pādau tathā ātmanaḥ teṣām tuṣyāmi martyānām yaḥ cakre ca balim haret vāmanam brāhmaṇam dṛṣṭvā varāham ca jala utthitam uddhṛtām dharaṇīm ca eva mūrdhnā dhārayate tu yaḥ na teṣām aśubham kim cit kalmaṣam ca upapadyate aśvattham rocanām gām ca pūjayet yaḥ naraḥ sadā tena rūpeṇa teṣām ca pūjām gṛhṇāmi tattvataḥ pūjā mama eṣā na asti anyā yāvat lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ anyathā hi vṛthak martyāḥ pūjayanti alpabuddhayaḥ na aham tat pratigṛhṇāmi na sā tuṣṭi karī mama cakram pādau varāham ca brāhmaṇam ca api vāmanam uddhṛtām dharaṇīm ca eva kimartham tvam praśaṃsasi bhavān sṛjati bhūtāni bhavān saṃharati prajāḥ bhīṣmaḥ prakṛtiḥ sarva bhūtānām sa martyānām sanātanī cakreṇa nihatāḥ daityāḥ padbhyām krāntā vasuṃdharā vārāham rūpam āsthāya uddhṛtā ca vasuṃdharā vāmanam rūpam āsthāya jitaḥ rājā mayā baliḥ parituṣṭaḥ bhavāmi evam mānuṣāṇām mahātmanām tat mām ye pūjayiṣyanti na asti teṣām parābhavaḥ api vā brāhmaṇam dṛṣṭvā brahmacāriṇam āgatam brāhmaṇāya āhutim dattvā amṛtam tasya bhojanam aindrīm saṃdhyām upāsitvā āditya abhimukhaḥ sthitaḥ saṃśayam pṛcchamānānām kim bhūyas kathayāmi aham śrūyatām paramam guhyam mānuṣāṇām sukha āvaham a jānantaḥ yat abudhāḥ kliśyante bhūta pīḍitāḥ kalye utthāya yaḥ martyaḥ spṛśet gām vai ghṛtam dadhi bhūtāni ca eva sarvāṇi agratas pṛṣṭhatas api vā ucchiṣṭam vā api chidreṣu varjayanti tapodhanāḥ devāḥ pragṛhya audumbaram pātram toya pūrṇam udak mukhaḥ upavāsam tu gṛhṇīyāt yat vā saṃkalpayet vratam upavāse balau ca api tāmra pātram viśiṣyate baliḥ bhikṣā tathā arghyam ca pitṝṇām ca tila udakam guhyam etat samuddiṣṭam yathā tuṣyanti devatāḥ rāja pauruṣike vipre ghāṇṭike paricārake gorakṣake vāṇijake tathā kāru kuśīlave mitra druhi an adhīyāne yaḥ ca syāt vṛṣalī patiḥ eteṣu daivam pitryam vā na deyam syāt katham cana piṇḍadāḥ tasya hīyante na ca prīṇāti vai pitṝn agniḥ pādam udyamya yaḥ martyaḥ spṛśet gāḥ ca su durmatiḥ brāhmaṇam vā mahābhāgam dīpyamānam tathā analam tasya doṣān pravakṣyāmi tat śṛṇudhvam samāhitāḥ vaimanasyam ca devānām kṛtam bhavati puṣkalam pāvakaḥ ca mahā tejāḥ havyam na pratigṛhṇati ājanmanām śatam ca eva narake pacyate tu saḥ tasmāt gāvaḥ na pādena spraṣṭavyāḥ vai kadā cana brāhmaṇaḥ ca mahā tejāḥ dīpyamānaḥ tathā analaḥ viśvāmitraḥ ete doṣāḥ mayā proktāḥ triṣu yaḥ pādam utsṛjet śrūyatām paramam guhyam rahasyam dharma saṃhitam paramānnena yaḥ dadyāt pitṝṇām aupahārikam gajacchāyāyām pūrvasyām kutupe dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ śrūyatām tasya dānasya yādṛśaḥ guṇa vistaraḥ kṛtam tena mahat śrāddham varṣāṇi iha trayodaśa gāvaḥ bhūyas ca yā viṣṇu pade sthitā yā vibhāvasoḥ ca api pathe sthitā yā etam hi mantram tridaśa abhijuṣṭam na tasya pāpam na bhayam na śokaḥ bhīṣmaḥ atha sapta mahābhāgāḥ ṛṣayaḥ loka viśrutāḥ vasiṣṭha pramukhāḥ sarve brahmāṇam padmasaṃbhavam pradakṣiṇam abhikramya sarve prāñjalayaḥ sthitāḥ uvāca vacanam teṣām vasiṣṭhaḥ brahma vittamaḥ sarva prāṇi hitam praśnam brahmakṣetre viśeṣataḥ dravya hīnāḥ katham martyāḥ daridrāḥ sādhu vṛttayaḥ aho praśnaḥ mahābhāgāḥ gūḍha arthaḥ paramaḥ śubhaḥ sūkṣmaḥ śreyān ca martyānām bhavadbhiḥ samudāhṛtaḥ śrūyatām sarvam ākhyāsye nikhilena tapodhanāḥ yathā yajña phalam martyaḥ labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ pauṣa māsasya śukle vai yadā yujyeta rohiṇī eka vastraḥ śuciḥ snātaḥ śraddadhānaḥ samāhitaḥ somasya raśmayaḥ pītvā mahāyajña phalam labhet vibhāvasuḥ yat mām bhavantaḥ pṛcchanti sūkṣma tattva artha darśinaḥ salilasya añjalim pūrṇam akṣatāḥ ca ghṛta uttarāḥ somasya uttiṣṭhamānasya tat jalam ca akṣatān ca tān agni kāryam kṛtam tena hutāḥ ca asya agnayaḥ trayaḥ vanaspatim ca yaḥ hanyāt amāvāsyām abuddhimān dantakāṣṭham tu yaḥ khādet amāvāsyām abuddhimān śrīḥ prakīrṇam bhājanam yatra pāna bhāṇḍam atha āsanam devatāḥ pitaraḥ ca eva utsave parvaṇīṣu vā nirāśāḥ pratigacchanti kaśmala upahatāt gṛhāt aṅgirāḥ yaḥ tu saṃvatsaram pūrṇam dadyāt dīpam karañjake gārgyaḥ ātithyam satatam kuryāt dīpam dadyāt pratiśraye varjayānaḥ divāsvapnam na ca māṃsāni bhakṣayet go brāhmaṇam na hiṃsyāt ca puṣkarāṇi ca kīrtayet eṣa śreṣṭhatamaḥ dharmaḥ sa rahasyaḥ mahā phalaḥ api kratu śataiḥ iṣṭvā kṣayam gacchati tat haviḥ na tu kṣīyanti te dharmāḥ śraddadhānaiḥ prayojitāḥ rajasvalā ca yā nārī śvitrikā putrikā ca yā etābhiḥ cakṣuṣā dṛṣṭam haviḥ na aśnanti devatāḥ pitaraḥ ca na tuṣyanti varṣāṇi asya trayodaśa śukla vāsāḥ śuciḥ bhūtvā brāhmaṇān svasti vācayet kīrtayet bhāratam ca eva tathā syāt akṣayam haviḥ bhinna bhāṇḍam ca khaṭvām ca kukkuṭam śunakam tathā apraśastāni sarvāṇi yaḥ ca vṛkṣaḥ gṛheruhaḥ bhinna bhāṇḍe kalim prāhuḥ khaṭvāyām tu dhana kṣayaḥ kukkuṭe śunake ca eva haviḥ na aśnanti devatāḥ vṛkṣa mūle dhruvam sattvam tasmāt vṛkṣam na ropayet avākśirāḥ vā lambeta satram vā sphītam āharet na ca asya hṛdayam śuddham narakam sa dhruvam vrajet tulyam yajñaḥ ca satyam ca hṛdayasya ca śuddha tā vāyuḥ kim cit dharmam pravakṣyāmi mānuṣāṇām sukha āvaham sa rahasyāḥ ca ye doṣāḥ tān śṛṇudhvam samāhitāḥ dīpakaḥ ca api kartavyaḥ pitṝṇām sa tila udakaḥ etena vidhinā martyaḥ śraddadhānaḥ samāhitaḥ caturaḥ vārṣikān māsān yaḥ dadāti tila udakam bhojanam ca yathāśaktyā brāhmaṇe vedapārage agneḥ tu vṛṣalaḥ netā haviḥ mūḍhāḥ ca yoṣitaḥ gavām mūtra purīṣeṇa payasā ca ghṛtena ca agni kāryam tri aham kuryāt nirāhāraḥ samāhitaḥ tatas saṃvatsare pūrṇe pratigṛhṇanti devatāḥ hṛṣyanti pitaraḥ ca asya śrāddha kāle upasthite lomaśaḥ martyānām svarga kāmānām pretya svarga sukha āvahaḥ paradāreṣu ye saktāḥ a kṛtvā dāra saṃgraham nirāśāḥ pitaraḥ teṣām śrāddha kāle bhavanti vai a saṃbhāṣyāḥ bhavanti ete pitṝṇām na atra saṃśayaḥ devatāḥ pitaraḥ ca eṣām na abhinandanti tat haviḥ tasmāt parasya vai dārān tyajet vandhyām ca yoṣitam śrūyatām ca aparam guhyam rahasyam dharma saṃhitam śraddadhānena kartavyam gurūṇām vacanam sadā dvādaśyām paurṇamāsyām ca māsi māsi ghṛta akṣatam aśvamedha catur bhāgam phalam sṛjati vāsavaḥ dānena etena tejasvī vīryavān ca bhavet naraḥ prītaḥ ca bhagavān somaḥ iṣṭān kāmān prayacchati śrūyatām ca aparaḥ dharmaḥ sa rahasyaḥ mahā phalaḥ imam kali yugam prāpya manuṣyāṇām sukha āvahaḥ kalyam utthāya yaḥ martyaḥ snātaḥ śuklena vāsasā tila pātram prayaccheta brāhmaṇebhyaḥ samāhitaḥ tila udakam ca yaḥ dadyāt pitṝṇām madhunā saha dīpakam kṛsaram ca eva śrūyatām tasya tat phalam tila pātre phalam prāha bhagavān pākaśāsanaḥ go pradānam ca yaḥ kuryāt bhūmi dānam ca śāśvatam agniṣṭomam ca yaḥ yajñam yajeta bahu dakṣiṇam dīpe ca kṛsare ca eva tuṣyante asya pitāmahāḥ evam etat mayā uddiṣṭam ṛṣi dṛṣṭam purātanam bhīṣmaḥ tatas tu ṛṣi gaṇāḥ sarve pitaraḥ ca sa devatāḥ arundhatīm tapaḥ vṛddhām apṛcchanta samāhitāḥ samāna śīlām vīryeṇa vasiṣṭhasya mahātmanaḥ tapaḥ vṛddhiḥ mayā prāptā bhavatām smaraṇena vai bhavatām ca prasādena dharmān vakṣyāmi śāśvatān sa guhyān sa rahasyān ca tān śṛṇudhvam aśeṣatas śraddadhāne prayoktavyāḥ yasya śuddham tathā manaḥ aśraddadhānaḥ mānī ca brahma hā guru talpa gaḥ a saṃbhāṣyāḥ hi catvāraḥ na eṣām dharmam prakāśayet ahani ahani yaḥ dadyāt kapilām dvādaśīḥ samāḥ gavām śata sahasram ca yaḥ dadyāt jyeṣṭhapuṣkare śrūyatām ca aparaḥ dharmaḥ manuṣyāṇām sukha āvahaḥ niṣiñceta gavām śṛṅge mastakena ca tat jalam pratīccheta nirāhāraḥ tasya dharma phalam śṛṇu śrūyante yāni tīrthāni triṣu lokeṣu kāni cit siddha cāraṇa juṣṭāni sevitāni mahā ṛṣibhiḥ abhiṣekaḥ samaḥ teṣām gavām śṛṅga udakasya ca sādhu sādhu iti ca uddiṣṭam daivataiḥ pitṛbhiḥ tathā pitāmahaḥ bhūtaiḥ ca eva su saṃhṛṣṭaiḥ pūjitā sā api arundhatī yamaḥ ramaṇīyā kathā divyā yuṣmattaḥ yā mayā śrutā śrūyatām citraguptasya bhāṣitam mama ca priyam rahasyam dharma saṃyuktam śakyam śrotum mahā ṛṣibhiḥ na hi puṇyam tathā pāpam kṛtam kim cit vinaśyati parva kāle ca yat kim cit ādityam ca adhitiṣṭhati pānīyam ca eva dīpam ca dātavyam satatam tathā puṣkare kapilā deyā brāhmaṇe vedapārage tatra durgam anuprāptāḥ kṣudh tṛṣṇā paripīḍitāḥ pānīyasya guṇāḥ divyāḥ preta loke viśeṣataḥ tatra puṇyodakā nāma nadī teṣām vidhīyate akṣayam salilam tatra śītalam hi amṛta upamam pradīpasya pradānena śrūyatām guṇa vistaraḥ prabhām ca asya prayacchanti soma bhāskara pāvakāḥ devatāḥ ca asya manyante vimalāḥ sarvatodiśaḥ tasmāt dīpaḥ pradātavyaḥ pānīyam ca viśeṣataḥ puṣkare ca viśeṣeṇa śrūyatām tasya yat phalam go śatam sa vṛṣam tena dattam bhavati śāśvatam śodhayet kapilā hi ekā pradattam go śatam yathā tasmāt tu kapilā deyā kaumudyām jyeṣṭhapuṣkare na teṣām viṣamam kim cit na duḥkham na ca kaṇṭakāḥ chatra dāne sukhām chāyām labhate para loka gaḥ citragupta matam śrutvā hṛṣṭa romā vibhāvasuḥ uvāca devatāḥ sarvāḥ pitṝn ca eva mahā dyutiḥ śraddadhānāḥ ca ye martyāḥ brāhmaṇeṣu mahātmasu dharma doṣāḥ tu ime pañca yeṣām na asti iha niṣkṛtiḥ a saṃbhāṣyāḥ anācārāḥ varjanīyāḥ nara adhamāḥ aśraddadhānaḥ ca naraḥ striyam yaḥ ca upajīvati pacyante vai yathā mīnāḥ pūya śoṇita bhojanāḥ a saṃbhāṣyāḥ pitṝṇām ca devānām ca eva pañca te bhīṣmaḥ snātakānām ca viprāṇām ye ca anye ca tapodhanāḥ tatas sarve mahābhāgāḥ devāḥ ca pitaraḥ ca ha ṛṣayaḥ ca mahābhāgāḥ pramathān vākyam abruvan bhavantaḥ vai mahābhāgāḥ aparokṣa niśācarāḥ ucchiṣṭān aśucīn kṣudrān katham hiṃsatha mānavān ke ca smṛtāḥ pratīghātāḥ yena martyān na hiṃsatha rakṣaḥ ghnāni ca kāni syuḥ yebhiḥ gṛheṣu praṇaśyatha pramathāḥ śrotum icchāma vaḥ sarvam etat niśācarāḥ mohāt māṃsāni khādetha vṛkṣa mūle ca yaḥ svapet āmiṣam śīrṣataḥ yasya pādataḥ yaḥ ca saṃviśet tatas ucchiṣṭakāḥ sarve bahu chidrāḥ ca mānavāḥ udake ca api amedhyāni śleṣmāṇam ca pramuñcati ete bhakṣyāḥ ca vadhyāḥ ca mānuṣāḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ evaṃśīla samācārān dharṣayāmaḥ hi mānavān śrūyatām ca pratīghātān yaiḥ na śaknuma hiṃsitum ghṛta akṣatam ca yaḥ dadyāt mastake tad parāyaṇaḥ ye ca māṃsam na khādanti tān na śaknuma hiṃsitum tarakṣoḥ carma daṃṣṭrāḥ ca tathā eva giri kacchapaḥ ājya dhūmaḥ biḍālaḥ ca chāgaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ atha piṅgalaḥ yeṣām etāni tiṣṭhanti gṛheṣu gṛhamedhinām tāni adhṛṣyāṇi agārāṇi piśitāśaiḥ su dāruṇaiḥ tasmāt etāni geheṣu rakṣaḥ ghnāni viśām pate bhīṣmaḥ etat vaḥ kathitam sarvam yatra vaḥ saṃśayaḥ mahān tatas padma pratīkāśaḥ padma udbhūtaḥ pitāmahaḥ uvāca vacanam devān vāsavam ca śacīpatim ayam mahā balaḥ nāgaḥ rasātala caraḥ balī tejasvī reṇukaḥ nāma mahā sattva parākramaḥ ati tejasvinaḥ sarve mahā vīryāḥ mahā gajāḥ dhārayanti mahīm kṛtsnām sa śaila vana kānanām bhavadbhiḥ samanujñātaḥ reṇukaḥ tān mahā gajān pitāmaha vacaḥ śrutvā te devāḥ reṇukam tadā reṇukaḥ preṣayām āsuḥ avyagrāḥ yatra te dharaṇīdharāḥ anujñātaḥ asmi devaiḥ ca pitṛbhiḥ ca mahā balāḥ dharma guhyāni yuṣmākam śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥ diggajāḥ kathayadhvam mahābhāgāḥ yat vaḥ tattvam manīṣitam kārttike māsi ca āśleṣā bahulasya aṣṭamī śivā imam mantram japan śrāddhe yata āhāraḥ hi akopanaḥ anantāḥ hi akṣayāḥ nityam bhoginaḥ su mahā balāḥ teṣām kula udbhavāḥ ye ca mahā bhūtāḥ bhujaṃgamāḥ yadā nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān ujjahāra vasuṃdharām gaja indra kusuma ākīrṇam nīla vastra anulepanam evam tuṣṭāḥ tatas sarve adhastāt bhāra pīḍitā śramam tam na avabudhyāmaḥ dhārayantaḥ vasuṃdharām evam manyāmahe dharmam bhāra ārtāḥ nirapekṣiṇaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vaiśyaḥ śūdraḥ vā yadi upoṣitaḥ evam saṃvatsaram kṛtvā dānam bahu phalam labhet ye ca nāgāḥ mahā vīryāḥ triṣu lokeṣu kṛtsnaśas kṛta ātithyāḥ bhaveyuḥ te śatam varṣāṇi tattvāt diggajānām ca tat śrutvā devatāḥ pitaraḥ tathā maheśvaraḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca mahābhāgāḥ pūjayanti sma reṇukam sāram uddhṛtya yuṣmābhiḥ sādhu dharmaḥ udāhṛtaḥ yeṣām dharma āśritā buddhiḥ śraddha dhānāḥ ca ye narāḥ teṣām syāt upadeṣṭavyaḥ sa rahasyaḥ mahā phalaḥ eka bhaktam tathā aśnīyāt śrūyatām tasya yat phalam imāḥ gāvaḥ mahābhāgāḥ pavitram paramam smṛtāḥ trīn lokān dhārayanti sma sa deva asura mānuṣān tāsu ca eva mahā puṇyam śuśrūṣā ca mahā phalam mayā hi etāḥ hi anujñātāḥ pūrvam āsan kṛte yuge tasmāt vraja sthāna gataḥ tiṣṭhati upari me vṛṣaḥ rame aham saha gobhiḥ ca tasmāt pūjyāḥ sadā eva tāḥ mahā prabhāvāḥ vara dāḥ varān dadyuḥ upāsitāḥ mama api anumataḥ dharmaḥ tam śṛṇudhvam samāhitāḥ nīlaṣaṇḍasya śṛṅgābhyām gṛhītvā mṛttikām tu yaḥ pragṛhya audumbaram pātram pakva annam madhunā saha somasya uttiṣṭhamānasya paurṇamāsyām balim haret sādhyāḥ rudrāḥ tathā ādityāḥ viśvedevāḥ tathā aśvinaḥ viṣṇuḥ eṣa dharmaḥ mayā uddiṣṭaḥ sa rahasyaḥ sukha āvahaḥ dharma guhyāni sarvāṇi devatānām mahātmanām ṛṣīṇām ca eva guhyāni yaḥ paṭhet āhnikam sadā śṛṇuyāt vā anasūyuḥ yaḥ śraddadhānaḥ samāhitaḥ ye ca dharmāḥ śubhāḥ puṇyāḥ sa rahasyāḥ udāhṛtāḥ teṣām dharma phalam tasya yaḥ paṭheta jita indriyaḥ paṭhet vā śrāvayet vā api śrutvā vā labhate phalam śrāvayan ca api vipra indrān parvasu prayataḥ naraḥ ṛṣīṇām devatānām ca pitṝṇām ca eva nityadā bhavati abhimataḥ śrīmān dharmeṣu prayataḥ sadā kṛtvā api pāpakam karma mahāpātaka varjitam bhīṣmaḥ vyāsa uddiṣṭam mayā proktam sarva deva namaskṛtam pṛthivī ratna saṃpūrṇā jñānam ca idam anuttamam na aśraddadhānāya na nāstikāya na naṣṭa dharmāya na nirguṇāya na hetu duṣṭāya guru dviṣe vā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bhīṣmaḥ tathā vaiśyasya ke bhojyāḥ ke ca śūdrasya bhārata brāhmaṇāḥ brāhmaṇasya iha bhojyāḥ ye ca eva kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ ca api tathā bhojyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca parivarjitāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ bhojyāḥ vai kṣatriyasya ha varjanīyāḥ tu vai śūdrāḥ sarva bhakṣyāḥ vikarmiṇaḥ vaiśyāḥ tu bhojyāḥ viprāṇām kṣatriyāṇām tathā eva ca nitya agnayaḥ viviktāḥ ca cāturmāsya ratāḥ ca ye śūdrāṇām atha yaḥ bhuṅkte sa bhuṅkte pṛthivī malam malam nṛṇām sa pibati malam bhuṅkte janasya ca śūdrāṇām yaḥ tathā bhuṅkte sa bhuṅkte pṛthivī malam pṛthivī malam aśnanti ye dvijāḥ śūdra bhojinaḥ śūdrasya karma niṣṭhāyām vikarma sthaḥ api pacyate svādhyāya niratāḥ viprāḥ tathā svastyayane nṛṇām rakṣaṇe kṣatriyam prāhuḥ vaiśyam puṣṭi artham eva ca kṛṣi gorakṣya vāṇijyam akutsā vaiśya karmaṇi sa vijñeyaḥ yathā śūdraḥ na ca bhojyaḥ kadā cana cikitsakaḥ kāṇḍapṛṣṭhaḥ purādhyakṣaḥ purohitaḥ sāṃvatsaraḥ vṛthak adhyāyī sarve te śūdra saṃmitāḥ puṃścalī annam ca mūtram syāt kārukā annam ca śoṇitam vacanīyasya yaḥ bhuṅkte tam āhuḥ śoṇitam hradam piśunam bhojanam bhuṅkte brahmahatyā samam viduḥ asatkṛtam avajñātam na bhoktavyam kadā cana vyādhim kula kṣayam ca eva kṣipram prāpnoti brāhmaṇaḥ bhuktvā annam jāyate vipraḥ rakṣasām kula vardhanaḥ nyāsa apahāriṇaḥ bhuktvā kṛtaghne klība vartini jāyate śabara āvāse madhyadeśa bahiṣkṛte abhojyāḥ ca eva bhojyāḥ ca mayā proktāḥ yathāvidhi yudhiṣṭhiraḥ vaktāḥ tu bhavatā bhojyāḥ tathā abhojyāḥ ca sarvaśas brāhmaṇānām viśeṣeṇa havya kavya pratigrahe bhīṣmaḥ nānāvidheṣu bhojyeṣu prāyaścittāni śaṃsa me hanta vakṣyāmi te rājan brāhmaṇānām mahātmanām āditya udayanam sthitvā pūtaḥ bhavati brāhmaṇaḥ kāñcanam pratigṛhya atha japamānaḥ guru śrutim kṛṣṇāyasam ca trivṛtam dhārayan mucyate dvijaḥ yāvake dadhi dugdhe ca sāvitrīm śataśas anvitām trīṇi rātrāṇi upoṣitvā tena pāpmā vimucyate kṛṣṇa pakṣe tu yaḥ śrāddham pitṝṇām aśnute dvijaḥ annam etat ahar rātrāt pūtaḥ bhavati brāhmaṇaḥ na saṃkiret tat annam ca tathā pūyeta brāhmaṇaḥ ityartham aparāhṇe tu pitṝṇām śrāddham ucyate yathā uktānām yat aśnīyuḥ brāhmaṇāḥ pūrva ketitāḥ mṛtakasya tṛtīya ahe brāhmaṇaḥ yaḥ annam aśnute dvādaśa ahe vyatīte tu kṛta śaucaḥ viśeṣataḥ mṛtasya mṛ daśan rātreṇa prāyaścittāni dāpayet sāvitrīm raivatīm iṣṭim kūṣmāṇḍam aghamarṣaṇam sapta triṣavaṇam snātvā pūtaḥ bhavati brāhmaṇaḥ yaḥ tu śūdraiḥ saha aśnīyāt brāhmaṇaḥ api eka bhojane yaḥ tu vaiśyaiḥ saha aśnīyāt brāhmaṇaḥ api eka bhojane sa vai tri rātram dīkṣitvā mucyate tena karmaṇā kṣatriyaiḥ saha yaḥ aśnīyāt brāhmaṇaḥ api eka bhojane śūdrasya tu kulam hanti vaiśyasya paśu bāndhavān prāyaścittam ca śāntim ca juhuyāt tena mucyate sāvitrīm raivatīm iṣṭim kūṣmāṇḍam aghamarṣaṇam atha ucchiṣṭam atha anyonyam saṃprāśet na atra saṃśayaḥ rocanā virajāḥ rātriḥ maṅgala ālambhanāni ca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kim svid pṛthivyām hi etat me bhavān śaṃsitum arhati bhīṣmaḥ śṛṇu yaiḥ dharma nirataiḥ tapasā bhāvitātmabhiḥ lokāḥ hi asaṃśayam prāptāḥ dāna puṇya rataiḥ nṛpaiḥ satkṛtaḥ ca tathā ātreyaḥ śiṣyebhyaḥ brahma nirguṇam śibiḥ auśīnaraḥ prāṇān priyasya tanayasya ca brāhmaṇa artham upākṛtya nāka pṛṣṭham itas gataḥ brāhmaṇāya atulām kīrtim iha ca amutra ca aśnute rantidevaḥ ca sāṃkṛtyaḥ vasiṣṭhāya mahātmane divyam śata śalākam ca yajña artham kāñcanam śubham chatram devāvṛdhaḥ dattvā brāhmaṇāya āsthitaḥ divam bhagavān ambarīṣaḥ ca brāhmaṇāya amita ojase pradāya sakalam rāṣṭram sura lokam avāptavān sāvitraḥ kuṇḍalam divyam yānam ca janamejayaḥ brāhmaṇāya ca gāḥ dattvā gataḥ lokān anuttamān vṛṣādarbhiḥ ca rājarṣiḥ ratnāni vividhāni ca ramyān ca āvasathān dattvā dvijebhyaḥ divam āgamat nimiḥ rāṣṭram ca vaidarbhiḥ kanyām dattvā mahātmane jāmadagnyaḥ ca viprāya bhūmim dattvā mahā yaśāḥ rāmaḥ akṣayān tathā lokān jagāma manasaḥ adhikān vasiṣṭhaḥ jīvayām āsa yena yātaḥ akṣayām gatim rāmaḥ dāśarathiḥ ca eva hutvā yajñeṣu vai vasu kakṣasenaḥ ca rājarṣiḥ vasiṣṭhāya mahātmane nyāsam yathāvat saṃnyasya jagāma su mahā yaśāḥ kanyām aṅgirase dattvā divam āśu jagāma saḥ brahmadattaḥ ca pāñcālyaḥ rājā dharma bhṛtām varaḥ nidhim śaṅkham anujñāpya jagāma paramām gatim rājā mitrasahaḥ ca eva vasiṣṭhāya mahātmane madayantīm priyām bhāryām dattvā ca tridivam gataḥ sahasracityaḥ rājarṣiḥ prāṇān iṣ mahā yaśāḥ sarva kāmaiḥ ca saṃpūrṇam dattvā veśma hiraṇmayam bhakṣya bhojya ca kṛtān rāśayaḥ parvata upamān śāṇḍilyāya purā dattvā sa manyuḥ divam āsthitaḥ nāmnā ca dyutimant nāma śālva rājaḥ mahā dyutiḥ dattvā rājyam ṛcīkāya gataḥ lokān anuttamān madirāśvaḥ ca rājarṣiḥ dattvā kanyām sumadhyamām lomapādaḥ ca rājarṣiḥ śāntām dattvā sutām prabhuḥ ṛṣyaśṛṅgāya vipulaiḥ sarvaiḥ kāmaiḥ ayujyata kautsāya dattvā kanyām tu haṃsīm nāma yaśasvinīm gataḥ akṣayān atas lokān rājarṣiḥ ca bhagīrathaḥ dattvā śata sahasram tu gavām rājā bhagīrathaḥ sa sa vatsānām kohalāya gataḥ lokān anuttamān yudhiṣṭhira gam svargam nivartante punar punar teṣām pratiṣṭhitā kīrtiḥ yāvat sthāsyati medinī śiṣṭānām caritam hi etat kīrtitam me yudhiṣṭhira dattvā tu satatam te astu kauravāṇām dhuraṃdhara yatra te nṛpa śārdūla saṃdehaḥ vai bhaviṣyati yudhiṣṭhiraḥ śvas prabhāte hi vakṣyāmi saṃdhyā hi samupasthitā dāna dharmeṇa mahatā ye prāptāḥ tridivam nṛpāḥ imān tu śrotum icchāmi dharmān dharma bhṛtām vara katham kebhyaḥ ca dharmyam ca dānam dātavyam iṣyate bhīṣmaḥ kaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ katividham śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥ yathā dānam pradātavyam sarva varṇeṣu bhārata dharmāt arthāt bhayāt kāmāt kāruṇyāt iti bhārata dānam pañcavidham jñeyam kāraṇaiḥ yad nibodha tat iti dānam pradātavyam brāhmaṇebhyaḥ anasūyatā dadāti vā dāsyati vā mahyam dattam anena vā na asya aham na madīyaḥ ayam pāpam kuryāt vimānitaḥ iti dadyāt bhayāt eva dṛḍham mūḍhāya paṇḍitaḥ vayasyāya evam akliṣṭam dānam dadyāt atandritaḥ dīnaḥ ca yācate ca ayam alpena api hi tuṣyati iti dadyāt daridrāya kāruṇyāt iti sarvathā yathāśaktyā pradātavyam evam āha prajāpatiḥ uvāca pitāmaha mahā prājña sarva śāstra viśārada āścarya bhūtam lokasya śrotum icchāmi ariṃdama ayam ca kālaḥ saṃprāptaḥ durlabha jñāti bāndhavaḥ śāstā ca na hi naḥ kaḥ cit tvām ṛte bharata ṛṣabha vaktum arhasi naḥ praśnam yat tvām pṛcchāmi pārthiva ayam nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān sarva pārthiva saṃmataḥ asya ca eva samakṣam tvam pārthivānām ca sarvaśas bhrātṝṇām ca priya artham me snehāt bhāṣitum arhasi uvāca tasya tat vacanam śrutvā snehāt āgata saṃbhramaḥ bhīṣmaḥ bhāgīrathī putraḥ idam vacanam abravīt asya viṣṇoḥ purā rājan prabhāvaḥ ayam mayā śru yaḥ ca go vṛṣabha aṅkasya prabhāvaḥ tam ca me śṛṇu rudrāṇyāḥ saṃśayaḥ yaḥ ca dampatiyoḥ tam ca mama śṛṇu vratam cacāra dharma ātmā kṛṣṇaḥ dvādaśa vārṣikam dīkṣitam ca āgatau draṣṭum ubhau nārada parvatau kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ ca eva dhaumyaḥ ca japatām varaḥ devalaḥ kāśyapaḥ ca eva hastikāśyapaḥ eva ca apare ṛṣayaḥ santaḥ dīkṣā dama samanvitāḥ hariteṣu suvarṇeṣu barhiṣkeṣu naveṣu ca upopaviviśuḥ prītāḥ viṣṭareṣu mahā ṛṣayaḥ rājarṣīṇām surāṇām ca ye vasanti tapodhanāḥ vaktrāt niḥsṛtya kṛṣṇasya vahniḥ adbhuta karmaṇaḥ saḥ agniḥ dadāha tam śailam sa drumam sa latā kṣupam sa pakṣi mṛga saṃghātam sa śvāpada sarīsṛpam mṛgaiḥ ca vividha ākāraiḥ hāhā bhūtam acetanam viṣṇoḥ samīpam āgamya pādau śiṣya vat aspṛśat tatas viṣṇuḥ vanam dṛṣṭvā nirdagdham ari karśanaḥ saumyaiḥ dṛṣṭi nipātaiḥ tat punar prakṛtim ānayat sa pakṣi gaṇa saṃghuṣṭaḥ sa śvāpada sarīsṛpaḥ tat adbhutam acintyam ca dṛṣṭvā muni gaṇaḥ tadā vismitaḥ hṛṣṭa lomā ca babhūva asra āvila īkṣaṇaḥ tatas nārāyaṇaḥ dṛṣṭvā tān ṛṣīn vismaya anvitān kim asya ṛṣi pūgasya tyakta saṅgasya nityaśas etam me saṃśayam sarvam yāthātathyam aninditāḥ ṛṣayaḥ vaktum arhanti niścita artham tapodhanāḥ ūcuḥ bhavān visṛjate lokān bhavān saṃharate punar bhavān śītam bhavān uṣṇam bhavān eva pravarṣati pṛthivyām yāni bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca teṣām pitā tvam mātā ca prabhuḥ prabhavaḥ eva ca yat śrutam yat ca dṛṣṭam naḥ tat pravakṣyāmahe hare uvāca kṛṣṇavartmā yuga anta ābhaḥ yena ayam mathitaḥ giriḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca ārtim āpannāḥ jita krodhāḥ jita indriyāḥ putram ca ātma samam vīrye tapasā sraṣṭum āgataḥ tatas mama ātmā yaḥ dehe saḥ agniḥ bhūtvā viniḥsṛtaḥ gataḥ ca vara dam draṣṭum sarva loka pitāmaham tena ca ātmā anuśiṣṭaḥ me putra tve muni sattamāḥ śiṣya vat paricarya atha śāntaḥ prakṛtim āgataḥ mayā premṇā samākhyātam na bhī kāryā tapodhanāḥ sarvatra gatiḥ avyagrā bhavatām dīrgha darśanāḥ tapasvi vrata saṃdīptāḥ jñāna vijñāna śobhitāḥ yat śrutam yat ca vaḥ dṛṣṭam divi vā yadi vā bhuvi tasya amṛta nikāśasya vāc madhoḥ asti me spṛhā divi vā bhuvi vā kim cit paśyāmi amala darśanāḥ śraddheyaḥ kathitaḥ hi arthaḥ sat jana śravaṇam gataḥ ciram tiṣṭhati medinyām śaile lekhyam iva arpitam tat aham sat jana mukhāt niḥsṛtam tad samāgame kathayiṣyāmi aharahar buddhi dīpa karam nṛṇām tatas muni gaṇāḥ sarve praśritāḥ kṛṣṇa saṃnidhau vāgbhiḥ ṛc bhūṣita arthābhiḥ stuvantaḥ madhusūdanam tatas muni gaṇāḥ sarve nāradam devadarśanam anubhūtam muni gaṇaiḥ tīrtha yātrā parāyaṇaiḥ tat bhavān ṛṣi saṃghasya hita artham sarva coditaḥ yathādṛṣṭam hṛṣīkeśe sarvam ākhyātum arhati evam uktaḥ sa munibhiḥ nāradaḥ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ kathayām āsa deva ṛṣiḥ pūrva vṛttām kathām śubhām uvāca tatas nārāyaṇa suhṛd nāradaḥ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ śaṃkarasya umayā sārdham saṃvādam pratyabhāṣata tapaḥ cacāra dharma ātmā vṛṣabhāṅkaḥ sureśvaraḥ nānā oṣadhi yute ramye nānā puṣpa samākule apsaraḥ gaṇa saṃkīrṇe bhūta saṃgha niṣevite nānā rūpaiḥ virūpaiḥ ca divyaiḥ adbhuta darśanaiḥ kroṣṭuka dvīpi vadanaiḥ ṛkṣa ṛṣabha mukhaiḥ tathā nānā varṇa mṛga prakhyaiḥ sarva jāti samanvayaiḥ divya puṣpa samākīrṇam divya mālā vibhūṣitam tat sadaḥ vṛṣabhāṅkasya divya vāditra nāditam mṛdaṅga paṇava udghuṣṭam śaṅkha bherī nināditam dṛṣṭi kāntam anirdeśyam divyam adbhuta darśanam ṣaṭpadaiḥ upagītaiḥ ca mādhava apratimaḥ giriḥ tam mahā utsava saṃkāśam bhīma rūpa dharam punar dṛṣṭvā muni gaṇasya āsīt parā prītiḥ janārdana munayaḥ ca mahābhāgāḥ siddhāḥ ca eva ūrdhvaretasaḥ marutaḥ vasavaḥ sādhyāḥ viśvedevāḥ sanātanāḥ yakṣāḥ nāgāḥ piśācāḥ ca lokapālāḥ hutāśanāḥ bhāvāḥ ca sarve nyagbhūtāḥ tatra eva āsan samāgatāḥ vihagāḥ ca mudā yuktāḥ prānṛtyan vyanadan ca ha giri pṛṣṭheṣu ramyeṣu vyāharantaḥ jana priyāḥ paryaṅke iva vibhrājan upaviṣṭaḥ mahā manāḥ vyāla yajña upavītī ca lohita aṅgada bhūṣaṇaḥ hari śmaśruḥ jaṭī bhīmaḥ bhaya kartā suradviṣām abhayaḥ sarva bhūtānām bhaktānām vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ dṛṣṭvā tam ṛṣayaḥ sarve śirobhiḥ avanīm gatāḥ vimuktāḥ sarva pāpebhyaḥ kṣāntāḥ vigata kalmaṣāḥ tad bhūtapateḥ sthānam bhīma rūpa dhara babhā tat sadaḥ vṛṣabhāṅkasya bhīma rūpa dharam babhau tam abhyayāt śailasutā bhūta strī gaṇa saṃvṛtā hara tulya ambara dharā samāna vrata cāriṇī giri sravābhiḥ puṇyābhiḥ sarvatas anugatā śubhā puṣpa vṛṣṭyā abhivarṣantī gandhaiḥ bahuvidhaiḥ tathā sevatī himavat pārśvam hara pārśvam upāgamat tatas smayantī pāṇibhyām narma artham cāru darśanā hara netre śubhe devī sahasā sā samāvṛṇot saṃvṛtābhyām tu netrābhyām tamaḥ bhūtam acetanam nirhomam nirvaṣaṭkāram tat sadaḥ sahasā bhavat nimīlite bhūtapatau naṣṭa sūryaḥ iva abhavat jvālā ca mahatī dīptā lalāṭāt tasya niḥsṛtā tṛtīyam ca asya saṃbhūtam netram āditya saṃnibham yuga anta sadṛśam dīptam yena asau mathitaḥ giriḥ tatas girisutā dṛṣṭvā dīpta agni sadṛśa īkṣaṇam haram praṇamya śirasā dadarśa āyata locanā mṛga yūthaiḥ drutaiḥ bhītaiḥ hara pārśvam upāgataiḥ śaraṇam ca api a vindadbhiḥ tat sadaḥ saṃkulam babhau dvādaśa āditya sadṛśaḥ yuga anta agniḥ iva aparaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā mathitam śailam śailarājasutā tatas bhagavantam prapannā sā sa añjali pragrahā sthitā umām śarvaḥ tadā dṛṣṭvā strī bhāva āgata mārdavām prakṛti stham girim dṛṣṭvā prītā devī maheśvaram uvāca sarva bhūtānām patim patim aninditā bhagavant sarva bhūta īśa śūlapāṇe mahāvrata saṃśayaḥ mama mahān jātaḥ tam me vyākhyātum arhasi kimartham ca punar deva prakṛti stha kṣaṇāt kṛ naṣṭa ālokaḥ tatas lokaḥ kṣaṇena samapadyata naṣṭa āditye tathā loke tamaḥ bhūte nagātmaje tṛtīyam locanam dīptam sṛṣṭam te rakṣatā prajāḥ tasya ca akṣṇaḥ mahat tejaḥ yena ayam mathitaḥ giriḥ tvad priya artham ca mama devi prakṛti sthaḥ kṣaṇāt kṛtaḥ pūrvam tathā eva śrī kāntam uttaram paścimam tathā dakṣiṇam ca mukham raudram kena ūrdhvam kapilāḥ jaṭāḥ kena kaṇṭhaḥ ca te nīlaḥ barhi barha nibhaḥ kṛtaḥ etam mama saṃśayam sarvam vada bhūtapate anagha sa dharma cāriṇī ca aham bhaktā ca iti vṛṣadhvaja evam uktaḥ sa bhagavant śailaputryā pinākadhṛk tasyāḥ vṛttyā ca buddhyā ca prītimān abhavat prabhuḥ tatas tām abravīt devaḥ subhage śrūyatām iti tilottamā nāma purā brahmaṇā yoṣit uttamā tilam tilam samuddhṛtya ratnānām nirmitā śubhā sā abhyagacchata mām devi rūpeṇa apratimā bhuvi pradakṣiṇam lobhayantī mām śubhe rucira ānanā yatas yatas sā sudatī mām upādhāvat antike tām didṛkṣuḥ aham yogāt catur mūrti tvam āgataḥ paścimam me mukham saumyam sarva prāṇi sukha āvaham dakṣiṇam bhīma saṃkāśam raudram saṃharati prajāḥ jaṭilaḥ brahmacārī ca lokānām hita kāmyayā indreṇa ca purā vajram kṣiptam śrī kāṅkṣiṇā mama dagdhvā kaṇṭham tu tat yātam tena śrīkaṇṭha tā mama vāhaneṣu prabhūteṣu śrīmatsu anyeṣu satsu te katham go vṛṣabhaḥ deva vāhana tvam upāgataḥ surabhīm sasṛje brahma amṛta dhenum payaḥ mucam sā sṛṣṭā bahudhā jātā kṣaramāṇā payaḥ amṛtam tasyāḥ vatsa mukha utsṛṣṭaḥ phenaḥ mad gātram āgataḥ tatas dagdhāḥ mayāḥ gāvaḥ nānā varṇa tvam āgatāḥ tatas aham lokaguruṇā śamam nītaḥ artha vedinā vṛṣam ca imam dhvaja artham me dadau vāhanam eva ca nivāsāḥ bahu rūpāḥ te viśva rūpa guṇa anvitāḥ tān ca saṃtyajya bhagavan śmaśāne ramase katham keśa asthi kalile bhīme kapāla ghaṭa saṃkule aśucau māṃsa kalile vasā śoṇita kardame vinikīrṇa āmiṣa caye śivā nāda vinādite medhya anveṣī mahīm kṛtsnām vicarāmi niśāsu aham tena me sarva vāsānām śmaśāne ramate manaḥ pinākapāṇe vara da saṃśayaḥ mama mahān ayam dharmaḥ kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ proktaḥ katham vā ācaritum naraiḥ uvāca tatas muni gaṇaḥ sarvaḥ tām devīm pratyapūjayat vāgbhiḥ ṛc bhūṣita arthābhiḥ stavaiḥ ca artha vidām vara śamaḥ dānam yathāśakti gārhasthyaḥ dharmaḥ uttamaḥ para dāreṣu a saṃkalpaḥ nyāsa strī parirakṣaṇam eṣa pañcavidhaḥ dharmaḥ bahu śākhaḥ sukha udayaḥ bhagavant saṃśayam pṛṣṭaḥ tam me vyākhyātum arhasi cāturvarṇyasya yaḥ dharmaḥ sve sve varṇe guṇa āvahaḥ brāhmaṇe kīdṛśaḥ dharmaḥ kṣatriye kīdṛśaḥ bhavet vaiśye kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ dharmaḥ śūdre kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ bhavet nyāyataḥ te mahābhāge saṃśayaḥ samudīritaḥ bhūmidevāḥ mahābhāgāḥ sadā loke dvijātayaḥ upavāsaḥ sadā dharmaḥ brāhmaṇasya na saṃśayaḥ guru daivata pūjā artham svādhyāya abhyasana ātmakaḥ guruṇā tu abhyanujñātaḥ samāvarteta vai dvijaḥ vindeta anantaram bhāryām anurūpām yathāvidhi āhitāgniḥ adhīyānaḥ juhvānaḥ saṃyata indriyaḥ vighasa āśī yata āhāraḥ gṛhasthaḥ satya vāc śuciḥ iṣṭīḥ ca paśubandhān ca vidhi pūrvam samācaret yajñaḥ ca paramaḥ dharmaḥ tathā ahiṃsā ca dehiṣu brāhmaṇasya gṛhasthasya śrotriyasya viśeṣataḥ dampatyoḥ sama śīla tvam dharmaḥ ca gṛhamedhinām gṛhyānām ca eva devānām nityam puṣpa bali kriyā su saṃmṛṣṭa upalipte ca sa ājya dhūma udgame gṛhe dvijātīnām satām nityam sadā eva eṣa pravartate tam aham te pravakṣyāmi tam mama śṛṇu samāhitā kṣatriyasya smṛtaḥ dharmaḥ prajā pālanam āditas prajāḥ pālayate yaḥ hi dharmeṇa manuja adhipaḥ tasya dharma arjitāḥ lokāḥ prajā pālana saṃcitāḥ yajñopavīta dhāraṇam yajñaḥ dharma kriyāḥ tathā bhṛtyānām bharaṇam dharmaḥ kṛte karmaṇi amogha tā go brāhmaṇa arthe vikrāntaḥ saṃgrāme nidhanam gataḥ aśvamedha jitān lokān prāpnoti tridiva ālaye vaiśyasya satatam dharmaḥ pāśupālyam kṛṣiḥ tathā vāṇijyam sat patha sthānam ātithyam praśamaḥ damaḥ viprāṇām svāgatam tyāgaḥ vaiśya dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ tilān gandhān rasān ca eva na vikrīṇīta vai kva cit vaṇikpatham upāsīnaḥ vaiśyaḥ sat patham āśritaḥ śūdra dharmaḥ paraḥ nityam śuśrūṣā ca dvijātiṣu sa śūdraḥ saṃśita tapāḥ satya saṃdhaḥ jita indriyaḥ śuśrūṣan atithim prāptam tapaḥ saṃcinute mahat tyakta hiṃsaḥ śubha ācāraḥ devatā dvija pūjakaḥ uktāḥ tvayā pṛthak dharmāḥ cāturvarṇya hitāḥ śubhāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ loka sāreṇa sṛṣṭāḥ dhātrā guṇa arthinā lokān tārayitum kṛtsnān martyeṣu kṣitidevatāḥ ime tu loka dharma artham trayaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ svayambhunā pṛthivyāḥ sarjane nityam sṛṣṭāḥ tān api mama śṛṇu śiṣṭa ācīrṇaḥ paraḥ proktaḥ trayaḥ dharmāḥ sanātanāḥ ṣaḍ imā tu karmāṇi provāca bhuvaneśvaraḥ vṛtti artham brāhmaṇānām vai śṛṇu tāni samāhitā adhyāpanam adhītam ca ṣaṣ karmā dharma bhāj dvijaḥ nitya svādhyāya tā dharmaḥ dharmaḥ yajñaḥ sanātanaḥ dānam praśasyate ca asya yathāśakti yathāvidhi gṛhastha tā viśuddhānām dharmasya nicayaḥ mahān pañcayajña viśuddha ātmā satya vāc anasūyakaḥ dātā brāhmaṇa satkartā su saṃmṛṣṭa niveśanaḥ a mānī ca sadā a jihmaḥ snigdha vāṇī pradaḥ tathā atithi abhyāgata ratiḥ śeṣa anna kṛta bhojanaḥ pādyam arghyam yathānyāyam āsanam śayanam tathā dīpam pratiśrayam ca api yaḥ dadāti sa dhārmikaḥ śūdra dharmaḥ samākhyātaḥ tri varṇa paricāraṇam tam aham kīrtayiṣyāmi sarva bhūta hitam śubham dātavyam asakṛt śaktyā yaṣṭavyam asakṛt tathā puṣṭi karma vidhānam ca kartavyam bhūtim icchatā ekena aṃśena dharma arthaḥ cartavyaḥ bhūtim icchatā ekena aṃśena kāma arthe ekam aṃśam vivardhayet tasya vṛttim pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu mama devi tattvāt āśā pāśa vimokṣaḥ ca śasyate mokṣa kāṅkṣiṇām na kuṇḍyām na udake saṅgaḥ na vāsasi na ca āsane na tridaṇḍe na śayane na agnau na śaraṇa ālaye vṛkṣa mūla śayaḥ nityam śūnya āgāra niveśanaḥ nadī pulina śāyī ca nadī tīra ratiḥ ca yaḥ ātmani eva ātmanaḥ bhāvam samāsajya aṭati dvijaḥ sthāṇu bhūtaḥ nirāhāraḥ mokṣa dṛṣṭena karmaṇā eṣa mokṣa vidām dharmaḥ veda uktaḥ sat pathaḥ satām caturvidhāḥ bhikṣavaḥ te kuṭī cara kṛta udakaḥ haṃsaḥ paramahaṃsaḥ ca yaḥ yaḥ paścāt saḥ uttamaḥ atas parataram na asti na adharam na tiras agratas tam dṛṣṭvā mama manaḥ prītam maheśvara sadā bhavet etam mama saṃśayam deva muni dharma kṛtam vibho nikhilena mayā pṛṣṭam mahādeva yathātatham yam kṛtvā munayaḥ yānti siddhim sva tapasā śubhe phenapānām ṛṣīṇām yaḥ dharmaḥ dharma vidām sadā tam mama śṛṇu mahābhāge dharma jñe dharmam āditas amṛtam brahmaṇā pītam madhuram prasṛtam divi eṣa teṣām viśuddhānām phenapānām tapodhane dharma caryā kṛtaḥ mārgaḥ vālakhilya gaṇe śṛṇu vālakhilyāḥ tapaḥ siddhāḥ munayaḥ sūrya maṇḍale uñcham uñchanti dharma jñāḥ śākunām vṛttim āsthitāḥ mṛga nirmoka vasanāḥ cīra valkala vāsasaḥ nirdvaṃdvāḥ sat patham prāptāḥ vālakhilyāḥ tapodhanāḥ aṅguṣṭha parva mātrāḥ te sveṣu aṅgeṣu vyavasthitāḥ tapaḥ caraṇam īhante teṣām dharma phalam mahat dyotayantaḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ tapasā dagdha kilbiṣāḥ ye tu anye śuddha manasaḥ dayā dharma parāyaṇāḥ santaḥ cakracarāḥ puṇyāḥ soma loka carāḥ ca ye saṃprakṣāla aśmakuṭṭāḥ ca dantolūkhalinaḥ tathā somapānām ca devānām ūṣmapāṇām tathā eva ca uñchanti ye samīpa sthāḥ svabhāva niyata indriyāḥ teṣām agni pariṣyandaḥ pitṛ deva arcanam tathā yajñānām ca api pañcānām yajanam dharmaḥ ucyate ṛṣi dharmaḥ sadā cīrṇaḥ yaḥ anyaḥ tam api mama śṛṇu soma yajña abhyanujñānam pañcamī yajña dakṣiṇā nityam yajña kriyā dharmaḥ pitṛ deva arcane ratiḥ sthaṇḍile śayanam yogaḥ śāka parṇa niṣevaṇam phala mūla aśanam vāyuḥ apaḥ śaivala bhakṣaṇam ṛṣīṇām niyamāḥ hi ete yaiḥ jayanti ajitām gatim atīta pātrasaṃcāre kāle vigata bhaikṣake atithim kāṅkṣamāṇaḥ vai śeṣa anna kṛta bhojanaḥ deśeṣu ramaṇīyeṣu girīṇām nirjhareṣu ca sravantīnām ca kuñjeṣu parvata upavaneṣu ca deśeṣu ca vicitreṣu phalavatsu samāhitāḥ teṣām api vidhim puṇyam śrotum icchāmi śaṃkara vānaprastheṣu deveśa sva śarīra upajīviṣu vānaprastha uñcha vṛttīnām tapaḥ vistṛta cetasām vānaprastheṣu yaḥ dharmaḥ tam me śṛṇu samāhitā vānaprasthaiḥ idam karma kartavyam śṛṇu yādṛśam tri kālam abhiṣeka arthaḥ pitṛ deva arcanam kriyā nīvāra grahaṇam ca eva phala mūla niṣevaṇam iṅgudaiḥ aṇḍa tailānām sneha artham ca niṣevaṇam vīraśayyām upāsadbhiḥ vīrasthāna upasevibhiḥ maṇḍūkayoga niyataiḥ yathā nyāya niṣevibhiḥ vīrāsana gataiḥ nityam sthaṇḍile śayanaiḥ tathā abbhakṣaiḥ vāyubhakṣaiḥ ca śaivāla uttara bhojanaiḥ aśmakuṭṭaiḥ tathā dāntaiḥ samprakṣālaiḥ tathā aparaiḥ cīra valkala saṃvītaiḥ mṛga carma nivāsibhiḥ kāryā yātrā yathākālam yathādharmam yathāvidhi vanam gurum iva āsādya vastavyam vana jīvibhiḥ teṣām homa kriyā dharmaḥ pañcayajña niṣevaṇam aṣṭamī yajña para tā cāturmāsya niṣevaṇam vimuktāḥ dāra saṃyogaiḥ vimuktāḥ sarva saṃkaraiḥ sruc bhāṇḍa paramāḥ nityam tretāgni śaraṇāḥ sadā brahma lokam mahā puṇyam soma lokam ca śāśvatam gacchanti munayaḥ siddhāḥ ṛṣi dharma vyapāśrayāt eṣa dharmaḥ mayā devi vānaprastha āśritaḥ śubhaḥ vistareṇa artha saṃpannaḥ yathāsthūlam udāhṛtaḥ siddhi vādeṣu saṃsiddhāḥ tathā vana nivāsinaḥ svairiṇaḥ dāra saṃyuktāḥ teṣām dharmaḥ katham smṛ svairiṇaḥ tāpasāḥ devi sarve dāra vihāriṇaḥ teṣām mauṇḍyam kaṣāyaḥ ca vāsa rātriḥ ca kāraṇam tri kālam abhiṣekaḥ ca hotram tu ṛṣi kṛtam mahat ye ca daṃpati dharmāṇaḥ sva dāra niyata indriyāḥ caranti vidhi dṛṣṭam tat ṛtu kāla abhigāminaḥ teṣām ṛṣi kṛtaḥ dharmaḥ dharmiṇām upapadyate na kāmakārāt kāmaḥ anyaḥ saṃsevyaḥ dharma darśibhiḥ sarva bhūteṣu yaḥ samyak dadāti abhaya dakṣiṇām hiṃsā roṣa vimukta ātmā sa vai dharmeṇa yujyate sarva bhūta anukampī yaḥ sarva bhūta ārjava vrataḥ sarva vedeṣu vā snānam sarva bhūteṣu ca ārjavam ubhe ete same syātām ārjavam vā viśiṣyate vyapeta tandraḥ dharma ātmā śakyā sat patham āśritaḥ āśrama abhiratāḥ deva tāpasāḥ ye tapodhanāḥ rājānaḥ rāja putrāḥ ca nirdhanāḥ vā mahā dhanāḥ nityam sthānam upāgamya divya candana rūṣitāḥ etam mama saṃśayam deva tapaḥ caryā gatam śubham śaṃsa sarvam aśeṣeṇa tryakṣa tripura nāśana upavāsa vrataiḥ dāntāḥ ahiṃsrāḥ satya vādinaḥ maṇḍūkayoga śayanaḥ yathāsthānam yathāvidhi dīkṣām carati dharma ātmā sa nāgaiḥ saha modate śaṣpam mṛga mukha utsṛṣṭam yaḥ mṛgaiḥ saha sevate śaivālam śīrṇa parṇam vā tat vrataḥ yaḥ niṣevate vāyubhakṣaḥ ambu bhakṣaḥ vā phala mūla aśanaḥ api vā yakṣeṣu
