aiśvaryam ādhāya modate apsarasām gaṇaiḥ agni yoga vahaḥ grīṣme vidhi dṛṣṭena karmaṇā cīrtvā dvādaśa varṣāṇi rājā bhavati pārthivaḥ āhāra niyamam kṛtvā muniḥ dvādaśa vārṣikam marum saṃsādhya yatnena rājā bhavati pārthivaḥ sthaṇḍile śuddham ākāśam parigṛhya samantataḥ praviśya ca mudā yuktaḥ dīkṣām dvādaśa vārṣikīm sthaṇḍilasya phalāni āhuḥ yānāni śayanāni ca gṛhāni ca mahārhāni candra śubhrāṇi bhāmini ātmānam upajīvan yaḥ niyataḥ niyata aśanaḥ deham vā anaśane tyaktvā sa svargam samupāśnute ātmānam upajīvan yaḥ dīkṣām dvādaśa vārṣikīm tyaktvā mahā arṇave deham vāruṇam lokam aśnute ātmānam upajīvan yaḥ dīkṣām dvādaśa vārṣikīm sādhayitvā ātmanā ātmānam nirdvaṃdvaḥ niṣparigrahaḥ cīrtvā dvādaśa varṣāṇi dīkṣām ekām manaḥ gatām ātmānam upajīvan yaḥ dīkṣām dvādaśa vārṣikīm yaḥ tu devi yathānyāyam dīkṣitaḥ niyataḥ dvijaḥ ātmani ātmānam ādhāya nirdvaṃdvaḥ niṣparigrahaḥ cīrtvā dvādaśa varṣāṇi dīkṣām ekām manaḥ gatām araṇī sahitam skandhe baddhvā gacchati anāvṛtaḥ vīrādhvānam anāḥ nityam vīrāsana rataḥ tathā vīra sthāyī ca satatam sa vīra gatim āpnuyāt divya puṣpa samākīrṇaḥ divya candana bhūṣitaḥ sattva sthaḥ sarvam utsṛjya dīkṣitaḥ niyataḥ śuciḥ vīrādhvānam prapadyet yaḥ tasya lokāḥ sanātanāḥ śakra loka gataḥ śrīmān modate ca nirāmayaḥ cāturvarṇyam bhagavatā pūrvam sṛṣṭam svayambhuvā kena vā karmaṇā vipraḥ śūdra yonau prajāyate kṣatriyaḥ śūdra tām eti kena vā karmaṇā vibho trayaḥ varṇāḥ prakṛtyā iha katham brāhmaṇyam āpnuyuḥ brāhmaṇyam devi duṣprāpam nisargāt brāhmaṇaḥ śubhe kṣatriyaḥ vaiśya śūdrau vā nisargāt iti mama matiḥ karmaṇā duṣkṛtena iha sthānāt bhraśyati vai dvijaḥ jyeṣṭham varṇam anuprāpya tasmāt rakṣeta vai dvijaḥ brāhmaṇyāt sa paribhraṣṭaḥ kṣatra yonau prajāyate brāhmaṇyam durlabham prāpya karoti alpa matiḥ sadā sa dvijaḥ vaiśya tām eti vaiśyaḥ vā śūdra tām iyāt tatra asau nirayam prāptaḥ varṇa bhraṣṭaḥ bahiṣkṛtaḥ brahma loka paribhraṣṭaḥ śūdraḥ samupajāyate kṣatriyaḥ vā mahābhāge vaiśyaḥ vā dharma cāriṇi svāni karmāṇi apāhāya śūdra karmāṇi sevate sva sthānāt sa paribhraṣṭaḥ varṇa saṃkara tām gataḥ brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vaiśyaḥ śūdra tvam yāti tādṛśaḥ yaḥ tu śuddhaḥ svadharmeṇa jñāna vijñānavān śuciḥ idam ca eva aparam devi brahmanā samudīritam ugra annam garhitam devi gaṇānnam śrāddha sūtakam ghuṣṭānnam na eva bhoktavyam śūdra annam na eva karhi cit śūdra annam garhitam devi deva devaiḥ mahātmabhiḥ pitāmaha mukha utsṛṣṭam pramāṇam iti mama matiḥ śūdra annena avaśeṣeṇa jaṭhare yaḥ mriyeta vai āhitāgniḥ tathā yajvā sa śūdra gati bhāj bhavet tena śūdra anna śeṣeṇa brahma sthānāt apākṛtaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ śūdra tām eti na asti tatra vicāraṇā yasya annena avaśeṣeṇa jaṭhare yaḥ mriyeta vai tām tām yonim vrajet vipraḥ yasya annam upajīvati brāhmaṇa tvam śubham prāpya durlabham yaḥ avamanyate abhojya annāni ca aśnāti sa dvija tvāt pateta vai svādhyāya varjitaḥ pāpaḥ lubdhaḥ naikṛtikaḥ śaṭhaḥ avratī vṛṣalī bhartā kuṇḍāśī soma vikrayī gurutalpī guru dveṣī guru kutsā ratiḥ ca yaḥ śūdraḥ brāhmaṇa tām gacchet vaiśyaḥ kṣatriya tām vrajet śūdra karmāṇi sarvāṇi yathānyāyam yathāvidhi śuśrūṣām paricaryām ca jyeṣṭhe varṇe prayatnāt kuryāt avimanāḥ śūdraḥ satatam sat pathe sthitaḥ ṛtu kāla abhigāmī ca niyataḥ niyata aśanaḥ caukṣaḥ caukṣa jana anveṣī śeṣa anna kṛta bhojanaḥ vṛthāmāṃsāni a bhuñjānaḥ śūdraḥ vaiśya tvam ṛcchati ṛta vāc an ahaṃvādī nirdvaṃdvaḥ śama kovidaḥ yajate nitya yajñaiḥ ca svādhyāya paramaḥ śuciḥ dāntaḥ brāhmaṇa satkartā sarva varṇa bubhūṣakaḥ gṛhastha vratam ātiṣṭhan dvi kāla kṛta bhojanaḥ śeṣa āśī vijita āhāraḥ niṣkāmaḥ nirahaṃvadaḥ agnihotram upāsan ca juhvānaḥ ca yathāvidhi sarva ātithyam upātiṣṭhan śeṣa anna kṛta bhojanaḥ sa vaiśyaḥ kṣatriyaḥ jātaḥ janma prabhṛti saṃskṛtaḥ dadāti yajate yajñaiḥ saṃskṛtaiḥ āpta dakṣiṇaiḥ adhīte svargam anvicchan tretāgni śaraṇaḥ sadā dharma daṇḍaḥ na nirdaṇḍaḥ dharma kārya anuśāsakaḥ yantritaḥ kārya karaṇe ṣaḍbhāga kṛta lakṣaṇaḥ ṛtu kāle tu dharma ātmā patnīm seveta nityadā sarva upavāsī niyataḥ svādhyāya paramaḥ śuciḥ barhiṣka antarite nityam śayānaḥ agni gṛhe sadā sarva ātithyam trivargasya kurvāṇaḥ su manāḥ sadā śūdrāṇām ca anna kāmānām nityam siddham iti bruvan sva arthāt vā yadi vā kāmāt na kim cit upalakṣayet pitṛ deva atithi kṛte sādhanam kurute ca yaḥ go brāhmaṇa hita arthāya raṇe ca abhimukhaḥ hataḥ jñāna vijñāna saṃpannaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ vedapāragaḥ śūdraḥ api āgama saṃpannaḥ dvijaḥ bhavati saṃskṛtaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ vā api asat vṛttaḥ sarva saṃkara bhojanaḥ brāhmaṇyam puṇyam utsṛjya śūdraḥ bhavati tādṛśaḥ svabhāva karma ca śubham yatra śūdre api tiṣṭhati na yoniḥ na api saṃskāraḥ na śrutam na ca saṃnatiḥ kāraṇāni dvija tvasya vṛttam eva tu kāraṇam vṛtte sthitaḥ ca suśroṇi brāhmaṇa tvam nigacchati brāhmaḥ svabhāvaḥ kalyāṇi samaḥ sarvatra me matiḥ ete yoni phalāḥ devi sthāna bhāga nidarśakāḥ svayam ca vara dena uktāḥ brahmaṇā sṛjatā prajāḥ yat tatra bījam vapati sā kṛṣiḥ pāralaukikī mita āśinā sadā bhāvyam sat patha ālambinā sadā saṃhitā dhyāyinā bhāvyam gṛhe vai gṛhamedhinā nityam svādhyāya yuktena dāna adhyayana jīvinā āhitāgniḥ adhīyānaḥ brahma bhūyāya kalpate brāhmaṇyam eva saṃprāpya rakṣitavyam yata ātmabhiḥ etat te sarvam ākhyātam yathā śūdraḥ bhavet dvijaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ vā cyutaḥ dharmāt yathā śūdra tvam āpnute dharma adharme nṛṇām deva brūhi mama saṃśayam vibho karmaṇā manasā vācā trividham hi naraḥ sadā kena śīlena vā deva karmaṇā kīdṛśena vā samācāraiḥ guṇaiḥ vākyaiḥ svargam yānti iha mānavāḥ sarva prāṇi hitaḥ praśnaḥ śrūyatām buddhi vardhanaḥ na adharmeṇa na dharmeṇa badhyante chinna saṃśayāḥ pralaya utpatti tattva jñāḥ sarva jñāḥ sama darśiṇaḥ vīta rāgāḥ vimucyante puruṣāḥ sarva bandhanaiḥ karmaṇā manasā vācā ye na hiṃsanti kim cana prāṇa atipātāt viratāḥ śīlavantaḥ dayā anvitāḥ sarva bhūta dayāvantaḥ viśvāsyāḥ sarva jantuṣu tyakta hiṃsā samācārāḥ te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ para dāreṣu vartante te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ stainyāt nivṛttāḥ satatam saṃtuṣṭāḥ sva dhanena ca svabhāgyāni upajīvanti te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ sva dāra niratāḥ ye ca ṛtu kāla abhigāminaḥ a grāmya sukha bhogāḥ ca te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ paradāreṣu ye nityam cāritra āvṛta locanāḥ yata indriyāḥ śīla pare te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ eṣa deva kṛtaḥ mārgaḥ sevitavyaḥ sadā naraiḥ a kaṣāya kṛtaḥ ca eva mārgaḥ sevyaḥ sadā budhaiḥ dāna dharma tapaḥ yuktaḥ śīla śauca dayā ātmakaḥ ātma hetoḥ para arthe vā narma hāsya āśrayāt tathā ye mṛṣā na vadanti iha te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ anṛtam ye na bhāṣante te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ ślakṣṇām vāṇīm nirābādhām madhurām pāpa varjitām svāgatena abhibhāṣante te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ kaṭukām ye na bhāṣante paruṣām niṣṭhurām giram a paiśunya ratāḥ santaḥ te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ piśunām ye na bhāṣante mitra bheda karīm giram ṛtām maitrīm prabhāṣante te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ varjayanti sadā sūcyam para droham ca mānavāḥ sarva bhūta samāḥ dāntāḥ te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ śaṭha pralāpāt viratāḥ viruddha parivarjakāḥ na kopāt vyāharante ye vācam hṛdaya dāraṇīm sāntvam vadanti kruddhāḥ api te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ eṣa vāṇī kṛtaḥ devi dharmaḥ sevyaḥ sadā naraiḥ śubhaḥ satya guṇaḥ nityam varjanīyāḥ mṛṣā budhaiḥ manasā badhyate yena karmaṇā puruṣaḥ sadā mānasena iha dharmeṇa saṃyuktāḥ puruṣāḥ sadā svargam gacchanti kalyāṇe tat me kīrtayataḥ śṛṇu duṣpraṇītena manasā duṣpraṇītatara ākṛtiḥ badhyate mānavaḥ yena śṛṇu ca anyat śubha ānane araṇye vijane nyastam para svam vīkṣya ye narāḥ manasā api na hiṃsanti te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ tathā eva para dārān ye kāma vṛttān rahaḥ gatān manasā api na hiṃsanti te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ śatrum mitram ca ye nityam tulyena manasā narāḥ bhajanti maitrāḥ saṃgamya te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ śrutavantaḥ dayāvantaḥ śucayaḥ satya saṃgarāḥ svaiḥ arthaiḥ parisaṃtuṣṭāḥ te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ a vairāḥ ye tu anāyāsāḥ maitra citta parāḥ sadā śraddhāvantaḥ dayāvantaḥ cokṣāḥ cokṣa jana priyāḥ śubhānām aśubhānām ca karmaṇām phala saṃcaye vipāka jñāḥ ca ye devi te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ nyāya upetāḥ guṇa upetāḥ deva dvija parāḥ sadā samatām samanuprāptāḥ te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ mahān me saṃśayaḥ kaḥ cit martyān prati maheśvara tasmāt tam naipuṇena adya mama ākhyātum tvam arhasi kena āyuḥ labhate dīrgham karmaṇā puruṣaḥ prabho kṣīṇa āyuḥ kena bhū karmaṇā bhuvi mānavaḥ akulīnāḥ tathā ca anye kulīnāḥ ca tathā apare durdarśāḥ ke cit ābhānti narāḥ kāṣṭha mayāḥ iva priya darśāḥ tathā ca anye darśanāt eva mānavāḥ duṣprajñāḥ ke cit ābhānti ke cit ābhānti paṇḍitāḥ mahā prajñāḥ tathā eva anye jñāna vijñāna darśinaḥ alpa ābādhāḥ tathā ke cit mahā bādhāḥ tathā apare dṛśyante puruṣāḥ deva tat me śaṃsitum arhasi prāṇa atipātī yaḥ raudraḥ daṇḍa hasta udyataḥ tathā nityam udyata daṇḍaḥ ca hanti bhūta gaṇān naraḥ nirdayaḥ sarva bhūtānām nityam udvega kārakaḥ api kīṭa pipīlānām aśaraṇyaḥ su nirghṛṇaḥ viparītaḥ tu dharma ātmā rūpavān abhijāyate nirayam yāti hiṃsā ātmā yāti svargam ahiṃsakaḥ yātanām niraye raudrām sa kṛcchrām labhate naraḥ mānuṣyam labhate ca api hīna āyūḥ tatra jāyate pāpena karmaṇā devi baddhaḥ hiṃsā ratiḥ naraḥ apriyaḥ sarva bhūtānām hīna āyuḥ upajāyate yaḥ tu śukla abhijātīyaḥ prāṇi ghāta vivarjakaḥ nikṣipta daṇḍaḥ nirdaṇḍaḥ na hinasti kadā cana īdṛśaḥ puruṣa utkarṣaḥ devi deva tvam aśnute upapannān sukhān bhogān upāśnāti mudā yutaḥ evam dīrgha āyuṣām mārgaḥ su vṛttānām su karmaṇām prāṇi hiṃsā vimokṣeṇa brahmaṇā samudīritaḥ kiṃśīlāḥ kiṃsamācārāḥ puruṣāḥ kaiḥ ca karmabhiḥ dātā brāhmaṇa satkartā dīna andha kṛpaṇa ādiṣu bhakṣya bhojya anna pānānām vāsasām ca pradāyakaḥ pratiśrayān sabhāḥ kūpān prapāḥ puṣkariṇīḥ tathā āsanam śayanam yānam dhanam ratnam gṛhān tathā sasya jātāni sarvāṇi gāḥ kṣetrāṇi atha yoṣitaḥ tatra uṣya su ciram kālam bhuktvā bhogān anuttamān tasmāt svargāt cyutaḥ lokāt mānuṣeṣu upajāyate tatra kāma guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ samupetaḥ mudā yutaḥ mahā bhogaḥ mahā kośaḥ dhanī bhavati mānavaḥ ete devi mahā bhogāḥ prāṇinaḥ dāna śīlinaḥ brahmaṇā vai purā proktāḥ sarvasya priya darśanāḥ apare mānavāḥ devi pradāna kṛpaṇāḥ dvijaiḥ dīna andha kṛpaṇān dṛṣṭvā bhikṣukān atithīn api yācyamānāḥ nivartante jihvā lobha samanvitāḥ na dhanāni na vāsāṃsi na bhogān na ca kāñcanam apravṛttāḥ tu ye lubdhāḥ nāstikāḥ dāna varjitāḥ evaṃbhūtāḥ narāḥ devi nirayam yānti abuddhayaḥ te ced manuṣya tām yānti yadā kālasya paryayāt kṣudh pipāsā parītāḥ ca sarva bhoga bahiṣkṛtāḥ nirāśāḥ sarva bhogebhyaḥ jīvanti adhama jīvikām apare stambhinaḥ nityam māninaḥ pāpataḥ ratāḥ gurum ca abhigatam premṇā guru vat na bubhūṣate saṃmānyān ca avamanyante vṛddhān paribhavanti ca śvapāka pulkasa ādīnām kutsitānām acetasām kuleṣu teṣu jāyante guru vṛddha apacāyinaḥ na stambhī na ca mānī yaḥ devatā dvija pūjakaḥ a dveṣī su mukhaḥ ślakṣṇaḥ snigdha vāṇī pradaḥ sadā svāgatena eva sarveṣām bhūtānām avihiṃsakaḥ tatas mānuṣa tām prāpya viśiṣṭa kula jaḥ bhavet saṃmataḥ sarva bhūtānām sarva loka namaskṛtaḥ udātta kula jātīyaḥ udātta abhijanaḥ sadā eṣa dharmaḥ mayā proktaḥ vidhātrā svayam īritaḥ hastābhyām yadi vā padbhyām rajjvā daṇḍena vā punar loṣṭaiḥ stambhaiḥ upāyaiḥ vā jantūn bādhati śobhane upakrāmati jantūn ca udvega jananaḥ sadā evaṃśīla samācāraḥ nirayam pratipadyate loka dviṣ adhamaḥ puṃsām svayam karma kṛ phalaiḥ eṣa devi manuṣyeṣu boddhavyaḥ jñāti bandhuṣu aparaḥ sarva bhūtāni dayāvān anupaśyati na rajjvā na ca daṇḍena na loṣṭaiḥ na āyudhena ca udvejayati bhūtāni ślakṣṇa karmā dayā paraḥ evaṃśīla samācāraḥ svarge samupajāyate sa ced karma kṣayāt martyaḥ manuṣyeṣu upajāyate alpa ābādhaḥ nirītīkaḥ sa jātaḥ sukham edhate sukha bhāgī nirāyāsaḥ nirudvegaḥ sadā naraḥ eṣa devi satām mārgaḥ bādhā yatra na vidyate ime manuṣyāḥ dṛśyante ūha apoha viśāradāḥ jñāna vijñāna saṃpannāḥ prajñāvantaḥ artha kovidāḥ duṣprajñāḥ ca apare deva jñāna vijñāna varjitāḥ alpa prajñaḥ virūpākṣa katham bhavati mānavaḥ jāti andhāḥ ca apare deva roga ārtāḥ ca apare tathā narāḥ klībāḥ ca dṛśyante kāraṇam brūhi tatra vai brāhmaṇān veda viduṣaḥ siddhān dharma vidaḥ tathā paripṛcchanti ahar ahar kuśala akuśalam tathā varjayanti aśubham karma sevamānāḥ śubham tathā sa ced mānuṣa tām yāti medhāvī tatra jāyate śrutam prajñā anugam ca asya kalyāṇam upajāyate paradāreṣu ye mūḍhāḥ cakṣuḥ duṣṭam prayuñjate roga ārtāḥ te bhavanti iha narāḥ duṣkṛta karmiṇaḥ ye tu mūḍhāḥ durācārāḥ viyonau maithune ratāḥ puruṣeṣu su duṣprajñāḥ klība tvam upayānti te prakīrṇa maithunāḥ ye ca klībāḥ jāyanti te narāḥ śreyāṃsam mārgam ātiṣṭhan sadā yaḥ pṛcchate dvijān dharma anveṣī guṇa ākāṅkṣī sa svargam samupāśnute medhāvī dhāraṇā yuktaḥ prājñaḥ tatra abhijāyate eṣa devi satām dharmaḥ mantavyaḥ bhūti kārakaḥ nṛṇām hita arthāya tava mayā vai samudāhṛtaḥ apare su alpa vijñānāḥ dharma vidveṣiṇaḥ narāḥ vratavantaḥ narāḥ ke cit śraddhā dama parāyaṇāḥ avratāḥ bhraṣṭa niyamāḥ tathā anye rākṣasa upamāḥ āgamāt loka dharmāṇām maryādāḥ pūrva nirmitāḥ prāmāṇyena anuvartante dṛśyante hi dṛḍha vratāḥ avratāḥ naṣṭa maryādāḥ te proktāḥ brahmarākṣasāḥ te ced kāla kṛta udyogāt saṃbhavanti iha mānuṣāḥ nirhomāḥ nirvaṣaṭkārāḥ te bhavanti nara adhamāḥ eṣa devi mayā sarvaḥ saṃśaya chedanāya te kuśala akuśalaḥ nṝṇām vyākhyātaḥ dharma sāgaraḥ uvāca evam uktvā mahādevaḥ śrotu kāmaḥ svayam prabhuḥ anukūlām priyām bhāryām pārśva sthām samabhāṣata pṛcchāmi tvām varārohe pṛṣṭā vada mama īpsitam sāvitrī brahmaṇaḥ sādhvī kauśikasya śacī satī mārtaṇḍa jasya dhūmorṇā ṛddhiḥ vaiśravaṇasya ca rohiṇī śaśinaḥ sādhvī svāhā ca eva vibhāvasoḥ aditiḥ kaśyapasya atha sarvāḥ tāḥ pati devatāḥ pṛṣṭāḥ ca upāsitāḥ ca eva tāḥ tvayā devi nityaśas strī dharmam śrotum icchāmi tvayā udāhṛtam āditas sahadharma carī me tvam sama śīlā sama vratā samāna sāra vīryā ca tapaḥ tīvram kṛtam ca te tvayā hi uktaḥ viśeṣeṇa pramāṇa tvam upaiṣyati guṇavān sa bhaviṣyati striyaḥ ca eva viśeṣeṇa strī janasya gatiḥ sadā gauḥ gām gacchati suśroṇi lokeṣu eṣā sthitiḥ sadā mama ca ardham śarīrasya mama ca ardhāt viniḥsṛtā sura kārya karī ca tvam loka saṃtāna kāriṇī tava sarvaḥ su viditaḥ strī dharmaḥ śāśvataḥ śubhe tasmāt aśeṣatas brūhi strī dharmam vistareṇa me etābhiḥ saha saṃmantrya pravakṣyāmi anupūrvaśas strī ca bhūteśa satatam striyam eva anudhāvati mayā saṃmānitāḥ ca eva bhaviṣyanti sarit varāḥ eṣā sarasvatī puṇyā nadīnām uttamā nadī prathamā sarva saritām nadī sāgara gāminī vipāśā ca vitastā ca candrabhāgā irāvatī śatadruḥ devikā sindhuḥ kauśikī gomatī tathā tathā devanadī ca iyam sarva tīrtha abhisaṃvṛtā gaganāt gām gatāḥ devī gaṅgā sarva sarit varā smita pūrvam iva ābhāṣya sarvāḥ tāḥ saritaḥ tadā strī dharma kuśalāḥ tāḥ vai gaṅgā ādyāḥ saritām varāḥ ayam bhagavatā dattaḥ praśnaḥ strī dharma saṃśritaḥ tam tu saṃmantrya yuṣmābhiḥ vaktum icchāmi śaṃkare na ca eka sādhyam paśyāmi vijñānam bhuvi kasya cit uvāca evam sarvāḥ sarit śreṣṭha pṛṣṭāḥ puṇyatamāḥ śiva tatas devanadī gaṅgā niyuktā pratipūjya tām bahvībhiḥ buddhibhiḥ sphītā strī dharma jñā śuci smitā śailarājasutām devīm puṇyā pāpa apahām śivām buddhyā vinaya saṃpannā sarva jñāna viśāradā sa smitam bahu buddhi āḍhyā gaṅgā vacanam abravīt dhanyāḥ smaḥ anugṛhītāḥ smaḥ devi dharma parāyaṇā yā tvam sarva jagat mānyā nadīḥ mānayase anaghe nūnam janam aduṣṭa ātmā paṇḍita ākhyām sa gacchati jñāna vijñāna saṃpannān ūha apoha viśāradān uvāca tatas sā ārādhitā devī gaṅgayā bahubhiḥ guṇaiḥ prāha sarvam aśeṣeṇa strī dharmam surasundarī strī dharmaḥ pūrva eva ayam vivāha bandhu kṛ su svabhāvā su vacanā su vṛttā sukha darśanā an anya cittā su mukhā bhartuḥ sā dharma cāriṇī daṃpatyoḥ eṣa vai dharmaḥ sahadharma kṛtaḥ śubhaḥ deva vat satatam sādhvī yā bhartāram prapaśyati śuśrūṣām paricāram ca deva vat yā karoti ca na anya bhāvā hi avimanāḥ suvratā sukha darśanā putra vaktram iva abhīkṣṇam bhartuḥ vadanam īkṣate yā sādhuḥ niyata ācārā sā bhavet dharma cāriṇī śrutvā daṃpati dharmam vai sahadharma kṛtam śubham an anya cittā su mukhā bhartuḥ sā dharma cāriṇī paruṣāṇi api ca uktā yā dṛṣṭā vā krūra cakṣuṣā su prasanna mukhī bhartuḥ yā nārī sā pativratā na candra sūryau na tarum puṃnāmnaḥ yā nirīkṣate bhartṛ varjam vara ārohā sā bhavet dharma cāriṇī patim putram iva upāste sā nārī dharma bhāginī yā nārī prayatā dakṣā yā nārī putriṇī bhavet pati priyā pati prāṇā sā nārī dharma bhāginī śuśrūṣām paricaryām ca karoti avimanas sadā su pratītā vinītā ca sā nārī dharma bhāginī spṛhā yasyāḥ yathā patau sā nārī dharma bhāginī kalya utthāna ratā nityam guru śuśrūṣaṇe ratā su saṃmṛṣṭa kṣayā ca eva go śakṛt kṛta lepanā agni kārya parā nityam sadā puṣpa bali pradā devatā atithi bhṛtyānām nirupya patinā saha śeṣa annam upabhuñjānāḥ yathānyāyam yathāvidhi tuṣṭa puṣṭa janā nityam nārī dharmeṇa yujyate śvaśrū śvaśurayoḥ pādau toṣayantī guṇa anvitā mātā pitṛ parā nityam yā nārī sā tapodhanā brāhmaṇān durbala anāthān dīna andha kṛpaṇān tathā bibharti annena yā nārī sā pati vrata bhāginī yā nārī bhartṛ paramā bhavet bhartṛ vratā śivā patiḥ hi devaḥ nārīṇām patiḥ bandhuḥ patiḥ gatiḥ patyā samā gatiḥ na asti daivatam vā yathā patiḥ yadi akāryam adharmam vā yadi vā prāṇa nāśanam āpannaḥ ripu saṃsthaḥ vā brahma śāpa arditaḥ api vā āpad dharmān anuprekṣya tat kāryam aviśaṅkayā yā tu evaṃbhāvinī nārī sā bhavet dharma bhāginī uvāca iti uktaḥ sa tu deveśaḥ pratipūjya gireḥ sutām tatas yayuḥ bhūta gaṇāḥ saritaḥ ca yathāgatam vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ anuśāsya śubhaiḥ vākyaiḥ bhīṣmaḥ tu āha mahāmatim prītyā punar sa śuśrūṣuḥ vacanam yat yudhiṣṭhire pitāmahaḥ me viprarṣe bhīṣmam kāla vaśam gatam kim apṛcchat tadā rājā sarvasāmāsikam hitam vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ tat me vada mahā prājña śrotum kautūhalam hi me bhūyas eva mahā rāja śṛṇu dharmasamuccayam yat apṛcchat tadā rājā kuntī putraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ śara talpa gatam bhīṣmam sarva pārthiva saṃnidhau yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ajātaśatruḥ prīta ātmā punar eva abhyabhāṣata pitāmaha mahā prājña sarva śāstra viśārada parāvara jña bhūtānām dayāvān sarva jantuṣu tvādṛśaḥ durlabhaḥ loke sāṃpratam jñāna darśanaḥ ayam sa kālaḥ saṃprāptaḥ durlabhaḥ jñāti bāndhavaiḥ śāstā nu na asti naḥ kaḥ cit tvat ṛte puruṣa ṛṣabha āścaryam paramam vākyam śrotum icchāmi bhārata ayam nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān sarva pārthiva saṃnidhau asya eva tu samakṣam naḥ pārthivānām tathā eva ca itivṛttam purāṇam ca śrotṝṇām paramam hitam vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ prapiban iva tam dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmaḥ vacanam abravīt śṛṇu rājan purā vṛttam itihāsam purātanam etāvat uktvā gāṅgeyaḥ praṇamya śirasā harim dharmarājam samīkṣya idam punar vaktum samārabhat ayam nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān putra artham vrata kāṅkṣayā dīkṣitaḥ abhūt mahābāhuḥ purā dvādaśa vārṣikam dīkṣitam keśavam draṣṭum abhijagmuḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ sevitum ca mahātmānaḥ prīyamāṇāḥ janārdanam nāradaḥ parvataḥ ca eva kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ tathā devalaḥ kāśyapaḥ ca eva hastikāśyapaḥ eva ca apare api tapaḥ siddhāḥ satya vrata parāyaṇāḥ keśavaḥ tān abhigatān prītyā saṃpratigṛhya ca teṣām atithi satkāram pūjana artham kula ucitam upaviṣṭeṣu sarveṣu viṣṭareṣu tadā anagha viśvasteṣu hi tuṣṭeṣu keśava arcanayā punar parasparam kathāḥ divyāḥ prāvartanta manoramāḥ viṣṇoḥ nārāyaṇasya eva prasādāt kathayāmi tāḥ yaḥ ca govṛṣabhāṅkasya prabhāvaḥ abhūt mahātmanaḥ yatra devī mahādevam apṛcchat saṃśayān purā kathayām āsa śarvaḥ tān devyāḥ priya cikīrṣayā umāpatyoḥ ca saṃvādam śṛṇu tāta manoramam varṇa āśramāṇām dharmaḥ ca tatra tāta samāhitaḥ ṛṣi dharmaḥ ca nikhilaḥ rāja dharmaḥ ca puṣkalaḥ prāṇamokṣa vidhiḥ ca eva tīrtha caryā ca puṣkalā strī dharmaḥ ca svayam devyāḥ devadevāya bhāṣitaḥ evamādi śubham sarvam tatra tāta samāhitam rudrāṇyāḥ saṃśaya praśnaḥ yatra tāta pravartate dhanyam yaśasyam āyuṣyam dharmyam ca paramam hitam puṣṭi yogam idam divyam kathyamānam mayā śṛṇu itihāsam imam divyam pavitram paramam śubham sāyam prātar sadā samyak śrotavyam ca bubhūṣatā tatas nārāyaṇaḥ devaḥ saṃkliṣṭaḥ vrata caryayā vahniḥ viniḥsṛtaḥ vaktrāt kṛṣṇasya adbhuta darśanaḥ agninā tena mahatā niḥsṛtena mukhāt vibhoḥ paśyatām eva sarveṣām dagdhaḥ eva naga uttamaḥ mṛga pakṣi samākīrṇaḥ śvāpadaiḥ abhisaṃkulaḥ vṛkṣa gulma latā ākīrṇaḥ mathitaḥ dīna darśanaḥ punar sa dṛṣṭa mātreṇa hariṇā saumya cetasā matta vāraṇa saṃyuktaḥ nānā pakṣi gaṇaiḥ yutaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭa romāṇaḥ sarve muni gaṇāḥ tadā vismitāḥ parama āyastāḥ sādhvasa ākula locanāḥ tān samīkṣya eva madhuram babhāṣe puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ etam me saṃśayam sarve yāthātathyam aninditāḥ ṛṣayaḥ vaktum arhanti niścayena artha kovidāḥ keśavasya vacaḥ śrutvā tuṣṭuvuḥ muni puṃgavāḥ bhavān sṛjati vai lokān bhavān saṃharati prajāḥ bhavān śītam bhavān uṣṇam bhavān satyam bhavān kratuḥ nityam hita artham lokānām bhavadbhiḥ kriyate tapaḥ tasmāt loka hitam guhyam śrūyatām kathayāmi vaḥ asuraḥ sāṃpratam kaḥ cit ahitaḥ loka nāśanaḥ babhūva sa mayā vadhyaḥ lokānām hita kāmyayā putreṇa me vadhaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tasya vai muni puṃgavāḥ tad artham putram eva aham sisṛkṣuḥ vanam āgataḥ ātmanaḥ sadṛśam putram aham janayitum vrataiḥ atha ātmā mama deha sthaḥ saḥ agniḥ bhūtvā viniḥsṛtaḥ viniḥsṛtya gataḥ draṣṭum kṣaṇena ca pitāmaham anujñātaḥ ca tena eva punar āyāt mama antikam dṛṣṭvā nāśam gireḥ tasya saumya bhāva tayā mama punar sa dṛṣṭa mātreṇa giriḥ āsīt yathāpuram etat guhyam mayā tathyam kathitam vaḥ samāsatas ṛṣīṇām evam uktvā tu tān punar pratyabhāṣata bhavatām darśanāt eva prītiḥ abhyadhikā mama sarvatra gatimantaḥ ca jñāna vijñāna bhāvitāḥ gatāgata jñāḥ lokānām sarve nirdhūta kalmaṣāḥ tasmāt bhavadbhiḥ yat kim cit dṛṣṭam vā api atha vā śrutam yuṣmābhiḥ kathitam yat syāt tapasā bhāvitātmabhiḥ tat syāt amṛta saṃkāśam vāc madhu śravaṇe spṛhā rāga dveṣa viyuktānām satatam satya vādinām śraddheyam śravaṇīyam ca vacanam hi satām bhavet tat aham sat jana mukhāt niḥsṛtam jana saṃsadi kathayiṣyāmi aharahar buddhi dīpa karam nṛṇām vāc śalya vigatāḥ ca anye praśaṃsanti purātanam bhīṣmaḥ evam bruvati govinde śravaṇa artham mahā ṛṣayaḥ vāgbhiḥ sa añjali mālābhiḥ idam ūcuḥ janārdanam ayuktam asmān evam tvam vācā vara da bhāṣitum tvad śāsana mukhāḥ sarve tvad adhīna pariśramāḥ evam pūjayitum ca asmān na ca eva arhasi keśava evam uktaḥ hṛṣīkeśaḥ sa smitam ca idam abravīt aham mānuṣa yoni sthaḥ sāṃpratam muni puṃgavāḥ tasmāt mānuṣa vat vīryam mama jānīta suvratāḥ bhīṣmaḥ evam saṃcoditāḥ sarve keśavena mahātmanā ṛṣayaḥ ca anuvartante vāsudevasya śāsanam tatas tu ṛṣi gaṇāḥ sarve nāradam devadarśanam ṛṣiḥ ugra tapāḥ ca ayam keśavasya priyaḥ adhikam purāṇa jñaḥ ca vāgmī ca kāraṇaiḥ tam ca menire sarve tad arhaṇam kṛtvā nāradam vākyam abruvan dṛṣṭam vai yat tat āścaryam śrotṝṇām paramam priyam tattvam tvam aviśeṣeṇa hita artham sarvam āditas bhīṣmaḥ tadā saṃcoditaḥ sarvaiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ nāradaḥ tathā praṇamya śirasā viṣṇum sarva loka hite ratam samudvīkṣya hṛṣīkeśam vaktum eva upacakrame tatas nārāyaṇa suhṛd nāradaḥ vadatām varaḥ nāradaḥ śaṃkarasya umayā sārdham saṃvādam anvabhāṣata bhagavan tīrthayātrā artham tathā eva caratā mayā divyam adbhuta saṃkāśam dṛṣṭam haimavatam vanam nānā vṛkṣa latā yuktam nānā pakṣi gaṇaiḥ yutam nānā ratna samākīrṇam nānā bhāva samanvitam siddha cāraṇa saṃvāsam bhūta saṃghaiḥ niṣevitam variṣṭha apsarasā ākīrṇam nānā gandharva saṃkulam mṛdaṅga muraja udghuṣṭam śaṅkha vīṇā abhināditam nānā rūpaiḥ virūpaiḥ ca bhīma rūpaiḥ bhayānakaiḥ evam bahuvidha ākāraiḥ bhūta saṃghaiḥ bhṛśa ākulam nānadyamānam bahudhā hara pāriṣadaiḥ bhṛśam ghora rūpam su durdarśam rakṣaḥ gaṇa śataiḥ vṛtam samājam tad vane dṛṣṭam mayā bhūtapateḥ purā ṣaṭpadaiḥ upagītam ca prathame māsi mādhave utkrośat krauñca kuraraiḥ sārasaiḥ jīvajīvakaiḥ mattābhiḥ parapuṣṭābhiḥ kūjantībhiḥ samākulam uttama utsava saṃkāśam bhīma rūpataram tatas mārtāṇḍa raśmi saṃcārāḥ viśvedeva gaṇāḥ tathā tathā nāgāḥ tathā ādityāḥ lokapālāḥ hutāśanāḥ vātāḥ ca sarve vāyanti divya puṣpa samākulāḥ kirantaḥ sarva puṣpāṇi kirantaḥ adbhuta darśanāḥ paryaṅke iva babhrāje upaviṣṭaḥ mahā dyutiḥ vyāla yajñopavītaḥ ca lohitāntra vibhūṣitaḥ hari śmaśru jaṭaḥ bhīmaḥ bhaya kartā suradviṣām bhaya ghnaḥ sarva bhūtānām bhaktānām abhayaṃkaraḥ ṛṣibhiḥ ca apsarobhiḥ ca sarvatas ca api śobhitaḥ mahā uraga samākīrṇam sarveṣām loma harṣaṇam tatra bhūtapatim devam āsīnam śikhara uttame ṛṣayaḥ bhūta saṃghāḥ ca praṇamya śirasā haram gīrbhiḥ parama śuddhābhiḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ ca maheśvaram ṛṣayaḥ vālakhilyāḥ ca tathā viprarṣayaḥ ca ye ayoni jāḥ yoni jāḥ ca tapaḥsiddhāḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ tatas tasmin kṣaṇe devī bhūta strī gaṇa sevitā hara tulya ambara dharā samāna vrata cāriṇī kāñcanam kalaśam gṛhya sarva tīrtha ambu pūritam puṣpa vṛṣṭyā abhivarṣantī divya gandha samāyutā sarit varābhiḥ sarvābhiḥ pṛṣṭhatas anugatā varā sevitum bhagavat pārśvam ājagāma śuci smitā manaḥ priyam cikīrṣantī krīḍā artham śaṃkara antike manoharābhyām pāṇibhyām hara netre pidhāya tu avekṣya hṛṣṭā sva gaṇān smayantī pṛṣṭhatas sthitā devyā ca andhīkṛte deve kaśmalam samapadyata nimīlite bhūtapatau naṣṭa candra arka tārakam niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkāram tamasā ca abhisaṃvṛtam viṣaṇṇam bhaya saṃtrastam jagant āsīt bhaya ākulam hāhākāraḥ tu ṛṣīṇām ca lokānām abhavat tadā tamas abhibhūte saṃbhrānte loke jīvita śaṅkite tṛtīyam ca asya saṃbhūtam lalāṭe netram āyatam dvādaśa āditya saṃkāśam lokān bhāsau abhāsayat paśyatām eva sarveṣām deva dānava rakṣasām tam dṛṣṭvā mathitam śailam śailaputrī sa viklavā pituḥ śamanam icchantī papāta bhuvi pādayoḥ tat dṛṣṭvā devadeveśaḥ devyāḥ duḥkham anuttamam dṛṣṭa mātraḥ bhagavatā saumya yuktena cetasā kṣaṇena himavant śailaḥ prakṛti sthaḥ abhavat punar hṛṣṭa puṣṭa vihaṃgaḥ ca praphulla druma kānanaḥ siddha cāraṇa saṃghaiḥ ca prīti yuktaiḥ samākulaḥ pitaram prakṛti stham tu dṛṣṭvā haimavatī bhṛśam devī vismaya saṃyuktā praṣṭu kāmā maheśvaram hita artham sarva lokānām prajānām hita kāmyayā devadevam mahādevī babhāṣa idam vacaḥ arthavat bhagavan devadeveśa śūlapāṇe mahā dyute kimartham devadeveśa lalāṭe asmin prakāśate ati sūrya agni saṃkāśam tṛtīyam netram āyatam punar sa dṛṣṭa mātraḥ tu prakṛti sthaḥ pitā mama nāradaḥ evam uktaḥ tayā devyā prīyamāṇaḥ abravīt bhavaḥ sthāne saṃśayitum devi dharma jñe priya bhāṣiṇi tvat ṛte mām hi vai praṣṭum na śakyam kena cit priye prakāśam yadi vā guhyam tvad priya artham bravīmi aham śṛṇu tat sarvam akhilam asyām saṃsadi bhāmini sarveṣām eva lokānām kūṭastham viddhi mām priye mad adhīnāḥ trayaḥ lokāḥ yathā viṣṇau tathā mayi sraṣṭā viṣṇuḥ aham goptā iti tat viddhi bhāmini tasmāt yadā mām spṛśati śubham vā yadi vā itarat netre me pihite devi krīḍana artham dṛḍha vrate tvad kṛte naṣṭa candra arkam jagant āsīt bhṛśa ākulam tṛtīyam locanam sṛṣṭam lokān saṃrakṣitum mayā asya eva tejasā akṣṇas me mathitaḥ ayam giriḥ śubha vṛkṣa gulma latā ākīrṇaḥ vyāla adhyuṣita kandaraḥ nāradaḥ kathitam saṃśaya sthānam nirviśaṅkā bhava priye kṣaṇajñā devadevasya śrotu kāmā priyam hitam dakṣiṇam ca mukham raudram kena ūrdhvam jaṭila āvṛtam yathādiśam mahādeva śrotum icchāmi kāraṇam maheśvaraḥ tayoḥ eva vināśāya nirmitā viśvakarmaṇā mṛga pakṣi gaṇānām ca sthāvarāṇām tathā eva ca sarvatas sāram uddhṛtya tilaśas loka pūjitā tilottamā iti vikhyātā apsarāḥ sā babhūva ha deva kāryam kariṣyantī hāva bhāva samanvitā sā tu paryantam āgamya rūpeṇa apratimā bhuvi mayā bahu matā ca iyam deva kāryam kariṣyati iti matvā tadā ca aham kurvantīm mām pradakṣiṇam aindram mukham idam pūrvam tapaḥ caryā param sadā dakṣiṇam me mukham divyam raudram saṃharati prajāḥ umā etat te sarvam ākhyātam kim bhūyas śrotum icchasi bhagavan śrotum icchāmi śūlapāṇe vara prada maheśvaraḥ kimartham nīla tā kaṇṭhe bhāti barha nibhā tava hanta te kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇu devi samāhitā purā yuga antare yatnāt amṛta artham sura asuraiḥ viṣam tatra samudbhūtam sarva loka vināśanam tat dṛṣṭvā vibudhāḥ sarve tadā vimanasaḥ abhavan grastam hi tat mayā devi lokānām hita kāraṇāt tad kṛtā nīla tā ca āsīt kaṇṭhe barhi nibhā śubhe tadā prabhṛti ca eva aham nīlakaṇṭhaḥ iti smṛtaḥ umā etat te sarvam ākhyātam kim bhūyas śrotum icchasi bahūnām āyudhānām tvam pinākam dhartum icchasi maheśvaraḥ śastra āgamam te vakṣyāmi śṛṇu dharmyam śuci smite yuga antare mahādevi kaṇvaḥ nāma mahā muniḥ dharamāṇaḥ ca tat sarvam tapaḥ caryām atha akarot tasmai brahmā varam dātum jagāma tapasā arcitaḥ dattvā tasmai varam devaḥ veṇum dṛṣṭvā tu acintayat loka kāryam samuddiśya veṇunā anena bhāmini viṣṇoḥ mama ca sāmarthyam jñātvā lokapitāmahaḥ dhanuṣī dve tadā prādāt viṣṇave ca mama eva ca pinākam nāma me cāpam śārṅgam nāma hareḥ dhanuḥ tṛtīyam avaśeṣeṇa gāṇḍīvam abhavat dhanuḥ umā ayam tu vṛṣabhaḥ kasmāt vāhana tvam upāgamat maheśvaraḥ eṣa me saṃśayaḥ deva tam me śaṃsitum arhasi ādisarge purā gāvaḥ śveta varṇāḥ śuci smite bala saṃhanana upetāḥ darpa yuktāḥ caranti tāḥ aham tu tapaḥ ātiṣṭhe tasmin kāle śubha ānane gāvaḥ me pārśvam āviśya darpa utsiktāḥ samantataḥ apacāreṇa ca etāsām manaḥ kṣobhaḥ abhavat mama tasmāt dagdhāḥ mayā gāvaḥ roṣa āviṣṭena cetasā anena vṛṣabheṇa aham śamitaḥ saṃprasādanaiḥ tadā prabhṛti śāntāḥ ca varṇa bheda tvam āgatāḥ śvetaḥ ayam vṛṣabhaḥ devi pūrva saṃskāra saṃyutaḥ umā prasannaḥ ca abhavam devi tadā gopati tām gataḥ bhagavant sarva bhūta īśa śūlapāṇe vṛṣadhvaja āvāseṣu vicitreṣu ramyeṣu ca śubheṣu ca satsu ca anyeṣu deśeṣu śmaśāne ramase katham keśa asthi kalile bhīme kapāla śata saṃkule sṛgāla gṛdhra saṃpūrṇe śava dhūma samākule maheśvaraḥ hanta te kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇu devi samāhitā āvāsa artham purā devi śuddha anveṣī śuci smite na adhyagaccham ciram kālam deśam śucitamam śubhe eṣa me abhiniveśaḥ abhūt tasmin kāle prajāḥ prati ākulam su mahat ghoram prādurāsīt samantataḥ saṃbhūtā bhūta sṛṣṭiḥ ca ghorā loka bhaya āvahā nānā varṇa virūpāḥ ca tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭrāḥ prahāriṇaḥ piśāca rakṣaḥ vadanāḥ prāṇinām prāṇa hāriṇaḥ evam loke kṣayam yāte prāṇi hīne pitāmahaḥ cintayan tad pratīkāram mām ca śaktam hi nigrahe evam jñātvā tadā brahmā tasmin karmaṇi ayojayat tasmāt saṃrakṣitāḥ devi bhūtebhyaḥ prāṇinaḥ bhayāt asmāt śmaśānāt medhyam tu na asti kim cit anindite niḥsaṃpātam manuṣyāṇām tasmāt śucitamam smṛtam bhūta sṛṣṭim tu tām ca aham śmaśāne saṃnyaveśayam tasmāt me saṃnivāsāya śmaśāne rocate manaḥ kapāla śata saṃpūrṇam bhīma rūpam bhayānakam tatrasthaḥ aham prajāḥ sarvāḥ pālayāmi dine dine tasmāt loka hita arthāya śmaśāne ramayāmi aham umā etat te sarvam ākhyātam kim bhūyas śrotum icchasi piṅgalam vikṛtam bhāti rūpam te su bhayānakam bhasma digdham virūpa akṣam tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭram jaṭā ākulam vyāghra uraga tvac saṃvītam kapila śmaśru saṃtatam raudram bhayānakam ghoram śūla paṭṭisa saṃyutam maheśvaraḥ kimartham īdṛśam rūpam tat me śaṃsitum arhasi tat aham kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇu tattvam samāhitā dvividhaḥ laukikaḥ bhāvaḥ śītam uṣṇam iti priye saumya tvam satatam viṣṇau mayi āgneyam pratiṣṭhitam raudra ākṛti virūpa akṣam śūla paṭṭasa saṃyutam yadi aham viparītaḥ syām etat tyaktvā śubha ānane tasmāt mayā idam dhriyate rūpam loka hita eṣiṇā umā bhagavan devadeveśa śūlapāṇe vṛṣadhvaja maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu kalyāṇe kāraṇam purā aham kāraṇāt devi kopa yuktaḥ śuci smite dakṣa yajña vadha arthāya bhūta saṃgha samāvṛtaḥ devāḥ vibhraṃśitāḥ te vai yeṣām bhāgaḥ kratau kṛtaḥ paśyan ca anaparādhī san pādāṅguṣṭhena pīḍitaḥ tathā vinikṛtena aham sāma pūrvam prasāditaḥ tat me cintayataḥ ca āsīt paścāttāpaḥ punar priye tadā prabhṛti somam hi śirasā dhārayāmi aham tadā prabhṛti vai somaḥ mūrdhni saṃdṛśyate sadā nāradaḥ evam bruvati deveśe vismitāḥ parama ṛṣayaḥ vāgbhiḥ sa añjali mālābhiḥ abhituṣṭuvuḥ īśvaram namaḥ deva ādidevāya namaḥ śaśi kalā dhara namaḥ śāntatarāt śānta namaḥ candrasya pālaka namaḥ triśūla hastāya pannaga ābharaṇāya ca namaḥ astu viṣama akṣāya dakṣa yajña pradāhaka aho devasya māhātmyam mahādevasya vai kṛpā prīti artham ca munīnām sā kṣaṇajñā paramam hitam varṇa āśrama gatam dharmam vaktum arhasi aśeṣatas na tṛptiḥ asti deveśa śravaṇīyam hi te vacaḥ vaktum arhasi deveśa lokānām hita kāmyayā maheśvaraḥ śṛṇu tat sarvam akhilam dharmam varṇa āśrama āśritam brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca iti caturvidhāḥ brahmaṇā vihitāḥ pūrvam lokatantram abhīpsatā karmāṇi ca tad arhāni śāstreṣu vihitāni vai mukhataḥ brāhmaṇāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ tasmāt te vāc viśāradāḥ bāhubhyām kṣatriyāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ tasmāt bāhu bala anvitāḥ udarāt udgatāḥ vaiśyāḥ tasmāt vārttā upajīvinaḥ śūdrāḥ ca pādataḥ sṛṣṭāḥ tasmāt te paricārakāḥ teṣām dharmān ca karmāṇi śṛṇu devi samāhitā viprāḥ kṛtāḥ bhūmidevāḥ lokānām dhāraṇe kṛtāḥ te kaiḥ cit na avamantavyāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ hitam icchubhiḥ yadi te brāhmaṇāḥ na syuḥ dāna yoga vahāḥ sadā abudhaḥ vā daridraḥ vā pūjanīyaḥ sadā eva saḥ prahareta haret vā api dhanam teṣām nara adhamaḥ kārayet dhīna karmāṇi kāma lobha vimohanāt mām eva praharet mūḍhaḥ mad dhanasya apahārakaḥ mama eva prekṣaṇam kṛtvā nandate mūḍha cetanaḥ karmāṇi adhyāpanam ca eva yājanam ca pratigrahaḥ satyam śāntiḥ tapaḥ śaucam tasya dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ vikrayaḥ rasadhānyānām brāhmaṇasya vigarhitaḥ anāpadi ca śūdra annam vṛṣalī saṃgrahaḥ tathā tapaḥ eva sadā dharmaḥ brāhmaṇasya na saṃśayaḥ sa tu dharma artham utpannaḥ pūrvam dhātrā tapaḥ balāt agni kāryam paraḥ dharmaḥ nityam yajña upavīti tā amṛtāśyam param dharmaḥ gṛha puṣpa baliḥ tathā gṛha saṃmārjanam dharmaḥ ālepana vidhiḥ tathā iṣṭayaḥ paśubandhāḥ ca vidhi pūrvam param tapaḥ daṃpatyoḥ sama śīla tvam dharmaḥ vai gṛhamedhinām tam aham te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu devi samāhitā kṣatriyāḥ tu tathā devi prajānām pālane smṛtāḥ rakṣaṇāt kṣatriyaiḥ eva jagat bhavati śāśvatam tasya api adhyayanam dānam yajanam dharmataḥ smṛtam bhītānām rakṣaṇam ca eva pāpānām anuśāsanam satām saṃpoṣaṇam ca eva kara ṣaṣ bhāga jīvanam utsāhaḥ śastra jīvi tvam tasya dharmāḥ sanātanāḥ bhṛtyānām bharaṇam dharmaḥ kṛte karmaṇi amogha tā evam te vihitāḥ pūrvaiḥ dharmāḥ karma vidhānāt tathā eva devi vaiśyāḥ ca lokayātrā hitāḥ smṛtāḥ teṣām adhyayanam dānam yajanam dharmaḥ iṣyate vaiśyasya satatam dharmaḥ pāśupālyam kṛṣiḥ tathā vāṇijyam sat pathe sthānam ātitheyam sadā bhavet viprāṇām svāgatam nyāyaḥ vaiśya dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ evam te vihitā devi lokayātrā svayambhunā tathā eva śūdrāḥ vihitāḥ sarva dharma prasādhakāḥ śūdrāḥ ca yadi te na syuḥ karma kartā na vidyate trayaḥ pūrve śūdra mūlāḥ tasmāt karmakarāḥ smṛtāḥ brāhmaṇa ādiṣu śuśrūṣā dāsa dharmaḥ iti smṛtaḥ vārtā ca kāru karmāṇi śilpam nāṭyam tathā eva ca ahiṃsakaḥ śubha ācāraḥ daivata dvija vandakaḥ te api evam vihitāḥ loke karma yogāḥ śubha ānane evam caturṇām varṇānām puṇya lokāḥ paratra ca vihitāḥ ca tathā dṛṣṭāḥ yathāvat dharma cāriṇām umā kathitam śrotu kāmāyāḥ kim bhūyas śrotum icchasi maheśvaraḥ śrotum icchāmi aham deva dharmam āśramiṇām vibho atha āśrama gatam dharmam śṛṇu devi samāhitā āśramāṇām tu yaḥ dharmaḥ kriyate brahma vādibhiḥ gṛhasthaḥ pravaraḥ teṣām gārhasthya vratam āśritaḥ pañcayajña kriyā śaucam dāra tuṣṭiḥ atandri tā ṛtu kāla abhigamanam dāna yajña tapāṃsi ca a vipravāsaḥ tasya iṣṭam svādhyāyaḥ ca agni pūjanam atithīnām ābhimukhyam śaktyā ca iṣṭa nimantraṇam anugrahaḥ ca sarveṣām manaḥ vāc kāya karmabhiḥ evamādi śubham ca anyat kuryāt tad vṛttavān gṛhī evam saṃcarataḥ tasya puṇya lokāḥ na saṃśayaḥ tathā eva vānaprasthasya dharmāḥ proktāḥ sanātanāḥ gṛha vāsam samutsṛjya niścitya ekamanāḥ śubhaiḥ bhūmi śayyā jaṭāḥ śmaśru carma valkala dhāraṇam devatā atithi satkāraḥ mahā kṛcchra abhipūjanam brahmacaryam kṣamā śaucam tasya dharmāḥ sanātanāḥ yati dharmāḥ tathā devi saṅgān tyaktvā yatas tatas ākiṃcanyam anārambhaḥ sarvatas śaucam ārjavam sadā dhyāna para tvam ca doṣa śuddhiḥ kṣamā dayā brahmacārī ca yaḥ devi janma prabhṛti dīkṣitaḥ sarva kāleṣu sarvatra guru pūjām samācaret bhaikṣa caryā agni kāryam ca sadā jala niṣevaṇam svādhyāyaḥ satatam devi tasya dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ tasya ceṣṭā tu guru artham āprāṇāntam iti sthitiḥ evam saḥ api amalān lokān brāhmaṇaḥ pratipadyate eṣa te kathitaḥ devi dharmaḥ ca āśrama vāsinām umā tapasā karśitāḥ nityam tapoḥ jana parāyaṇāḥ asya kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ dharmaḥ kīdṛśaḥ ca āgamaḥ tathā nāradaḥ evam vadantyām rudrāṇyām ṛṣayaḥ sādhu sādhu iti abruvan hṛṣṭa manasaḥ sarve tad gata mānasāḥ śṛṇvantīm ṛṣi dharmān tu ṛṣayaḥ ca abhyapūjayan tvad prasādāt vayam devi śroṣyāmaḥ paramam hitam dhanyāḥ khalu vayam sarve pāda mūlam tava āśritāḥ maheśvaraḥ iti sarve tadā devīm vācā samabhipūjayan nyāyataḥ tvam mahābhāge śrotu kāmā manasvini bahu śākhaḥ bahuvidhaḥ ṛṣi dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ prāyaśas svarga bhoga artham ṛṣibhiḥ kriyate tapaḥ tathā saṃcaratām teṣām devi dharma vidhim śṛṇu bhūtvā pūrvam gṛhasthaḥ tu putra ānṛṇyam avāpya ca kalatra kāryam saṃsthāpya kāraṇāt saṃtyajet gṛham avasthāpya manaḥ dhṛtyā vyavasāya puraḥsaraḥ nirdvaṃdvaḥ vā sa dāraḥ vā vana vāsāya saṃvrajet deśāḥ parama puṇyāḥ ye nadī vana samanvitāḥ ābādha muktāḥ prāyeṇa tīrtha āyatana saṃyutāḥ tatra gatvā vidhim jñātvā dīkṣām kuryāt yathākramam dīkṣitvā ekamanāḥ bhūtvā paricaryām samācaret kālya utthānam ca śaucam ca sarva deva praṇāmanam śakṛt ālepanam kāye tyakta doṣa apramādi tā sāyam prātar ca abhiṣekam agnihotram yathāvidhi kāya śaucam ca kāryam ca jaṭā valkala dhāraṇam nīvāra grahaṇam kāle śāka mūla upacāyanam atithīnām ābhimukhyam tad para tvam ca sarvaśas pādya āsanābhyām saṃpūjā tathā āhāra nimantraṇam a grāmyapacanam kāle pitṛ deva arcanam tathā paścāt atithi satkāraḥ tasya dharmāḥ sanātanāḥ śiṣṭaiḥ dharma āsane ca eva dharma artha sahitāḥ kathāḥ pratiśraya vibhāgaḥ ca bhūmi śayyā śilāsu vā divā rātrau yathāyogam śaucam dharma artha cintanā evam dharmāḥ purā dṛṣṭāḥ sāmānyāḥ vana vāsinām paribhraṣṭaḥ yadā svargāt viśiṣṭaḥ tu bhavet nṛpa evam dharmaḥ sadā devi sarveṣām vana vāsinām umā bhagavan devadeveśaḥ ṛṣīṇām caritam śubham maheśvaraḥ viśeṣa dharmān icchāmi śrotum kautūhalam hi me tat aham te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu devi samāhitā vīraśayyām upāsadbhiḥ vīrasthāna upasevibhiḥ pañcayajña paraiḥ nityam paurṇamāsya parāyaṇaiḥ maṇḍūkaśāyaiḥ hemante śaivāla aṅkura bhojanaiḥ cāturmāsya paraiḥ kaiḥ cit deva dharma parāyaṇaiḥ evam kṛtvā śubham karma paścāt yāti triviṣṭapam umā tapaḥ viśeṣa saṃyuktāḥ kathitāḥ te śuci smite bhagavant sarva bhūta īśa teṣu ye dāra saṃyutāḥ maheśvaraḥ kīdṛśam caritam teṣām tat me śaṃsitum arhasi ye eka patnī dharmāṇaḥ caranti vipulam tapaḥ puṣkareṣu ca ye ca anye nadī vana samāśritāḥ hiṃsā droha vimuktāḥ ca sarva bhūta anukampinaḥ śāntāḥ dāntāḥ jita krodhāḥ sarva ātithya parāyaṇāḥ prāṇiṣu ātma upamāḥ nityam ṛtu kāla abhigāminaḥ teṣām paricchada ārambhāḥ kṛtyā upakaraṇāni ca gṛhastha vat vidhīyante yathāyogam pramāṇataḥ poṣaṇa artham ca dārāṇām agni kārya artham eva ca gāvaḥ ca karṣaṇam ca eva sarvam etat vidhīyate te sva dāraiḥ samāyānti puṇyān lokān dṛḍha vratāḥ patibhiḥ saha ye dārāḥ caranti vipulam tapaḥ umā maheśvaraḥ vānaprastha gatam sarvam phala pākam śṛṇu priye agniyogam vrajan grīṣme naraḥ dvādaśa vārṣikam rudra loke hi jāyeta vidhi dṛṣṭena karmaṇā uda vāsa vratam kurvan varṣa kāle dṛḍha vrataḥ kāṣṭha vat maunam āsthāya naraḥ dvādaśa vārṣikam kaṇṭaśarkara saṃyukte sthaṇḍile saṃviśet muniḥ varṣāṇām bhoga saṃyuktaḥ naraḥ dvādaśa vārṣikam vīrāsana gataḥ yaḥ tu kaṇṭaka āphalaka āśritaḥ vīra sthāyī ca ūrdhvabāhuḥ naraḥ dvādaśa vārṣikam pādāṅguṣṭhena yaḥ tiṣṭhet ūrdhvabāhuḥ jita indriyaḥ āhāra niyamam kṛtvā muniḥ dvādaśa vārṣikam nāga loke abhijāyeta saṃvatsara gaṇān bahūn evam dṛḍha vratāḥ devi vānaprasthāḥ ca karmabhiḥ sthāneṣu teṣu tiṣṭhanti tadvat bhoga samanvitāḥ tebhyaḥ bhraṣṭāḥ punar devi jāyante nṛṣu bhoginaḥ umā eṣām yāyāvarāṇām tu dharmam icchāmi mānada maheśvaraḥ kṛpayā parayā āviṣṭaḥ tam me brūhi maheśvara dharmam yāyāvarāṇām tu śṛṇu bhāmini tad parā vrata upavāsa śuddha aṅgāḥ tīrtha snāna parāyaṇāḥ dhṛtimantaḥ kṣamā yuktāḥ satya vrata parāyaṇāḥ pakṣa māsa upavāsaiḥ ca karśitāḥ dharma darśinaḥ varṣa śīta ātapaiḥ eva kurvantaḥ paramam tapaḥ divya bhūṣaṇa saṃyuktāḥ vimāna varam āsthitāḥ vicaranti yathākāmam divya strī gaṇa saṃyutāḥ umā maheśvaraḥ teṣām cakracarāṇām tu dharmam icchāmi vai prabho hanta te kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇu śākaṭikam śubhe saṃvahantaḥ dhuram dāraiḥ śākaṭānām tu sarvadā prārthayante yathā grāmyāḥ śakaṭaiḥ bhaikṣa caryayā tapoḥ jana para adhīnāḥ tapasā kṣīṇa kalmaṣāḥ paryaṭantaḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ kāma krodha vivarjitāḥ sva vaśāt eva te mṛtyum abhikāṅkṣanti nityaśas indra loke tathā teṣām nirmitāḥ bhoga saṃcayāḥ vara apsarobhiḥ saṃyuktāḥ cira kālam anindite umā maheśvaraḥ vaikhānasānām vai dharmam śrotum icchāmi aham prabho teṣu vaikhānasāḥ nāma vānaprasthāḥ śubha īkṣaṇe tīvreṇa tapasā yuktāḥ dīptimantaḥ sva tejasā satya vrata para adhīnāḥ teṣām niṣkalmaṣam tapaḥ aśmakuṭṭāḥ tathā anye ca dantolūkhalinaḥ tathā śīrṇa parṇa āśinaḥ ca anye uñchayanti tathā apare kapotavratinaḥ ca anye kāpotīm vṛttim āsthitāḥ paśu pracāra niratāḥ phenapāḥ ca tathā apare mṛga vat mṛga caryāyām saṃcaranti tathā apare abbhakṣāḥ vāyubhakṣāḥ ca nirāhārāḥ tathā eva ca sva vaśāt eva te mṛtyum abhikāṅkṣanti nityaśas indra loke tathā teṣām nirmitāḥ bhoga saṃcayāḥ vara apsarobhiḥ saṃyuktāḥ cira kālam anindite umā maheśvaraḥ bhagavan śrotum icchāmi vālakhilyān tapodhanān dharma caryām tathā devi vālakhilya gatām śṛṇu aṅguṣṭha mātrāḥ suśroṇi sveṣu eva aṅgeṣu saṃyutāḥ te mṛtyu viṣaya atītāḥ tapaḥ siddhāḥ tapaḥ balāḥ jita āhārāḥ jita krodhāḥ sarva bhogeṣu niḥspṛhāḥ dyotayante diśaḥ sarvāḥ dharma jñāḥ satya vādinaḥ teṣu eva nirmalam satyam loka artham tu pratiṣṭhitam kṣamayā ca mahābhāge bhūtānām saṃsthitim viduḥ amara tvam vaśi tvam ca tapasā prārthayet sadā etat te kathitam sarvam śṛṇvantyāḥ te śrutam priye priya artham ṛṣi saṃghasya lokānām hita kāmyayā nāradaḥ iti bruvantam deveśam ṛṣayaḥ ca api tuṣṭuvuḥ umā maheśvaraḥ brāhmaṇāḥ loka saṃsāre sṛṣṭāḥ dhātrā guṇa arthinā lokān tārayitum yuktāḥ martyeṣu kṣitidevatāḥ brāhmaṇeṣu abhayaḥ dharmaḥ paramaḥ śubha lakṣaṇaḥ ime hi dharmāḥ loka artham pūrvam sṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvā pṛthivyām sat janaiḥ nityam kīrtyamānam nibodha me śūdraḥ dharma paraḥ nityam śuśrūṣā abhimanāḥ bhavet ṣaḍ karmāṇi ca proktāni sṛṣṭāni brahmaṇā purā dharmiṣṭhāni variṣṭhāni yāni tāni śṛṇu uttame yajanam yājanam ca eva dānam pātre pratigrahaḥ adhyāpanam adhyayanam ṣaṣ karmā dharma bhāj ṛjuḥ dānam praśasyate nityam brāhmaṇeṣu tri karmasu pañcayajña viśuddha ātmā kratu nityaḥ anasūyakaḥ dāntaḥ brāhmaṇa satkartā su saṃmṛṣṭa niveśanaḥ atithi abhyāgata rataḥ śeṣa anna kṛta bhojanaḥ pādyam arghyam yathānyāyam āsanam śayanam tathā dīpam pratiśrayam ca eva yaḥ dadāti sa dhārmikaḥ tat aham kīrtayiṣyāmi trivargeṣu ca yat yathā ekena aṃśena kāma artham ekam aṃśam vivardhayet nivṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ puṇyaḥ dharmaḥ mokṣe vidhīyate tasya vṛttim pravakṣyāmi tām śṛṇuṣva samāhitā bubhukṣitam pipāsā ārtam atithim śrāntam āgatam pātram iti eva dātavyam sarvasmai dharma kāṅkṣibhiḥ āgamiṣyati yat pātram tat pātram tārayiṣyati kedārāḥ ca taṭākāni sarāṃsi saritaḥ tathā toya pūrṇāni dṛśyante apratarkyāṇi śobhane pīḍayā api ca bhṛtyānām dānam eva viśiṣyate putra dārāḥ dhanam dhānyam na mṛtān anugacchati śreyaḥ dānam ca bhogaḥ ca dhanam prāpya yaśasvini dānena hi mahābhāgāḥ bhavanti manuja adhipāḥ na asti bhūmi samam dānam na asti dāna samaḥ nidhiḥ na asti satyāt paraḥ dharmaḥ na anṛtāt pātakam param āśrame yaḥ tu tapyeta tapaḥ mūla phala aśanaḥ āditya abhimukhaḥ bhūtvā jaṭā valkala saṃvṛtaḥ maṇḍūkaśāyī hemante grīṣme pañcatapāḥ bhavet samyak tapaḥ caranti iha śraddadhānāḥ vana āśrame gṛha āśramasya te devi kalām na arhanti ṣoḍaśīm umā gṛhāśramasya yā caryā vratāni niyamāḥ ca ye yathā ca devatāḥ pūjyāḥ satatam gṛhamedhinā maheśvaraḥ gṛha āśramasya yat mūlam phalam dharmaḥ ayam uttamaḥ pādaiḥ caturbhiḥ satatam dharmaḥ yatra pratiṣṭhitaḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi śrūyatām dharma cāriṇi śuśrūṣate yaḥ pitaraḥ mātaram ca gṛha āśrame bhartāram ca eva yā nārī agnihotram ca ye dvijāḥ teṣu teṣu ca prīṇanti devāḥ indra purogamāḥ umā mātā pitṛ viyuktānām kā caryā gṛhamedhinām vidhavānām ca nārīṇām bhavān etat bravītu me maheśvaraḥ devatā atithi śuśrūṣā guru vṛddha abhivādanam ahiṃsā sarva bhūtānām alobhaḥ satyasaṃdhatā brahmacaryam śaraṇya tvam śaucam pūrva abhibhāṣaṇam kṛtajña tvam apaiśunyam satatam dharma śīla tā gavāhnika pradānam ca saṃvibhāgaḥ atithiṣu api dīpam pratiśrayam ca eva dadyāt pādya āsanam tathā pañcame ahani ṣaṣṭhe vā dvādaśe vā api atha aṣṭame caturdaśe pañcadaśe brahmacārī sadā bhavet śmaśrukarma śiraḥ abhyaṅgam añjanam dantadhāvanam na eteṣu ahaḥsu kurvīta teṣu alakṣmīḥ pratiṣṭhitā para dāra nivṛttiḥ ca sva dāreṣu ratiḥ sadā śarīram ekam daṃpatyoḥ vidhātrā pūrva nirmitam śīla vṛtta vinītasya nigṛhīta indriyasya ca ārjave vartamānasya sarva bhūta hita eṣiṇaḥ gṛha āśrama pada sthasya kim anyaiḥ kṛtyam āśramaiḥ yathā mātaram āśritya sarve jīvanti jantavaḥ tathā gṛhāśramam prāpya sarve jīvanti ca āśramāḥ rājānaḥ sarva pāṣaṇḍāḥ sarve raṅga upajīvinaḥ vyāla grāhāḥ ca dambhāḥ ca corāḥ rāja bhaṭāḥ tathā sa vidyāḥ sarva śilpa jñāḥ sarve ca eva cikitsakāḥ dūra adhvānam prapannāḥ ca kṣīṇa pathya odanāḥ narāḥ mārjārāḥ mūṣikāḥ śvānaḥ sūkarāḥ ca śukāḥ tathā kapota kāka caṭakāḥ sarīsṛpa niṣeviṇaḥ araṇya vāsinaḥ ca anye saṃghāḥ ye mṛga pakṣiṇām gṛhe kṣetre bile ca eva śataśas atha sahasraśas upayuktam ca yat teṣām matimān na anuśocati āśā pāśa vimokṣaḥ ca viddhi dharmam anuttamam vṛkṣa mūla caraḥ nityam śūnya āgāra niveśanam nadī pulina śāyī ca nadī tīram anuvrajan ātma bhūtaḥ yata āhāraḥ mokṣa dṛṣṭena karmaṇā umā saṃgṛhītam mayā tat ca tava vākyam anuttamam idānīm asti saṃdehaḥ mānuṣeṣu eva kaḥ cana tulya pāṇi śiraḥ kāyaḥ rājā ayam iti dṛśyate pretyabhāve katham lokān labhate puṇya karmaṇām maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi rāja dharmam śubha ānane rāja āyattam hi tat sarvam loka vṛttam śubha aśubham tapaḥ dāna mayam rājyam param sthānam vidhīyate tasmāt rājñaḥ sadā martyāḥ praṇamanti yatas tatas nyāyataḥ tvam mahābhāge śrotu kāmā asi bhāmini arājake purā tu āsīt prajānām saṃkulam mahat tat dṛṣṭvā saṃkulam brahmā manum rājye nyaveśayat tadā prabhṛti saṃdṛṣṭam rājñām vṛttam śubha aśubham yathā pretya labhet svargam yathā vīryam yaśaḥ tathā pitryam vā bhūta pūrvam vā svayam utpādya vā punar anu bhṛtyān prajāḥ paścāt iti eṣa vinaya kramaḥ svāminam ca upamām kṛtvā prajāḥ tad vṛtta kāṅkṣayā svayam vinaya saṃpannāḥ bhavanti iha śubha īkṣaṇe tasmāt pūrvataram rājā ātmānam vinaye nayet yaḥ vinītaḥ svayam rājā vinayati eva vai prajāḥ apahāsyaḥ bhavet tādṛś sva doṣasya anavekṣaṇāt vidyā abhyāsaiḥ vṛddha yogaiḥ ātmānam vinayam nayet vidyā dharma artha phalinī tad vidaḥ vṛddha saṃjñitāḥ indriyāṇām jayaḥ devi atas ūrdhvam udāhṛtam ajaye su mahān doṣaḥ rājānam vinipātayet pañca eva sva vaśān kṛtvā tad arthān pañca śoṣayet ṣaḍ utsṛjya yathāyogam jñānena vinayena ca śāstra cakṣuḥ naya paraḥ bhūtvā bhṛtyān samāharet vṛtta śruta kula upetān upadhābhiḥ parīkṣitān amātyān upadhā atītān sa apasarpān jita indriyān amātyāḥ buddhi saṃpannāḥ rāṣṭram bahu jana priyam durādharṣam pura śreṣṭham kośaḥ kṛcchra sahaḥ smṛtaḥ etāḥ prakṛtayaḥ ṣaḍ ca svāmī ca naya tattva vid prajānām rakṣaṇa arthāya sarvam etat vinirmitam ābhiḥ karaṇa bhūtābhiḥ kuryāt loka hitam nṛpaḥ ātma rakṣā nṛpa indrasya prajā rakṣā artham iṣyate tasmāt satatam ātmānam saṃrakṣet apramādavān bhojana ācchādanāt snānāt bahis niṣkramaṇāt api nityam strī gaṇa saṃyogāt rakṣet ātmānam ātmavān satatam putra dārebhyaḥ rakṣet ātmānam ātmavān prajānām rakṣaṇa arthāya prajā hita karaḥ bhavet prakṛtīnām vivāda artham rāga dveṣau vyudasya ca ubhayayoḥ pakṣayoḥ vādam śrutvā ca eva yathātatham tam artham vimṛśet buddhyā svayam ā tattva darśanāt kartāram aparādham ca deśa kālau naya anayau jñātvā samyak yathāśāstram tatas daṇḍam nayet nṛṣu pratyakṣa āpta upadeśābhyām anumānena vā punar boddhavyam satatam rājñā deśa vṛttam śubha aśubham cāraiḥ karma pravṛttyā ca tat vijñāya vicārayan daṇḍyān ca daṇḍayet devi na atra kāryā vicāraṇā pañca apekṣam sadā mantram kuryāt buddhi yutaiḥ naraiḥ rājā rāṣṭra hita apekṣaḥ satya dharmāṇi kārayet sarva udyogam svayam kuryāt durga ādiṣu sadā nṛpaḥ deśa vṛddhi karān bhṛtyān apramādena kārayet su mukhaḥ su priyaḥ bhūtvā samyak vṛttam samādiśet adharmyam paruṣam tīkṣṇam vākyam vaktum na ca arhati sva iṅgitam vṛṇuyāt dhairyāt na kuryāt kṣudra saṃvidam para iṅgita jñaḥ loka jñaḥ bhūtvā saṃsargam ācaret amānuṣa bhayebhyaḥ ca svāḥ prajāḥ pālayet nṛpaḥ lubdhāḥ kaṭhorāḥ ca adhyakṣāḥ mānavāḥ dasyu vṛttayaḥ nigrāhyāḥ eva te rājñā saṃgṛhītāḥ yatas tatas teṣām ātma guṇa upetam yauvarājye niyojayet prakṛtīnām yathā na syāt rājya bhraṃśa udbhavam bhayam arājakam kṣaṇam api rāṣṭram na syāt hi śobhane ātmanaḥ anuvidhānāya yauvarājyam sadā iṣyate kula jānām ca vaidyānām śrotriyāṇām tapasvinām anyeṣām vṛtta yuktānām viśeṣam kartum arhati ātma artham rājya tantra artham kośa saṃcayam ārabhet durgāt rāṣṭrāt samudrāt ca vaṇigbhyaḥ puruṣātyayāt parātma guṇa sārābhyām bhṛtya poṣaṇam ācaret vāhanānām vidhāya agre poṣaṇam yaudha karmasu sa ādaraḥ satatam bhūtvā apekṣā vratam ācaret caturdhā vibhajet kośam dharma bhṛtya ātma kāraṇāt āpad artham ca nīti jñaḥ deśa kāla vaśena tu anāthān vyādhitān vṛddhān sva deśe poṣayet nṛpaḥ saṃdhim ca vigraham ca eva tad viśeṣān tathā aparān yathāvat saṃvimṛśya eva buddhi pūrvam samācaret sarveṣām sa priyaḥ bhūtvā maṇḍalam satatam caret śubheṣu api ca kāryeṣu na ca ekaḥ antar samācaret pareṇa dhārmikān nyāyān na atīyāt dveṣa lobhataḥ ku nṛpaiḥ pīḍitāḥ tasmāt prajāḥ sarvatra pālayet yātrā kālam avekṣya eva paścāt kopaḥ phala udayam tad yuktāḥ ca āpadaḥ ca eva prāk yānāt iti cintayet prāyaśas varjayet yuddham prāṇa rakṣaṇa kāraṇāt kāraṇāt eva yoddhavyam na ātmanaḥ para doṣataḥ abhiyuktaḥ balavatā kuryāt āpad vidhim nṛpaḥ anunīya tathā sarvān prajānām hita kāraṇāt anya prakṛti yuktānām rājñām vṛtta vicāriṇām anyān ca āpad prapannānām na tān saṃyoktum arhati śubha aśubham yadā devi vṛttam tu ubhayatas smṛtam etat evam samāsena rāja dharmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ evam saṃvartamānaḥ tu daṇḍayan bhartsayan prajāḥ svarga loke tadā rājā tridaśaiḥ saha toṣyate evam nyāya anugam vṛttam kathitam te śubha īkṣaṇe rājyam nyāya anugam nāma buddhi śāstra anugam bhavet daivapakṣye sati nṛpe rājyam nyāya anugam bhavet kriyante yatra karmāṇi śāstra yuktim vimṛśya vai rājyam bhoga anugam nāma ayathāvat pradṛśyate yatra bhāgya vaśāt bhṛtyāḥ labhante na viśeṣataḥ yatra daṇḍyāḥ na daṇḍyante pūjyante vā nara adhamāḥ śubha aśubham yadā yatra viparītam pradṛśyate rājñi vāsura pakṣe tu tatra bhāgya anugam bhavet bhāgya anuge tu rājānaḥ vartamānāḥ yathā tathā prāpya a kīrtim anartham ca iha loke śubha īkṣaṇe mokṣaṇam duṣkṛtīnām tu vidyate kāla paryayāt na asti eva mokṣaṇam devi rājñām duṣkṛta kāriṇām etat sarvam samāsena rāja vṛttam śubha aśubham umā kathitam te mahābhāge bhūyas śrotum kim icchasi maheśvaraḥ rahasyam śrūyatām devi mānuṣāṇām sukha āvaham yatra vā tatra vā bījam dharma arthī na utsṛjet punar naraḥ bīja vināśena lipyate bhrūṇahatyayā ahiṃsā paramaḥ dharmaḥ ahiṃsā paramam sukham ahiṃsā dharma śāstreṣu sarveṣu paramam padam devatā atithi śuśrūṣā satatam dharma śīla tā veda adhyayana yajñāḥ ca tapaḥ dānam damaḥ tathā ācārya guru śuśrūṣā tīrtha abhigamanam tathā ahiṃsāyāḥ varārohe kalām na arhanti ṣoḍaśīm umā katham ca bhagavan bhūyas hiṃsamānāḥ narādhipāḥ yasya eva go sahasrāṇi viṃśatiḥ sādhakāni tu ahani ahani hanyante dvijānām māṃsa kāraṇāt sa māṃsam tu sa dattvā annam rantidevaḥ narādhipaḥ kim nu dharmam na śṛṇvanti na śraddadhati vā śrutam mṛgayāyai vinirgatya mṛgān ghnanti narādhipāḥ etat sarvam viśeṣeṇa vistareṇa vṛṣadhvaja maheśvaraḥ bahu mānyam idam devi na asti kaḥ cit ahiṃsakaḥ śrūyatām kāraṇam ca atra yathā anekavidham bhavet dṛśyate ca api loke asmin na kaḥ cit avihiṃsakaḥ dharaṇī saṃśritān jīvān su sūkṣmān ca eva madhyamān saṃcaran caraṇābhyām ca hanti jīvān anekaśas ajñānāt jñānataḥ vā api ye jīvāḥ śayana āsane upāviśan śayānaḥ ca hanti jīvān anekaśas śiraḥ vastreṣu ye jīvāḥ narāṇām sveda saṃbhavāḥ tān ca hiṃsanti satatam daṃśān ca maśakān api jale jīvāḥ tathā ākāśe pṛthivī jīva mālinī evam jīva ākule loke kaḥ asau syāt yaḥ tu ahiṃsakaḥ sthūla madhyama sūkṣmaiḥ ca sveda vāta mahīruhaiḥ dṛśya rūpaiḥ adṛśyaiḥ ca nānā rūpaiḥ ca bhāmini jīvaiḥ tatam idam sarvam ākāśam pṛthivī tathā matsyāḥ matsyān grasanti iha khagān ca eva khagāḥ tathā sarīsṛpaiḥ ca jīvanti kapota ādyāḥ vihaṃgamāḥ bhūcarāḥ khecarāḥ ca anye kravyādāḥ māṃsa gṛddhinaḥ samṛddhāḥ para māṃsaiḥ tu bhakṣeran ye api ca aparaiḥ sattvaiḥ sattvāni jīvanti śataśas atha sahasraśas a pīḍayitvā na eva anyam jīvāḥ jīvanti sundari jīvasya ekasya māṃsena payasā rudhireṇa vā tṛpyante bahavaḥ jīvāḥ kravyādāḥ māṃsa bhojinaḥ ekaḥ jīva sahasrāṇi sadā khādati mānavaḥ annādi alpa upabhogena dhānya saṃjñāni yāni tu māṃsa dhānyaiḥ sa bījaiḥ ca bhojanam parivarjayet tri rātram pañca rātram vā sapta rātram atha api vā dhānyāni yaḥ na hiṃseta ahiṃsakaḥ parikīrtitaḥ na aśnāti yāvataḥ jīvān tāvat puṇyena yujyate tapyamāne śarīre tu śarīram ca indriyāṇi api vaśe tiṣṭhanti suśroṇi nṛpāṇām iva kiṃkarāḥ niruṇaddhi indriyāṇi eva sa sukhī sa vicakṣaṇaḥ etat mūlam ahiṃsāyāḥ upavāsaḥ prakīrtitaḥ āhāram kurute yaḥ tu bhūmim ākramate ca yaḥ sarve te hiṃsakāḥ devi yathā dharmeṣu dṛśyate yathā iha ahiṃsakaḥ devi tattva jñaḥ jñāyate naraḥ tathā te aham pravakṣyāmi śrūyatām dharma cāriṇi phalāni jīrṇa parṇāni bhasma vā yaḥ api bhakṣayet ālekhyam iva niśceṣṭam tam manye aham ahiṃsakam ārambhāḥ hiṃsayā yuktāḥ dhūmena agniḥ iva āvṛtāḥ yaḥ tu sarvam samutsṛjya dīkṣitaḥ niyataḥ śuciḥ kṛtvā maṇḍala maryādām saṃkalpam kurute naraḥ yāvajjīvam an āśitvā kāla ākāṅkṣī dṛḍha vrataḥ anyathā hi na paśyāmi naraḥ yaḥ syāt ahiṃsakaḥ yatas yatas mahābhāge hiṃsā syāt mahatī tatas nivṛttau madhu māṃsābhyām hiṃsā tu alpatarā bhavet manasā vinivṛttānām dharmasya nicayaḥ mahān manaḥ pūrvaṃgamāḥ dharmāḥ adharmāḥ ca na saṃśayaḥ āyuḥ kṣayam gate adya eṣām mṛte tu praharāmi aham vidhinā nihataḥ pūrvam nimittam sa tu ghātakaḥ jīvāḥ purākṛtena eva tiryagyoni sarīsṛpāḥ nānā yoniṣu jāyante sva karma pariveṣṭitāḥ nānāvidha vicitra aṅgāḥ nānā vīrya parākramāḥ nānā bhūmi pradeśeṣu nānā āhārāḥ ca jantavaḥ jāyamānasya jīvasya mṛtyuḥ pūrvam prajāyate sukham vā yadi vā duḥkham yathā pūrvam kṛtam tathā na atikrāntum hi śakyam syāt nideśaḥ pūrva karmaṇaḥ samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu kālaḥ kālam nirīkṣate gata āyuṣaḥ hi ākṣipati jīvam sarvasya dehinaḥ araṇye sva gṛhe vā api rātrau vā ahani vā tathā maheśvaraḥ śrūyatām kāraṇam devi yathā hi duratikramaḥ āyuḥ kṣayeṇa upahatāḥ samāgamya varānane kīṭāḥ pataṃgāḥ bahavaḥ sthūlāḥ sūkṣmāḥ ca madhyamāḥ bahūnām mṛga yūthānām nānā vana niṣeviṇām sūnā artham devi baddhānām kṣīṇa āyūḥ yaḥ nibadhyate yathā pakṣi gaṇāḥ kṣipram vistīrṇa ākāśa gāminaḥ kṣīṇa āyuṣaḥ nibadhyante śaktāḥ api palāyitum yathā vāricarāḥ mīnāḥ bahavaḥ bahu jātayaḥ āyuḥ kṣayeṇa upahatāḥ nipadyante sarīsṛpāḥ kṛṣatām karṣakāṇām ca na asti buddhiḥ vihiṃsane atha eṣām lāṅgala agra ādyaiḥ hanyante jantavaḥ akṣayāḥ pāda agreṇa eva ca ekena yām hiṃsām kurute naraḥ mātaṃgaḥ api na tām kuryāt krūraḥ janma śataiḥ api kṛṣāmi iti matiḥ tasya na asti cintā vihiṃsane vidhinā vihitaḥ pūrvam paścāt prāṇī vipadyate gata āyuṣā na śakyam hi muhūrtam api jīvitum tathā tābhiḥ ca martavyam bhoktavyāḥ ca eva tāḥ tathā gavām vai hanyamānānām rudhira prabhavā nadī carmaṇvatī iti vikhyātā khura śṛṅga asthi durgamā rudhiram tām nadīm prāpya toyam bhavati śobhane tatra abhiṣekam kurvanti kṛta japyāḥ kṛta āhnikāḥ dvijāḥ deva gaṇāḥ ca api lokapālāḥ maheśvarāḥ vidhinā pūrva dṛṣṭena tad māṃsam upakalpitam sa māṃsam ca sadā hi annam śataśas atha sahasraśas bhuñjānānām dvijātīnām astam eti divākaraḥ paṭhyamāneṣu mantreṣu yathānyāyam yathāvidhi tāḥ ca svargam gatāḥ gāvaḥ rantidevaḥ ca pārthivaḥ bhogānām saṃvibhāgena vastra ābharaṇa bhūṣaṇaiḥ sahāya kāle saṃprāpte saṃgrāme śastram uddharet vyūḍha anīke yathā śastram senayoḥ ubhayayoḥ api hasti aśva ratha saṃpūrṇe padāti bala saṃkule śakti tomara kunta asi śūla paṭṭisa dhāribhiḥ kūṭamudgara cāpa iṣu bhusuṇḍhī juṣṭa muṣṭibhiḥ yuddha śauṇḍaiḥ pragarjadbhiḥ vṛṣeṣu vṛṣabhaiḥ iva śaṅkha dundubhi nādena nānā tūrya raveṇa ca haya heṣita śabdena kuñjarāṇām ca bṛṃhitaiḥ yodhānām siṃhanādaiḥ ca ghaṇṭānām śiñjita svanaiḥ diśaḥ ca vidiśaḥ ca eva samantāt badhirīkṛtāḥ grīṣma anteṣu vigarjadbhiḥ nabhasi iva balāhakaiḥ kapilābhiḥ iva ākāśe chādyamāne samantataḥ pravṛtte śastra saṃpāte yodhānām tatra senayoḥ palāśa aśoka puṣpāṇām jaṃgamāḥ iva rāśayaḥ śobhamānāḥ raṇe śūrāḥ āhvayantaḥ parasparam hanyamāneṣu abhighnatsu śūreṣu raṇa saṃkaṭe pṛṣṭham dattvā atha ye tatra nāyakasya nara adhamāḥ te duṣkṛtam prapadyante nāyakasya akhilam narāḥ yat ca asti sukṛtam teṣām yujyate tena nāyakaḥ saṃgrāmeṣu na yudhyante bhṛtāḥ ca eva anurūpatas narakam yānti te ghoram bhartṛ piṇḍa apahāriṇaḥ āviṣṭaḥ ca eva sattvena nirghṛṇaḥ jāyate naraḥ yaḥ tu svam nāyakam rakṣan ati ghore raṇa aṅgaṇe tāpayan ari sainyāni siṃhaḥ mṛga gaṇān iva ādityaḥ iva madhyāhne durnirīkṣyaḥ raṇa ajire yajate sa tu pūta ātmā saṃgrāmeṇa mahā kratum varma kṛṣṇājinam tasya daṇḍa kāṣṭham dhanuḥ smṛtam rathaḥ vediḥ dhvajaḥ yūpaḥ kuśāḥ ca ratha raśmayaḥ mānaḥ darpaḥ tu ahaṃkāraḥ trayaḥ tretāgnayaḥ smṛtāḥ sruc bhāṇḍam ca api yat kim cit yajña upakaraṇāni ca āyudhāni asya tat sarvam samidhaḥ sāyakāḥ smṛtāḥ sveda srāvaḥ ca gātrebhyaḥ kṣaudram tasya yaśasvinaḥ puroḍāśāḥ nṛ śīrṣāṇi rudhiram ca āhutiḥ smṛ tūṇaḥ ca eva caruḥ jñeyaḥ vasoḥ dhārā vasā smṛtā kravyādāḥ bhūta saṃghāḥ ca tasmin yajñe dvijātayaḥ teṣām bhakṣa anna pānāni hatā nṛ gaja vājinaḥ nihatānām tu yodhānām vastra ābharaṇa bhūṣaṇam hiraṇyam ca suvarṇam ca yat vai yajñasya dakṣiṇā yathā nadī sahasrāṇi praviṣṭāni mahā udadhim praviṣṭāḥ rāja dharmeṇa ācārya vinayaḥ tathā veda uktāḥ ca eva ye dharmāḥ pāṣaṇḍeṣu ca kīrtitāḥ tathā eva mānavāḥ dharmāḥ dharmāḥ ca anye tathā apare deśa jāti kulānām ca grāma dharmāḥ tathā eva ca ye dharmāḥ pārvatīyeṣu ye dharmāḥ pattana ādiṣu teṣām pūrva pravṛttānām kartavyam parirakṣaṇam ṣaṭkarma niratāḥ viprāḥ pūjyante pitṛ devatāḥ na eva tasmin anāvṛṣṭiḥ na rogāḥ na api upadravāḥ dharma śīlāḥ prajāḥ sarvāḥ svadharma nirate nṛpe iṣṭavyaḥ satatam devi yukta ācāraḥ narādhipaḥ chidra jñaḥ ca eva śatrūṇām apramattaḥ pratāpavān śūdrāḥ pṛthivyām bahavaḥ rājñām bahu vināśakāḥ tasmāt pramādam suśroṇi na kuryāt paṇḍitaḥ nṛpaḥ teṣu mitreṣu tyakteṣu tathā martyeṣu hastiṣu yaḥ tu rāṣṭra hita arthāya go brāhmaṇa kṛte tathā bandi grāhāya mitra arthe prāṇān tyajati dustyajān sarva kāma dughām dhenum dharaṇīm loka dhāriṇīm samudra antām varārohe sa śaila vana kānanām dadyāt devi dvijātibhyaḥ vasu pūrṇām vasuṃdharām na tad samam varārohe prāṇatyāgī viśiṣyate yajñaiḥ tasya kim āścaryam prāṇatyāgaḥ su duṣkaraḥ tasmāt sarveṣu yajñeṣu śastra yajñaḥ viśiṣyate maheśvaraḥ evam saṃgrāma yajñāḥ te yathātattvam udāhṛtāḥ mṛga yātrām tu vakṣyāmi śṛṇu tām dharma cāriṇi mṛgān hatvā mahīpālaḥ yathā pāpaiḥ na lipyate nirmānuṣām imām sarve mṛgāḥ icchanti medinīm bhakṣayanti ca sasyāni śāsitavyāḥ nṛpeṇa te duṣṭānām śāsanam dharmaḥ śiṣṭānām paripālanam kartavyam bhūmipālena nityam kāryeṣu ca ārjavam svargam mṛgāḥ ca gacchanti svayam nṛpatinā hatāḥ yathā gāvaḥ hi a gopālāḥ tathā rāṣṭram anāyakam tasmāt aṃśāḥ tu devānām gandharva uraga rakṣasām rājye niyuktāḥ rāṣṭreṣu prajā pālana kāraṇāt aśiṣṭa śāsane ca eva śiṣṭānām paripālane teṣām caryām pravakṣyāmi śrūyatām anupūrvaśas yathā pracaratām teṣām pārthivānām yaśasvini rāṣṭram dharmaḥ dhanam ca eva yaśaḥ kīrtiḥ ca vardhate nṛpāṇām pūrvam eva ayam dharmaḥ dharma bhṛtām vare sabhā prapāta ṭākāni devatāyatanāni ca brāhmaṇa āvasathāḥ ca eva kartavyāḥ nṛpa sattamaiḥ brāhmaṇāḥ na avamantavyāḥ bhasma channāḥ iva agnayaḥ kulam utsādayeyuḥ te krodha āviṣṭāḥ dvijātayaḥ tathā krodha agninā viprāḥ daheyuḥ pṛthivīm imām na hi vipreṣu kruddheṣu rājyam bhuñjanti bhūmipāḥ paribhūya dvijān mohāt vātāpi nahuṣa ādayaḥ sa bandhu mitrāḥ naṣṭāḥ te dagdhāḥ brāhmaṇa manyubhiḥ śarīram ca api śakrasya kṛtam bhaga nirantaram prasādam kārayām āsuḥ praṇāma stuti vandanaiḥ indrasya vṛṣaṇau bhūtvā kṣipram vai śleṣam āgatau evam vipreṣu kruddheṣu devarājaḥ śatakratuḥ aśaktaḥ śāsitum rājyam kim punar mānuṣaḥ bhuvi krodha āviṣṭaḥ dahet vipraḥ śuṣka indhanam iva analaḥ adevān api devān sa kuryāt devān adevatāḥ tasmāt na utpādayet manyum manyu praharaṇāḥ dvijāḥ mahatsu api aparādheṣu śāsanam na arhati dvijaḥ dṛśyate triṣu lokeṣu brāhmaṇānām anindite krodhāḥ ca vipulāḥ ghorāḥ prasādāḥ ca api anuttamāḥ tasmāt na utpādayet krodham nityam pūjyāḥ dvijātayaḥ kruddheṣu yaḥ vai vipreṣu rājyam bhuṅkte narādhipaḥ saṃprahāsaḥ ca bhṛtyeṣu na kartavyaḥ narādhipaiḥ bhṛtyānām saṃprahāsena pārthivaḥ paribhūyate tasmāt bhṛtyeṣu nṛpatiḥ saṃprahāsam vivarjayet sagotreṣu viśeṣeṇa sarva upāyaiḥ na viśvaset viśvāsāt bhayam utpannam hanyāt vṛkṣam iva aśaniḥ pramādāt dhanyate rājā lobhena ca vaśīkṛtaḥ bhaya ārtānām paritrātā dīna anugraha kārakaḥ tasmāt kṛtya viśeṣa jñaḥ nityam rāṣṭra hite rataḥ alubdhaḥ nyāya vādī ca ṣaḍbhāgam ca upajīvati kārya akārya viśeṣa jñaḥ sarvam dharmeṇa paśyati sva rāṣṭreṣu dayām kuryāt akāryam na pravartate aparādha anurūpeṇa duṣṭam daṇḍena śāsayet aśiṣṭa śāsanam dharmaḥ śiṣṭānām paripālanam avadhyāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ gāvaḥ dūtaḥ ca eva pitā tathā vidyām grāhayate yaḥ ca ye ca pūrva upakāriṇaḥ dharaṇīm gām hiraṇyam ca siddha annam ca tilān ghṛtam evam carati yaḥ nityam rājā rāṣṭra hite rataḥ tasya rāṣṭram dhanam dharmaḥ yaśaḥ kīrtiḥ ca vardhate ṣaḍbhāgam upayuñjan yaḥ prajāḥ rājā na rakṣati nirudyogaḥ nṛpaḥ yaḥ ca para rāṣṭra nighātane sva rāṣṭram niṣpratāpasya para cakreṇa hanyate tat pāpam sakalam rājā hatarāṣṭraḥ prapadyate mātulam bhāgineyam vā mātaram śvaśuram gurum svasya rāṣṭrasya rakṣā artham yudhyamānaḥ tu yaḥ hataḥ saṃgrāme para cakreṇa śrūyatām tasya yā gatiḥ śakra lokam itas yāti saṃgrāme nihataḥ nṛpaḥ yāvantaḥ lomakūpāḥ syuḥ tasya gātreṣu sundari tāvat varṣa sahasrāṇi śakra loke mahīyate rājā vā rājamātraḥ vā bhūyas bhavati vīryavān vyavahāraḥ ca cāraḥ ca satatam satya saṃdhā tā apramādaḥ pramodaḥ ca vyavasāye api a caṇḍa tā bharaṇam ca eva bhṛtyānām vāhanānām ca poṣaṇam yodhānām ca eva satkāraḥ kṛte karmaṇi amogha tā maheśvaraḥ yūpe nibaddhāḥ mantraiḥ ca yathānyāyam yathāvidhi tarpitāḥ yajña bhāgeṣu teṣām māṃsaiḥ varānane agnayaḥ tridaśāḥ ca eva lokapālāḥ saha īśvarāḥ teṣu tuṣṭeṣu jāyeta tasya yajñasya yat phalam sa patnīkaḥ sa putraḥ sa sa pitṛ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha umā etat te sarvam ākhyātam bhūyas śrotum kim icchasi bhagavan sarva bhūta īśa śūlapāṇe mahā dyute śrotum icchāmi aham vṛttam sarveṣām gṛhamedhinām kīdṛśam caritam teṣām trivarga sahitam prabho pratyāyatiḥ katham teṣām jīvana artham udāhṛ vartamānāḥ katham sarve prāpnuvanti uttamām gatim maheśvaraḥ nyāyataḥ tvam mahābhāge śrotu kāmā asi bhāmini prāyaśas loka sat vṛttam iṣyate gṛha vāsinām teṣām saṃrakṣaṇa arthāya rājānaḥ saṃsmṛtāḥ bhuvi sarveṣām atha martyānām vṛttim sāmānyatas śṛṇu vidyā vārttā ca sevā ca kāru tvam nāṭya tā tathā iti ete jīvana arthāya martyānām vihitāḥ priye api janma phalam tāvat mānuṣāṇām viśeṣataḥ vihitam tat sva vṛttena tat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu karma kṣetram hi mānuṣyam bhoga duḥkha yutāḥ pare sarveṣām prāṇinām tasmāt mānuṣye vṛttam iṣyate vidyā yogaḥ tu sarveṣām pūrvam eva vidhīyate kārya akāryam vijānāti vidyayā devi na anyathā vidyayā sphīyate jñānam jñānāt tattva vidarśanam dṛṣṭa tattvaḥ vinīta ātmā sarva arthasya ca bhājanam śakyam vidyā vinītena loke saṃjīvanam sukham ātmānam vidyayā tasmāt pūrvam kṛtvā tu bhājanam bhāvayitvā tathā ātmānam pūjanīyaḥ satām api kula anuvṛttam vṛttam vā pūrvam eva samāśrayet iṣyate gṛha vāsāya dārakarma yathāpuram yadi ced vidyayā ca eva vṛttim kāṅkṣet atha ātmanaḥ rāja vidyām tu vāde api loka vidyām atha api vā tīrthataḥ ca api gṛhṇīyāt śuśrūṣā ādi guṇaiḥ yutaḥ granthataḥ ca arthataḥ ca eva dṛḍhīkuryāt prayatnataḥ evam vidyā phalam devi prāpnuyāt na anyathā naraḥ yadi ced vārttayā vṛttim kāṅkṣeta vidhi pūrvakam kṣetre jala upapanne ca tat yogyām kṛṣim ācaret vāṇijyam vā yathākālam kuryāt tad deśa yogataḥ paśu saṃjīvakaḥ ca eva deśe gāḥ poṣayet dhruvam bahu prakārāḥ bahavaḥ paśavaḥ tasya sādhakāḥ yaḥ kaḥ cit sevayā vṛttim kāṅkṣeta matimān naraḥ yata ātmā śravaṇīyānām bhavet vai saṃprayojakaḥ buddhyā vā karma yogāt vā yodhanāt vā samāśrayet yathā yathā sa tuṣyeta tathā saṃtoṣayeta tam anujīvi guṇa upetaḥ kuryāt ātma artham āśritaḥ vipriyam na ācaret tasya eṣā sevā samāsatas kāru karma ca nāṭyam ca prāyaśas nīca yoniṣu sarveṣām pūrvam ārambhān cintayet naya pūrvakam ātma śaktim upāyān ca deśa kālau ca śaktitaḥ kāraṇāni pravāsam ca prakṣepam ca phala udayam evamādīni saṃcintya dṛṣṭvā daiva anukūla tām vṛttim evam samāsādya tām sadā paripālayet pālayan vardhayan bhuñjan tām prāpya na vināśayet kṣīyate giri saṃkāśam aśnataḥ hi anapekṣayā dharmāya arthāya kāmāya āpad praśamanāya ca caturṣu api vibhāgeṣu vidhānam śṛṇu śobhane yajña artham ca anna dāna artham dīna anugraha kāraṇāt deva brāhmaṇa pūjā artham pitṛ pūjā artham eva ca kula artham saṃnivāsa artham kriyā nityaiḥ ca dhārmikaiḥ evamādiṣu ca anyeṣu dharma artham saṃtyajet dhanam aiśvarya sthāna lābha artham rāja vāllabhya kāraṇāt āvāhe ca vivāhe ca putrāṇām vṛtti kāraṇāt anubandham phalam hetum dṛṣṭvā vittam parityajet na adhanāḥ prāpnuvanti arthān narāḥ yatna śataiḥ api tasmāt dhanam rakṣitavyam dātavyam ca vidhānataḥ śarīra poṣaṇa arthāya āhārasya viśeṣaṇe naṭa gāndharva saṃyoge kāma yātrā vihārayoḥ manaḥ priyāṇām saṃyoge prīti dāne tathā eva ca evamādiṣu ca anyeṣu kāma artham visṛjet dhanam vicārya guṇa doṣau tu mātrayā tatra saṃtyajet rājya bhraṃśa vināśa artham durbhikṣa artham ca śobhane mahā vyādhi vimokṣa artham vārddhakasya eva kāraṇāt śatrūṇām pratikārāya sāhasaiḥ ca api amarṣaṇāt prasthāne ca anya deśa artham āpadām vipramokṣaṇe sukham arthavatām loke kṛcchrāṇām vipramokṣaṇam aśanāt indriyāṇi iva sarvam arthāt pravartate nidhānam mātrayā kuryāt anyathā vilayam vrajet evam devi manuṣyāṇām loke tu ājīvanam prati evam yuktasya lokasya laukyam vṛttam punar śṛṇu dhanyam yaśasyam āyuṣyam svargīyam paramam vacaḥ trivarge ca yathā yuktam sarveṣām saṃvidhīyate tathā saṃvartamānāḥ tu lokayoḥ hitam āpnuyuḥ kālya utthānam ca śaucam ca deva brāhmaṇa bhakta tā gurūṇām eva śuśrūṣā brāhmaṇeṣu abhivādanam pratyutthānam ca vṛddhānām deva sthāna praṇāmanam vṛddha upadeśa karaṇam śravaṇam hita pathyayoḥ poṣaṇam bhṛtya vargasya sāntva dāna parigrahaiḥ samyak vṛttam sva dāreṣu doṣāṇām pratiṣedhanam putrāṇām vinayam kuryāt tad tad kārye niyojayet varjanam ca aśubha arthānām śubhānām joṣaṇam tathā kula ucitānām dharmāṇām yathāvat paripālanam varjanam kalaha ādīnām bhaktyā saṃśamanam tathā dīnānām saṃgraham ca eva na ānṛśaṃsya vyapekṣayā abaddha anṛta ghorāṇām vacanānām vivarjanam kula saṃdhāraṇam ca eva pauruṣeṇa eva sarvaśas evamādi śubham sarvam tasya vṛttam iti smṛtam vṛddha sevī bhavet nityam hita artham jñāna kāṅkṣayā na yāceta parān dhīraḥ sva bāhu balam āśrayet sva śarīram sadā rakṣet āhāra ācārayoḥ api hitam pathyam sat āhāram jīrṇam bhuñjīta mātrayā devatā atithi satkāram kṛtvā sarvam yathāvidhi śeṣam bhuñjet śuciḥ bhūtvā na ca bhāṣeta vipriyam pratiśrayam ca pānīyam balim bhikṣām ca sarvaśas gṛhasthaḥ pravahet dadyāt gāḥ ca vatsān ca poṣayet bahis niṣkramaṇam ca eva kuryāt kāraṇatas divā viṣamān na avagāheta sva śaktyā samam ācaret yathā āya vyaya tā loke gṛhasthānām prapūjitā bhayāt vā yadi vā lobhāt na kurvīta kadā cana buddhi pūrvam samālokya dūratas guṇa doṣataḥ ātmā sākṣī bhavet nityam ātmanaḥ tu śubha aśubhe umā manasā karmaṇā vācā na ca kāṅkṣeta pātakam ime tu varṇāḥ catvāraḥ vihitāḥ svid svabhāvataḥ uta aho kriyayā varṇāḥ saṃbhavanti maheśvara maheśvaraḥ svabhāvāt eva vidyante catvāraḥ brāhmaṇa ādayaḥ eka jātyāḥ su duṣprāpam anya varṇa tvam āgatam tasmāt te saṃpravakṣyāmi tat sarvam karma pākataḥ brāhmaṇaḥ tu naraḥ bhūtvā sva jātim anupālayet dṛḍham brāhmaṇa karmāṇi veda uktāni samācaret satya ārjava paraḥ bhūtvā dāna yajña paraḥ tathā tasyām jātyām samuditaḥ jāti dharmān na hāpayet evam saṃvartamānaḥ tu kāladharmam gataḥ punar tad kṣaye brāhmaṇaḥ bhūtvā tathā eva nṛṣu jāyate evam sva karmaṇā martyaḥ sva jātim labhate punar avamatya eva tām jātim ajñāna tamasā āvṛtaḥ śūdra vat vicaret loke śūdra karma abhilāṣayā śūdraiḥ saha caran nityam śauca maṅgala varjitaḥ sa ca api kāladharma sthaḥ yama lokeṣu daṇḍitaḥ yadi jāyeta martyeṣu śūdraḥ eva abhijāyate śūdraḥ eva bhavet devi brāhmaṇaḥ api sva karmaṇā tathā eva śūdraḥ tu aparaḥ śūdra karmāṇi varjayan mantra brāhmaṇa satkartā manasā brāhmaṇa priyaḥ evaṃyukta samācāraḥ śūdraḥ api maraṇam gataḥ brāhmaṇānām kule mukhye veda svādhyāya saṃyute evam eva sadā loke śūdraḥ brāhmaṇyam āpnuyāt evam kṣatriya vaiśyāḥ ca jāti dharmeṇa saṃyutāḥ sva karmaṇā eva jāyante viśiṣṭeṣu adhameṣu ca evam jāti viparyāsaḥ pretyabhāve bhavet nṛṇām anyathā tu na śakyante loka saṃsthiti kāraṇāt tasmāt jātim viśiṣṭām tu katham cit prāpya paṇḍitaḥ umā maheśvaraḥ śobhana aśobhanam sarvam adhikāra vaśāt svayam śaṭheṣu śaṭha vat kuryāt āryeṣu ṛju vat ācaret āpatsu na avasīdet ca ghorān saṃkrāmayet parān sāmnā eva sarva kāryāṇi kartum pūrvam samārabhet anartha adharma śokān tu yathā na prāpnuyāt svayam etat vṛttam samāsādya gṛham āśritya mānavāḥ nirābādhāḥ nirudvegāḥ prāpnuvanti uttamām gatim etat janma phalam nityam sarveṣām gṛha vāsinām etat sarvam mayā proktam kim bhūyas śrotum icchasi umā mānuṣeṣu eva ye ke cit āḍhyāḥ kleśa vivarjitāḥ bhuñjānāḥ vividhān bhogān dṛśyante nirupadravāḥ apare kleśa saṃyuktāḥ daridrāḥ bhoga varjitāḥ maheśvaraḥ nyāyataḥ tvam mahābhāge śrotu kāmā asi bhāmini śṛṇu tat sarvam akhilam mānuṣāṇām hitam vacaḥ ādi sarge purā brahmā sama tvena asṛjat prajāḥ tadā tasmāt samāḥ sarve babhūvuḥ sarvatas narāḥ teṣām hānim tatas dṛṣṭvā tulyānām eva bhāmini brahmāṇam te samājagmuḥ tad kāraṇa nivedakāḥ kartum na arhasi deveśa pakṣapātam tvam īdṛśam yūyam mā kārṣṭa me roṣam sva kṛtam smarata prajāḥ yuṣmābhiḥ eva tvaṣmākam grathitam hi śubha aśubham yādṛśam kurute karma tādṛśam phalam aśnute evam vijñāta tattvāḥ te dāna dharma parāyaṇāḥ śubhāni vidhivat kṛtvā kāladharma gatāḥ punar kadaryāḥ niranukrośāḥ prāyeṇa ātma parāyaṇāḥ tādṛśāḥ maraṇam prāptāḥ punar janmani śobhane umā daridrāḥ kleśa saṃyuktāḥ bhavanti eva na saṃśayaḥ mānuṣeṣu eva ye ke cit dhana dhānya samanvitāḥ maheśvaraḥ tādṛśāḥ maraṇam prāptāḥ punar janmani śobhana phalāni tāni saṃprāpya bhuñjate na kadā cana umā maheśvaraḥ mānuṣāḥ saṃpradṛśyante tat me śaṃsitum arhasi ānṛśaṃsya pare ye tu dharma kāmāḥ ca durgatāḥ para upakāram kurvanti dīna anugraha kāraṇāt pratidadyuḥ para dhanam naṣṭam vā anyaiḥ hṛtam dhanam kāladharma vaśam prāptāḥ punarjanmani te narāḥ dharma dāna upadeśam vā kartavyam iti niścayaḥ umā mānuṣāḥ trividhāḥ deva dṛśyante satatam vibho āsīnāḥ eva bhuñjante sthāna aiśvarya parigrahaiḥ maheśvaraḥ nyāyataḥ tvam mahābhāge śrotu kāmā asi bhāmini ye loke mānuṣāḥ devi dāna dharma parāyaṇāḥ pātrāṇi vidhivat jñātvā dūratas hi anumānataḥ dānāni ca iṅgitaiḥ eva taiḥ a vijñātam eva vā punarjanmani deveśi tādṛśāḥ śobhanāḥ narāḥ āsīnāḥ eva bhuñjante bhogān sukṛta bhoginaḥ yathā yathā te dīna tvāt punar dāsyanti yācitāḥ tāvat kālam tathā devi punarjanmani te narāḥ yatnatas śrama saṃyuktāḥ punar tāni āpnuvanti uta umā maheśvaraḥ hanta te kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇu tat tvam samāhitā dharma kāryam ciram kālam vismṛtya dhana saṃyutāḥ prāṇānta kāle saṃprāpte vyādhibhiḥ ca nipīḍitāḥ ārabhante punar dharmam dātum dānāni vā narāḥ labhante pūrva dattānām phalāni śubha lakṣaṇe umā maheśvaraḥ vyādhi yoga parikliṣṭāḥ ye nirāśāḥ sva jīvite ārabhante tadā kartum dānāni śubha lakṣaṇe umā rūpa yuktāḥ pradṛśyante śubha aṅgā priya darśanāḥ maheśvaraḥ hanta te kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇu tat tvam samāhitā ye purā manujāḥ devi lajjā yuktāḥ priyaṃvadāḥ śaktāḥ su madhurāḥ nityam bhūtvā ca eva svabhāvataḥ a māṃsa bhojinaḥ ca eva sadā prāṇi dayā yutāḥ bhūmi śuddhi karāḥ vā api kāraṇāt agni pūjakāḥ evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani te narāḥ umā rūpeṇa spṛhaṇīyāḥ tu bhavanti eva na saṃśayaḥ virūpāḥ ca pradṛśyante mānuṣeṣu eva ke cana maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu kalyāṇi kāraṇam rūpa yogāt purā martyāḥ darpa ahaṃkāra saṃyutāḥ virūpa hāsakāḥ ca eva stuti nindā ādibhiḥ bhṛśam para upatāpinaḥ ca eva māṃsa ādāḥ ca tathā eva ca abhyasūyā pare ca eva aśuddhāḥ ca tathā eva ca evaṃyukta samācārāḥ yama loke su daṇḍitāḥ katham cit prāpya mānuṣyam tatra te rūpa varjitāḥ virūpāḥ saṃbhavanti eva na asti tatra vicāraṇā umā rūpa bhoga vihīnāḥ ca dṛśyante pramadā priyāḥ maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ devi saumya śīlāḥ priyaṃvadāḥ sva dāraiḥ eva saṃtuṣṭāḥ dāreṣu sama vṛttayaḥ na tu pratyādiśanti eva strī doṣān guhya saṃśritān anna pānīya dāḥ kāle nṛṇām svādu pradāḥ ca ye evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani śobhane mānuṣāḥ te bhavanti eva satatam subhagāḥ bhṛśam umā durbhagāḥ saṃpradṛśyante āḍhyāḥ bhoga yutāḥ api maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu sarvam samāhitā ye purā manujāḥ devi sva dāreṣu anapekṣayā yathā iṣṭa vṛttayaḥ ca eva nirlajjāḥ vīta saṃbhramāḥ pareṣām vipriya karāḥ vāc manaḥ kāya karmabhiḥ nirāśrayāḥ nirannādyāḥ strīṇām hṛdaya kopanāḥ evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani te narāḥ durbhagāḥ saṃbhavanti eva strīṇām hṛdaya vipriyāḥ umā na asti teṣām rati sukham sva dāreṣu api kim cana jñāna vijñāna saṃpannāḥ buddhimantaḥ vicakṣaṇāḥ durgatāḥ tu pradṛśyante yatamānāḥ yathāvidhi maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu kalyāṇe kāraṇam nirāśrayāḥ nirannādyāḥ bhṛśam ātma parāyaṇāḥ umā mūrkhāḥ loke pradṛśyante dṛḍham mūḍhāḥ vicetasaḥ jñāna vijñāna rahitāḥ samṛddhāḥ ca samantataḥ maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ devi bāliśāḥ api sarvatas samācaranti dānāni dīna anugraha kāraṇāt paṇḍitaḥ apaṇḍitaḥ vā api bhuṅkte dāna phalam naraḥ umā medhāvinaḥ śruti dharāḥ bhavanti viśada akṣarāḥ maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ devi guru śuśrūṣakāḥ bhṛśam jñāna artham te tu saṃgṛhya tīrthataḥ vidhi pūrvakam aślāghamānāḥ jñānena praśāntāḥ yata vācakāḥ tādṛśāḥ maraṇam prāptāḥ punarjanmani śobhane umā medhāvinaḥ śruti dharāḥ bhavanti viśada akṣarāḥ bahiṣkṛtāḥ pradṛśyante śruta vijñāna buddhibhiḥ maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ devi jñāna darpa samanvitāḥ ślāghamānāḥ ca tat prāpya jñāna ahaṃkāra mohitāḥ tapanti ye parān nityam jñāna ādhikyena darpitāḥ jñānāt asūyām kurvanti na sahanti eva ca aparān tādṛśāḥ maraṇam prāptāḥ punar janmani śobhane mānuṣyam su ciram prāpya tatra bodha vivarjitāḥ umā bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cid sarva kalyāṇa saṃyutāḥ vyādhi hīnāḥ nirābādhāḥ rūpa ārogya balaiḥ yutāḥ dhana dhānyena saṃpannāḥ prāsādaiḥ yāna vāhanaiḥ maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu sarvam samāhitā ye purā manujāḥ devi āḍhyāḥ vā itare api vā śruta vṛtta samāyuktāḥ dāna kāmāḥ śruta priyāḥ para iṅgita pare nityam dātavyam iti niścitāḥ satya saṃdhāḥ kṣamā śīlāḥ lobha moha vivarjitāḥ dātāraḥ pātratas dānam vrataiḥ niyama saṃyutāḥ sva duḥkham iva saṃsmṛtya para duḥkham mahātmanaḥ saumya śīlāḥ śubha ācārāḥ deva brāhmaṇa pūjakāḥ evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani śobhane mānuṣeṣu api ye jātāḥ tādṛśāḥ saṃbhavanti te yādṛśāḥ tu tvayā proktāḥ sarve kalyāṇa saṃyutāḥ rūpam dravyam balam ca āyuḥ bhoga aiśvaryam kulam śrutam iti etat sarva sādguṇyam dānāt bhavati na anyathā umā atha ke cit pradṛśyante mānuṣeṣu eva mānuṣāḥ durgatāḥ kleśa bhūyiṣṭhāḥ dāna bhoga vivarjitāḥ bhayaiḥ tribhiḥ sadā juṣṭāḥ vyādhi kṣudh bhaya pīḍitāḥ duṣkalatra abhibhūtāḥ ca satatam vighna darśakāḥ maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ devi āsuram bhāvam āśritāḥ krodha lobha ratāḥ nityam nirannādyāḥ ca niṣkriyāḥ nāstikāḥ ca eva dhūrtāḥ ca mūrkhāḥ ca ātma parāyaṇāḥ para upatāpinaḥ devi prāyaśas prāṇi nirdayāḥ evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani śobhane katham cit prāpya mānuṣyam tatra te duḥkha pīḍitāḥ śubha aśubham kṛtam karma sukha duḥkha phala udayam umā jāti andhāḥ ca eva dṛśyante jātāḥ vā naṣṭa cakṣuṣaḥ maheśvaraḥ hanta te kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇu kalyāṇi kāraṇam ye purā kāma rāgeṇa para veśmasu lolupāḥ para striyaḥ abhivīkṣante duṣṭena eva sva cakṣuṣā lakṣaṇa jñāḥ ca rūpeṣu ayathāvat pradarśakāḥ evaṃyukta samācārāḥ kāladharma gatāḥ tu te daṇḍitāḥ yama daṇḍena niraya sthāḥ ciram priye yadi ced mānuṣam janma labheran tādṛśāḥ narāḥ svabhāvataḥ vā jātāḥ vā andhāḥ eva bhavanti te akṣi roga yutā vā api na asti tatra vicāraṇā umā ādi prabhṛti martyāḥ vā jātāḥ vā api atha kāraṇāt maheśvaraḥ hanta te kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇu devi samāhitā ku vaktāraḥ tu ye devi jihvayā kaṭukam bhṛśam jihvā bādhām tathā anyeṣām kurvate kopa kāraṇāt prāyaśas anṛta bhūyiṣṭhāḥ narāḥ kārya vaśena vā teṣām jihvā pradeśa sthāḥ vyādhayaḥ saṃbhavanti te ku śrotāraḥ tu ye ca artham pareṣām karṇa nāśakāḥ umā anye mukha āśritāḥ doṣāḥ sarve ca ātma kṛtam phalam pīḍyante satatam deva mānuṣeṣu eva ke cana kukṣi pakṣa āśritaiḥ doṣaiḥ vyādhibhiḥ ca udara āśritaiḥ tīkṣṇa śūlaiḥ ca pīḍyante narāḥ duḥkha pariplutāḥ maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ devi kāma krodha yutāḥ bhṛśam ātma artham eva ca āhāram bhuñjate nirapekṣakāḥ abhakṣya āhāra dāḥ ca eva viśvastānām viṣa pradāḥ abhakṣya bhakṣya dāḥ ca eva śauca maṅgala varjitāḥ evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani śobhane katham cit prāpya mānuṣyam tatra te vyādhi pīḍitāḥ taiḥ taiḥ bahuvidha ākāraiḥ vyādhibhiḥ duḥkha pīḍitāḥ umā dṛśyante satatam deva vyādhibhiḥ mehana āśritaiḥ pīḍyamānāḥ tathā martyāḥ aśmarī śarkarā ādibhiḥ maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ devi para dāra pradharṣakāḥ kāma doṣeṇa ye dhūrtāḥ kanyāsu vidhavāsu ca balātkāreṇa gacchanti rūpa darpa dhana anvitāḥ tādṛśāḥ maraṇam prāptāḥ punar janmani śobhane yadi ced mānuṣam janma labheran te tathāvidhāḥ umā bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cit dṛśyante śoṣiṇaḥ kṛśāḥ maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ devi māṃsa lubdhāḥ su lolupāḥ ātma artham svādu gṛddhāḥ ca para bhoga upatāpinaḥ abhyasūyā pare ca eva para bhogeṣu ye narāḥ evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani śobhane śoṣa vyādhi yutāḥ tatra narāḥ dhamani saṃtatāḥ umā bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cit kliśyante kuṣṭha rogiṇaḥ maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ devi pareṣām rūpa nāśakāḥ āghāta vadha bandhaiḥ ca vṛthak daṇḍena mohitāḥ iṣṭa nāśa karāḥ ye tu apathya āhāra dāḥ narāḥ cikitsakāḥ vā duṣṭāḥ ca lobha moha samanvitāḥ nirdayāḥ prāṇi hiṃsāyām mala dāḥ citta nāśakāḥ evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani śobhane yadi vai mānuṣam janma labheran te su duḥkhitāḥ atra te kleśa saṃyuktāḥ kuṣṭha roga samanvitāḥ ke cit tvac doṣa saṃyuktāḥ vraṇa kuṣṭhaiḥ ca saṃyutāḥ śvitra kuṣṭha yutāḥ vā api bahudhā kuṣṭha saṃyutāḥ umā bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cid aṅga hīnāḥ ca paṅgavaḥ maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ devi lobha moha samāvṛtāḥ prāṇinām prāṇa hiṃsā artham aṅga hīnam prakurvate śastreṇa utkṛtya vā devi prāṇinām ceṣṭana aśakāḥ evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani śobhane umā svabhāvataḥ vā jātāḥ vā paṅgavaḥ tu bhavanti te bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cid granthibhiḥ piṭakaiḥ tathā maheśvaraḥ kliśyamānāḥ pradṛśyante tat me śaṃsitum arhasi ye purā manujāḥ devi granthibheda karāḥ nṛṇām muṣṭi prahāra paruṣāḥ nṛśaṃsāḥ pāpa kāriṇaḥ pāṭakāḥ todakāḥ ca eva śūlatunnāḥ tathā eva ca evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani śobhane umā granthibhiḥ piṭakaiḥ ca eva kliśyante bhṛśa duḥkhitāḥ bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cid pāda roga samanvitāḥ maheśvaraḥ manujāḥ devatā sthānam sva pādaiḥ bhraṃśayanti uta jānubhiḥ pārṣṇibhiḥ ca eva prāṇi hiṃsām prakurvate evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani śobhane umā bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cit dṛśyante bahavaḥ bhuvi rogaiḥ bahuvidhaiḥ deva kliśyamānāḥ su duḥkhitāḥ asamastaiḥ samastaiḥ ca āḍhyāḥ vā durgatāḥ tathā maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu kalyāṇe kāraṇam ye purā manujāḥ devi āsuram bhāvam āśritāḥ sva vaśāḥ kopana parāḥ guru vidveṣiṇaḥ tathā pareṣām duḥkha janakāḥ manaḥ vāc kāya karmabhiḥ chindan bhindan tudan eva nityam prāṇiṣu nirdayāḥ evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani śobhane yadi vai mānuṣam janma labheran te tathāvidhāḥ ke cit ślīpada saṃyuktāḥ ke cid kāsa samanvitāḥ jvara atisāra tṛṣṇābhiḥ pīḍyamānāḥ tathā apare pāda rogaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ vraṇa kuṣṭha bhagaṃdaraiḥ āḍhyāḥ vā durgatāḥ vā api dṛśyante vyādhi pīḍitāḥ umā hrasvāṅgāḥ ca eva vakrāṅgāḥ kubjāḥ vāmanakāḥ tathā apare mānuṣāḥ deva dṛśyante kuṇi bāhavaḥ maheśvaraḥ tulā doṣam tathā devi dhṛta māneṣu nityaśas argha apakaraṇam ca eva sarveṣām kraya vikraye aṅga doṣa karāḥ ye tu pareṣām kopa kāraṇāt māṃsa ādāḥ ca eva ye mūrkhāḥ ayathāvat vṛthak sadā evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani śobhane umā hrasva aṅgāḥ vāmanāḥ ca eva kubjāḥ ca eva bhavanti te bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cit dṛśyante mānuṣeṣu vai unmattāḥ ca piśācāḥ ca paryaṭantaḥ yatas tatas maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ devi darpa ahaṃkāra saṃyutāḥ vṛddhān gurūn ca ye mūrkhāḥ vṛthak eva apahasanti ca śauṇḍāḥ vidagdhāḥ śāstreṣu tathā eva anṛta vādinaḥ evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani śobhane unmattāḥ ca piśācāḥ ca bhavanti eva na saṃśayaḥ umā bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cit nirapatyāḥ su duḥkhitāḥ maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ devi sarva prāṇiṣu nirdayāḥ ghnanti bālān ca bhuñjante mṛgāṇām pakṣiṇām api guru vidveṣiṇaḥ ca eva para putra abhyasūyakāḥ pitṛ pūjām na kurvanti yathoktam ca aṣṭaka ādibhiḥ evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani śobhane umā putra śoka yutā vā api na asti tatra vicāraṇā bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cid pradṛśyante su duḥkhitāḥ udvega vāsa niratāḥ sa udvegāḥ ca yatas tatas nitya śoka samāviṣṭāḥ durgatāḥ ca tathā eva ca maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ nityam utkocana parāyaṇāḥ ṛṇaiḥ vṛddhim ca ye kṛtvā daridrebhyaḥ yatheṣṭataḥ ṛṇa artham abhigacchanti satatam vṛddhi rūpakāḥ udvijante hi tān dṛṣṭvā dhārakāḥ tu atha kāraṇāt ye śvabhiḥ krīḍamānāḥ ca trāsayanti vane mṛgān prāṇi hiṃsām tathā devi kurvanti ca yatas tatas yeṣām gṛheṣu vai śvānaḥ trāsayanti vṛthak narān evaṃyukta samācārāḥ kāladharma gatāḥ punar pīḍitāḥ yama daṇḍena niraya sthāḥ ciram priye katham cit prāpya mānuṣyam tatra te duḥkha saṃyutāḥ ku deśe duḥkha bhūyiṣṭhe vyāghāta śata saṃkule umā bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cid aiśvarya sthāna saṃyutāḥ maheśvaraḥ apātrebhyaḥ ca ye dānam śauca maṅgala varjitāḥ dadati eva ca ye mūrkhāḥ ślāghayā avajñayā api vā evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani śobhane umā klībāḥ napuṃsakāḥ ca eva dṛśyante paṇḍakāḥ tathā nīca karma ratāḥ nīcāḥ nīca saukhyāḥ tathā bhuvi maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu kalyāṇe kāraṇam ye purā manujāḥ bhūtvā ghora karma ratāḥ tathā puṃstva upaghātinaḥ ca eva
