narāṇām kopa kāraṇāt ye dhūrtāḥ strīṣu gacchanti ayathāvat yatheṣṭataḥ kāma vighna karāḥ ye tu dveṣa paiśunya kāraṇāt evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani śobhane daṇḍitāḥ yama daṇḍena niraya sthāḥ ciram priye yadi ced mānuṣam janma labheran te tathāvidhāḥ klībāḥ varṣa varāḥ ca eva paṇḍakāḥ ca bhavanti te nīca karma ratāḥ loke nirlajjāḥ vīta saṃbhramāḥ strīṇām api tathā devi yathā puṃsām tu karma jam umā bhagavan devadeveśa śūlapāṇe vṛṣadhvaja puṃścalyaḥ iti yāḥ strīṣu nīca vṛtta ratāḥ smṛtāḥ maheśvaraḥ yāḥ purā pramadāḥ devi buddhi moha samanvitāḥ kāma rāga samāyuktāḥ patīn apacaranti vai pratikūla parāḥ yāḥ tu patīn prati yathā tathā śaucam lajjām tu vismṛtya yatheṣṭa paricārakāḥ evaṃyukta samācārāḥ yama loke su daṇḍitāḥ yadi ced mānuṣam janma labheran tāḥ tathāvidhāḥ bahu sādhāraṇāḥ evam puṃścalyaḥ ca bhavanti tāḥ pauṃścalyam yat tu tat vṛttam strīṇām kaṣṭatamam smṛtam tatas prabhṛti tāḥ devi patanti eva na saṃśayaḥ umā śocanti ced tu tat vṛttam manasā hitam āpnuyuḥ dṛśyante mānuṣe loke sarva kalyāṇa varjitāḥ maheśvaraḥ kuṭumbam tatra vai pateḥ nāśayanti vṛthak tathā viṣa dāḥ ca agni dāḥ ca eva patīn prati su nirdayāḥ anyāsām hi patīn yānti sva pati dveṣa kāraṇāt evaṃyukta samācārāḥ yama loke su daṇḍitāḥ niraya sthāḥ ciram kālam katham cit prāpya mānuṣam umā liṅginyaḥ saṃpradṛśyante pāṣaṇḍam dharmam āśritāḥ maheśvaraḥ yāḥ purā bhāva doṣeṇa lobha moha samanvitāḥ para dravya pare lobhāt pareṣām dravya hārakāḥ abhyasūyā parāḥ yāḥ tu sapatnīnām pradūṣakāḥ īrṣyā parāḥ kopanāḥ ca bandhūnām viphalāḥ sadā evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani tāḥ priye apalakṣaṇa saṃpannāḥ pāṣaṇḍam dharmam āśritāḥ umā striyaḥ pravrāja śīlāḥ ca bhavanti eva na saṃśayaḥ bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cid kāru vṛttim samāśritāḥ pradṛśyante manuṣyeṣu nīca karma ratāḥ janāḥ maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ devi stabdhāḥ māna yutāḥ bhṛśam darpa ahaṃkāra saṃyuktāḥ kevala ātma parāyaṇāḥ tādṛśāḥ manujāḥ devi punarjanmani śobhane kāravaḥ naṭa gandharvāḥ saṃbhavanti yathā tathā nāpitāḥ bandinaḥ ca eva tathā vaitālikāḥ priye evaṃbhūtāḥ tu adhas vṛttim jīvanti āśritya mānavāḥ para prasādana karāḥ te paraiḥ kṛta vetanāḥ umā dāsa bhūtāḥ pradṛśyante sarva karmakarāḥ bhṛśam āghāta bhartsana sahāḥ pīḍyamānāḥ ca sarvaśas maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu kalyāṇe kāraṇam ye purā manujāḥ devi pareṣām vitta hārakāḥ ṛṇa vṛddhi karam kuryāt nyāsadattam tathā eva ca nikṣepa kāraṇāt dattam pareṣām dravya hāriṇaḥ pramādāt vismṛtam naṣṭam pareṣām dhana hārakāḥ tādṛśāḥ maraṇam prāptāḥ daṇḍitāḥ yama śāsanaiḥ dāsa bhūtāḥ bhavanti eva janma prabhṛti mānavāḥ teṣām karmāṇi kurvanti yeṣām te dhana hārakāḥ ā samāpteḥ sva pāpasya kurvanti iti viniścayaḥ paśu bhūtāḥ tathā ca anye bhavanti dhana hārakāḥ tat tathā kṣīyate karma teṣām pūrva aparādha jam kim tu mokṣa vidhiḥ teṣām sarvathā tad prasādanam mokṣa kāmī yathānyāyam kurvan karmāṇi sarvaśas bhartuḥ prasādam ākāṅkṣet āghātān sarvadā sahan prīti pūrvam tu yaḥ bhartrā muktaḥ muktaḥ sva pāpataḥ tathābhūtān karmakarān sadā saṃpoṣayet patiḥ yathārham kārayet karma daṇḍam kāraṇataḥ kṣipet vṛddhān bālān tathā kṣīṇān pālayan dharmam āpnuyāt umā bhagavat mānuṣeṣu eva mānuṣāḥ sama darśanāḥ caṇḍālāḥ iva dṛśyante sparśa mātreṇa dūṣakāḥ nīca karma karāḥ deva sarveṣām mala hārakāḥ durgatāḥ kleśa bhūyiṣṭhāḥ virūpāḥ duṣṭa cetasaḥ maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi tvam ekāgra manāḥ śṛṇu ye purā manujāḥ ghorāḥ atimāna yutāḥ bhṛśam ātma saṃbhāvanā yuktāḥ stabdhāḥ darpa samanvitāḥ praṇāmam na tu kurvanti gurūṇām api pāpakāḥ parān saṃnāmayanti eva ājñayā ātmani ye balāt pānapāḥ sarva bhakṣāḥ ca paruṣāḥ kaṭukāḥ narāḥ evaṃyukta samācārāḥ daṇḍitāḥ yama śāsanaiḥ katham cit prāpya mānuṣyam caṇḍālāḥ saṃbhavanti te nīca karma ratāḥ ca eva sarveṣām mala hārakāḥ pareṣām vandana parāḥ te bhavanti avamānitāḥ virūpāḥ pāpa yoni sthāḥ sparśanāt api varjitāḥ kuvṛttim upajīvanti bhūtvā te rajaka ādayaḥ purā ati māna doṣāt tu bhuñjate sva kṛtam phalam tān api avasthā kṛpaṇān caṇḍālān api buddhimān umā caṇḍālāḥ api tām jātim śocantaḥ śuddhim āpnuyuḥ bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cid āśā pāśa śataiḥ vṛtāḥ pareṣām dvāri tiṣṭhanti pratiṣiddhāḥ praveśane draṣṭum jñāpayitum ca eva na labhante ca yatnataḥ maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ devi aiśvarya sthāna saṃyutāḥ dvārāṇi na dadati eva dveṣa lobha ādibhiḥ vṛtāḥ avasthā moha saṃyuktāḥ sva artha mātra parāyaṇāḥ lubdhāḥ bhoga yutāḥ vā api sarveṣām niṣphalāḥ bhṛśam api śaktāḥ na kuryuḥ ye para anugraha kāraṇāt evam yukta samācārāḥ punarjanmani śobhane yadi ced mānuṣam janma labheran te tathāvidhāḥ durgatāḥ duravasthāḥ ca karma vyākṣepa saṃyutāḥ rājñām vā rājamātrāṇām dvāri tiṣṭhanti vāritāḥ umā praveṣṭum api te dvāri bahis tiṣṭhanti kāṅkṣayā bhagavat mānuṣe loke mānuṣeṣu bahuṣu api sahasā naṣṭa sarvasvāḥ bhraṣṭa kośa parigrahāḥ dṛśyante mānuṣāḥ ke cid rāja cora udaka ādibhiḥ maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ devi āsuram bhāvam āśritāḥ pareṣām vṛtti nāśam tu kurvate dveṣa lobhataḥ utkocana pare ca eva piśunāḥ ca tathāvidhāḥ para dravya harāḥ ghorāḥ cauryāt vā anyena karmaṇā nirdayāḥ niranukrośāḥ pareṣām vṛtti nāśakāḥ nāstika anṛta bhūyiṣṭhāḥ para dravya apahāriṇaḥ evaṃyukta samācārāḥ daṇḍitāḥ yama śāsanaiḥ niraya sthāḥ ciram kālam tatra duḥkha samanvitāḥ yadi ced mānuṣam janma labheran te tathāvidhāḥ kaṣṭam ca prāpnuvanti eva kāraṇa akāraṇāt api umā nāśam vināśam dravyāṇām upaghātān ca sarvaśas bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cid bāndhavaiḥ sahasā pṛthak kāraṇa akāraṇāt eva sahasā prāṇa nāśanam śastreṇa vā anyathā vā api prāpnuvanti vadham narāḥ maheśvaraḥ āsurāḥ prāyaśas mūrkhāḥ prāṇi hiṃsā priyāḥ bhṛśam nirdayāḥ prāṇi hiṃsāyām tathā prāṇa vighātakāḥ viśvasta ghātakāḥ ca eva tathā supta vighātakāḥ prāyaśas anṛta bhūyiṣṭhāḥ nāstikāḥ māṃsa bhojinaḥ evam yukta samācārāḥ prāṇi dharma gatāḥ punar daṇḍitāḥ yama daṇḍena niraya sthāḥ ciram priye yadi ced mānuṣam janma labheran te tathāvidhāḥ āḍhyāḥ vā durgatāḥ vā api bhuñjate sva kṛtam phalam suptāḥ mattāḥ ca viśvastāḥ tathā te prāpnuvanti uta prāṇa ābādha kṛtam duḥkham bāndhavaiḥ sahasā pṛthak umā putra dāra vināśam vā śastreṇa anyena vā vadham bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cid rājabhiḥ nīti kovidaiḥ daṇḍyante mānuṣe loke mānuṣāḥ satatam bhuvi maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ devi manujān ca itarān ca vā kliṣṭa ghātena nighnanti prāṇān prāṇiṣu nirdayāḥ asurāḥ ghora karmāṇaḥ krūra daṇḍa vadha priyāḥ ye daṇḍayanti a daṇḍyān tu rājānaḥ kopa mohitāḥ hiṃsā vihārāḥ puruṣāḥ māṃsa ādāḥ nāstikāḥ śubhe ke cit strī puruṣa ghnāḥ ca guru ghnāḥ ca tathā priye evam yukta samācārāḥ prāṇi dharma gatāḥ punar daṇḍitāḥ yama daṇḍena niraya sthāḥ ciram priye pūrva deha kṛtam karma bhuñjate tat iha prajāḥ eṣā vyavasthitiḥ devi mānuṣeṣu eva dṛśyate na ṛṣīṇām na devānām amara tvāt tapaḥ balāt umā na tathā mānuṣāṇām syāt antardhāya bhavet hi tam kimartham mānuṣāḥ loke daṇḍyante pṛthivīśvaraiḥ kṛta aparādham uddiśya hantā hartā ayam iti uta putra arthī putra kāma iṣṭyā iha eva labhate sutān tena eva hi śarīreṇa bhuñjānāḥ karmaṇām phalam maheśvaraḥ etat me saṃśaya sthānam tat tvam śaṃsitum arhasi sthāne saṃśayitam devi tat tvam śṛṇu samāhitā teṣām tad pūrvakam karma daṇḍyate yatra rājabhiḥ daihikam duṣkṛtam teṣām hetuḥ bhavati śāsane aparādha apadeśena rājā daṇḍayati prajāḥ ihaloke vyavasthā artham rājbhiḥ daṇḍanam smṛtam udvejana artham śeṣāṇām aparādham tam uddiśan purā kṛta phalam daṇḍaḥ daṇḍyamānasya tat dhruvam umā prāk eva ca mayā proktam tatra niḥsaṃśayā bhava bhagavan bhuvi martyānām daṇḍitānām nareśvaraiḥ daṇḍena eva tu tena iha pāpa nāśaḥ bhavet na vā maheśvaraḥ etat mayā saṃśayitam tat bhavān chettum arhati sthāne saṃśayitam devi śṛṇu tat tvam samāhitā ye nṛpaiḥ daṇḍitāḥ bhūmau aparādha apadeśataḥ a daṇḍitāḥ vā ye mithyā martyāḥ vā daṇḍitāḥ bhuvi tān yamaḥ daṇḍayati eva sa hi veda kṛta akṛtam na atikramet yamam kaḥ cit karma kṛtvā iha mānuṣaḥ rājā yamaḥ ca kurvāte daṇḍa mātram tu śobhane ubhābhyām yama rājabhyām daṇḍitaḥ a daṇḍitaḥ api vā paścāt karma phalam bhuṅkte narake mānuṣeṣu vā umā kimartham duṣkṛtam kṛtvā mānuṣāḥ bhuvi nityaśas punar tad karma nāśāya prāyaścittāni kurvate prāyaścittāni ca anyāni pāpa nāśāya kurvate maheśvaraḥ tasmāt mama saṃśayaḥ jātaḥ tvam tam chettum iha arhasi sthāne saṃśayitam devi śṛṇu tat tvam samāhitā saṃśayaḥ hi mahān eṣa pūrveṣām ca manīṣiṇām abhisaṃdhāya vā nityam anyathā vā yadṛcchayā abhisaṃdhi kṛtasya iha nā eva nāśaḥ asti karmaṇaḥ anyathā yat kṛtam pāpam pramādāt vā yadṛcchayā prāyaścitta aśvamedhābhyām śodhanāt tu praṇaśyati loka saṃvyavahāra artham prāyaścitta ādiḥ iṣyate umā bhagavan devadeveśa mānuṣāḥ ca itare api mriyante bahudhā loke kāraṇa akāraṇāt api maheśvaraḥ ye purā manujāḥ devi kāraṇa akāraṇāt api yathā asubhiḥ viyojyante prāṇinaḥ prāṇi nirdayaiḥ viṣadaḥ tu viṣeṇa eva śastraiḥ śastreṇa ghātakaḥ evam eva yathā loke mānuṣāḥ ghnanti mānuṣān kāraṇaiḥ eva te tena tathā sva prāṇa nāśanam bhūyas tava samāsena kathayiṣyāmi tat śṛṇu yena eva kāraṇena api karma yat tu śubha aśubham prāpnuvanti narāḥ pretya niḥsaṃdeham śubha aśubham na śakyam karma ca ā bhoktum sa deva asura mānuṣaiḥ umā kathitam śrotu kāmāyāḥ kim bhūyas śrotum icchasi prasādāt te mahādeva śrutā me karmaṇām gatiḥ saṃgṛhītam ca tat sarvam tattvataḥ amṛta saṃnibham kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ ca iha na nāśaḥ asti iti niścayaḥ karmaṇām gatim āśritya saṃśayān moktum arhasi maheśvaraḥ umā tat sarvam nirviśaṅkā tvam pṛccha mām śubha lakṣaṇe kṛtvā tat puruṣaḥ karma śubham vā yadi vā itarat karmaṇaḥ sva kṛtasya iha kadā bhuṅkte phalam punar maheśvaraḥ sthāne saṃśayitam devi tat hi guhyatamam śṛṇu tvad priya artham pravakṣyāmi deva guhyam śubha ānane pūrva deha kṛtam karma bhuñjate tat iha prajāḥ eṣā vyavasthitiḥ devi mānuṣeṣu eva dṛśyate devānām asurāṇām ca amara tvāt tapaḥ balāt ekena eva śarīreṇa bhujyate karmaṇām phalam umā bhagavan bhaga netra ghna mānuṣāṇām viceṣṭitam loke graha kṛtam sarvam matvā karma śubha aśubham maheśvaraḥ sthāne saṃśayitam devi śṛṇu tattva viniścayam nakṣatrāṇi grahāḥ ca eva śubha aśubha nivedakāḥ mānavānām mahābhāge na tu karmakarāḥ svayam prajānām tu hita arthāya śubha aśubha vidhim prati graha sāmye śubham kuryāt jātyām jātyām purā kṛtam umā iti te kathitam sarvam viśaṅkām jahi śobhane bhagavan vividham karma kṛtvā jantuḥ śubha aśubham kim tayoḥ pūrvakataram bhuṅkte janmāntare punar maheśvaraḥ sthāne saṃśayitam devi tat te vakṣyāmi tattvāt bhuñjānāḥ ca eva dṛśyante kramaśas bhuvi mānavāḥ ṛddhim hānim sukham duḥkham abhayam bhayam eva ca duḥkhāni anubhavanti āḍhyāḥ daridrāḥ ca sukhāni ca yaugapadyāt ca bhuñjānāḥ dṛśyante loka sākṣikam śubha aśubhānām ādhikyāt karmaṇā tatra sevyate tatra api su mahat kṛtvā pūrvam alpam punar śubhe umā etat te sarvam ākhyātam bhūyas śrotum kim icchasi jātāḥ jātāḥ na tiṣṭhanti tat me śaṃsitum arhasi maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu tattvam samāhitā ātma karma kṣayāt deham yathā muñcanti tat śṛṇu śarīra ātma samāhāraḥ jantuḥ iti abhidhīyate tat tu kāla vaśāt loke jīrṇam bhavati śobhane kālaḥ chinatti ca āyūṃṣi dina māsa ṛtu hāyanaiḥ kālaḥ pacati bhūtāni kālena ākulitam jagat kālam na atikrameran hi sa deva asura mānavāḥ yathā ākāśe na tiṣṭheta dravyam kim cit acetanam tathā dhāvati kālaḥ ayam kṣaṇam kim cit na tiṣṭhati evam kālena saṃkrāntam śarīram jarjarīkṛtam akarma yogyam saṃśīrṇam tyaktvā dehī tatas vrajet nityasya anitya saṃtyāgāt loke tat maraṇam viduḥ sa punar jāyate anyatra śarīram navam āviśan umā bhagavan prāṇinām bālāḥ dṛśyante maraṇam gatāḥ ati vṛddhāḥ ca jīvantaḥ dṛśyante cira jīvinaḥ kevalam kāla maraṇam na pramāṇam maheśvara maheśvaraḥ tasmāt me saṃśayam brūhi prāṇinām jīva kāraṇam śṛṇu tad kāraṇam devi nirṇayaḥ tu ekaḥ eva saḥ jīrṇa tva mātram kurute kālaḥ deham na pātayet jīrṇe karmaṇi saṃghātaḥ svayam eva viśīryate pūrva karma pramāṇena jīvitam mṛtyuḥ eva vā yāvat pūrva kṛtam karma tāvat jīvati mānavaḥ tadvat kāla vaśāt bālāḥ mriyante bhoga saṃkṣayāt jīvanti cira vṛddhāḥ ca tathā karma pramāṇataḥ umā maheśvaraḥ alpa āyuṣaḥ narāḥ kena tat me śaṃsitum arhasi śṛṇu tat sarvam akhilam guhyam pathyataram nṛṇām ye narāḥ vṛtta saṃpannāḥ bhavanti cira jīvinaḥ gurūṇām nitya śuśrūṣā vṛddhānām api pūjanam śaucam ca akārya saṃtyāgaḥ sadā pathyasya bhojanam evamādi śubham vṛttam narāṇām dīrgha jīvinām tapasā brahmacaryeṇa rasāyana niṣevaṇāt svarge vā mānuṣe vā api ciram tiṣṭhanti dhārmikāḥ apare pāpa karmāṇaḥ prāyaśas anṛta vādinaḥ hiṃsā priyāḥ guru dviṣṭāḥ niṣkriyāḥ śauca varjitāḥ nāstikāḥ ghora karmāṇaḥ satatam māṃsa pānapāḥ pāpa ācārāḥ guru dveṣāḥ kopanāḥ kalaha priyāḥ evam eva aśubha ācārāḥ tiṣṭhanti niraye ciram tasmāt alpa āyuṣaḥ martyāḥ tādṛśāḥ saṃbhavanti te agamya deśa gamanāt apathyānām ca bhojanāt āyuḥ kṣayaḥ bhavet nṝṇām āyuḥ kṣaya karāḥ hi te umā ātmanaḥ jāti saṃbandham brūhi strī puruṣa antare strī prāṇaḥ puruṣa prāṇaḥ ekaḥ sa pṛthak eva vā maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu sarvam samāhitā puṃs tvam strī tvam iti prāṇe sthitiḥ na asti śubha īkṣaṇe nirvikārī sadā eva ātmā strī tvam puṃs tvam na ca ātmani karma prakāreṇa tathā jātyām jātyām prajāyate akartā ca avikārī ca nityaḥ ca puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ strī śarīra kṛtam karma strī bhāvena upabhujyate puruṣeṇa kṛtam karma puruṣeṇa eva bhujyate śarīram karma nānātvāt dṛśyate viparīta vat kṛtvā tu pauruṣam karma strī pumān api jāyate umā strī bhāva yuj pumān kṛtvā karmaṇā pramadā bhavet maheśvaraḥ śṛṇu bhāmini kartāram ātmā hi na ca karma kṛt śarīram prāṇinām loke yathā pitta kapha anilaiḥ sattvam rajaḥ tamaḥ iti guṇāḥ tu ete śarīriṇaḥ prakāśa ātmakam eteṣām sattvam satatam iṣyate satyam prāṇi dayā śaucam śreyaḥ prītiḥ kṣamā damaḥ anṛtam ca eva pāruṣyam śruti vidveṣa tā bhṛśam hiṃsā para tvam nāstikyam nidrā ālasya bhayāni ca tasmāt guṇa mayaḥ sarvaḥ kārya ārambhaḥ śubha aśubhaḥ sāttvikāḥ puṇya lokeṣu rājasāḥ mānuṣe pade umā tiryagyonau ca narake tiṣṭheyuḥ tāmasāḥ narāḥ svayam praṇaśyate dehī tat me śaṃsitum arhasi tat aham te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu kalyāṇe kāraṇam karma kṣaye tu saṃprāpte prāṇinām dehadhāriṇām tad nimittam śarīrī tu śarīram prāpta saṃkṣayam umā yathāyogam phalam jantuḥ prāpnoti iti viniścayaḥ pareṣām vipriyam kurvan yathā saṃprāpnuyāt śubham tat api asti mahābhāge abhisaṃdhi phalam nṛṇām hita artham duḥkham anyeṣām kṛtvā aśubham avāpnuyāt daṇḍayan bhartsayan rājā prajāḥ puṇyam avāpnuyāt guruḥ saṃtarjayan śiṣyān bhartā bhṛtya janam svakam unmārga pratipannān ca śāstā dharma phalam labhet yajña artham paśu hiṃsām ca kurvan api na hiṃsakaḥ umā etat kṛtvā tu pāpiṣṭhān doṣān na prāpnuyāt kva cit bhagavan sarva martyānām jñānī bhavati sattamaḥ nāradaḥ kṛtrimam tat svabhāvam vā tat me śaṃsitum arhasi maheśvaraḥ catasraḥ jātayaḥ tatra prajānām kramaśas yathā teṣām udbheda jāḥ vṛkṣāḥ latāḥ vallyaḥ ca vīrudhaḥ daṃśa yūka ādayaḥ ca anye sveda jāḥ kṛmi jātayaḥ pakṣiṇaḥ chidra karṇāḥ ca prāṇinaḥ tu aṇḍajāḥ smṛtāḥ mṛga vyāla manuṣyān ca viddhi teṣām jarāyu jān evam caturvidhām jātim ātmā saṃśritya tiṣṭhati sparśena eka indriyeṇa ātmā tiṣṭhati udbheda jeṣu vai śarīra sparśa rūpābhyām kleda jeṣu api tiṣṭhati pañcabhiḥ ca indriya dvāraiḥ jīvanti aṇḍa jarāyu jāḥ śīta uṣṇayoḥ tu saṃyogāt jāyante kleda jāḥ priye aṇḍa jāḥ ca api saṃyogāt jāyante kṣetra bījayoḥ śukla śoṇita saṃyogāt saṃbhavanti jarāyu jāḥ jarāyu jānām sarveṣām mānuṣam padam uttamam dharma adharmau ca vijñānam na eva pakṣi mṛga ādiṣu buddhiḥ sattvam dhṛtiḥ lajjā jñānam vijñānam eva ca ūha apohau ca martyeṣu guṇāḥ nānāvidhāḥ smṛtāḥ mānuṣam hi padam tasmāt viśiṣṭam iha lakṣyate mahatā dharma kāryeṇa prāpyate janma mānuṣam atas param tama utpattim śṛṇu devi samāhitā dvividham hi tamaḥ loke śārvaram deha jam tathā jyotirbhiḥ ca agninā loke nāśam gacchati śārvaram tapaḥ cakāra vipulam lokakartā pitāmahaḥ caturaḥ tu samudbhūtāḥ vedāḥ sa aṅgāḥ saha uttarāḥ tān labdhvā mumude brahmā lokānām hita kāraṇāt kārya akāryam idam ca iti vācya avācyam idam tu iti paśubhiḥ nirviśeṣam tu ceṣṭante mānuṣāḥ tu iti yajña ādīnām samārambhaḥ śrutena eva vidhīyate prīti yuktāḥ punar devāḥ mānuṣāṇām phalanti uta jñānāt viśiṣṭam jantūnām na asti lokatraye api ca sahajam tat pradhānam syāt aparam kṛtrimam śrutam saṃpragṛhya śrutam sarvam kṛtakṛtyāḥ bhavanti uta upari iva ca martyānām deva vat saṃprakāśate kāmam krodham bhayam darpam ajñānam ca eva buddhi jam tat śrutam nudati kṣipram yathā vāyuḥ balāhakān alpa mātram kṛtaḥ dharmaḥ bhavet jñānavatām mahān parāvara jñaḥ bhūtānām jñānavān tattva vid bhavet umā evam śruta phalam sarvam kathitam te śubha īkṣaṇe bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cit jāti smaraṇa saṃyutāḥ maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi kāraṇam śṛṇu śobhane ye mṛtāḥ sahasā martyāḥ jāyante sahasā punar teṣām paurāṇikaḥ abhyāsaḥ kaṃ cit kālam sa tiṣṭhati tasmāt jātismarāḥ loke jāyante bodha saṃyutāḥ teṣām vivardhatām saṃjñā svapna vat sā praṇaśyati umā para lokasya ca astitve mūḍhānām kāraṇam ca tat bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cit mṛtāḥ bhūtvā hi saṃprati nivartamānāḥ dṛśyante deheṣu eva punar narāḥ maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi kāraṇam śṛṇu śobhane prāṇaiḥ viyojyamānānām bahu tvāt prāṇinām kṣaye tathā eva nāma sāmānyāt yamadūtāḥ nṛṇām bhuvi vahanti te kva cit mohāt anyān te iti yāmikāḥ nirvikāram hi tat sarvam yamaḥ veda kṛta akṛtam tasmāt saṃyaminīm prāpya yamena ete vimokṣitāḥ umā bhagavan supta mātrāṇām martyānām svapna darśanam maheśvaraḥ suptānām tu punar ceṣṭā svapnaḥ iti abhidhīyate anāgatam atikrāntam paśyate saṃcarat manaḥ nimittam ca bhavet tasmāt prāṇinām svapna darśanam umā evam te kathitam sarvam bhūyas śrotum kim icchasi apare ceṣṭayā ca iti dṛṣṭvā pratyakṣataḥ kriyām tat tvam vada mahādeva śrotum kautūhalam hi mama maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu tat tvam samāhitā lakṣyate dvividham karma mānuṣāṇām śubha ānane purākṛtam tayoḥ ekam aihikam ca param tathā aihikam dṛṣṭa karaṇam tat mānuṣam iti smṛtam mānuṣam ca kriyā mātram daivāt saṃbhavate phalam evam tat ubhayam sarvam mānuṣam vidyate nṛṣu kṛṣau tu dṛśyate karma karṣaṇam vapanam tathā ropaṇam ca eva lavanam yat ca anyat pauruṣam smṛtam kāle vṛṣṭiḥ suvāpaḥ ca prarohaḥ paktiḥ eva ca daivāt asiddhiḥ ca bhavet duṣkṛtam ca asti pauruṣe umā katham ātmā sadā garbham saṃviśet karma kāraṇāt maheśvaraḥ śṛṇu bhāmini tat guhyam guhyānām paramam priye adṛśyaḥ hi sa devānām śaighryāt saukṣmyāt nirāśrayāt atimātra atimāyānām ātma māyā sadā iṣyate saḥ ayam caturvidhām jātim saṃviśati ātma māyayā maithunam śoṇitam bījam daivam ca api atra kāraṇam bīja śoṇita saṃyogaḥ yadā saṃbhavate śubhe tad ātmā viśate garbham evam aṇḍa jarāyu je śīta uṣṇayoḥ tu saṃyoge kleda jeṣu avatiṣṭhati bīja bhūmi jalānām tu yogāt udbheda jeṣu ca evam saṃyoga kāle tu ātmā garbha tvam eyivān kalalāt jāyate piṇḍam piṇḍāt peśī arbudam bhavet evam strī puruṣa saṃyogam pauruṣam viddhi bhāmini pañcabhūta sthitiḥ ca eva jyotiṣām ayanam tathā tādṛśam kāraṇam daivam śubham vā yadi vā itarat yādṛśam ca ātmanā śakyam tat pauruṣam iti smṛtam tayoḥ samāhitam karma śīta uṣṇam yugapad tathā pauruṣam tu tayoḥ pūrvam ārabdhavyam vijānatā ātmanā na eva śakyam hi na tathā kīrtim āpnuyāt khananāt mathanāt loke jala agni prāpaṇam yathā tathā puruṣakāre tu daiva saṃpad samāhitā asurāḥ rākṣasāḥ ca eva manyante loka nāyakāḥ na paśyante ca te pāpāḥ kevalam māṃsa bhakṣakāḥ pracchāditam hi tat sarvam guhya kāmāḥ hi devatāḥ ādi kāle prajāḥ sarvāḥ kṛtvā karma śubha aśubham bhuñjate paśyamānāḥ te vṛttāntam lokayoḥ dvayoḥ yathā eva ātma kṛtam vidyuḥ deśa antara gatāḥ narāḥ acireṇa eva kālena svargaḥ saṃpūritaḥ tadā devānām api saṃbādham dṛṣṭvā brahmā api acintayat saṃcarante katham devāḥ mānuṣāḥ praviśanti hi kāma krodhau ca tad kāle mānuṣeṣu nyapātayat purā kṛtasya avijñānāt kāma krodha abhipīḍanāt na etat asti iti manvānāḥ vikārān cakrire punar akārya ādīn mahā doṣān ārabhanta ātma kāraṇāt lokānām ca eva vedānām kṣayāya eva tadā priye narakāḥ pūritāḥ ca āsan prāṇibhiḥ pāpa kāribhiḥ punar eva tu tat dṛṣṭvā lokakartā pitāmahaḥ acintayat tam eva artham lokānām hita kāraṇāt cintayitvā tadā brahmā jñānena tapasā priye umā akarot jñāna dṛśyam tu para lokam na cakṣuṣā bhagavat mṛta mātraḥ tu yaḥ ayam jātaḥ iti smṛtaḥ garbha ādau eva saṃviṣṭaḥ ātmā iti bhagavat matam maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu tat tvam samāhitā sūtikāyāḥ hita artham ca mohana artham ca dehinām māyā sā yāmikā nāma yat janma maraṇa antare umā svabhāvāt jāyate sarvam yathā vṛkṣa phalam tathā tapaḥ dāna ādi yat karma tatra ātmā dṛśyate vṛthak parokṣa vacanam śrutvā na pratyakṣasya darśanāt tat sarvam na asti vā asti iti saṃśaya sthāḥ tathā apare nāradaḥ praśnam etam tu pṛcchatyām rudrāṇyām pariṣad tadā maheśvaraḥ kautūhala yutā śrotum samāhita manāḥ bhavat na etat asti mahābhāge yat vadanti iha nāstikāḥ etat eva abhiśastānām śruti vidveṣiṇām matam sarvam artham śrutam dṛṣṭam yat prāk uktam mayā tava tadā prabhṛti martyānām śrutam āśritya paṇḍitāḥ kāmān saṃchindya parighān dhṛtyā vai parama asinā abhiyānti eva te svargam paśyantaḥ karmaṇām phalam buddhiḥ śraddhā ca śuśrūṣā kāraṇāni hita eṣiṇām anye karaṇa hīna tvāt nāstikyam bhāvam āśritāḥ śruta vidveṣiṇaḥ mūrkhāḥ nāstikāḥ dṛḍha niścayāḥ niṣkriyāḥ ca nirannādyāḥ patanti eva adhamām gatim eṣā brahma kṛtā māyā durvijñeyā sura asuraiḥ kim punar mānuṣaiḥ loke jñātu kāmaiḥ sva karmabhiḥ kevalam śraddhayā devi śruti mātra niviṣṭayā umā kīdṛśāḥ yama daṇḍāḥ te kīdṛśāḥ paricārakāḥ kīdṛśam bhavanam tasya katham daṇḍayati prajāḥ maheśvaraḥ śṛṇu kalyāṇe tat sarvam yat tat devi manaḥ priyam dakṣiṇasyām diśi śubhe yamasya sadanam mahat vicitram ramaṇīyam ca nānā bhāva samanvitam pitṛbhiḥ preta saṃghaiḥ ca yamadūtaiḥ ca saṃtatam prāṇi saṃghaiḥ su bahubhiḥ karma vaśyaiḥ tu pūritam māyayā satatam vetti prāṇinām yat śubha aśubham māyayā saṃharan tatra prāṇi saṃghān yatas tatas tasya māyā mayāḥ pāśāḥ na vedyante sura asuraiḥ evam hi śāsataḥ tasya yamasya paricārakāḥ gṛhītvā saṃnayanti eva prāṇinaḥ kṣīṇa karmiṇaḥ karmaṇā prāṇinaḥ loke uttama adhama madhyamāḥ yathārham tān samādāya nayanti yama sādanam dhārmikān uttamān viddhi svargīyāḥ te yathā amarāḥ nṛṣu janma labhante ye karmaṇā madhyamāḥ smṛtāḥ panthānaḥ trividhā dṛṣṭā sarveṣām gati jīvinām ramaṇīyam nirābādham durdarśam iti nāmataḥ ramaṇīyam tu sat mārgam patākā dhvaja saṃkulam dhūpitam sikta saṃmṛṣṭam puṣpa mālā abhisaṃkulam nirābādham yathā loke su praśastam tathā bhavet tṛtīyam tat tu durdarśam durgandhi tamasā āvṛtam paruṣam śarkarā ākīrṇam śva daṃṣṭra bahulam bhṛśam kṛmi kīṭa samākīrṇam gacchatām ati durgamam saṃnayanti yathā kāle tat me śṛṇu śuci smite uttamān antakāle tu yama dūtāḥ su saṃyatāḥ umā bhagavan tatra ca ātmānam tyakta deham nirāśrayam maheśvaraḥ adṛśyam katham ādāya saṃnayanti yama antikam śṛṇu bhāmini tat sarvam trividham dehadhāraṇam mānuṣam karma vaśyam syāt svargīyam bhoga sādhanam tṛtīyam yātanā vaśyam śarīram māyayā kṛtam śarīraiḥ yātanā vaśyaiḥ jīvam āmucya bhāmini nayanti yāmikāḥ tatra prāṇinaḥ māyayā mṛtān caṇḍāla veṣāḥ tu adhamān gṛhītvā bhartsya tarjanaiḥ ākarṣantaḥ tathā pāśaiḥ durdarśeṇa nayanti tān dharma āsana gatam dakṣam bhrājamānam sva tejasā darśayanti mahābhāge yāmikāḥ tān nivedya te pūjayan daṇḍayan kān cit teṣām śṛṇvan śubha aśubham gatānām tu yamaḥ teṣām uttamān abhipūjayā abhisaṃgamya vidhivat pṛṣṭvā svāgata kauśalam prastutya sat kathām teṣām lokam saṃdiśate yama yamena evam anujñātāḥ yānti paścāt triviṣṭapam madhyamānām yamaḥ teṣām śrutvā karma yathātatham jāyantām mānuṣeṣu eva iti saṃdiśate ca tān adhamān pāpa saṃyuktān yamaḥ na avekṣate āgatān yamasya puruṣāḥ ghorāḥ caṇḍāla sama darśanāḥ yātanāḥ yāpayanti etān lokapālasya śāsanāt krośataḥ pātayanti etān mithas garteṣu avāṅmukhān saṃghātinyaḥ śilāḥ ca eṣām patanti śirasi priye ayomukhāḥ kāka balāḥ bhakṣayanti su dāruṇāḥ tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭrāḥ tathā śvānaḥ kān cit tatra daśanti vai tatra vaitaraṇī nāma nadī grāha samākulā duṣpraveśā ca ghorā ca mūtra śoṇita vāhinī tasyām saṃmajjayanti etān tṛṣitān pāyayanti tān āropayanti vai kān cit tatra kaṇṭaka śalmalīm aṅgāreṣu ca dahyante tathā duṣkṛta kāriṇaḥ pāṭyante taru vat śastraiḥ pīḍyante locana ādiṣu bhidyante atha aṅgaśas śūlaiḥ tudyante sūkṣma sūcibhiḥ evam tvayā kṛtaḥ doṣaḥ tad artham daṇḍanam tu idam vācā evam ghoṣayanti sma daṇḍyamānān samantataḥ evam te yātanāḥ prāpya śarīraiḥ yātanā vaśaiḥ evam bahuvidhāḥ daṇḍāḥ bhujyante pāpa kāribhiḥ pāpa doṣa kṣaya karā yātanā saṃsmṛtā nṛṇām umā maheśvaraḥ kati te nirayāḥ ghorāḥ kīdṛśāḥ te maheśvara śṛṇu bhāmini tat sarvam pañca ete naraka āhvayāḥ bhūmeḥ adhastāt vihitā ghorā duṣkṛta karmaṇām tāvat pramāṇam vistīrṇam tāmasam pāpa pīḍitam bhṛśam durgandhi paruṣam kṛmibhiḥ dāruṇaiḥ yutam kṛmibhiḥ bhakṣyamāṇāḥ ca visra gandha samāyutāḥ evaṃpramāṇam udvignāḥ yānti tiṣṭhanti tatra te yātanābhyaḥ daśaguṇam narake duḥkham iṣyate bhramanti duḥkha mokṣa artham trātā kaḥ cit na vidyate duḥkhasya antara mātram tu dvāram vā na ca labhyate mahāraurava saṃjñam tu dvitīyam narakam priye tṛtīyam narakam tatra kaṇṭakāvana saṃjñitam tatas dvi guṇitam tam ca pūrvābhyām duḥkha mānayoḥ mahāpātaka saṃyuktāḥ ghorāḥ tasmin viśanti hi etat dvi guṇitam tasmāt yathā aniṣṭa sukham tathā bhuñjate tatra tatra eva duḥkham duṣkṛta kāriṇaḥ pañcakaṣṭam iti khyātam pañcamam narakam priye bhuñjate tatra tatra eva duḥkham duṣkṛta kāriṇaḥ amānuṣa arham tat duḥkham mahābhūtaiḥ tu bhujyate ati ghoram ciram kṛtvā mahābhūtāni yānti tam pañca kaṣṭena hi samam nā asti duḥkham tathāvidham duḥkhasya antam iti prāhuḥ pañca kaṣṭam sadā priye evam te teṣu tiṣṭhanti prāṇinaḥ duḥkha bhāginaḥ krośantaḥ ca rudantaḥ ca vedanā ārtāḥ bhṛśa āturāḥ rujā arditāḥ tṛṣā yuktāḥ prāṇinaḥ pāpa kāriṇaḥ kṛmibhiḥ bhakṣyamāṇāḥ ca vedanā ārtāḥ tṛṣā anvitāḥ saṃsmarantaḥ svakam karma kṛtam ātma aparādha jam śocantaḥ tatra tiṣṭhanti yāvat pāpa kṣayam priye evam bhuktvā tu narakam mucyante pāpa saṃkṣayāt umā maheśvaraḥ śatam sahasram varṣāṇām ādim kṛtvā hi jantavaḥ umā tiṣṭhanti naraka āvāsāḥ pralaya antam iti sthitiḥ maheśvaraḥ raurave śata sāhasram varṣāṇām iti saṃsthitiḥ mānuṣa ghnāḥ kṛtaghnāḥ ca tathā eva anṛta vādinaḥ jāra corāḥ ca nārī ca sarvatas ca apacāriṇī utkocakāḥ ca piśunāḥ varṇa saṃbheda kārakāḥ tādṛśāḥ paripacyante raurave narake narāḥ deśa ghnāḥ ca eva rāja ghnāḥ pitṛ mātṛ vighātinaḥ rājā ca anyāyataḥ śāstā sākṣi tve anṛta vādinaḥ bahu ghnāḥ ca kula ghnāḥ ca bhrūṇa ghnāḥ guru ghātinaḥ viśvasta ghātakāḥ ca evam ātma ghnāḥ kopa kāraṇāt dvitīye dviguṇam kālam pacyante tādṛśāḥ narāḥ mahāpātaka yuktāḥ tu tṛtīye duḥkham āpnuyuḥ etāvat mānuṣa saham param anyeṣu lakṣyate yakṣāḥ vidyādharāḥ ca eva kādraveyāḥ ca kiṃnarāḥ gandharvāḥ bhūta saṃghāḥ ca teṣām pāpa yutāḥ bhṛśam sahantaḥ tādṛśam ghoram pañca kaṣṭe ca yādṛśam tādṛgvidhasya duḥkhasya ayogyān viddhi mānuṣān evam te narakān bhuktvā tatra kṣapita kalmaṣāḥ narakebhyaḥ vimuktāḥ ca jāyante kṛmi jātiṣu udbheda jeṣu vā ke cid tatra api kṣīṇa kalmaṣāḥ umā mṛga pakṣiṣu tat bhuktvā labhante mānuṣam padam nānā jātiṣu kena eva jāyante pāpa kāriṇaḥ maheśvaraḥ sarvathā ātmā karma vaśāt nānā jātiṣu dṛśyate yaḥ ca māṃsa priyaḥ nityam kaṅka gṛdhrān sa saṃspṛśet abhakṣya bhakṣaṇaḥ martyaḥ kāka jātiṣu saṃspṛśet ātma ghnaḥ yaḥ naraḥ kopāt preta jātiṣu tiṣṭhati paiśunyāt parivādāt ca kukkuṭa tvam samaśnuyāt hiṃsā vihāraḥ tu naraḥ kṛmi kīṭeṣu jāyate asatyam paruṣam vākyam yaḥ vadet matsya tām vrajet agamyā gamanāt ca eva para dāra abhimarśanāt mūṣika tvam vrajet martyaḥ na asti tatra vicāraṇā kṛtaghnaḥ mitra ghātī ca sṛgāla vṛka jātiṣu guru ghnaḥ pitṛ ghātī ca sthāvareṣu avatiṣṭhati vācikaiḥ pakṣi mṛga tām mānasaiḥ anya jāti tām śarīra jaiḥ karma doṣaiḥ yāti sthāvara tām naraḥ evamādi aśubham kṛtvā narāḥ nirayam āśritāḥ tān tān bhāvān prapadyante sva kṛtasya eva kāraṇāt evam jātiṣu nirdagdhāḥ prāṇinaḥ pāpa kāriṇaḥ bahu kṛtvas ati saṃtaptam loham śucitamam yathā bahu duḥkha abhisaṃtaptaḥ tathā ātmā śudhyate malāt umā bhagavan devadeveśa śūlapāṇe vṛṣadhvaja śrotum bhūyas aham icchāmi prajānām hita kāraṇāt śubha aśubham iti proktam karma sarvam samāsatas aśubham kīdṛśam karma prāṇinaḥ adhas nipātayet maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi tat sarvam śṛṇu śobhane sukṛtam duṣkṛtam ca iti dvividhaḥ karma vistaraḥ manaḥ pūrvam tu vāc karma vartate vāc mayam tatas jāyate vai kriyā yogam evam ceṣṭā kramam priye abhidrohaḥ abhyasūyā ca para arthe cakṣuṣā spṛhā śubha aśubhānām martyānām vartanam viparītataḥ dharma kārye yat aśraddhā pāpa karmaṇi harṣaṇam asatyam parivādaḥ ca pāpam etat tu vāc mayam cauryam pareṣām dravyāṇām haraṇam nāśanam tathā abhakṣya bhakṣaṇam ca eva vyasaneṣu abhiṣaṅga tā darpāt stambha abhimānāt ca pareṣām upatāpanam akāryāṇām ca karaṇam aśaucam pānam eva ca dauḥśīlyam kṣudra saṃparkaḥ sāhāyyam pāpa karmaṇi evamādi aśubham ca anyat śarīram pāpam ucyate mānasāt vāc mayam pāpam viśiṣṭam iti vakṣyate vāc mayāt api vai pāpam śārīram gaṇyate bahu dvividham tat kṛtam pāpam kartāram narakam nayet umā maheśvaraḥ yaḥ naraḥ anaparādhī san ātma prāṇasya rakṣaṇāt śatrum udyata śastram vā pūrvam tena hataḥ api vā cora āṭavika saṃtrastāḥ tad pratīkāra ceṣṭayā grāma artham bhartṛ piṇḍa artham dīna anugraha kāraṇāt akāryam vā api abhakṣyam vā kṛtvā pāpaiḥ na lipyate anṛtam dharma yuktam ca dākṣiṇyāt strīṣu bhāṣitam ātma prāṇa bhayāt uktam mokṣa artham ca api adhārmikāt vidhiḥ eṣa gṛhasthānām prāyeṇa eva upadiśyate avācyam vā api akāryam vā deśa kāla vaśena tu umā evam devi vijānīhi na asti tatra vicāraṇā bhagavan pāna doṣān ca peya apeya tva kāraṇam maheśvaraḥ śucayaḥ subhaga ācārāḥ sarve sumanasaḥ priye preṣya abhāvāt manuṣyāṇām karma ārambhaḥ nanāśa ha ubhayoḥ lokayoḥ nāśam dṛṣṭvā karma kṣayāt prabhuḥ ājñāpayat surān devi mohayasva iti mānuṣān tamasaḥ sāram uddhṛtya pānam buddhi praṇāśanam nyapātayat manuṣyeṣu pāpa doṣa āvaham priye tadā prabhṛti tat pītvā mumuhuḥ mānuṣāḥ bhuvi kārya akāryam a jānantaḥ vācya avācyam guṇa aguṇam nṛtyanti muditāḥ ke cid gāyanti ca śubha aśubham nagnāḥ vikṣipya gātrāṇi naṣṭa saṃjñāḥ mṛtāḥ iva evam bahuvidhān pāpān kurvanti hṛta cetasaḥ ye pibanti mahā moham pānam pāpa yutāḥ narāḥ dhṛtim lajjām ca buddhim ca pānam pītam praṇāśayet tasmāt narāḥ saṃbhavanti nirlajjāḥ nirapatrapāḥ buddhi sattvaiḥ parikṣīṇāḥ tejaḥ hīnāḥ mala anvitāḥ pītvā pītvā tṛṣā yuktāḥ pānapāḥ saṃbhavanti ca pāna kāmāḥ pāna kathāḥ pāna kāla abhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ pāna artham karma vaśyāḥ te saṃbhavanti nara adhamāḥ pāna kāmāḥ tṛṣā yogāt buddhi sattva parikṣayāt pānapānām preṣya karāḥ pānapāḥ tu abhavan bhṛśam tadā prabhṛti vai loke nīcaiḥ pāna vaśaiḥ naraiḥ kāru tvam atha dāsa tvam preṣya tām etya pānapāḥ pānapāḥ tu mada andha tvāt tadā buddhi praṇāśanāt kārya akāryasya ca ajñānāt yathā iṣṭa karaṇāt svayam viśiṣṭaiḥ jñātibhiḥ dveṣyaḥ satatam kali bhāvanaḥ kaṭukam paruṣam ghoram vākyam vadati sarvatas saṃvidam kurute śauṇḍaiḥ na śṛṇoti hitam kva cit evam bahuvidhāḥ doṣāḥ pānape santi śobhane kevalam narakam yānti na asti tatra vicāraṇā tasmāt tat varjitam sadbhiḥ pānam ātma hita eṣibhiḥ yadi pānam na varjeran santaḥ cāritra kāraṇāt maheśvaraḥ vidhānam su kṛtasya api bhūyas śṛṇu śuci smite tathā eva sa upakaraṇam tāvatā sukṛtam viduḥ manaḥ vāc kāya jāḥ doṣāḥ śṛṇu me varjanāt śubham tathā dharmam avāpnoti doṣa tyāgaḥ hi duṣkaraḥ doṣa sākalya saṃtyāgāt muniḥ bhavati mānavaḥ ātmanā sthāpanā mātrāt labhyate sukṛtam param aho nṛśaṃsāḥ pacyante mānuṣāḥ su alpabuddhayaḥ ye tādṛśam na budhyante ātma adhīnam ca nirvyayam duṣkṛta tyāga mātreṇa padam ūrdhvam hi labhyate pāpa bhīru tva mātreṇa doṣāṇām parivarjanāt śrutāt ca vṛddha saṃyogāt indriyāṇām ca nigrahāt saṃtoṣāt ca dhṛteḥ ca eva śakyate doṣa varjanam īśvarāṇām prabhavatām daridrāṇām ca vai nṛṇām saphalaḥ doṣa saṃtyāgaḥ dānāt api śubhāt api su kṛtam yāmikam proktam pathyam nirupasādhanam sukha abhisaṃdhiḥ lokānām satyam śaucam atha ārjavam vrata upavāsaḥ prītiḥ ca brahmacaryam damaḥ śamaḥ evamādi śubham karma su kṛtam niyama āśritam śṛṇu teṣām viśeṣān ca kīrtayiṣyāmi bhāmini na asti satyāt param dānam na asti satyāt param tapaḥ yathā śrutam yathā dṛṣṭam ātmanā yat yathā kṛtam tathā tasya avikāreṇa vacanam satya lakṣaṇam yat chalena abhisaṃyuktam satya rūpam mṛṣā eva tat nityam eva pravaktavyam pārāvaryam vijānatā dīrgha āyūḥ ca bhavet satyāt kula saṃtāna pālakaḥ umā maheśvaraḥ katham saṃdhārayan martyaḥ vratam śubham avāpnuyāt pūrvam uktam tu yat pāpam manaḥ vāc kāya karmabhiḥ maṅgalam śubha karmāṇi vratena eva samācaret tyājyam vā yadi vā joṣyam avratena vṛthak caran śuddha kāyaḥ naraḥ bhūtvā snātvā tīrthe yathāvidhi pañca bhūtāni candra arkau saṃdhye dharmam yamam pitṝn vratamāḥ maraṇāt vā api kāla chedena vā caret śāka ādiṣu vratam kuryāt tathā puṣpa phala ādiṣu evam anyeṣu bahuṣu vratam kāryam hita eṣiṇā vrata bhaṅgaḥ yathā na syāt rakṣitavyam tathā budhaiḥ auṣadha artham yat ajñānāt gurūṇām vacanāt api anugraha artham bandhūnām vrata bhaṅgaḥ na duṣyate vrata apavarga kāleṣu deva brāhmaṇa pūjanam umā nareṇa tu yathāśakti kāryam siddhim tathā āpnuyāt maheśvaraḥ mānasam su kṛtam yat tat śaucam ābhyantaram smṛtam sat āhāra viśuddhiḥ ca kāya prakṣālanam ca yat mṛd ca eva śuddha deśa sthā go śakṛt mūtram eva ca dravyāṇi gandha yuktāni yāni puṣṭi karāṇi ca etaiḥ saṃmārjayet kāyam ambhasā ca punar punar prāyaśas tādṛśe majjet anyathā ca api varjayet tris ācamanakam śreṣṭham niṣphenaiḥ nirmalaiḥ jalaiḥ tathā viṣ mūtrayoḥ śuddhiḥ adbhiḥ bahu mṛdā bhavet tadā eva jala saṃśuddhiḥ yat saṃśuddham tu saṃspṛśet śakṛtā bhūmi śuddhiḥ syāt lohānām bhasmanā smṛtā takṣaṇam gharṣaṇam ca eva dāravāṇām viśodhanam dahanam mṛd mayānām ca martyānām kṛcchra dhāraṇam śeṣāṇām devi sarveṣām ātapena jalena ca brāhmaṇānām ca vākyena sadā saṃśodhanam bhavet aduṣṭam adbhiḥ nirṇiktam yat ca vācā praśasyate evam āpadi saṃśuddhiḥ evam śaucam vidhīyate umā maheśvaraḥ kṛmi kīṭa malaiḥ hīnam saṃbhṛtam śuddha bhājane evaṃvidham sat āhāram deva brāhmaṇa satkṛtam grāmyāt āraṇyakaiḥ siddham śuddham iti avadhāraya yajña śeṣam haviḥ śeṣam pitṛ śeṣam ca nirmalam umā maheśvaraḥ māṃsasya bhakṣaṇe doṣaḥ yaḥ ca asya a bhakṣaṇe guṇaḥ iṣṭam dattam adhītam ca kratavaḥ ca sa dakṣiṇāḥ a māṃsa bhakṣaṇasya ete kalām na arhanti ṣoḍaśīm ātma artham yaḥ para prāṇān hiṃsyāt svādu phala īpsayā vyāla gṛdhra sṛgālaiḥ ca rākṣasaiḥ ca samaḥ tu saḥ yaḥ vṛthak nitya māṃsa āśī sa pumān adhamaḥ bhavet tatas kaṣṭataram na asti svayam āhṛtya bhakṣaṇāt yaḥ tu sarvāṇi māṃsāni yāvajjīvam na bhakṣayet sa svarge vipulam sthānam labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ yaḥ tu varṣa śatam pūrṇam tapyate paramam tapaḥ yaḥ ca api varjayet māṃsam samam etat na vā samam tasmāt prāṇi dayā kāryā yathā ātmani tathā pare yat māṃsa rasam āsvādya punar māṃsāni varjayet iti evam munayaḥ prāhuḥ māṃsasya a bhakṣaṇe guṇān evam bahuguṇam devi nṛṇām māṃsa vivarjanam na śaknuyāt yadā jīvan tyaktum māṃsam katham cana tripuṇya māsa mātram vā varjanīyam viśeṣataḥ varjanīyam tathā māṃsam paratra hitam icchatā aśaktaḥ kāraṇāt martyaḥ bhoktum icchet vidhim śṛṇu sūnāyām ca gata prāṇam krītvā nyāyena bhāmini brāhmaṇa atithi pūjā artham bhoktavyam hitam icchatā bhaiṣajya kāraṇāt vyādhau khādan pāpaiḥ na lipyate pitṛ śeṣam tathā eva aśnan māṃsam na aśubham ṛcchati umā maheśvaraḥ guru pūjā katham deva kriyate dharma kāṅkṣibhiḥ guru pūjām pravakṣyāmi yathāvat tava śobhane kṛtajñānām paraḥ dharmaḥ iti veda anuśāsanam tasmāt sva guravaḥ pūjyāḥ te hi pūrva upakāriṇaḥ gurūṇām ca garīyāṃsaḥ trayaḥ lokeṣu pūjitāḥ upādhyāyaḥ pitā mātā saṃpūjyāḥ te viśeṣataḥ ye pitṛ bhrātaraḥ jyeṣṭhāḥ ye ca tasya anujāḥ tathā pituḥ pitā ca sarve te pūjanīyāḥ yathā pitā mātuḥ yā bhaginī jyeṣṭhā mātuḥ yā ca yavīyasī mātāmahī ca dhātrī ca sarvāḥ tāḥ mātaraḥ smṛtāḥ ṛtvij guruḥ pitā ca iti guravaḥ parikīrtitāḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ bhrātā narendraḥ ca mātulaḥ śvaśuraḥ tathā iti eṣa kathitaḥ svargyaḥ gurūṇām sarva saṃgrahaḥ anuvṛttim ca pūjām ca teṣām api nibodha me yena prīṇāti ca pitā tena prītaḥ prajāpatiḥ yena prīṇāti ced mātā prītāḥ syuḥ deva mātaraḥ yena prīṇāti upādhyāyaḥ brahmā tena abhipūjitaḥ na brūyāt vipriyam teṣām aniṣṭe na pravartayet veda anuśāsana samam guru śāsanam iṣyate kalahān ca vivādān ca gurubhiḥ saha varjayet kaitavam parihāsān ca manyu kāma āśrayāḥ kathāḥ gurūṇām yaḥ an ahaṃvādī karoti ājñām atandritaḥ asūyām apavādān ca gurūṇām parivarjayet teṣām priya hita anveṣī bhūtvā paricaret sadā yat kuryāt puruṣasya iha guru pūjā sadā kṛtā anuvṛtteḥ vinā dharmaḥ na asti sarva āśrameṣu api tasmāt samādṛtaḥ kāle guru vṛttim samācaret upādhyāyam pitaram mātaram ca teṣām pāpam bhrūṇahatyā viśiṣṭam umā maheśvaraḥ śarīra mala kārśya artham indriya ucchoṣaṇāya ca bahūnām uparodham tu na kuryāt ātma kāraṇāt jīva upaghātam ca tathā dhānyam saṃjīvyam iṣyate tasmāt puṇyam labhet martyaḥ svayam āhāra karśanāt umā bhuñjan na vrata ghātī syāt brāhmaṇān anumānya ca maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu devi samāhitā brahmacaryam param śaucam brahmacaryam param tapaḥ saṃsparśāt atha saṃyogāt pañcadhā rakṣitam param nitya saṃrakṣaṇam tasya naiṣṭhikānām vidhīyate tat iṣyate gṛhasthānām kālam uddiśya kāraṇam umā tīrtha caryā katham deva kriyate dharma kāṅkṣibhiḥ maheśvaraḥ kāni tīrthāni lokeśa tat me śaṃsitum arhasi pāvana artham ca śauca artham brahmaṇā nirmitāḥ purā yāḥ tu loke mahā nadyaḥ tāḥ sarvāḥ tīrtha saṃjñitāḥ tāsām prāk srotasaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ saṃgamaḥ ca parasparam tāsām sāgara saṃyogaḥ variṣṭhaḥ ca iti vidyate tāsām ubhayatas kūlam yatra tatra mahā ṛṣibhiḥ samudraḥ ca mahā tīrtham pāvanam paramam śubham tasya kūla gatāḥ tīrthāḥ mahadbhiḥ ca samāplutāḥ srotasām parvatānām ca joṣitānām mahā ṛṣibhiḥ api kūpa taṭākam vā munibhiḥ sevitam priye evam tīrtha udbhavam viddhi tasya snāna vidhim śṛṇu tad manāḥ vrata bhūyiṣṭhaḥ gatvā tīrtha abhikāṅkṣayā upavāsa trayam kuryāt ekam vā niyama anvitaḥ puṇya māsa yute kāle paurṇamāsyām yathāvidhi bahis eva śuciḥ bhūtvā tat tīrtham tad manāḥ āviśet tris āplutya jala abhyāśe dattvā brāhmaṇa dakṣiṇām etat vidhānam sarveṣām tīrtham tīrtham prati priye samīpa tīrtha snānāt tu dūra tīrtham su pūjitam ādi prabhṛti śuddhasya tīrtha snānam śubham bhavet tapaḥ rtham pāpa nāśa artham śauca artham tīrtha gāhanam evam puṇyeṣu māseṣu tīrtha snānam śubham bhavet maheśvaraḥ dānāni deva pūjām ca pitṛ pūjām tathā eva ca anyāni dharma kāryāṇi sukṛtam sa upasādhanam tat sarvam śṛṇu kalyāṇe prajānām hita kāmyayā umā maheśvaraḥ loke bhūta mayam dravyam sarva sādhāraṇam tathā dātā pratigrahītā ca deyam sa upakramam tathā deśa kālau ca yat tu etat dānam ṣaḍguṇam ucyate teṣām saṃpad viśeṣān ca kīrtyamānān nibodha me ādi prabhṛti yaḥ śuddhaḥ manaḥ vāc kāya karmabhiḥ śraddhāvān āstikaḥ ca eva evam dātā praśasyate pañcayajña paraḥ nityam nirvikāra śarīravān etān pātra guṇān viddhi tādṛś pātram praśasyate evam pātreṣu nānātvam iṣyate puruṣam prati jāraḥ ca uraḥ ca ṣaṇḍaḥ ca hiṃsraḥ samayabhedakaḥ loka vighna karāḥ ca anye varjitāḥ sarvaśas priye para upaghātāt yat dravyam cauryāt vā labhyate nṛbhiḥ adharmāt atha mohāt vā bahūnām uparodhanāt tādṛśena kṛtam dharmam niṣphalam viddhi bhāmini tasmāt nyāya āgatena eva dātavyam śubham icchatā upakramam imam viddhi dātṝṇām paramam hitam dātā dānam tathā dadyāt yathā tuṣyeta tena saḥ eṣa dāna vidhiḥ śreṣṭhaḥ samāhūya tu madhyamaḥ pūrvam ca pātra tām jñātvā samāhūya nivedya ca śauca arcana samāyuktam dātavyam śraddhayā priye yācitṝṇām tu paramam ābhimukhya puraskṛtam saṃmāna pūrvam saṃgṛhya dātavyam deśa kālayoḥ pātrāṇi saṃparīkṣya eva dātā vai dāna mātrayoḥ atiśaktyā param dānam yathāśakti tu madhyamam tṛtīyam ca aparam dānam na anurūpam iva ātmanaḥ yathā saṃbhāvitam pūrvam dātavyam tat tathā eva ca puṇya kṣetreṣu yat dattam puṇya kāleṣu vā tathā umā yaḥ ca puṇyatamaḥ deśaḥ tathā kālaḥ ca śaṃsa me maheśvaraḥ giriḥ varaḥ ca tīrthāni deśa bhāgena pūjitāḥ śuklapakṣaḥ ca pakṣāṇām paurṇamāsī ca parvasu pitṛ daivata nakṣatram nirmalāḥ divasāḥ tathā pratigrahītuḥ yaḥ kālaḥ manasā kīrtitaḥ śubhe evamādiṣu kāleṣu dattam dānam mahat bhavet dātā deyam ca pātram ca upakrama yutā kriyā deśaḥ kālaḥ ca iti eṣām saṃpad śuddhiḥ prakīrtitā bhūtvā anantam nayet svargam dātāram doṣa varjitam su mahat vā api yat dānam guṇaiḥ ebhiḥ vinākṛtam umā evam guṇa yutam dānam dattam tu aphalatām vrajet maheśvaraḥ tat api asti mahābhāge narāṇām bhava doṣataḥ kṛtvā tu dharmam vidhivat paścāttāpam karoti ced ślāghayā vā yadi brūyāt vṛthā saṃsadi yat kṛtam dharma kāryam kṛtam yat ca satatam phala kāṅkṣayā evam kṛtam vā dattam vā paratra viphalam bhavet ete doṣāḥ vivarjyāḥ ca dātṛbhiḥ puṇya kāṅkṣibhiḥ sanātanam idam vṛttam sadbhiḥ ācaritam tathā anugrahaḥ pareṣām tu gṛhasthānām ṛṇam hi tat iti evam manaḥ āveśya dātavyam satatam budhaiḥ umā maheśvaraḥ annam pratiśrayaḥ dīpaḥ pānīyam tṛṇam indhanam snehaḥ gandhaḥ ca bhaiṣajyam tilāḥ ca lavaṇam tathā sāmānyam sarva varṇānām dānam śṛṇu samāhitā annam prāṇāḥ manuṣyāṇām anna daḥ prāṇa daḥ bhavet tasmāt annam viśeṣeṇa dātum icchanti mānavāḥ brāhmaṇāya abhirūpāya yaḥ dadyāt annam īpsitam nidadhāti nidhim śreṣṭham saḥ anantam pāralaukikam śrāntam adhva pariśrāntam atithim gṛham āgatam brāhmaṇānām viśeṣeṇa saḥ apahanti svakam tamaḥ pitaraḥ tasya nandanti su vṛṣṭyā karṣakāḥ iva api caṇḍāla śūdrāṇām anna dānāt na garhyate kalatram pīḍayitvā api poṣayet atithīn sadā bhavanāni prakāśante divi teṣām mahātmanām vaiḍūrya arciḥ prakāśāṇi rukma rūpya nibhāni ca nānā saṃsthāna rūpāṇi nānā ratna mayāni ca candra maṇḍala śubhrāṇi kiṅkiṇī jālavanti ca taruṇa āditya varṇāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca sarva kāma phalāḥ ca atra vṛkṣāḥ bhavana saṃsthitāḥ vāpyaḥ bahvyaḥ ca kūpāḥ ca dīrghikāḥ ca sahasraśas bhavanāni viviktāni prāṇadānām triviṣṭape tatra te su ciram kālam vihṛtya apsarasām gaṇaiḥ jāyante mānuṣe loke sarva kalyāṇa saṃyutāḥ bala saṃhanana upetāḥ nīrogāḥ cira jīvinaḥ tasmāt annam viśeṣeṇa dātavyam bhūtim icchatā tasmāt tat varṇayiṣyāmi yathāvat anupūrvaśas api pāpam kṛtam krūram dattam rukmam praṇāśayet agniḥ hi devatāḥ sarvāḥ suvarṇam ca agniḥ ucyate tasmāt suvarṇa dānena dattāḥ syuḥ sarva devatāḥ tasmāt suvarṇa dātāraḥ sarvān kāmān avāpnuyuḥ ādityasya hutāśasya lokān nānāvidhān śubhān kāñcanam saṃpradāya āśu praviśanti na saṃśayaḥ alaṃkāra kṛtam ca api kevalāt praviśiṣyate sauvarṇaiḥ brāhmaṇān kāle taiḥ alaṃkṛtya bhojayet dyutim medhām vapuḥ kīrtim punar jāte labhet dhruvam tasmāt sva śaktyā dātavyam kāñcanam bhuvi mānavaiḥ atas ūrdhvam pravakṣyāmi gavām dānam anindite lokān sisṛkṣuṇā pūrvam gāvaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvā vṛtti artham sarva bhūtānām tasmāt tāḥ mātaraḥ smṛ loka jyeṣṭhā loka vṛttyām pravṛttā mayi āyattāḥ soma viṣyanda bhūtāḥ saumyāḥ puṇyāḥ kāma dāḥ prāṇa dāḥ ca tasmāt pūjyāḥ puṇya kāmaiḥ manuṣyaiḥ dhenum hi dattvā nibhṛtām arogām kalyāṇa vatsām ca payasvinīm ca tāvat samāḥ svarga phalāni bhuṅkte prayacchate yaḥ kapilām sa celām kāṃsya upadohām kanaka agra śṛṅgīm putrān ca pautrān ca kulam ca sarvam antarjātāḥ krītakāḥ dyūta labdhāḥ prāṇa krītāḥ sa udakāḥ ca ojasā vā kṛcchra utsṛṣṭāḥ poṣaṇa artha āgatāḥ ca dvāraiḥ etaiḥ tāḥ pralabdhāḥ pradadyāt kṛśāya bahu putrāya śrotriyāya āhitāgnaye pradāya nīrujām dhenum lokān prāpnoti anuttamān nṛśaṃsasya kṛtaghnasya lubdhasya anṛta vādinaḥ su vastrām vastra saṃdānām soma loke mahīyate samāna vatsām yaḥ dhenum kṛṣṇām dadyāt payasvinīm su vṛttām vastra saṃdānām lokān prāpnoti apām pateḥ samāna vatsām yaḥ dhenum dadyāt gaurīm payasvinīm su vṛttām vastra saṃdānām agni loke mahīyate hiraṇya varṇām piṅga akṣīm sa vatsām kāṃsya dohanām pradāya vastrasaṃdānām yāti kaubera sadma saḥ vāyu reṇu savarṇām tu sa vatsām kāṃsya dohanām pradāya vastra saṃdānām vāyu loke mahīyate yuvānam balinam śyāmam śatena saha yūthapam gavendram brāhmaṇa indrāya bhūri śṛṅgam alaṃkṛtam ṛṣabham ye prayacchanti śrotriyāṇām mahātmanām aiśvaryam abhijāyante jāyamānāḥ punar punar gavām mūtra purīṣāṇi na udvijeta kadā cana na ca āsām māṃsam aśnīyāt goṣu bhaktaḥ sadā bhavet grāsa muṣṭim para gave dadyāt saṃvatsaram śuciḥ a kṛtvā svayam āhāram vratam tat sārvakāmikam gāvaḥ pavitram paramam goṣu lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ katham cit na avamantavyāḥ gāvaḥ lokasya mātaraḥ tasmāt eva gavām dānam viśiṣṭam iti kathyate goṣu pūjā ca bhaktiḥ ca narasya āyuṣyam āvahet atas param pravakṣyāmi bhūmi dānam mahā phalam bhūmi dāna samam dānam na kila asti iti niścayaḥ gṛha yuj kṣetra yuj vā api bhūmi bhāgaḥ pradīyate sukha bhogyam nirākrośam vāstu pūrvam prakalpya ca grahītāram alaṃkṛtya vastra puṣpa anulepanaiḥ sa bhṛtyam sa parīvāram bhojayitvā yatheṣṭataḥ yaḥ dadyāt dakṣiṇā kāle tris adbhiḥ gṛhyatām iti evam bhūmyām pradattāyām śraddhayā vīta matsaraiḥ yāvat tiṣṭhati sā bhūmiḥ tāvat tasya phalam viduḥ bhūmi daḥ svargam āruhya ramate śāśvatīḥ samāḥ acalā hi akṣayā bhūmiḥ sarvān kāmān dudhukṣati yat yat ca kurute pāpam puruṣaḥ vṛtti karśitaḥ suvarṇa rajatam vastram maṇi muktā vasūni ca sarvam etat mahā prājñe bhūmi dāne pratiṣṭhitam bhartuḥ niḥśreyase yuktāḥ tyaktātmānaḥ raṇe hatāḥ hala kṛṣṭām mahīm dadyāt yaḥ sa bīja phala anvitām sa kūpa śaraṇām vā api sā bhavet sarva kāma dā niṣpanna sasyām pṛthivīm yaḥ dadāti dvijanmanām brāhmaṇam vṛtta saṃpannam āhitāgnim śuci vratam grāhayitvā nijām bhūmim na yāti yama sādanam yathā bījāni rohanti prakīrṇāni mahī tale tathā kāmāḥ prarohanti bhūmi dāna guṇa arjitāḥ pitaraḥ pitṛ loka sthāḥ devatāḥ ca divi sthitāḥ dīrgha āyuḥ tvam aroga tvam sphītām ca śriyam uttamām atas param pravakṣyāmi kanyā dānam yathāvidhi kanyā deyā tathā devi pareṣām ātmanaḥ api vā kanyām śuddha vrata ācārām kula rūpa samanvitām yasmai ditsati pātrāya tena api bhṛśa kāmi tām kārayitvā gṛham pūrvam dāsī dāsa paricchadaiḥ dāra arthine tad arhāya kanyām tām samalaṃkṛtām sa vivāham yathānyāyam prayacchet agni sākṣikam vṛtti āyatim tathā kṛtvā sat gṛhe tau niveśayet evam kṛtvā vadhū dānam tasya dānasya gauravāt punar jātau ca saubhāgyam kula vṛddhim tathā āpnuyāt vidyā dānam tathā devi pātra bhūtāya vai dadat pretyabhāve labhet martyaḥ medhām vṛddhim dhṛtim smṛtim anurūpāya śiṣyāya svām vidyām yaḥ prayacchati evam te kathitāni eva mahā dānāni bhāmini tvad priya artham mahādevi bhūyas śrotum kim icchasi umā maheśvaraḥ tila kalpa vidhim devi tvam me śṛṇu samāhitā samṛddhaiḥ asamṛddhaiḥ vā tilāḥ deyāḥ viśeṣataḥ tilāḥ pavitrāḥ pāpa ghnāḥ su puṇyāḥ iti saṃsmṛtāḥ nyāyataḥ tu tilān śuddhān saṃbhṛtya atha sva śaktitaḥ tila rāśim punar kuryāt parvata ābham sa ratnakam mahāntam yadi vā stokam nānā dravya samāyutam suvarṇa rajatābhyām ca maṇi muktā pravālakaiḥ alaṃkṛtya yathāyogam sa patākam sa vedikam sa bhūṣaṇam sa vastram ca śayana āsana saṃyutam prāyaśas kaumudī māse paurṇamāsyām viśeṣataḥ svayam kṛtvā upavāsam ca vṛtta śauca samanvitaḥ dadyāt pradakṣiṇīkṛtya tila rāśim sa dakṣiṇam ekasya vā bahūnām vā dātavyam bhūtim icchatā kevalam vā tilaiḥ eva bhūmau kṛtvā gavākṛtim sa ratnakam sa vastram ca puṃsā go dāna kāṅkṣiṇā śarāvān tila saṃpūrṇān sa hiraṇyān sa campakān nānā dāna phalam bhūyas śṛṇu devi samāhitā balam āyuṣyam ārogyam anna dānāt labhet naraḥ pānīya daḥ tu saubhāgyam rasa jñānam labhet naraḥ vastra dānāt vapuḥ śobhām alaṃkāram labhet naraḥ dīpa daḥ buddhi vaimalyam dyutim śobhām labhet punar dāsī dāsa pradānāt tu bhavet karmānta bhāj naraḥ dāsī dāsam ca vividham labhet pretya guṇa anvitam yānāni vāhanam ca eva tad arhāya dadan naraḥ vicitram ramaṇīyam ca labhate yāna vāhanam setu kūpa taṭākānām kartā tu labhate naraḥ dīrgha āyuḥ tvam ca saubhāgyam tathā pretya etīm śubhām vṛkṣa paṅkti karaḥ yaḥ tu chāyā puṣpa phala pradaḥ yaḥ tu saṃkrama kṛt loke nadīṣu jala tāriṇām mārga kṛt satatam martyaḥ bhavet saṃtānavān punar auṣadhānām pradātā ca satatam kṛpayā anvitaḥ bhavet vyādhi vihīnaḥ ca dīrgha āyuḥ ca viśeṣataḥ anāthān poṣayet yaḥ tu kṛpaṇa andhaka paṅgukān devagoṣṭhān sabhāḥ śālāḥ bhikṣūṇām ca pratiśrayam prāsāda vāsam vividham pakṣa śobhām labhet naraḥ vividham vividha ākāram bhakṣya bhojya guṇa anvitam ramyam sadā eva go vāṭam yaḥ kuryāt labhate naraḥ pretyabhāve śubhām jātim vyādhi mokṣam tathā eva ca umā evam nānāvidham dravyam dātā kartā labhet phalam maheśvaraḥ dānam vā ṣaḍguṇa yutam tad arhāya yathāvidhi yathā vibhavataḥ dānam dātavyam iti mānavaiḥ buddhim āyuṣyam ārogyam kulam bhāgyam tathā āgamam rūpeṇa saptadhā bhūtvā mānuṣyam phalati dhruvam idam dattam idam me syāt iti evam phala kāṅkṣayā umā bhagavan devadeveśa viśiṣṭam yajñam ucyate maheśvaraḥ devatānām ca saṃpūjā yajñeṣu eva samāhitā yajñāḥ vedeṣu adhīnāḥ ca vedāḥ brāhmaṇa saṃyutāḥ yajña artham viddhi tat sṛṣṭam lokānām hita kāmyayā evam vijñāya tad kartā sa dāraḥ satatam dvijaḥ tasmāt vipraiḥ yathāśāstram vidhi dṛṣṭena karmaṇā brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ ca eva yajña arhāḥ prāyaśas smṛtāḥ tathā kṛteṣu yajñeṣu devānām toṣaṇam bhavet tuṣṭeṣu deva saṃgheṣu yajvā yajña phalam labhet devāḥ saṃtoṣitāḥ yajñaiḥ lokān saṃvardhayanti uta na asti yajña samam dānam na asti yajña samaḥ nidhiḥ eṣā yajña kṛtā pūjā laukikīm aparām śṛṇu deva goṣṭhān hi saṃskṛtya ca utsavam yaḥ karoti vai yāgān deva upahārān ca śuciḥ bhūtvā yathāvidhi devān saṃtoṣayitvā sa devi dharmam avāpnuyāt nṛttaiḥ vādyaiḥ ca gāndharvaiḥ anyaiḥ dṛṣṭi vilobhanaiḥ teṣām bhakti kṛtena eva satkāreṇa abhipūjitāḥ tathā eva toṣam saṃyānti devi devāḥ triviṣṭape mānuṣaiḥ aparaiḥ vā api śucibhiḥ tad parāyaṇaiḥ prayataiḥ śuddha gātraiḥ tu śuddha deśe su pūjitāḥ saṃtoṣam yānti vai devāḥ bhaktaiḥ saṃpūjitāḥ tathā umā triviṣṭapa sthāḥ vai devāḥ bhūmau mānuṣa ceṣṭitam maheśvaraḥ prāṇinām tu śarīreṣu antarātmā vyavasthitaḥ ātmānam paramam devam iti viddhi śubha īkṣaṇe ātmā manaḥ vyavasthānāt sarvam vetti śubha aśubham satām manaḥ vyavasthānāt śubham bhavati vai nṛṇām tasmāt deva abhisaṃpūjā pitṛ pūjā tathā eva ca yajñāḥ ca dharma kāryāṇi guru pūjāḥ ca śobhane evam kṛtvā śubha ākāṅkṣī paratra iha ca modate umā sarveṣām pitaraḥ pūjyāḥ sarva saṃpad pradāyinaḥ maheśvaraḥ pitṛ medham pravakṣyāmi yathāvat tad manāḥ śṛṇu deśa kālau vidhānam ca tad kriyāyāḥ śubha aśubham lokeṣu pitaraḥ pūjyāḥ devatānām ca devatāḥ śucayaḥ nirmalāḥ puṇyāḥ dakṣiṇām diśam āśritāḥ yathā vṛṣṭim pratīkṣante bhūmiṣṭhāḥ sarva jantavaḥ pitaraḥ ca tathā loke pitṛmedham śubha īkṣaṇe tasya deśāḥ kurukṣetram gayā gaṅgā sarasvatī prabhāsam puṣkaram ca iti teṣu dattam mahā phalam tīrthāni saritaḥ puṇyāḥ viviktāni vanāni ca nadīnām pulināni iti deśāḥ śrāddhasya pūjitāḥ maghā prauṣṭhapadau māsau śrāddha karmaṇi pūjitau pakṣayoḥ kṛṣṇapakṣaḥ ca pūrvapakṣāt praśasyate amāvāsyām trayodaśyām navamyām pratipatsu ca tithiṣu etāsu tuṣyanti dattena iha pitāmahāḥ pūrvāhṇe śuklapakṣe vā rātrau janma dineṣu vā yugmeṣu ahaḥsu ca śrāddham na ca kurvīta paṇḍitaḥ eṣa kālaḥ mayā proktaḥ pitṛ medhasya pūjitaḥ yasmin vā brāhmaṇam pātram paśyet kālaḥ sa ca smṛ a pāṅkteyāḥ dvijāḥ varjyāḥ grāhyāḥ te paṅkti pāvanāḥ pūjayet yadi pāpiṣṭhān śrāddheṣu narakam vrajet vṛtta śruta kula upetān sa kalatrān guṇa anvitān tad arhān śrotriyān viddhi brāhmaṇān ayujaḥ śubhe tatra śrāddha kriyām paścāt ārabheta yathāvidhi trīṇi śrāddhe pavitrāṇi dauhitraḥ kutapaḥ tilāḥ trīṇi ca atra praśaṃsanti śaucam akrodham a tvarām nīla śākam gajacchāyā pavitram śrāddha karmasu tilān avakiret tatra nānā varṇān samantataḥ aśuddham pitṛ yajñeṣu tilaiḥ śudhyati śobhane nīla kāṣāya vastram ca bhinna karṇam nava vraṇam hīna aṅgam aśucim vā api varjayet tatra dūratas kukkuṭān ca varāhān ca nagnam klībam rajasvalām āyasam trapu sīsam ca śrāddha karmaṇi varjayet māṃsaiḥ prīṇanti pitaraḥ mudga māṣa yavaiḥ iha śaśa raurava māṃsena ṣaṣ māsam tṛptiḥ iṣyate vārdhrāṇasasya māṃsena tṛptiḥ dvādaśa vārṣikī ānantyāya bhavet dattam khaḍga māṃsam pitṛ kṣaye pāyasam sa tilam kṣaudram khaḍga māṃsena saṃmitam mahā śaphariṇaḥ matsyāḥ chāgaḥ vā sarva lohitaḥ kālaśākakam iti eva tad ānantyam prakīrtitam sa apūpam sa āmiṣam snigdham āhāram upakalpayet upakalpya tad āhāram brāhmaṇān arcayet tatas śmaśrukarma śiraḥsnātān samāropya āsanam kramāt su gandha mālya ābharaṇaiḥ sragbhiḥ etān vibhūṣayet alaṃkṛta upaviṣṭān tān piṇḍa āvāpam nivedayet tatas prastīrya darbhāṇām prastaram dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ samīpe tu agnīṣomābhyām pitṛbhyaḥ juhuyāt tathā tatas darbheṣu piṇḍān trīn nivapet dakṣiṇā mukham apasavyam apāṅguṣṭham nāmadheya puraskṛtam etena vidhinā dattam pitṝṇām akṣayam bhavet tatas viprān yathākāmam pūjayet niyataḥ śuciḥ sa dakṣiṇam sa saṃbhāram yathā tuṣyanti te dvijāḥ tatas nirvapaṇe vṛtte tān piṇḍān tad antaram patnīm vā madhyamam piṇḍam putra kāmaḥ hi prāśayet tṛptān utthāpya tān viprān anna śeṣam nivedayet tad śeṣam bahubhiḥ paścāt sa bhṛtyaḥ bhakṣayet naraḥ eṣa proktaḥ samāsena pitṛ yajñaḥ sanātanaḥ ahani ahani vā kuryāt māse māse atha vā punar dīrgha āyuḥ ca bhavet svasthaḥ pitṛ medhena mānavaḥ śrāddhāni puṣṭi kāmāḥ ye prakurvanti ca paṇḍitāḥ teṣām puṣṭim prajāḥ ca eva dāsyanti pitaraḥ sadā dhanyam yaśasyam āyuṣyam svargyam śatru vināśanam umā kula saṃdhāraṇam ca iti śrāddham āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ nānā jātiṣu jāyante śīghram karma vaśāt punar pitṝṇām katamaḥ deśaḥ piṇḍān aśnanti te katham anne datte mṛtānām tu katham āpyāyanam bhavet nāradaḥ evam mayā saṃśayitam bhagavan chettum arhasi etat viruddham rudrāṇyām pṛcchatyām pariṣad bhṛśam maheśvaraḥ babhūva sarvā muditā śrotum paramakam hi tat sthāne saṃśayitam devi śṛṇu kalyāṇe tattvāt guhyānām paramam guhyam khilānām paramam khilam yathā deva gaṇāḥ devi tathā pitṛ gaṇāḥ priye dakṣiṇasyām diśi śubhe sarve pitṛ gaṇāḥ sthitāḥ pretān uddiśya yā pūjā kriyate mānuṣaiḥ iha tena tuṣyanti pitaraḥ na pretāḥ pitaraḥ smṛtāḥ dakṣiṇasyām tathā te ca tuṣyanti vividhaiḥ makhaiḥ āpyāyitāḥ ca te śrāddhaiḥ punar āpyāyayanti tān an iṣṭvā ca pitṝn pūrvam yaḥ kriyām prakaroti ced rakṣāṃsi ca piśācāḥ ca phalam bhokṣyanti tasya tat kavyena saṃtatiḥ dṛṣṭā havye bhūtiḥ pṛthagvidhā umā maheśvaraḥ pramāṇam phala mānānām tat me śaṃsitum arhasi pramāṇa kalpanām devi dānasya śṛṇu bhāmini koṭisāraḥ tu tām koṭim dadan mahat avāpnuyāt ānantyam ca mahat ca eva samam hīnam ca pātakam teṣām viśeṣān vakṣyāmi śṛṇu devi samāhitā dānam ṣaḍguṇa yuktam tu mahat iti abhidhīyate yathāśraddham tu vai dānam yathārham samam ucyate guṇataḥ tu tathā hīnam dānam hīnam iti smṛtam dānam pātakam iti āhuḥ ṣaḍguṇānām viparyaye samasya tu tathā dānam mānuṣam bhogam āvahet dānam niṣphalam iti āhuḥ vihīnam kriyayā śubhe umā maheśvaraḥ aśubhasya api dānasya śubham syāt ca phalam katham manasā tattvataḥ śuddham anṛśaṃsa puraḥsaram prītyā tu sarva dānāni dattvā phalam avāpnuyāt rahasyam sarva dānānām etat viddhi śubha īkṣaṇe anyāni sarva kāryāṇi śṛṇu sadbhiḥ kṛtāni ca ārāmam devagoṣṭhāni saṃkramāḥ kūpaḥ eva ca go vāṭam ca taṭākam ca sabhāḥ śālāḥ ca sarvaśas bhikṣuka āvasathāḥ ca eva pānīyam go tṛṇāni ca vyādhitānām ca bhaiṣajyam anāthānām ca bhojanam anātha śava saṃskāraḥ tīrtha mārga viśodhanam vyasana abhyavapattiḥ ca sarveṣām ca sva śaktitaḥ tat kartavyam manuṣyeṇa sva śaktyā śraddhayā śubhe pretyabhāve labhet puṇyam na asti tatra vicāraṇā rūpam saubhāgyam ārogyam balam saukhyam labhet naraḥ umā svarge vā mānuṣe vā api taiḥ taiḥ āpyāyate hi saḥ maheśvaraḥ śṛṇu devi samuddeśāt nānātvam dharma saṃkaṭe smṛti dharmaḥ ca bahudhā sadbhiḥ ācāraḥ iṣyate jāti dharmāḥ ca vai dharmāḥ gaṇa dharmāḥ ca śobhane śarīra kāla vaiṣamyāt āpad dharmaḥ ca dṛśyate evam dharmasya nānātvam phalam kurvan labhet naraḥ śrautaḥ smārtaḥ tu dharmāṇām prākṛtaḥ dharmaḥ ucyate umā śrutam pāpa kṛtam duḥkham yama loke vara prada śrotum icchāmi aham deva nṛṇām su kṛta karmaṇām kathitāḥ kīdṛśāḥ lokāḥ nṛṇām sukṛta kāriṇām maheśvaraḥ śṛṇu kalyāṇe tat sarvam yat tvam icchasi bhāmini vividhāḥ puṇya lokāḥ te karma akarmaṇya tām gatāḥ merum hi kanaka ātmānam paritas sarvatodiśam bhadrāśvaḥ ketumālaḥ ca uttarāḥ kuravaḥ tathā jambu vana ādayaḥ svargāḥ iti ete karma varjitāḥ teṣu bhogāḥ svayam bhūtāḥ pradṛśyante yatas tatas yojanānām sahasram tu ekaikam māna mātrayā nitya puṣpa phala upetāḥ tatra vṛkṣāḥ samantataḥ āsakta vastra ābharaṇāḥ sarve kanaka saṃnibhāḥ dvirephāḥ ca aṇḍajāḥ tatra pravāla maṇi saṃnibhāḥ vicitrāḥ ca manojñāḥ ca kūjitaiḥ śobhayanti tān kuśeśaya vanaiḥ channāḥ nalinyaḥ ca manoramāḥ tatra vānti anilāḥ nityam divya gandhāḥ sukha āvahāḥ sarve ca a mlāna mālyāḥ ca viraja umbara saṃvṛtāḥ evam bahuvidhāḥ devi divi bhogāḥ sukha āvahāḥ striyaḥ ca puruṣāḥ ca eva sarve sukṛta kāriṇaḥ ramante tatra ca anyonyam kāma rāga samanvitāḥ divya bhūṣaṇa saṃyuktāḥ divya gandha samanvitāḥ manoramāḥ mahābhāgāḥ sarve lalita kuṇḍalāḥ evam tatra gatāḥ martyāḥ pramadāḥ priya darśanāḥ nānā bhāva samāyuktāḥ yauvana sthāḥ sadā eva tu kamanīyāḥ kāma yutāḥ kāma jñāḥ lalitāḥ tathā manonukūlāḥ madhurāḥ bhoginām upakalpitāḥ evaṃvidhāḥ striyaḥ ca atra puruṣāḥ ca parasparam kāma harṣau guṇau āstām na anye krodha ādayaḥ priye kṣudh pipāsā na ca asti atra gātra kleśāḥ ca śobhane yāvat puṇya phalam tāvat ramante tatra saṃgatāḥ tatra bhogān yathāyogam bhuktvā puṇya kṣayāt punar naśyanti jāyamānāḥ te śarīraiḥ sahasā priye svarga lokāt paribhraṣṭāḥ jāyante mānuṣe punar pūrva puṇya avaśeṣeṇa viśiṣṭāḥ saṃbhavanti te eṣā svarga gatiḥ proktā pṛcchantyāḥ tava bhāmini atas ūrdhvam padāni aṣṭau karmaṇyāni śṛṇu priye vidyādharāḥ kiṃpuruṣāḥ yakṣa gandharva kiṃnarāḥ apsaraḥ dānavāḥ devāḥ yathākramam udāhṛtāḥ teṣu sthāneṣu jāyante prāṇinaḥ puṇya karmiṇaḥ teṣām api ca ye lokāḥ svarga loka upamāḥ smṛtāḥ rūpa sattva bala upetāḥ sarve dīrgha āyuṣaḥ tathā teṣām sarva kriyā ārambhaḥ mānuṣeṣu eva dṛśyate ati mānuṣam āścaryam astra māyā balātkṛtam jarā prasūti maraṇam teṣu sthāneṣu dṛśyate guṇa doṣāḥ ca santi atra ākāśagamanam tathā antardhānam balam sarvam āyuḥ ca cira jīvanam tapaḥ viśeṣāt jāyante teṣām karmāṇi bhāmini na tathā deva lokaḥ hi tad viśiṣṭāḥ surāḥ smṛtāḥ umā mānuṣeṣu eva jīvatsu gatiḥ vijñāyate na vā maheśvaraḥ tat aham te pravakṣyāmi jīvatām vidyate yathā dvividhāḥ prāṇinaḥ loke daiva āsura samāśritāḥ manasā karmaṇā vācā pratikūlāḥ bhavanti ye tādṛśān āsurān viddhi martyāḥ te naraka ālayāḥ rāga dveṣa yutāḥ ye tu nirlajjāḥ nirapatrapāḥ darpa ahaṃkāra saṃyuktāḥ narāḥ naraka gāminaḥ nāstikāḥ ca śaṭhāḥ ghorāḥ pareṣām upatāpinaḥ yathā iṣṭa vṛttayaḥ ca eva narāḥ naraka gāminaḥ duṣpratīta manāḥ yaḥ tu cala cittaḥ nirākṛtiḥ śiśna udara ratiḥ mūḍhaḥ nirayam yāti saḥ adhamaḥ māṃsa pāna priyāḥ nityam kaṭhorāḥ nīca vṛttayaḥ tādṛśān āsurān viddhi sarve te naraka ālayāḥ hiṃsā vihārāḥ ye nityam nirdayāḥ prāṇi nāśane svadharma vimukhāḥ ca eva para sveṣu abhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ yuddha mātsarya saṃyuktāḥ grāmya bhoga parāyaṇāḥ tādṛśān āsurān viddhi narān naraka gāminaḥ darpa utseka samāyuktāḥ mūrkhāḥ tattva bahiṣkṛtāḥ śruti vidveṣiṇaḥ nityam te narāḥ naraka ālayāḥ nityam vadanti ye mohāt anṛtam kaṭukam vacaḥ kṛtaghnāḥ piśunāḥ ghorāḥ bhavanti naraka ālayāḥ hiṃsrāḥ corāḥ ca dhūrtāḥ ca paradāra abhimarśinaḥ nīca karma karāḥ ye ca śauca maṅgala varjitāḥ śruti vidveṣiṇaḥ pāpāḥ loka cāritra dūṣakāḥ evam yukta samācārāḥ jīvantaḥ naraka ālayāḥ loka udvega karāḥ ca anye paśavaḥ ca sarīsṛpāḥ vṛkṣāḥ kaṇṭakinaḥ rūkṣāḥ tādṛśān viddhi ca asurān aparān deva pakṣān tu śṛṇu devi samāhitā tādṛśān amarān viddhi te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ śauca ārjava para adhīnāḥ para artham na haranti ye ye samāḥ sarva bhūteṣu te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ bhayāt vā vṛtti hetoḥ vā anṛtam na bruvanti ye dhārmikāḥ śauca saṃpannāḥ śuklāḥ madhura bhāṣiṇaḥ na akāryam manasā icchanti te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ daridrāḥ api ye ke cid yācitāḥ prīti pūrvakam āstikāḥ maṅgala parāḥ satatam vṛddha sevinaḥ puṇya karma pare nityam te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ śaktyā ca abhyavapadyante te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ vratinaḥ dāna śīlāḥ ca sukha śīlāḥ ca mānavāḥ ṛjavaḥ mṛdavaḥ nityam te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ guru śuśrūṣaṇa parāḥ deva brāhmaṇa pūjakāḥ kṛtajñāḥ kṛtavidyāḥ ca te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ jita indriyāḥ jita krodhāḥ jita māna mada spṛhāḥ lobha mātsarya hīnāḥ ye te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ nirmamāḥ nirahaṃkārāḥ sva anukrośāḥ sva bandhuṣu dīna anukampinaḥ nityam te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ evaṃvidhāḥ narāḥ loke jīvantaḥ svarga gāminaḥ paśavaḥ ca eva vṛkṣāḥ ca prajānām hita kāriṇaḥ tādṛśān deva pakṣa sthān iti viddhi śubha ānane śubha aśubha mayam loke sarvam sthāvara jaṅgamam umā daivam śubham iti prāhuḥ āsuram hi aśubham priye bhagavat mānuṣāḥ ke cit kāladharmam upasthitāḥ prāṇamokṣam katham kṛtvā paratra hitam āpnuyuḥ maheśvaraḥ hanta te kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇu devi samāhitā tayoḥ svabhāvam na upāyam yatna jam kāraṇa udbhavam etayoḥ ubhayoḥ devi vidhānam śṛṇu śobhane yatna jam nāma maraṇam ātmatyāgaḥ mumūrṣayā tatra akalya śarīrasya jarā vyādhiḥ ca kāraṇam mahāprasthāna gamanam tathā prāya upaveśanam evam caturvidhaḥ proktaḥ ātmatyāgaḥ mumūrṣatām eteṣām krama yogena vidhānam śṛṇu śobhane svadharma yuktam gārhasthyam ciram ūḍhvā vidhānataḥ tatra ānṛṇyam ca saṃprāpya vṛddhaḥ vā vyādhitaḥ api vā saṃvidhāya sva bandhūn ca karmaṇām bharaṇam tathā dānāni vidhivat kṛtvā dharma kārya artham ātmanaḥ anujñāpya janam sarvam vācā madhurayā bruvan upaspṛśya pratijñāya vyavasāya puraḥsaram mahāprasthānam icchet ced pratiṣṭheta uttarām diśam bhūtvā tāvat nirāhāraḥ yāvat prāṇa vimokṣaṇam ceṣṭā hānau śayitvā api tanmanāḥ prāṇam utsṛjet evam puṇya kṛtām lokān amalān pratipadyate deśe puṇyatame śreṣṭhe nirāhāraḥ tu saṃviśet āprāṇāntam śuciḥ bhūtvā kurvan dānam sva śaktitaḥ harim smaran tyajet prāṇān eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ kṛtvā kāṣṭha mayam cityam puṇya kṣetre nadīṣu vā daivatebhyaḥ namaskṛtya kṛtvā ca agnim pradakṣiṇam saḥ api lokān yathānyāyam prāpnuyāt puṇya karmaṇām saḥ api puṇya kṛtām lokān nisargāt pratipadyate tatas kalya śarīrasya saṃtyāgam śṛṇu tattvataḥ rakṣā artham kṣatriyasya iṣṭaḥ prajā pālana kāraṇāt yodhānām bhartṛ piṇḍa artham guru artham brahmacāriṇām go brāhmaṇa artham grāma artham sarveṣām ca vidhīyate sva rāṣṭra rakṣaṇa artham vā ku nṛpaiḥ pīḍitāḥ prajāḥ su saṃnaddhaḥ vyavasitaḥ saṃpraviśya a parāṅmukhaḥ evam rājā mṛtaḥ sadyas svarga loke mahīyate tādṛśī sugatiḥ na asti kṣatriyasya viśeṣataḥ bhṛtyaḥ vā bhartṛ piṇḍa artham bhartṛ karmaṇi upasthite kurvan tatra tu sāhāyyam ātma prāṇa anapekṣayā svāmi artham saṃtyajet prāṇān puṇyān lokān sa gacchati spṛhaṇīyaḥ sura gaṇaiḥ tatra na asti vicāraṇā evam go brāhmaṇa artham vā dīna artham vā tyajet tanum saḥ api puṇyam avāpnoti ānṛśaṃsya vyapekṣayā iti ete jīvita tyāge mārgāḥ te samudāhṛtāḥ saḥ anantam narakam yāti ātma hantṛ tva kāraṇāt tathā mṛtānām yat kāryam tat me śṛṇu yathāvidhi tatra api bodha saṃtyāgāt mūḍha tyāgaḥ viśiṣyate bhūmau saṃveśayet deham narasya vinaśiṣyataḥ nirjīvam vṛṇuyāt sadyas vāsasā tu kalevaram śmaśāne dakṣiṇe deśe citā agnau pradahet mṛtam atha vā nikṣipet bhūmau śarīram jīva varjitam divā ca śuklapakṣaḥ ca uttarāyaṇam eva ca mumūrṣūṇām praśastāni viparītam tu garhitam audakam ca aṣṭakā śrāddham bahubhiḥ bahuśas kṛtam āpyāyanam mṛtānām tat para loke bhavet śubham etat sarvam mayā proktam mānuṣāṇām hitāya ca umā lokeṣu vividhāḥ dharmāḥ tvad prasādāt mayā śrutāḥ viśiṣṭam sarva dharmebhyaḥ śāśvatam dhruvam avyayam ke cit mokṣam praśaṃsanti ke cid yajña phalam dvijāḥ vānaprastham punar ke cit gārhasthyam ke cit āśramam brahmacarya āśramam ke cit ke cid vāc saṃyama āśrayam mātaram pitaram ke cid sevamānāḥ divam gatāḥ āhave abhimukhāḥ ke cit nihatāḥ tridivam gatāḥ ke cit uñcha vrate siddhāḥ svarga mārgam samāśritāḥ ārjavena apare yuktāḥ hatāḥ ca anārjavaiḥ janaiḥ ṛjavaḥ nāka pṛṣṭhe tu śuddha ātmānaḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ nāradaḥ vacanam brūhi deveśa niścaya jñāna saṃjñitam evam pṛṣṭaḥ svayam devyā mahādevaḥ pinākadhṛk provāca madhuram vākyam sūkṣmam adhyātma saṃjñitam maheśvaraḥ nyāyataḥ tvam mahābhāge śrotu kāmā asi niścayam etat eva viśiṣṭam te yat tvam pṛcchasi mām priye tam tam eva abhijānāti na anyam dharmam śuci smite śṛṇu devi samāsena mokṣa jñānam anuttamam etat hi sarva dharmāṇām viśiṣṭam guhyam avyayam na asti mokṣāt param devi mokṣaḥ eva parā gatiḥ na atra devi jarā mṛtyū śokaḥ vā duḥkham eva vā jñānānām uttamam jñānam mokṣa jñānam viduḥ budhāḥ nityam akṣaram akṣobhyam ajaram śāśvatam śivam uśanti tat padam prājñāḥ spṛhaṇīyam sura asuraiḥ tasmāt mokṣaḥ pradhānaḥ tu trivargāt ca viśeṣataḥ mokṣasya tasya mārgaḥ ayam śrūyatām śubha lakṣaṇe brahma ādi sthāvara antar ca saṃsāraḥ ayam pravartate śoka vyādhi jarā doṣaiḥ maraṇena ca saṃyutaḥ saṃsāre prāṇinaḥ sarve nivartante tathā punar tatra saṃsāra cakrasya mokṣaḥ jñānena dṛśyate adhyātma tattva vijñānam jñānam iti abhidhīyate jñānasya grahaṇa upāyam ācāram jñāninaḥ tathā yathāvat saṃpravakṣyāmi tattvam ekamanāḥ śṛṇu brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vā api bhūtvā pūrvam gṛhe sthitaḥ ānṛṇyam sarvatas prāpya tatas tān saṃtyajet gṛhān tatas saṃtyajya gārhasthyam niścitaḥ vanam āśrayet vane guru samājñātaḥ dīkṣeta vidhi pūrvakam dīkṣām prāpya yathānyāyam sva vṛttam paripālayet gṛhṇīyāt api upādhyāyān mokṣa jñānam atandritaḥ dvividhaḥ ca punar mokṣaḥ sāṃkhyaḥ yogaḥ iti smṛtaḥ pañcaviṃśati vijñānam sāṃkhyam iti abhidhīyate aiśvaryam deva sāyujyam yoga śāstrasya nirṇaye tayoḥ anyataram jñānam śṛṇuyāt śiṣya tām gataḥ na a muṇḍaḥ na api a kāṣāyī na api a saṃvatsara uṣitaḥ sāṃkhya yogau na ca śrāvyau guruṇā sneha pūrvakam samaḥ śīta uṣṇa harṣa ādīn viṣaheta sadā muniḥ adhṛṣyaḥ kṣudh pipāsābhyām bhavet jñāna samādhinā kuṇḍikām carma saṃśikyam chatram yaṣṭim upānahau guroḥ pūrvam samuttiṣṭhet jaghanyam tasya saṃviśet na an anujñāpya bhartāram āvaśyakam api vrajet dvis ahnaḥ snāna śāṭena saṃdhyayoḥ abhiṣecanam eka kāla aśanam ca asya vihitam yatibhiḥ purā bhaikṣam sarvatra gṛhṇīyāt cintayet satatam niśi kāraṇe ca api saṃprāpte na kupyeta kadā cana dayā ca sarva bhūteṣu tasya dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ ātma yuktaḥ parām buddhim labhate pāpa nāśinīm yadā bhāvam na kurute sarva bhūteṣu pāpakam karmaṇā manasā vācā brahma saṃpadyate tadā vīta śoka bhaya ābādhaḥ padam prāpnoti anuttamam tulya nindā stutiḥ maunī sama loṣṭa aśma kāñcanaḥ maheśvaraḥ jñāna abhyāsena tena eva prāpnoti paramām gatim śoka vyādhi jarā duḥkhe nirvāṇam na upapadyate jñānam te saṃpravakṣyāmi tad mūlam amṛtam hi vai śoka sthāna sahasrāṇi bhaya sthāna śatāni ca divase divase mūḍham āviśanti na paṇḍitam naṣṭe dhane vā dāre vā putre pitari vā mṛte dravyeṣu samatīteṣu ye guṇāḥ tān na cintayet tān an ādriyamāṇasya śoka bandhaḥ praṇaśyati mānuṣāḥ mānasaiḥ duḥkhaiḥ saṃyujyante alpabuddhayaḥ mṛtam vā yadi vā naṣṭam yaḥ atītam anuśocati sukham prāpya na saṃhṛṣyet duḥkham prāpya na saṃjvaret aniṣṭena anvitam paśyet yathā kṣipram virajyate yathā kāṣṭham ca kāṣṭham ca sameyātām mahā udadhau sametya ca vyapeyātām tadvat jñāti samāgamaḥ adarśanāt āpatitāḥ punar ca adarśanam gatāḥ kuṭumbam putra dāram ca śarīram dhana saṃcayaḥ pārakyam adhruvam sarvam kim svam sukṛta duṣkṛte putra dāra kuṭumbeṣu saktāḥ sīdanti jantavaḥ saraḥ paṅka arṇave magnāḥ jīrṇāḥ iva mahā gajāḥ mātā pitṛ sahasrāṇi putra dāra śatāni ca asaṃkhyeyāni atītāni tathā eva anāgatāni ca na teṣām ca mayā kāryam na kāryam mama taiḥ api duḥkha upaghāte śārīre mānase vā samutthite āyāsaḥ vā yatas mūlaḥ tat ekāṅgam api tyajet anityam yauvanam rūpam jīvitam ratna saṃcayaḥ sukham ekāntataḥ na asti śakrasya api triviṣṭape kṣaya antāḥ nicayāḥ sarve patana antāḥ samucchrayāḥ saṃyogāḥ viprayoga antāḥ maraṇa antam ca jīvitam ucchrayān vinipātān ca dṛṣṭvā pratyakṣatas svayam arthānām ārjane duḥkham ārjitānām ca rakṣaṇe nāśe duḥkham vyaye duḥkham dhik artham duḥkha bhājanam rāja taskara dāyādāḥ bhūtāni kṣayaḥ eva ca upadraveṣu ca arthānām duḥkham hi niyatam bhavet dhana lābhena tṛṣṇāyāḥ na tṛptiḥ upalabhyate jitvā api pṛthivīm kṛtsnām catur sāgara mekhalām sāgarāṇām punar pāram jetum icchati asaṃśayam yaḥ ekām pṛthivīm kṛtsnām eka chatrām praśāsti ca ekasmin eva rāṣṭre tu sa ca api nivaset nṛpaḥ tasmin rāṣṭre api nagaram ekam eva adhitiṣṭhati ekaḥ eva pratiṣṭhā syāt āvāsam tad gṛhe api ca āvāse śayanam ca ekam niśi yatra pralīyate sarvam mama iti saṃmūḍhaḥ janaḥ paśyati bāliśaḥ taṇḍula prastha mātreṇa yātrā syāt sarva dehinām na asti tṛṣṇā samam duḥkham na asti tyāga samam sukham yaḥ asau prāṇāntikaḥ rogaḥ tām tṛṣṇām tyajataḥ sukham na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyati haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmā iva bhūyas eva abhivardhate alābhena iha kāmānām kāmān tyajati paṇḍitaḥ yat pṛthivyām vrīhi yavam hiraṇyam paśavaḥ striyaḥ tṛṣṇā kṣaya sukhasya ete na arhataḥ ṣoḍaśīm kalām manaḥ ṣaṣṭhāni saṃyamya nityam ātmani yojayet indriyāṇām visargeṇa doṣam ṛcchati asaṃśayam ṣaṇṇām ātmani yuktānām aiśvaryam yaḥ adhigacchati na sa pāpaiḥ na ca anarthaiḥ saṃyujyeta vicakṣaṇaḥ apramattaḥ sadā rakṣet indriyāṇi vicakṣaṇaḥ hṛdi kāma mayaḥ citraḥ moha saṃcaya saṃbhavaḥ ajñāna rūḍha mūlaḥ tu vidhitsā pariṣecanaḥ roṣa lobha mahā skandhaḥ purā duṣkṛta sāravān āyāsa viṭapaḥ tīvraḥ śoka puṣpaḥ bhaya aṅkuraḥ nānā saṃkalpa pattra āḍhyaḥ pramāda parivardhitaḥ mahatībhiḥ pipāsābhiḥ samantāt parivardhitaḥ saṃrohati a kṛta prajñaḥ pādapaḥ kāma saṃbhavaḥ kṛcchra upāyeṣu anityeṣu niḥsāreṣu caleṣu ca duḥkha ādiṣu duranteṣu kāma bhogeṣu kā ratiḥ yena saṃvatsaraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sakṛt kāmaḥ ca sevitaḥ tena sarvam idam dṛṣṭam punarāvartakam jagat purastāt ca sthite mṛtyau kim sukham paśyataḥ śubhe vyādhibhiḥ pīḍyamānasya nityam śārīra mānasaiḥ saṃcinvānakam eva artham kāmānām avitṛptakam vyāghraḥ paśum iva araṇye mṛtyuḥ ādāya gacchati umā saṃsāre pacyamānaḥ tu pāpāt na udvijate janaḥ tapasā vā su mahatā karmaṇā vā śrutena vā maheśvaraḥ sarva lokeṣu jānīhi mokṣāt anyatra bhāmini maraṇam na ativartante vinā muktyā śarīriṇaḥ na taranti jarā mṛtyū nirvāṇa adhigamāt vinā aiśvaryam dhana dhānyam ca vidyā lābhaḥ tapaḥ tathā dāna yajña tapaḥ śīlāḥ rasāyana vidaḥ api vā na hi ahāni nivartante na māsāḥ na punar kṣapāḥ āyuḥ ādāya martyānām ahar rātrāṇi saṃtatam jīvitam sarva bhūtānām akṣayaḥ kṣapayan asau yasyām rātryām vyatītāyām āyuḥ alpataram bhavet tiṣṭhan eva kṣaṇam sarvaḥ kālasya eti vaśam punar na ca aniṣṭam pravarteta śokaḥ vā prāṇinām kva cit apramattaḥ pramatteṣu kālaḥ bhūteṣu tiṣṭhati śvas kāryam adya kurvīta pūrvāhṇe ca āparāhṇikam kaḥ hi tat veda yatra asau mṛtyunā na abhivīkṣitaḥ varṣāsu idam kariṣyāmi idam grīṣma vasantayoḥ idam me syāt idam me syāt iti evaṃmanasaḥ narāḥ an avāpteṣu kāmeṣu hriyante maraṇam prati kāla pāśena baddhānām ahani ahani jīryatām kā śraddhā prāṇinām mārge viṣame bhramatām sadā phalānām iva pakvānām sadā hi patanāt bhayam eka ahnā sarvam utsṛjya mṛtyoḥ hi vaśam eyivān jāyamānān ca saṃprekṣya mriyamāṇān tathā eva ca na saṃvegaḥ asti ced puṃsaḥ kāṣṭha loṣṭa samaḥ hi saḥ udvegaḥ jāyate nityam nirvāṇasya puraḥsaraḥ vairāgyeṇa parām śāntim labhante mānavāḥ śubhe maheśvaraḥ sāṃkhya jñānam pravakṣyāmi yathāvat te śuci smite yat jñātvā na punar martyaḥ saṃsāreṣu pravartate jñānena eva vimuktāḥ te sāṃkhyāḥ saṃnyāsa kovidāḥ śārīram tu tapaḥ ghoram sāṃkhyāḥ prāhuḥ nirarthakam pañcaviṃśatikam jñānam teṣām jñānam iti smṛtam asya kṣetrasya saṃkṣepaḥ caturviṃśatiḥ iṣyate pañcaviṃśatiḥ iti āhuḥ puruṣeṇa iha saṃkhyayā sattvam rajaḥ tamaḥ iti guṇāḥ prakṛti saṃbhavāḥ taiḥ sṛjati akhilam lokam prakṛtiḥ sva ātma jaiḥ guṇaiḥ icchā dveṣaḥ sukham duḥkham saṃghātaḥ cetanā dhṛtiḥ vikārāḥ prakṛteḥ ca ete veditavyāḥ manīṣibhiḥ lakṣaṇam ca api sarveṣām vikalpam ca āditas pṛthak vistareṇa pravakṣyāmi tasya vyākhyām imām śṛṇu avyaktasya eva nāmāni śabdaiḥ paryāya vācakaiḥ tad mūlam ca jagat sarvam tad mūlā sṛṣṭiḥ iṣyate sattva ādayaḥ prakṛti jāḥ guṇāḥ tān prabravīmi aham sukham tuṣṭiḥ prakāśaḥ ca trayaḥ te sāttvikāḥ guṇāḥ rāga dveṣau sukham duḥkham stambhaḥ ca rajasaḥ guṇāḥ aprakāśaḥ bhayam mohaḥ tandrā ca tamasaḥ guṇāḥ śraddhā praharṣaḥ vijñānam asaṃmohaḥ dayā dhṛtiḥ kāmaḥ krodhaḥ manaḥ tāpaḥ drohaḥ lobhaḥ tathā tṛṣā viṣādaḥ saṃśayaḥ mohaḥ tandrā nidrā bhayam tathā yadā saṃtāpa saṃyuktam citta kṣobha karam bhavet yadā saṃmoha saṃyuktam yat viṣāda karam bhavet samāsāt sāttvikaḥ dharmaḥ samāsāt rājasam dhanam samāsāt tāmasaḥ kāmaḥ trivarge triguṇa kramāt brahma ādi deva sṛṣṭiḥ yā sāttvikā iti prakīrtyate rājasī mānuṣī sṛṣṭiḥ tiryagyoniḥ tu tāmasī ūrdhvam gacchanti sattva sthāḥ madhye tiṣṭhanti rājasāḥ deva mānuṣa tiryakṣu yat bhūtam sacarācaram ādi prabhṛti saṃyuktam vyāptam ebhiḥ tribhiḥ guṇaiḥ atas param pravakṣyāmi mahat ādīni liṅgataḥ vijñānam ca vivekaḥ ca mahataḥ lakṣaṇam bhavet mahān buddhiḥ matiḥ prajñā nāmāni mahataḥ viduḥ ahaṃkāraḥ sa vijñeyaḥ lakṣaṇena samāsatas ahaṃkāreṇa bhūtānām sarveṣām prabhava apyayau ahaṃkāra nivṛttiḥ hi nirvāṇāya upapadyate kham vāyuḥ agniḥ salilam pṛthivī ca iti pañcamī mahābhūtāni bhūtānām sarveṣām prabhava apyayau śabdaḥ śrotram tathā khāni trayam ākāśa saṃbhavam sparśaḥ tvac prāṇinām ceṣṭā pavanasya guṇāḥ smṛtāḥ rūpam pākaḥ akṣiṇī jyotiḥ catvāraḥ tejasaḥ guṇāḥ rasaḥ snehaḥ tathā jihvā śaityam ca jala jāḥ guṇāḥ gandhaḥ ghrāṇam śarīram ca pṛthivyāḥ te guṇāḥ trayaḥ iti sarva guṇāḥ devi vyākhyātāḥ pāñcabhautikāḥ guṇān pūrvasya pūrvasya prāpnuvanti uttarāṇi tu tasmāt na eka guṇāḥ ca iha dṛśyante bhūta sṛṣṭayaḥ apām gandha guṇam prājñāḥ na icchanti kamala īkṣaṇe tat gandha tvam apām na asti pṛthivyāḥ eva tad guṇaḥ prāṇa apāna āśrayaḥ vāyuḥ kheṣu ākāśaḥ śarīriṇām keśa asthi nakha danta tvac pāṇi pāda śirāṃsi ca pṛṣṭha udara kaṭi grīvāḥ sarvam bhūmi ātmakam smṛ yat kim cit api kāye asmin dhātu doṣa mala āśritam buddhīndriyāṇi karṇaḥ tvac akṣi jihvā atha nāsikā karmendriyāṇi vāc pāṇiḥ pādaḥ meḍhram gudam tathā śabdaḥ sparśaḥ ca rūpam ca rasaḥ gandhaḥ ca pañcamaḥ buddhīndriya arthān jānīyāt bhūtebhyaḥ tu abhiniḥsṛtān vākyam kriyā gatiḥ prītiḥ utsargaḥ ca iti pañcadhā karmendriya arthān jānīyāt te ca bhūta udbhavāḥ matāḥ indriyāṇām tu sarveṣām īśvaram manaḥ ucyate prārthanā lakṣaṇam tat ca indriyam tu manaḥ smṛtam niyuṅkte ca sadā tāni bhūtātmā manasā saha indriyāṇi indriya arthāḥ ca svabhāvaḥ cetanā dhṛtiḥ bhūta abhūta vikāraḥ ca śarīram iti saṃjñitam śarīrāt ca paraḥ dehī śarīram ca vyapāśritaḥ śarīriṇaḥ śarīrasya yaḥ antaram vetti vai muniḥ aśarīram śarīreṣu didṛkṣeta nirindriyam na eva ayam cakṣuṣā grāhyaḥ na aparaiḥ indriyaiḥ api manasā eṣa pradīpena mahān ātmā pradṛśyate sa hi sarveṣu bhūteṣu sthāvareṣu careṣu ca vasati ekaḥ mahā vīryaḥ nānā bhāva samanvitaḥ nava dvāram puram gatvā haṃsaḥ asau nīyate vaśam īśvaraḥ sarva bhūteṣu sthāvarasya carasya ca bahudhā sarva bhūtāni vyāpya tiṣṭhati śāśvataḥ kṣetrajñam ekatas kṛtvā sarvam kṣetram atha ekatas evam saṃvimṛśet jñānī saṃyataḥ satatam hṛdā puruṣaḥ prakṛti sthaḥ hi bhuṅkte prakṛti jān guṇān kārya kāraṇa kartṛ tve hetuḥ prakṛtiḥ ucyate puruṣaḥ sukha duḥkhānām bhoktṛ tve hetuḥ ucyate jñānam ūṣmā ca vāyuḥ ca śarīre jīva saṃjñitaḥ apare sarva lokān ca vyāpya tiṣṭhantam īśvaram apare nāstikāḥ mūḍhāḥ hīna tvāt sūkṣma lakṣaṇaiḥ na asti ātmā iti viniścitya prāhuḥ te niraya ālayāḥ evam nānā vidhānena vimṛśanti maheśvaram ṛṣibhiḥ ca api devaiḥ ca vyaktam eṣa tu dṛśyate dṛṣṭvā ātatam mahātmānam punar tat na nivartate maheśvaraḥ kapila ādibhiḥ ācāryaiḥ sevitaḥ parama ṛṣibhiḥ sāṃkhya jñānena yuktānām tat etat kīrtitam mayā yoga dharmam punar kṛtsnam kīrtayiṣyāmi me śṛṇu sa ca aṣṭaguṇam aiśvaryam adhikṛtya vidhīyate sāyujyam sarva devānām yoga dharmaḥ paraḥ smṛ aikātmyam buddhi manasoḥ indriyāṇām ca sarvaśas ātmani avyayini prājñe jñānam etat tu yoginām arcayet brāhmaṇān agnīn devatāyatanāni ca varjayet aśivām vācam bhavet sattvam upāśritaḥ dānam adhyayanam śraddhā vratāni niyamāḥ tathā dhūta pāpmā ca tejasvī laghu āhāraḥ jita indriyaḥ niḥśokaḥ nirmalaḥ dāntaḥ paścāt yogam samācaret avadadhyāt manaḥ pūrvam matsya ghāte iva āmiṣam ekānte vijane deśe sarvatas saṃvṛte śucau kalpayet āsanam tatra su āstīrṇam mṛdubhiḥ kuśaiḥ upaviśya āsane tasmin ṛju kāya śirodharaḥ avyagraḥ sukham āsīnaḥ sva aṅgāni na vikampayet saṃprekṣya nāsikā agram svam diśaḥ ca anavalokayān bhruvoḥ madhye manaḥ kṛtvā cintayitvā śarīriṇam tvac śrotram ca tatas jihvām ghrāṇam cakṣuḥ ca saṃharet pañca indriyāṇi saṃdhāya manasi sthāpayet budhaḥ yadā etāni avatiṣṭhante manaḥ ṣaṣṭhāni ca ātmani prāṇa apānau tadā tasya yugapad tiṣṭhataḥ vaśe śarīram cintayet sarvam vipāṭya ca samīpatas antar deha gatim ca api prāṇānām paricintayet tatas mūrdhānam agnim ca śārīram paripālayan prāṇaḥ mūrdhani ca agnau ca vartamānaḥ viceṣṭate sa jantuḥ sarva bhūta ātmā puruṣaḥ sa sanātanaḥ manaḥ buddhiḥ ahaṃkāraḥ bhūtāni viṣayān ca saḥ vasti mūlam gudam ca eva pāvakam ca samāśritaḥ vahat mūtram purīṣam ca api apānaḥ parivartate udānaḥ iti tam vidyuḥ adhyātma kuśalāḥ janāḥ saṃdhau saṃdhau saṃniviṣṭaḥ sarva ceṣṭā pravartakaḥ śarīreṣu manuṣyāṇām vyānaḥ iti upadiśyate dhātuṣu agnau ca vitataḥ samānaḥ agniḥ samīraṇaḥ saḥ eva sarva ceṣṭānām anta kāle nivartakaḥ prāṇānām saṃnipāteṣu saṃsargāt yaḥ prajāyate ūṣmā saḥ agniḥ iti jñeyaḥ saḥ annam pacati dehinām apāna prāṇayoḥ madhye prāṇa apāna samāhitaḥ pṛṣṭhatas tu samānena svām svām gatim upāśritaḥ śarīra madhye nābhiḥ syāt nābhyām agniḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ agnau prāṇāḥ ca saṃsaktāḥ prāṇeṣu ātmā vyavasthitaḥ pakvāśayaḥ tu adhas nābheḥ ūrdhvam āmāśayaḥ smṛtaḥ nābhiḥ madhye śarīrasya sarva prāṇāḥ tam āśritāḥ sthitāḥ prāṇa ādayaḥ sarve tiryak ūrdhvam adhas carāḥ vahanti anna rasān nāḍyaḥ daśa prāṇa pracoditāḥ yoginām eṣa mārgaḥ tu pañcasu eteṣu tiṣṭhati jita śramaḥ samāsīnaḥ mūrdhani ātmānam ādadhet saṃnirudhya tatas prāṇān ātmānam cintayet param prāṇe tu apānam yuñjīta prāṇān ca apāna karmaṇi prāṇa apāna gatīḥ ruddhvā prāṇāyāma paraḥ bhavet evam antar prayuñjīta pañca prāṇān parasparam vijane saṃmita āhāraḥ muniḥ tūṣṇīm nirucchvasan prasīdati manaḥ kṣipram prasanne dṛśyate paraḥ vaidyutaḥ agniḥ iva ākāśe dṛśyate puruṣaḥ avyayaḥ dṛṣṭvā tat ātmānaḥ jyotiḥ aiśvarya aṣṭaguṇaiḥ yutam prāpnoti paramam sthānam spṛhaṇīyam suraiḥ api imān yogasya doṣān ca daśa eva paricakṣate doṣaiḥ vighnaḥ varārohe yoginām kavibhiḥ smṛtaḥ kāmam krodham bhayam svapnam sneham ati aśanam tathā vaicityam vyādhim ālasyam lobham ca daśamam smṛtam tasmāt etān apāsya ādau yuñjīta capalam manaḥ imān api guṇān aṣṭau yogasya paricakṣate aṇimā mahimā ca eva prāptiḥ prākāśya lāghave īśitvam ca vaśitvam ca yatra kāmāvasāyi tā etān aṣṭau guṇān prāpya katham cit yoginām vara īśāḥ sarvasya lokasya devān api atiśerate na ca ati svapna śīlasya na ati jāgarataḥ tathā sāyujyam devasātkṛtya prayuñjīta ātma bhaktitaḥ arcayitvā yathāśakti svakam devam viśanti te sāyujyānām viśiṣṭe dve māmakam vaiṣṇavam tathā mām prāpya na nivartante viṣṇum vā śubha locane umā triyakṣa tridaśa śreṣṭha tryambaka tridaśādhipa dakṣa yajña pramathana śūlapāṇe ari sūdana bhavatā parituṣṭena śṛṇvantyā mama bhāṣitam idānīm śrotum icchāmi sāyujyam tvad gatam vibho ācāraḥ kīdṛśaḥ teṣām kena tuṣṭaḥ bhavet bhavān maheśvaraḥ varṇyamānam tvayā sākṣāt prīṇayati adhikam hi mām sāṃkhya yogau mayā sṛṣṭau sarvam ca api carācaram arcanīyaḥ aham īśaḥ aham avyayaḥ aham sanātanaḥ aham prasannaḥ bhaktānām dadāmi amara tām api na mām viduḥ sura gaṇāḥ munayaḥ ca tapodhanāḥ āśramebhyaḥ caturbhyaḥ aham caturaḥ brāhmaṇān śubhe mad bhaktān nirmalān puṇyān samānīya tapasvinaḥ vyācakhye aham tadā devi yogam pāśupatam mahat gṛhītam tat ca taiḥ sarvam mukhāt ca mama dakṣiṇāt śrutvā ca triṣu lokeṣu sthāpitam ca api taiḥ punar idānīm ca tvayā pṛṣṭaḥ tvad priya artham anindite tat sarvam kathayiṣyāmi tat tvam ekamanāḥ śṛṇu aham paśupatiḥ nāma mad bhaktāḥ ye ca mānavāḥ sarve pāśupatāḥ jñeyāḥ bhasma digdha tanūruhāḥ rakṣā artham maṅgala artham ca pavitra artham ca bhāmini liṅga artham ca eva bhaktānām bhasma dattam mayā purā tena saṃdigdha sarva aṅgāḥ bhasmanā brahmacāriṇaḥ jaṭilāḥ muṇḍitāḥ vā api nānākṛta śikhaṇḍinaḥ vikṛtāḥ piṅgala ābhāḥ ca nagnāḥ nānā prahāriṇaḥ bhaikṣam carantaḥ sarvatra niḥspṛhāḥ niṣparigrahāḥ mama pāśupatam divyam yoga śāstram anuttamam sūkṣmam sarveṣu lokeṣu vimṛśantaḥ caranti te evam nitya abhiyuktānām mad bhaktānām tapasvinām upāyam cintayāmi āśu yena mām upayānti te sthāpitam triṣu lokeṣu śiva liṅgam mayā priye yaṣṭam dattam adhītam ca yajñāḥ ca saha dakṣiṇāḥ śiva liṅga praṇāmasya kalām na arhanti ṣoḍaśīm arcayā śiva liṅgasya parituṣyāmi aham priye śiva liṅga arcanāyām tu vidhānam api me śṛṇu go kṣīra navanītābhyām arcayet yaḥ śivam mama sa phalam prāpnuyāt martyaḥ brāhmaṇasya agnihotriṇaḥ sa ghṛtam guggulum samyak dhūpayet yaḥ śiva antike yaḥ tu deśa antaram gatvā śiva liṅgam samarcayet evam nānāvidhaiḥ dravyaiḥ śiva liṅgam samarcayet mad prasādāt manuṣyeṣu na punar jāyate naraḥ palāśa bilva patrāṇi rājavṛkṣa srajaḥ tathā arka puṣpāṇi medhyāni mad priyāṇi viśeṣataḥ phalam vā yadi vā śākam puṣpam vā yadi vā jalam mad bhaktāḥ na vinaśyanti mad bhaktāḥ vīta kalmaṣāḥ mad bhaktāḥ sarva lokeṣu pūjanīyāḥ viśeṣataḥ mad dveṣiṇaḥ ca ye martyāḥ mad bhakta dveṣiṇaḥ tathā yānti te narakam kṣipram iṣṭvā kratu śataiḥ api etat te sarvam ākhyātam yogam pāśupatam mama śṛṇuyāt yaḥ paṭhet vā api mama etam dharma niścayam nāradaḥ svargam kīrtim dhanam dhānyam labheta sa nara uttamaḥ evam uktvā mahādevaḥ śrotu kāmaḥ svayam prabhuḥ maheśvaraḥ anukūlām priyām bhāryām pārśva sthām samabhāṣata parāvara jñe dharmāṇām tapovana nivāsinām dīkṣā dama śama upete satatam vrata cāriṇi pṛcchāmi tvā varārohe pṛṣṭā vada mama īpsitam sāvitrī brahmaṇaḥ patnī kauśikasya śacī śubhā lakṣmīḥ viṣṇoḥ priyatamā dhṛtiḥ bhāryā yamasya tu mārkaṇḍeyasya dhūmorṇā ṛddhiḥ vaiśravaṇasya tu rohiṇī śaśinaḥ bhāryā svāhā vahneḥ aninditā kaśyapasya aditiḥ ca eva vasiṣṭhasya api arundhatī etāḥ ca anyāḥ ca devyaḥ tu sarvāḥ tāḥ pati devatāḥ śrūyante loka vikhyātāḥ tvayā ca eva saha uṣitāḥ tābhiḥ ca pūjitā sā tvam anuvṛttya anubhāṣaṇaiḥ tasmāt tvām paripṛcchāmi dharma jñe loka saṃmate sa dharma cāriṇī me tvam samāna vrata cāriṇī samāna sārā vīryeṇa mayā eva tvam śubha ānane sura kāryam karoṣi tvam loka saṃdhāraṇā tathā ayam hi strī gaṇaḥ tvām tu anuyāti na muñcati tvad prasādāt hitam śrotum strī vṛttam śubha lakṣaṇe tvayā ca uktam viśeṣeṇa guru bhūtam hi tiṣṭhati tvayā eva vid hi arthaḥ strīṇām dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ tasmāt tvā paripṛcchāmi pṛṣṭā vada mama īpsitam nāradaḥ evam uktā tadā devī mahādevena śobhanā punar punar tadā devaḥ devīm kim iti ca abravīt bahuśas
