coditā devī sa vrīḍā ca idam abravīt umā maheśvaraḥ tvad antike mayā vaktum strīṇām dharmam katham bhavet umā imāḥ nadyaḥ mahādeva sarva tīrtha udaka anvitāḥ nāradaḥ mayā saṃmānitāḥ ca eva bhaviṣyanti sarit varāḥ iti matvā mahādevī nadīḥ devīḥ samāhvayat vipāśām ca vitastām ca candrabhāgām sarasvatīm śatadrum devikām sindhum gomatīm kauśikīm tathā yamunām narmadām ca eva kāverīm atha nimnagām tathā devanadīm gaṅgām prāptām tripathagām śubhām sarva tīrtha udaka vahām sarva pāpa vināśanīm umā etāḥ nadīḥ samāhūya samudvīkṣya idam abravīt he he puṇyāḥ sarit śreṣṭhāḥ sarva pāpa vinodakāḥ jñāna vijñāna saṃpannāḥ śṛṇudhvam vacanam mama ayam bhagavatā praśnaḥ uktaḥ strī dharmam āśritaḥ yuṣmābhiḥ tat vicārya eva vaktum icchāmi śobhanāḥ nāradaḥ iti pṛṣṭāḥ tayā devyā deva nadyaḥ cakampire tāsām śreṣṭhatamā gaṅgā vacanam ca idam abravīt dhanyāḥ ca anugṛhītāḥ sma anena vacanena te yā tvam sura asuraiḥ mānyā nadīḥ mānayase anaghe aśakyam api ye mūrkhāḥ sva ātma saṃbhāvanā yutāḥ yaḥ śaktaḥ ca an ahaṃvādī sudurlabhatamaḥ mataḥ tvam hi śaktā satī devī vaktum praśnam aśeṣatas vyāhartum na icchasi strī tvāt saṃpūjayasi naḥ tathā tvam hi deva samā devi ūha apoha viśāradā divya jñāna yutā devi divya jñāna indhana idhitā tvam eva arhasi tat vaktum strīṇām dharmam śubha aśubham nāradaḥ evam prasāditā devī gaṅgayā loka pūjitā umā prāha sarvam aśeṣeṇa strī dharmam surasundarī tvad prasādāt suraśreṣṭha tava eva priya kāmyayā nāradaḥ evam bruvantyām strī dharmam devyām devasya śāsanāt ṛṣi gandharva yakṣāṇām yoṣitaḥ ca apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ nāga bhūta striyaḥ ca eva nadyaḥ ca eva samāgatāḥ śrotu kāmāḥ param vākyam sarvāḥ paryavatasthire umā devī mudā yuktā pūjyamānā aṅganā gaṇaiḥ ānṛśaṃsya parā devī satatam strī gaṇam prati strī gaṇasya hita arthāya bhava priya cikīrṣayā umā vaktum vacanam ārebhe strīṇām dharma āśritam hitam ṛtu prāptā su śuddhā yā kanyā sā iti abhidhīyate tām tu kanyām pitā mātā bhrātā mātulaḥ eva vā pitṛvyaḥ ca iti pañca ete dātum prabhava tām gatāḥ vivāhāḥ ca tathā pañca tāsām dharma artha kāraṇāt kāmatas ca mithas dānam bhayāt ca prasabhāt tathā dattā yasya bhavet bhāryā eteṣām yena kena cit dātāraḥ saṃvimṛśya eva dātum arhanti na anyathā uttamānām tu varṇānām mantravat pāṇi saṃgrahaḥ vivāha karaṇam ca āhuḥ śūdrāṇām saṃprayogataḥ tadā prabhṛti sā nārī daśa rātram vivarjya ca manasā karmaṇā vācā hi anukūlā ca sā bhavet pativratā tvam nārīṇām etat eva samāsatas tādṛśā sā bhavet nityam yādṛśaḥ tu bhavet patiḥ śubha aśubha samācāre etat vṛttam samāsatas daivatam satatam sādhvī bhartāram yā anupaśyati etasmin kāraṇe deva paurāṇī śrūyate śrutiḥ kathayāmi prasādāt te śṛṇu deva samāhitaḥ tayoḥ ekā dharma kāmā devān uddiśya bhaktitaḥ cakāra vipulam dharmam pūjana arcanayā anvitam aparā dharma kāmā ca patim uddiśya śobhanā devapriyāyām tiṣṭhantyām puṇya lokam jagāma sā devapriyā ca tiṣṭhantī vilalāpa su duḥkhitā tām yamaḥ lokapālaḥ tu babhāṣe puṣkalam vacaḥ mā śocīḥ tvam nivartasva na lokāḥ santi te śubhe daivatam hi patiḥ nāryāḥ sthāpitam sarva daivataiḥ tadā gantāsi lokān tān yān gacchanti pativratāḥ na anyathā śakyate prāptum patnīnām lokaḥ uttamaḥ umā patimatyāḥ divārātram vṛttāntaḥ śrūyatām śubhaḥ patyuḥ pūrvam samutthāya prātaḥkarma samādiśet tatas paurvāhṇikam kāryam svayam kuryāt yathāvidhi nivedya ca tathā āhāram yathā saṃpadyatām iti śuśrūṣā poṣaṇa vidhau pati priya cikīrṣayā bhartuḥ niṣkramaṇe kāryam saṃsmaret apramādataḥ āgatam tu patim dṛṣṭvā sahasā paricārakaiḥ svayam kurvīta saṃprītyā kāya śrama haram param pādya āsanābhyām śayanaiḥ vākyaiḥ ca hṛdaya priyaiḥ atithīnām āgamane prīti yuktā sadā bhavet karmaṇā vacanena api toṣayet atithīn sadā maṅgalyam gṛha śaucam ca sarva upakaraṇāni ca sā yatnam paramam kuryāt tasya sāhāyya kāraṇāt yugaṃdharā bhavet sādhvī patyuḥ dharma arthayoḥ sadā vihāra kāle vai bhartuḥ jñātvā bhāvam hṛdi sthitam alaṃkṛtya yathāyogam hāva bhāva samanvitā kaṭhorāṇi na vācyāni anyadā pramadā antare yasyām kāmī bhavet bhartā tasyāḥ prīti karā bhavet anantaram tathā anyeṣām bhojana avekṣaṇam caret dāsī dāsa balīvardān caṇḍālān ca śvnaḥ tathā anāthān kṛpaṇān ca eva bhikṣukān ca tathā eva ca kupitam vā artha hīnam vā śrāntam vā upacaret patim yathā sa tuṣṭaḥ svasthaḥ ca bhavet saṃtoṣayet patim tathā kuṭumba cintāyām vivāde ca artha saṃśaye āhūtā ca sahāya artham tadā priya hitam vadet apriyam vā hitam brūyāt tasya kāma artha kāṅkṣayā bahis ālokanam ca eva moham vrīḍām ca paiśunam bahu āśi tvam divāsvapnam evamādīni varjayet rahasi eka āsanam sādhvī na kuryāt ātmajaiḥ api vismṛtam vā pati dravyam pratidadyāt sva śaucataḥ atiyācñām atīrṣyām ca dūratas parivarjayet bāla vat vṛddha vat nāryāḥ sadā eva ātura vat patiḥ spṛhā yasyāḥ yathā patyau sā nārīṇām pativratā patiḥ hi daivatam strīṇām patiḥ bandhuḥ patiḥ gatiḥ na anyām gatim aham paśye pramadānām yathā patiḥ jātiṣu api ca vai strī tvam viśiṣṭam iti me matiḥ kāya kleśena mahatā puruṣaḥ prāpnuyāt phalam yathāsukham patimatī sarvam pati anukūlataḥ īdṛśam dharma saukaryam paśyadhvam pramadāḥ prati rūpam kulam yaśaḥ svargaḥ sarvam tasmin pratiṣṭhitam evaṃvṛtta samācārā sva vṛttena eva śobhanā evaṃbhūtaḥ api bhartā vai strīṇām bhūṣaṇam uttamam āḍhyam vā rūpa yuktam vā virūpam dhana varjitam yā patim toṣayet sādhvī sā nārīṇām pativratā daridrān ca virūpān ca pramūḍhān kuṣṭha saṃyutān evaṃvidhān patīn deva toṣayitvā pativratā evam pravartamānāyāḥ patiḥ pūrvam mriyeta ced umā etat evam mayā proktam strīṇām dharma āśritam hitam saumya śīlāḥ śubha ācārāḥ sarvāḥ tāḥ saṃbhavanti hi atha aśubham pravakṣyāmi strīṇām vṛttam maheśvara āsuryaḥ ca eva paiśācyaḥ rākṣasyaḥ ca bhavanti yāḥ tāsām vṛttam aśeṣeṇa śrūyatām loka kāraṇāt nyāyataḥ vā anyathā proktāḥ bhāva doṣa samanvitāḥ bhartṝn apacaranti eva rāga dveṣa balātkṛtāḥ punar bhavanti pāpiṣṭhāḥ viṣamam vṛttam āśritāḥ anavasthita maryādāḥ bahu veṣāḥ vyaya priyāḥ asaṃtuṣṭāḥ ca lubdhāḥ ca īrṣyā krodha yutāḥ bhṛśam bhoga priyāḥ hita dveṣyāḥ kāma bhoga parāyaṇāḥ patīn paribhavanti eva pratikūla parāyaṇāḥ prāyaśas anṛta bhūyiṣṭhāḥ gurūṇām pratilomakāḥ evam yukta samācārāḥ āsuram bhāvam āśritāḥ aparāḥ pāpa kāriṇyaḥ satatam kalaha priyāḥ paruṣāḥ rūkṣa vacanāḥ nirghṛṇāḥ nirapatrapāḥ niḥsnehāḥ kopanāḥ ca eva bhartṛ putra sva bandhuṣu bandhubhiḥ bhartsitāḥ bhūtvā gṛha kāryāṇi kurvate atha vā bhartsitāḥ deva nīca vṛttāḥ sva bandhuṣu nirdayāḥ niranukrośāḥ kuṭumba artha vilopanāḥ dharma artha rahitāḥ ghorāḥ satatam kurvate kriyāḥ anartha nipuṇāḥ pāpāḥ para prāṇeṣu nirdayāḥ evaṃyukta samācārāḥ striyaḥ paiśācyam āśritāḥ aparāḥ moha saṃyuktāḥ nirlajjāḥ rodana priyāḥ aśuddhāḥ mala digdha aṅgāḥ pāna māṃsa ratāḥ bhṛśam duṣprasādāḥ mahā krodhāḥ svapna śīlāḥ nirantaram tāmasyaḥ naṣṭa tattva arthāḥ manda śīlāḥ mahā udarāḥ bhuñjanti vividham siddham bhojanam tīvra saṃbhramāḥ hitvā anyān eva gacchanti sarvathā bhṛśa pāpakāḥ nirlajjāḥ dharma saṃdigdhāḥ pratikūlāḥ samantataḥ evaṃyukta samācārāḥ striyaḥ rākṣasyam āśritāḥ evaṃvidhānām sarvāsām na paratra iha vā sukham etāsām eva ku strīṇām mṛtānām ca maheśvara asaṃśayam ciram kālam narake vāsaḥ iṣyate narakāt hi vimuktānām katham cit kāla paryayāt iṣyate janma mānuṣyam kaṣṭam tatra api bhuñjate tāsām duṣkṛta saṃyogāt duḥkham janma antareṣu api daridrāḥ kleśa bhūyiṣṭhāḥ virūpāḥ kutsitāḥ paraiḥ vidhavāḥ durbhagāḥ vā api labhante duḥkham īdṛśam śata varṣa sahasra antam ātmānam vyabhicāriṇī abhisaṃyānti tāḥ lokān puṇyān parama śobhanān avamatya tu yāḥ pūrvam patim duṣṭena cetasā vartamānāḥ ca satatam bhartṝṇām pratikūla tām bhartrā anumaraṇam kāle yāḥ kurvanti tathāvidhāḥ kāmāt krodhāt bhayāt mohāt apahāsyāḥ bhavanti tāḥ ādi prabhṛti ku strīṇām tathā anumaraṇam vṛthak ādi prabhṛti yā sādhvī bhartuḥ priya parāyaṇā ūrdhvam gacchati sā tatra bhartrā anumaraṇam gatā evam mṛtāyāḥ vai lokān aham paśyāmi cakṣuṣā spṛhaṇīyān sura gaṇaiḥ yān gacchanti pativratāḥ mṛtam ca patim uddiśya kuryāt ca evaṃvidham tapaḥ evam gacchati sā nārī patīnām lokam uttamam ramaṇīyam anirdeśyam duṣprāpam deva mānuṣaiḥ prāpnuyāt tādṛśam lokam kevalam yā pativratā nāradaḥ evam vadantīm rudrāṇīm lajjā bhāva samanvitām toṣayām āsa deveśaḥ vācā saṃpūjayan priyām ṛṣayaḥ deva gandharvāḥ sa asurāḥ sa apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ daivata pramadāḥ ca api deva nadyaḥ ca saṃgatāḥ praṇamya śirasā devīm stutibhiḥ ca api tuṣṭuvuḥ pūjayām āsuḥ apare devadevam mudā yutāḥ saṃprahṛṣṭa manāḥ śarvaḥ saṃvādam cintayan muhur śṛṇu kalyāṇe mad vākyam yat idam tu tvayā mayā puṇyam pavitram ākhyānam bhavitā tat na saṃśayaḥ yaḥ idam śrāvayet vidvān saṃvādam tu āvayoḥ priye śuciḥ bhūtvā narān yuktān sa yajña phalam āpnuyāt ye tu enam śṛṇuyuḥ nityam dharmyam tad gata mānasāḥ śravaṇāt eva teṣām tu mahat dharma phalam bhavet kathayet śṛṇuyāt vā api yaḥ kaḥ cit nityam āhnikam yaḥ imam paṭhate nityam saṃvādam ca āvayoḥ śubham nāradaḥ devīm devam vayam tatra na apaśyāma prabhāvataḥ evam purā mayā āścaryam dṛṣṭam haimavate vane caratā tīrtha yātrā artham purā keśiniṣūdana bhīṣmaḥ tat adya kathitam sarvam tava keśava śṛṇvataḥ vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ ṛṣayaḥ maheśvaraḥ māhātmyam vāsudevasya śrotum icchāma śaṃkara pitāmahāt api varaḥ śāśvataḥ puruṣaḥ hariḥ kṛṣṇaḥ jāmbūnada ābhāsaḥ vyabhre sūryaḥ iva uditaḥ daśa bāhuḥ mahā tejāḥ devatā ari niṣūdanaḥ śrīvatsa aṅkaḥ hṛṣīkeśaḥ sarva daivata pūjitaḥ śiroruhebhyaḥ jyotīṃṣi romabhyaḥ ca sura asurāḥ ṛṣayaḥ deha saṃbhūtāḥ tasya lokāḥ ca śāśvatāḥ pitāmaha gṛham sākṣāt sarva deva gṛham ca saḥ saḥ asyāḥ pṛthivyāḥ kṛtsnāyāḥ sraṣṭā tribhuvana īśvaraḥ saṃhartā ca eva bhūtānām sthāvarasya carasya ca sa deva ripu jit sākṣāt devanāthaḥ paraṃtapaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva saṃśliṣṭaḥ sarvagaḥ sarvatomukhaḥ paramātmā hṛṣīkeśaḥ sarvavyāpī maheśvaraḥ na tasmāt paramam bhūtam triṣu lokeṣu kim cana sura kārya artham utpannaḥ mānuṣam vapuḥ āsthitaḥ na hi deva gaṇāḥ śaktāḥ trivikrama vinākṛtāḥ bhuvane deva kāryāṇi kartum nāyaka varjitāḥ nāyakaḥ sarva devānām sarva bhūta namaskṛtaḥ sarvāḥ sukha sthitāḥ ca eva śarīre tasya devatāḥ sa devaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ śrī garbhaḥ śrī saha uṣitaḥ śārṅga cakra āyudhaḥ khaḍgī sarva nāga ripu dhvajaḥ parākrameṇa vīryeṇa vapuṣā darśanena ca āroheṇa pramāṇena dhairyeṇa ārjava saṃpadā ānṛśaṃsyena rūpeṇa balena ca samanvitaḥ yoga māyaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ niravadyaḥ mahāmanāḥ dhīraḥ mitra jana ślāghī jñāti bandhu jana priyaḥ kṣamāvān an ahaṃvādī brahmaṇyaḥ brahma nāyakaḥ bhaya hartā bhaya ārtānām mitrāṇām nandi vardhanaḥ śaraṇyaḥ sarva bhūtānām dīnānām pālane rataḥ śrutavān artha saṃpannaḥ sarva bhūta namaskṛtaḥ samāśritānām upakṛt śatrūṇām api dharma vid bhava artham iha devānām buddhyā paramayā yutaḥ prājāpatye śubhe mārge mānave dharma saṃhite aṅga nāmā manoḥ putraḥ tu antardhāmā tatas paraḥ tasya pracetaḥ pramukhāḥ bhaviṣyanti daśa ātmajāḥ dākṣāyiṇyāḥ tathā ādityaḥ manuḥ ādityāt tathā manoḥ ca vaṃśa jaḥ iḍā sudyumnaḥ ca bhaviṣyati budhāt purūravāḥ ca api tasmāt āyuḥ bhaviṣyati nahuṣaḥ bhavitā tasmāt yayātiḥ tasya ca ātmajaḥ yaduḥ tasmāt mahā sattvaḥ kroṣṭā tasmāt bhaviṣyati kroṣṭuḥ ca eva mahān putraḥ vṛjinīvān bhaviṣyati vṛjinīvataḥ hi bhavitā uṣadguḥ aparājitaḥ uṣadgoḥ bhavitā putraḥ śūraḥ citrarathaḥ tathā tasya tu avarajaḥ putraḥ śūraḥ nāma bhaviṣyati teṣām vikhyāta vīryāṇām cāritra guṇa śālinām yajvinām su viśuddhānām vaṃśe brāhmaṇa saṃmate sa śūraḥ kṣatriya śreṣṭhaḥ mahā vīryaḥ mahā yaśāḥ sva vaṃśa vistara karam janayiṣyati mānadaḥ dātā brāhmaṇa satkartā brahma bhūtaḥ dvija priyaḥ rājñaḥ sarvān ca ruddhān sa mokṣayiṣyati mānadaḥ jarāsaṃdham ca rājānam nirjitya giri gahvare śūraseneṣu saṃbhūtaḥ dvārakāyām vasan prabhuḥ pālayiṣyati gām devīm vijitya naya vat sadā tam bhavantaḥ samāsādya vāc mālyaiḥ arhaṇaiḥ varaiḥ arcayantu yathānyāyam brahmāṇam iva śāśvatam yaḥ hi mām draṣṭum iccheta brahmāṇam vā pitāmaham draṣṭavyaḥ tena bhagavant vāsudevaḥ pratāpavān dṛṣṭe tasmin aham dṛṣṭaḥ na me atra asti vicāraṇā sa yasya puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ prīti yuktaḥ bhaviṣyati yaḥ ca tam mānavaḥ loke saṃśrayiṣyati keśavam dharmāṇām deśikaḥ sākṣāt sa bhaviṣyati dharma bhāj sa hi devaḥ mahā tejāḥ prajā hita cikīrṣayā dharma artham puruṣa vyāghraḥ ṛṣi koṭīḥ sasarja ha tāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ tena vibhunā parvate gandhamādane sanatkumāra pramukhāḥ tiṣṭhanti tapasā anvitāḥ tasmāt sa vāgmī dharma jñaḥ namasyaḥ dvija puṃgavāḥ dṛṣṭaḥ paśyet ahar ahar saṃśritaḥ pratisaṃśrayet karmaṇā manasā vācā namasyaḥ sa dvijaiḥ sadā tam dṛṣṭvā sarvaśas devāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ syuḥ muni sattamāḥ mahāvarāham tam devam sarva loka pitāmaham tatra vaḥ tritayam dṛṣṭam bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ śiraḥ nāgaiḥ mahā bhogaiḥ parikīrṇam mahātmanaḥ cintitāni sameṣyanti śastrāṇi astrāṇi ca eva ha suparṇaḥ yasya vīryeṇa kaśyapasya ātmajaḥ balī antam na eva aśakat draṣṭum devasya paramātmanaḥ taḥ eṣa viṣṇuḥ saḥ anantaḥ bhagavant vasudhādharaḥ yaḥ rāmaḥ sa hṛṣīkeśaḥ yaḥ acyutaḥ sa dharādharaḥ draṣṭavyau mānanīyau ca cakra lāṅgala dhāriṇau eṣa yaḥ anugrahaḥ proktaḥ mayā puṇyaḥ tapodhanāḥ nāradaḥ yam bhavantaḥ dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ pūjayeyuḥ prayatnāt prāvṛṣi iva ca parjanyaḥ vavṛṣe nirmalam payaḥ nabhaḥ ca eva bhavat ghoram diśaḥ ca na cakāśire na śarvam bhūta saṃgham vā dadṛśuḥ munayaḥ tadā tīrtha yātrām tatas viprāḥ jagmuḥ ca anye yathāgatam śaṃkarasya umayā sārdham saṃvādam tad kathā āśrayam bhagavān puruṣa vyāghraḥ brahma bhūtaḥ sanātanaḥ yad artham anuśiṣṭāḥ smaḥ giri pṛṣṭhe mahātmanā dṛṣṭvā ati vismitāḥ kṛṣṇa sā ca naḥ smṛtiḥ āgatā iti uktaḥ sa tadā kṛṣṇaḥ tapaḥ vana nivāsibhiḥ mānayām āsa tān sarvān ṛṣīn devakī nandanaḥ atha ṛṣayaḥ saṃprahṛṣṭāḥ punar te kṛṣṇam abruvan tādṛśam ca mahat bāho yathā āha bhagavant bhava tvam eva hi artha tattva jñaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ asmān pṛcchase sadā vayam tu baṭu cāpalyāt aśaktāḥ guhya dhāraṇe sādhayāma vayam deva vṛddhim puṣṭim avāpnuhi putraḥ te sadṛśaḥ tāta viśiṣṭaḥ vā bhaviṣyati bhīṣmaḥ tatas praṇamya deveśam yādavam puruṣottamam saḥ ayam nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān dīptyā paramayā yutaḥ vratam yathāvat tat cīrtvā dvārakām punar āgamat pūrṇe ca daśame māsi putraḥ asya parama adbhutaḥ rukmiṇyām saṃmataḥ jajñe śūraḥ vaṃśa dharaḥ prabho sa kāmaḥ sarva jantūnām sarva bhāgavataḥ nṛpa surāṇām asurāṇām ca carati antargataḥ sadā saḥ ayam puruṣa śārdūlaḥ megha varṇaḥ catur bhujaḥ saṃśritaḥ pāṇḍavān premṇā bhavantaḥ ca enam āśritāḥ sa indrāḥ devāḥ trayastriṃśat sthitāḥ na atra vicāraṇā ādidevaḥ mahādevaḥ bhūtānām ca pratiśrayaḥ svayaṃjātaḥ mahā tejāḥ surāṇām artha siddhaye tava iyam pṛthivī kṛtsnā nārāyaṇa samāśrayāt ayam nāthaḥ tava acintyaḥ yasya nārāyaṇaḥ hṛdi sa bhavān bhūmipa adhvaryuḥ raṇa agnau hutavan nṛpān kṛṣṇaḥ sruveṇa mahatā yuga anta agni samena vai kṛtavān yaḥ abudhaḥ kopāt hari gāṇḍīva vigraham daiteyāḥ dānava indrāḥ ca mahā kāyāḥ mahā balāḥ cakra agnau kṣayam āpannāḥ dāva agnau śalabhāḥ iva pratiyoddhum na śakyaḥ hi mānuṣaiḥ eṣa saṃyuge nihīnaiḥ puruṣa vyāghra sattva śakti bala ādibhiḥ jayaḥ yaḥ ayam yuga anta ābhaḥ savyasācī raṇa agra gaḥ yat tu vai vṛṣabhāṅkena munibhyaḥ samudāhṛtam purāṇam himavat pṛṣṭhe tat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu yāvat asya udbhavaḥ tuṣṭiḥ tejaḥ vīryam parākramaḥ yatra kṛṣṇaḥ hi bhagavān tatra tuṣṭiḥ anuttamā vayam hi bāla matayaḥ para netrāḥ su viklavāḥ jñāna pūrvam prapannāḥ smaḥ mṛtyoḥ panthānam uttamam bhavān ca api ārjava paraḥ sarvam kṛtvā pratiśrayam rāja vṛttāt na calate pratijñā pālane rataḥ na hi pratijñayā dattam tam prahātum ariṃdama kālena ayam janaḥ sarvaḥ nihataḥ raṇa mūrdhani vayam ca kālena hatāḥ kālaḥ hi parameśvaraḥ na hi kālena kāla jña spṛṣṭaḥ śocitum arhati kālaḥ lohita rakta akṣaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ daṇḍī sanātanaḥ tasmāt kuntī suta jñātīn na iha śocitum arhasi mādhavasya ca māhātmyam śrutam yat kathitam mayā vyāsasya vacanam śrutvā nāradasya ca dhīmataḥ svayam ca eva mahā rāja kṛṣṇasya arhattamasya vai prabhāvaḥ ca ṛṣi pūgasya kathitaḥ su mahān mayā maheśvarasya saṃvādaḥ śailaputryāḥ ca bhārata dhārayiṣyati yaḥ ca imam mahā puruṣa saṃbhavam śṛṇuyāt kathayet vā yaḥ sa vai śreyaḥ labhet param bhavitāraḥ ca tasya atha sarve kāmāḥ yathā īpsitāḥ pretya māheśvaram lokam labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ na ayam śreyaḥ abhikāmena pratipattum janārdane eṣa vai ca akṣayaḥ vipraiḥ smṛtaḥ rājan janārdanaḥ maheśvara mukha utsṛṣṭāḥ ye ca dharma guṇāḥ smṛtāḥ te tvayā manasā dhāryāḥ kuru rāja divāniśam dharmeṇa hi sadā rājā prajāḥ rakṣitum arhati śaṃkarasya umayā sārdham saṃvādaḥ dharma saṃhitaḥ śrutvā vā śrotu kāmaḥ vā api arcayet vṛṣabhadhvajam saṃdeśaḥ deva pūjā artham tam tathā kuru pāṇḍava daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi badaryām eṣa sātvataḥ tapaḥ cacāra vipulam saha gāṇḍīvadhanvanā tri yugau puṇḍarīka akṣau vāsudeva dhanaṃjayau bālaḥ eva mahā bāhuḥ cakāra kadanam mahat kaṃsasya puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ jñāti trāṇa artha kāraṇāt śāśvatasya purāṇasya puruṣasya yudhiṣṭhira yasya te puruṣa vyāghraḥ sahāyaḥ ayam janārdanaḥ yad kṛte pṛthivī sarvā vinaṣṭā sa haya dvipā vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ duḥśāsana caturthānām kuravaḥ nidhanam gatāḥ evam prabhāṣamāṇe tu gāṅgeye puruṣa ṛṣabhe tūṣṇīm babhūva kauravyaḥ madhye teṣām mahātmanām tat śrutvā vismayam jagmuḥ dhṛtarāṣṭra ādayaḥ nṛpāḥ saṃpūjya manasā kṛṣṇam sarve prāñjalayaḥ abhavan ṛṣayaḥ ca api te sarve nārada pramukhāḥ tathā iti etat akhilam sarvam pāṇḍavaḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha śrutavān su mahat citram puṇyam bhīṣma anuśāsanam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tu gāṅgeyam viśrāntam bhūri dakṣiṇam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kaḥ upāyaḥ vara prāptau sarveṣām pāpa karmaṇām bhīṣmaḥ upāyaḥ ayam vara prāptau paramaḥ parikīrtitaḥ nārāyaṇasya tu dhyānam arcanam yajanam stutiḥ śravaṇam tad kathānām ca vidvas saṃrakṣaṇam tathā vidvas śuśrūṣaṇa prītiḥ upadeśa anupālanam saṃdhyā anena japena āśu mucyate prākṛtaḥ api ca dvija śuśrūṣayā jñānam vidvas saṃrakṣaṇena vā na asādhyam jñāninām kim cit tasmāt rakṣyāḥ dvijāḥ tvayā āsīt āśvāsitā vidvas saṃrakṣaṇa phalāt kila vaiśyā tvam abhilāṣā iyam vipra kanyā iti sāṃpratam iti uktā āśvāsitā apṛcchat kena evam pāpa saṃyutā yamaḥ jātāḥ vipra kule samyak śreyaḥ ca api bravīhi me cora śaṅkā vimokṣeṇa mokṣayitvā sujanmikā iti ukta aṣṭa akṣara dhyāna japa ādi śreyasā tu sā puṇya loka nivāsinī tat nityam viduṣām rakṣā tatparaḥ bhava bhūpate teṣām saṃrakṣaṇāt tuṣṭaḥ sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate uvāca śrutvā dharmān aśeṣeṇa pāvanāni ca sarvaśas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ śāṃtanavam punar eva abhyabhāṣata kim ekam daivatam loke kim vā api ekam parāyaṇam stuvantaḥ kam kam arcantaḥ prāpnuyuḥ mānavāḥ śubham kaḥ dharmaḥ sarva dharmāṇām bhavataḥ paramaḥ mataḥ uvāca an ādi nidhanam viṣṇum sarva loka maheśvaram brahmaṇyam sarva dharma jñam lokānām kīrti vardhanam eṣa me sarva dharmāṇām dharmaḥ adhikatamaḥ mataḥ yat bhaktyā puṇḍarīkākṣam stavaiḥ arcet naraḥ sadā pavitrāṇām pavitram yaḥ maṅgalānām ca maṅgalam daivatam devatānām ca bhūtānām yaḥ avyayaḥ pitā yatas sarvāṇi bhūtāni bhavanti ādi yuga āgame viṣṇoḥ nāma sahasram mama śṛṇu pāpa bhaya apaham yāni nāmāni gauṇāni vikhyātāni mahātmanaḥ ṛṣibhiḥ parigītāni tāni vakṣyāmi bhūtaye viṣṇoḥ nāma sahasrasya vedavyāsaḥ mahān ṛṣiḥ chandaḥ anuṣṭubh tathā devaḥ bhagavant viśva rūpadhṛk ṛṣiḥ nāmnām sahasrasya vedavyāsaḥ mahā muniḥ chandaḥ anuṣṭubh tathā devaḥ bhagavant devakī sutaḥ amṛtāṃśu udbhavaḥ bījam śaktiḥ devakīnandanaḥ tri sāmā hṛdayam tasya śānti arthe viniyujyate viṣṇum jiṣṇum mahāviṣṇum prabhaviṣṇum maheśvaram viśvam viṣṇuḥ vaṣaṭkāraḥ bhūta bhavya bhavat prabhuḥ bhūta kṛt bhūta bhṛt bhāvaḥ bhūtātmā bhūtabhāvanaḥ pūta ātmā paramātmā ca muktānām paramā gatiḥ avyayaḥ puruṣaḥ sākṣī kṣetrajñaḥ akṣaraḥ eva ca yogaḥ yoga vidām netā pradhāna puruṣa īśvaraḥ nārasiṃha vapūḥ śrīmān keśavaḥ puruṣottamaḥ sarvaḥ śarvaḥ śivaḥ sthāṇuḥ bhūtādiḥ nidhiḥ avyayaḥ saṃbhavaḥ bhāvanaḥ bhartā prabhavaḥ prabhuḥ īśvaraḥ svayambhuḥ śaṃbhuḥ ādityaḥ puṣkarākṣaḥ mahā svanaḥ an ādi nidhanaḥ dhātā vidhātā dhātuḥ uttamaḥ aprameyaḥ hṛṣīkeśaḥ padmanābhaḥ amaraprabhuḥ viśvakarmā manuḥ tvaṣṭā sthaviṣṭhaḥ sthaviraḥ dhruvaḥ agrāhyaḥ śāśvataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ lohita akṣaḥ pratardanaḥ īśānaḥ prāṇadaḥ prāṇaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ prajāpatiḥ īśvaraḥ vikramī dhanvī medhāvī vikramaḥ kramaḥ anuttamaḥ durādharṣaḥ kṛtajñaḥ kṛtiḥ ātmavān sureśaḥ śaraṇam śarma viśvaretāḥ prajā bhavaḥ ahar saṃvatsaraḥ vyālaḥ pratyayaḥ sarva darśanaḥ ajaḥ sarveśvaraḥ siddhaḥ siddhiḥ sarvādiḥ acyutaḥ vṛṣākapiḥ ameya ātmā sarva yoga viniḥsṛtaḥ vasuḥ vasu manāḥ satyaḥ sama ātmā saṃmitaḥ samaḥ amoghaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ vṛṣakarmā vṛṣa ākṛtiḥ rudraḥ bahu śirāḥ babhruḥ viśvayoniḥ śuciśravāḥ amṛtaḥ śāśvataḥ sthāṇuḥ varārohaḥ mahātapāḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ pitāmaha mahā prājña sarva śāstra viśārada prasthāne vā praveśe vā pravṛtte vā api karmaṇi daive vā śrāddha kāle vā kim japyam karma sādhanam śāntikam pauṣṭikam rakṣā śatru ghnam bhaya nāśanam bhīṣmaḥ vyāsa proktam imam mantram śṛṇuṣva ekamanāḥ nṛpa śṛṇu mantra vidhim kṛtsnam procyamānam mayā anagha yam śrutvā pāṇḍava śreṣṭha sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate tat te aham saṃpravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣva ekamanāḥ nṛpa āyuṣmān bhavate ca eva yam śrutvā pārthiva ātmaja sevitam satatam rājan purā rājarṣi sattamaiḥ nṛpaiḥ bharata śārdūla prāpyate śrīḥ anuttamā namaḥ vasiṣṭhāya mahāvratāya parāśaram veda nidhim praṇamya namaḥ astu ṛṣibhyaḥ paramam pareṣām deveṣu devam vara dam varāṇām sahasra śīrṣāya namaḥ śivāya sahasra nāmāya janārdanāya ajaikapād ahirbudhnyaḥ pinākī ca aparājitaḥ ṛtaḥ ca pitṛrūpaḥ ca tryambakaḥ ca maheśvaraḥ vṛṣākapiḥ ca śaṃbhuḥ ca havanaḥ atha īśvaraḥ tathā ekādaśā ete prathitāḥ rudrāḥ tribhuvana īśvarāḥ śatam etat samākhyātam śatarudre mahātmanām aṃśaḥ bhagaḥ ca mitraḥ ca varuṇaḥ ca jaleśvaraḥ tvaṣṭā pūṣā tathā eva indraḥ dvādaśaḥ viṣṇuḥ ucyate iti ete dvādaśa ādityāḥ kāśyapeyāḥ iti śrutiḥ pratyūṣaḥ ca prabhāsaḥ ca vasavaḥ aṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ nāsatyaḥ ca api dasraḥ ca smṛtau dvau aśvinau api mārtaṇḍasya ātmajau etau saṃjñā nāsā vinirgatau atas param pravakṣyāmi lokānām karma sākṣiṇaḥ adṛśyāḥ sarva bhūteṣu paśyanti tridaśeśvarāḥ śubha aśubhāni karmāṇi mṛtyuḥ kālaḥ ca sarvaśas viśvedevāḥ pitṛ gaṇāḥ mūrtimantaḥ tapodhanāḥ munayaḥ ca eva siddhāḥ ca tapaḥ mokṣa parāyaṇāḥ śuci smitāḥ kīrtayatām prayacchanti śubham nṛṇām prajāpati kṛtān etān lokān divyena tejasā prāṇānām īśvarān etān kīrtayan prayataḥ naraḥ lokān ca labhate puṇyān viśveśvara kṛtān śubhān ete devāḥ trayastriṃśat sarva bhūta gaṇa īśvarāḥ nandīśvaraḥ mahākāyaḥ grāmaṇīḥ vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ īśvarāḥ sarva lokānām gaṇeśvara vināyakāḥ saumyāḥ raudra gaṇāḥ ca eva yoga bhūta gaṇāḥ tathā jyotīṃṣi saritaḥ vyoma suparṇaḥ pataga īśvaraḥ pṛthivyām tapasā siddhāḥ sthāvarāḥ ca carāḥ ca ha himavant girayaḥ ca eva catvāraḥ ca mahā arṇavāḥ bhavasya anucarāḥ sarve hara tulya parākramāḥ viṣṇuḥ devaḥ atha jiṣṇuḥ ca skandaḥ ca ambikayā saha atas ūrdhvam pravakṣyāmi mānavān ṛṣi sattamān yavakrītaḥ ca raibhyaḥ ca arvāvasu parāvasū auśijaḥ ca eva kakṣīvān balaḥ ca āṅgirasaḥ sutaḥ ṛṣiḥ medhātitheḥ putraḥ kaṇvaḥ barhiṣadaḥ tathā brahma tejaḥ mayāḥ sarve kīrtitāḥ loka bhāvanāḥ mahendra guravaḥ sapta prāñcam vai diśam āśritāḥ prayataḥ kīrtayan etān śakra loke mahīyate dṛḍhavyaḥ ca ūrdhvabāhuḥ ca tṛṇasoma aṅgirāḥ tathā mitrāvaruṇayoḥ putraḥ tathā agastyaḥ pratāpavān dharmarāja ṛtvijaḥ sapta dakṣiṇām diśam āśritāḥ dṛḍheyuḥ ca ṛteyuḥ ca parivyādhaḥ ca kīrtimān ekataḥ ca dvitaḥ ca eva tritaḥ ca āditya saṃnibhāḥ atreḥ putraḥ ca dharma ātmā ṛṣiḥ sārasvataḥ tathā varuṇasya ṛtvijaḥ sapta paścimām diśam āśritāḥ atriḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ bhagavān kaśyapaḥ ca mahān ṛṣiḥ ṛcīka tanayaḥ ca ugraḥ jamadagniḥ pratāpavān dhaneśvarasya guravaḥ sapta ete uttarām śritāḥ apare munayaḥ sapta dikṣu sarvāsu dhiṣṭhitāḥ kīrti svasti karāḥ nṝṇām kīrtitāḥ loka bhāvanāḥ dharmaḥ kāmaḥ ca kālaḥ ca vasuḥ vāsukiḥ eva ca rāmaḥ vyāsaḥ tathā drauṇiḥ aśvatthāmā ca lomaśaḥ śānti svasti karāḥ loke diśām pālāḥ prakīrtitāḥ yasyām yasyām diśi hi ete tad mukhaḥ śaraṇam vrajet sraṣṭāraḥ sarva bhūtānām kīrtitāḥ loka pāvanāḥ saṃvartaḥ merusāvarṇaḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ ca dhārmikaḥ sāṃkhya yogau nāradaḥ ca durvāsāḥ ca mahān ṛṣiḥ atyanta tapasaḥ dāntāḥ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutāḥ apare rudra saṃkāśāḥ kīrtitāḥ brahma laukikāḥ pṛthum vainyam nṛpa varam pṛthvī yasya abhavat sutā gavāmayena yajñena yena iṣṭam vai kṛte yuge viśvajit tapasā upetam lakṣaṇyam kāma lakṣaṇam tathā śvetam ca rājarṣim kīrtayet parama dyutim mahādeva prasādena yena gaṅgā avatāritā sagarasya ātmajāḥ yena plāvitāḥ tāritāḥ tathā hutāśana samān etān mahā rūpān mahā ojasaḥ devān ṛṣi gaṇān ca eva nṛpān ca jagatī īśvarān sāṃkhyam yogam ca paramam havyam kavyam tathā eva ca maṅgalyam sarva bhūtānām pavitram bahu kīrtitam vyādhi praśamanam śreṣṭham pauṣṭikam sarva karmaṇām prayataḥ kīrtayet ca etān kalyam sāyam ca bhārata ete vināyakāḥ śreṣṭhāḥ dakṣāḥ kṣāntāḥ jita indriyāḥ narāṇām aśubham sarve vyapohanti prakīrtitāḥ sākṣi bhūtāḥ mahātmānaḥ pāpasya sukṛtasya ca etān kīrtayatām nityam duḥsvapnaḥ naśyate nṛṇām mucyate sarva pāpebhyaḥ svastimān ca gṛhān vrajet dīkṣā kāleṣu sarveṣu yaḥ paṭhet niyataḥ dvijaḥ nyāyavān ātma nirataḥ kṣāntaḥ dāntaḥ anasūyakaḥ gacchataḥ kṣemam adhvānam grāma antara gataḥ paṭhan ātmanaḥ ca sutānām ca dārāṇām ca dhanasya ca bījānām oṣadhīnām ca rakṣām etām prayojayet etān saṃgrāma kāle tu paṭhataḥ kṣatriyasya tu kaśmalam laghu tām yāti pāpmanā ca pramucyate yānapātre ca yāne ca pravāse rāja veśmani parām siddhim avāpnoti sāvitrīm hi uttamām paṭhan na ca rāja bhayam teṣām na piśācāt na rākṣasāt caturṇām api varṇānām āśramasya viśeṣataḥ karoti satatam śāntim sāvitrīm uttamām paṭhan na agniḥ dahati kāṣṭhāni sāvitrī yatra paṭhyate na teṣām vidyate duḥkham gacchanti paramām gatim ye śṛṇvanti mahat brahma sāvitrī guṇa kīrtanam gavām madhye tu paṭhataḥ gāvaḥ asya bahu vatsalāḥ prasthāne vā praveśe vā sarva avasthā gataḥ paṭhet japatām juhvatām ca eva nityam ca prayata ātmanām ṛṣīṇām paramam japyam guhyam etat narādhipa yāthātathyena saṃgamya itihāsam purātanam parāśara matam divyam śakrāya kathitam purā hṛdayam sarva bhūtānām śrutiḥ eṣā purātanī soma āditya anvayāḥ sarve rāghavāḥ kuravaḥ tathā paṭhanti śucayaḥ nityam sāvitrīm prāṇinām gatim abhyāśe nityam devānām saptarṣīṇām dhruvasya ca mokṣaṇam sarva kṛcchrāṇām mocayati aśubhāt sadā vṛddhaiḥ kāśyapa gautama prabhṛtibhiḥ bhṛgu aṅgiraḥ tri ādibhiḥ bhāradvāja matam ṛcīka tanayaiḥ prāptam vasiṣṭhāt punar sāvitrīm adhigamya śakra
