śatānandaḥ nandiḥ jyotiḥ gaṇeśvaraḥ vijita ātmā vidheya ātmā sat kīrtiḥ chinna saṃśayaḥ udīrṇaḥ sarvatas cakṣuḥ anīśaḥ śāśvataḥ sthiraḥ bhūśayaḥ bhūṣaṇaḥ bhūtiḥ viśokaḥ śokanāśanaḥ arciṣmān arcitaḥ kumbhaḥ viśuddha ātmā viśodhanaḥ vīraḥ śūraḥ śauriḥ janeśvaraḥ triloka ātmā triloka īśaḥ keśavaḥ keśi hā hariḥ kāmadevaḥ kāmapālaḥ kāmī kāntaḥ kṛta āgamaḥ mahā kramaḥ mahā karmā mahā tejāḥ mahoragaḥ mahā kratuḥ mahā yajvā mahā yajñaḥ mahā haviḥ pūrṇaḥ pūrayitā puṇyaḥ puṇya kīrtiḥ anāmayaḥ sat gatiḥ satkṛtiḥ sattā sat bhūtiḥ sat parāyaṇaḥ śūrasenaḥ yadu śreṣṭhaḥ sannivāsaḥ suyāmunaḥ bhūta āvāsaḥ sarva āsu nilayaḥ analaḥ viśvamūrtiḥ mahā mūrtiḥ dīpta mūrtiḥ a mūrtimān aneka mūrtiḥ avyaktaḥ śata mūrtiḥ śata ānanaḥ suvarṇavarṇaḥ hemāṅgaḥ varāṅgaḥ candanāṅgadī vīra hā viṣamaḥ śūnyaḥ ghṛta āśīḥ acalaḥ calaḥ amānī mānadaḥ mānyaḥ lokasvāmī tejaḥ vṛṣa dyuti dharaḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām vara catur mūrtiḥ catur bāhuḥ catur vyūhaḥ catur gatiḥ śubhāṅgaḥ lokasāraṅgaḥ sutantuḥ tantuvardhanaḥ indrakarmā mahākarmā kṛtakarmā kṛta āgamaḥ arkaḥ vājasanaḥ śṛṅgī jayantaḥ sarva vid jayī suvarṇa binduḥ akṣobhyaḥ sarva vāc īśvara īśvaraḥ mahā hradaḥ mahā gartaḥ mahā bhūtaḥ mahā nidhiḥ amṛta aṃśaḥ amṛta vapūḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvatomukhaḥ nyagrodha udumbaraḥ aśvatthaḥ cāṇūra andhra niṣūdanaḥ sahasra arcis saptajihvaḥ saptaidhāḥ sapta vāhanaḥ aṇuḥ bṛhat kṛśaḥ sthūlaḥ guṇa bhṛt nirguṇaḥ mahān a dhṛ sva dhṛ sva āsyaḥ prāgvaṃśaḥ vaṃśa vardhanaḥ bhārabhṛt kathitaḥ yogī yogīśaḥ sarva kāma daḥ āśramaḥ śramaṇaḥ kṣāmaḥ suparṇaḥ vāyuvāhanaḥ sattvavān sāttvikaḥ satyaḥ satya dharma parāyaṇaḥ abhiprāyaḥ priya arhaḥ arhaḥ priya kṛt prīti vardhanaḥ anirviṇṇaḥ sadā amarṣī loka adhiṣṭhānam adbhutam a raudraḥ kuṇḍalī cakrī vikramī ūrjita śāsanaḥ śabdātigaḥ śabdasahaḥ śiśiraḥ śarvarīkaraḥ akrūraḥ peśalaḥ dakṣaḥ dakṣiṇaḥ kṣamiṇām vara vidvattamaḥ vītabhayaḥ puṇya śravaṇa kīrtanaḥ uttāraṇaḥ duṣkṛti hā puṇyaḥ duḥsvapna nāśanaḥ vīra hā rakṣaṇaḥ santaḥ jīvanaḥ paryavasthitaḥ catur asraḥ gabhīra ātmā vidiśaḥ vyādiśaḥ diśaḥ anādiḥ bhūḥ bhuvaḥ lakṣmī suvīraḥ rucira aṅgadaḥ ādhāra nilayaḥ dhātā puṣpahāsaḥ prajāgaraḥ ūrdhva gaḥ sat patha ācāraḥ prāṇadaḥ praṇavaḥ paṇaḥ pramāṇa prāṇa nilayaḥ prāṇa kṛt prāṇa jīvana bhūḥ bhuvaḥ svar taruḥ tāraḥ savitā prapitāmahaḥ yajñaḥ yajñapatiḥ yajvā yajña aṅgaḥ yajña vāhanaḥ yajñabhṛt yajñakṛt yajñī yajñabhuj yajñasādhanaḥ ātmayoniḥ svayaṃjātaḥ vaikhānas sāma gāyana devakīnandanaḥ sraṣṭā kṣitīśaḥ pāpanāśanaḥ śaṅkhabhṛt nandakī cakrī śārṅgadhanvā gadā dharaḥ rathāṅga pāṇiḥ akṣobhyaḥ sarva praharaṇa āyudhaḥ iti idam kīrtanīyasya keśavasya mahātmanaḥ nāmnām sahasram divyānām aśeṣeṇa prakīrtitam yaḥ idam śṛṇuyāt nityam yaḥ ca api parikīrtayet na aśubham prāpnuyāt kim cit saḥ amutra iha ca mānavaḥ veda antagaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ syāt kṣatriyaḥ vijayī bhavet vaiśyaḥ dhana samṛddhaḥ syāt śūdraḥ sukham avāpnuyāt dharma arthī prāpnuyāt dharmam artha arthī ca artham āpnuyāt kāmān avāpnuyāt kāmī prajā arthī ca āpnuyāt prajāḥ yaśaḥ prāpnoti vipulam jñāti prādhānyam eva ca acalām śriyam āpnoti śreyaḥ ca āpnoti anuttamam bhayāt mucyeta bhītaḥ ca mucyeta āpannaḥ āpadaḥ durgāṇi atitarati āśu puruṣaḥ puruṣottamam vāsudeva āśrayaḥ martyaḥ vāsudeva parāyaṇaḥ sarva pāpa viśudh ātman yā brahman sanātana janma mṛtyu jarā vyādhi bhayam vā api upajāyate imam stavam adhīyānaḥ śraddhā bhakti samanvitaḥ yujyeta ātma sukha kṣānti śrī dhṛti smṛti kīrtibhiḥ bhavanti kṛta puṇyānām bhaktānām puruṣottame dyauḥ sa candra arka nakṣatrā kham diśaḥ bhūḥ mahodadhiḥ vāsudevasya vīryeṇa vidhṛtāni mahātmanaḥ jagat vaśe vartata idam kṛṣṇasya sacarācaram indriya manas buddhi sattva tejas bala dhṛti vāsudeva ātmakāni āhuḥ kṣetram kṣetrajñaḥ eva ca sarva āgamānām ācāraḥ prathamam parikalpyate ṛṣayaḥ pitaraḥ devāḥ mahābhūtāni dhātavaḥ jaṅgama ajaṅgamam ca idam jagant nārāyaṇa udbhavam yogaḥ jñānam tathā sāṃkhyam vidyāḥ śilpa karman ca vedāḥ śāstrāṇi vijñānam etat sarvam janārdanāt ekaḥ viṣṇuḥ mahat bhūtam pṛthak bhūtāni anekaśas trīn lokān vyāpya bhūtātmā bhuṅkte viśva bhuj avyayaḥ paṭhet yaḥ icchet puruṣaḥ śreyaḥ prāptum sukhāni ca yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api śreyaḥ prāpnoti anuttamam śrī bhagavant uvāca bhaktānām anuraktānām trātā bhava janārdana yaḥ mām nāma sahasreṇa stotum icchati pāṇḍava sahasra pāda akṣi śira ūru bāhave sahasra nāmne puruṣāya śāśvate sahasra koṭi yuga dhāriṇe namaḥ yena tvayā bhārata taila pūrṇaḥ prajvālitaḥ jñāna mayaḥ pradīpaḥ eṣa niṣkaṇṭakaḥ pathī yatra saṃpūjyate hariḥ kupatham tam vijānīyāt govinda rahita āgamam śrī sahasranāma tad tulyam rāma nāma varānane iti stutvā hṛṣīkeśam pārthaḥ tūṣṇīm sthitaḥ tatas jagat hitāya kṛṣṇāya govindāya namaḥ namaḥ ākāśāt patitam toyam yathā gacchati sāgaram jitam te puṇḍarīkākṣa namaḥ te viśvabhāvana namaḥ te astu hṛṣīkeśa mahāpuruṣa pūrvaja uvāca ke pūjyāḥ ke namaskāryāḥ katham varteta keṣu ca kimācāraḥ kīdṛśeṣu pitāmaha na riṣyate uvāca brāhmaṇānām paribhavaḥ sādayet api devatāḥ brāhmaṇānām namaskartā yudhiṣṭhira na riṣyate te hi lokān imān sarvān dhārayanti manīṣiṇaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ sarva lokānām mahāntaḥ dharma setavaḥ dhana tyāga abhirāmāḥ ca vāc saṃyama ratāḥ ca ye ramaṇīyāḥ ca bhūtānām nidhānam ca dhṛta vratāḥ praṇetāraḥ ca lokānām śāstrāṇām ca yaśasvinaḥ tapaḥ yeṣām dhanam nityam vāc ca eva vipulam balam mahātmanām jñāna vidām tapaḥ eva dhanam param prabhavaḥ ca api dharmāṇām dharma jñāḥ sūkṣma darśiṇaḥ yān upāśritya jīvanti prajāḥ sarvāḥ caturvidhāḥ panthānaḥ sarva netāraḥ yajña vāhāḥ sanātanāḥ pitṛpaitāmahīm gurum udvahanti dhuram sadā dīpāḥ sarvasya lokasya cakṣuḥ cakṣuṣmatām api sarva śilpa ādi nidhayaḥ nipuṇāḥ sūkṣma darśiṇaḥ gati jñāḥ sarva bhūtānām adhyātma gati cintakāḥ ādi madhya avasānānām jñātāraḥ chinna saṃśayāḥ parāvara viśeṣa jñāḥ gantāraḥ paramām gatim vimuktāḥ dhuta pāpmānaḥ nirdvaṃdvāḥ niṣparigrahāḥ māna arhāḥ mānitāḥ nityam jñāna vidbhiḥ mahātmabhiḥ samam yeṣām dukūlam ca śāṇa kṣauma ajināni ca tiṣṭheyuḥ api a bhuñjānāḥ bahūni divasāni api śoṣayeyuḥ ca gātrāṇi svādhyāyaiḥ saṃyata indriyāḥ lokān anyān sṛjeyuḥ ca lokapālān ca kopitāḥ apeyaḥ sāgaraḥ yeṣām abhiśāpāt mahātmanām yeṣām kopa agniḥ adya api daṇḍake na upaśāmyati devānām api ye devāḥ kāraṇam kāraṇasya ca pramāṇasya pramāṇam ca kaḥ tān abhibhavet budhaḥ yeṣām vṛddhaḥ ca bālaḥ ca sarvaḥ saṃmānam arhati teṣām vṛddhāḥ ca bālāḥ ca sarve sat mārga darśinaḥ a vidvān brāhmaṇaḥ devaḥ pātram vai pāvanam mahat vidvān bhūyastaraḥ devaḥ pūrṇa sāgara saṃnibhaḥ a vidvān ca eva vidvān ca brāhmaṇaḥ daivatam mahat praṇītaḥ ca apraṇītaḥ ca yathā agniḥ daivatam mahat śmaśāne hi api tejasvī pāvakaḥ na eva duṣyati uvāca kām tu brāhmaṇa pūjāyām vyuṣṭim dṛṣṭvā janādhipa kam vā karma udayam matvā tān arcasi mahāmate uvāca atra api udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam asya lokasya sarvasya māhiṣmatyām mahā balaḥ sa tu ratna ākaravatīm sa dvīpām sāgarāmbarām śaśāsa sarvām pṛthivīm haihayaḥ satya vikramaḥ sva vittam tena dattam tu dattātreyāya kāraṇe ārādhayām āsa ca tam kṛtavīrya ātmajaḥ munim nyamantrayata saṃhṛṣṭaḥ sa dvijaḥ ca varaiḥ tribhiḥ sahasra bāhuḥ bhūyām vai camū madhye gṛhe anyathā mama bāhu sahasram tu paśyantām sainikāḥ raṇe vikrameṇa mahīm kṛtsnām jayeyam vipula vrata tām ca dharmeṇa saṃprāpya pālayeyam atandritaḥ anuśāsantu mām santaḥ mithyā vṛttam tad āśrayam abravīt vīrya saṃmohāt kaḥ nu asti sadṛśaḥ mayā vīrya dhairya yaśaḥ śaucaiḥ vikrameṇa ojasā api vā tad vākya ante ca antarikṣe vāc uvāca aśarīriṇī na tvam mūḍha vijānīṣe brāhmaṇam kṣatriyāt varam sahitaḥ brāhmaṇena iha kṣatriyaḥ rakṣati prajāḥ kuryām bhūtāni tuṣṭaḥ aham kruddhaḥ nāśam tathā naye karmaṇā manasā vācā na mattaḥ asti varaḥ dvijaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ saṃśritāḥ kṣatram na kṣatram brāhmaṇa āśritam śritān brahma upadhāḥ viprāḥ khādanti kṣatriyān bhuvi kṣatriyeṣu āśritaḥ dharmaḥ prajānām paripālanam kṣatrāt vṛttiḥ brāhmaṇānām taiḥ katham brāhmaṇaḥ varaḥ sarva bhūta pradhānān tān bhaikṣa vṛttīn aham sadā ātma saṃbhāvitān viprān sthāpayāmi ātmanaḥ vaśe vijeṣyāmi avaśān sarvān brāhmaṇān carma vāsasaḥ na ca mām cyāvayet rāṣṭrāt triṣu lokeṣu kaḥ cana devaḥ vā mānuṣaḥ vā api tasmāt jyeṣṭhaḥ dvijāt aham arjunasya vacaḥ śrutvā vitrastā abhūt niśācarī tyaja enam kaluṣam bhāvam brāhmaṇebhyaḥ namaskuru eteṣām kurvataḥ pāpam rāṣṭra kṣobhaḥ hi te bhavet atha vā tvām mahīpāla śamayiṣyanti vai dvijāḥ nirasiṣyanti vā rāṣṭrāt hata utsāham mahā balāḥ tam rājā kaḥ tvam iti āha tatas tam prāha mārutaḥ yādṛśam pṛthivī bhūtam tādṛśam brūhi vai dvijam vāyoḥ vā sadṛśam kim cit brūhi tvam brāhmaṇa uttamam apām vai sadṛśam brūhi sūryasya nabhasaḥ api vā uvāca śṛṇu mūḍha guṇān kān cit brāhmaṇānām mahātmanām ye tvayā kīrtitāḥ rājan tebhyaḥ atha brāhmaṇaḥ varaḥ tyaktvā mahī tvam bhūmiḥ tu spardhayā aṅga nṛpasya ha nāśam jagāma tām vipraḥ vyaṣṭambhayata kaśyapaḥ akṣayāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ rājan divi ca iha ca nityadā apibat tejasā hi apaḥ svayam eva aṅgirāḥ purā sa tāḥ piban kṣīram iva na atṛpyata mahā tapāḥ apūrayat mahā oghena mahīm sarvām ca pārthiva ahalyām kāmayānaḥ vai dharma artham ca na hiṃsitaḥ tathā samudraḥ nṛpate pūrṇaḥ mṛṣṭena vāriṇā brāhmaṇaiḥ abhiśaptaḥ san lavaṇodaḥ kṛtaḥ vibho suvarṇa varṇaḥ nirdhūmaḥ saṃhata ūrdhva śikhaḥ kaviḥ suvarṇa dhāriṇā nityam avaśaptāḥ dvijātinā samaḥ na tvam dvijātibhyaḥ śreṣṭham viddhi narādhipa daṇḍakānām mahat rājyam brāhmaṇena vināśitam tālajaṅgham mahat kṣatram aurveṇa ekena nāśitam tvayā ca vipulam rājyam balam dharmaḥ śrutam tathā atha vā brāhmaṇa śreṣṭham anu bhūta anupālakam yena idam nikhilam viśvam janitam sthāvaram caram aṇḍa jātam tu brahmāṇam ke cid icchanti apaṇḍitāḥ aṇḍāt bhinnāt babhuḥ śailāḥ diśaḥ ambhaḥ pṛthivī divam draṣṭavyam na etat evam hi katham jyāyastamaḥ hi saḥ smṛtam ākāśam aṇḍam tu tasmāt jātaḥ pitāmahaḥ na asti aṇḍam asti tu brahmā sa rājan loka bhāvanaḥ iti uktaḥ sa tadā tūṣṇīm abhūt vāyuḥ tam abravīt uvāca imām bhūmim brāhmaṇebhyaḥ ditsuḥ vai dakṣiṇām purā aṅgaḥ nāma nṛpaḥ rājñ tatas cintām mahī yayau dhāraṇīm sarva bhūtānām ayam prāpya varaḥ nṛpaḥ katham icchati mām dātum dvijebhyaḥ brahmaṇaḥ sutām sā aham tyaktvā gamiṣyāmi bhūmi tvam brahmaṇaḥ padam ayam sa rāṣṭraḥ nṛpatiḥ mā bhūt iti tatas agamat tatas tām kaśyapaḥ dṛṣṭvā vrajantīm pṛthivīm tadā praviveśa mahīm sadyas muktvā ātmānam samāhitaḥ ruddhā sā sarvatas jajñe tṛṇa oṣadhi samanvitā dharma uttarā naṣṭa bhayā bhūmiḥ āsīt tatas nṛpa evam varṣa sahasrāṇi divyāni vipula vrataḥ triṃśat kaśyapaḥ rājan bhūmiḥ āsīt atandritaḥ pṛthivī kāśyapī jajñe sutā tasya mahātmanaḥ eṣa rājan īdṛśaḥ vai brāhmaṇaḥ kaśyapaḥ abhavat anyam prabrūhi vā api tvam kaśyapāt kṣatriyam varam tūṣṇīm babhūva nṛpatiḥ pavanaḥ tu abravīt punar śṛṇu rājan utathyasya jātasya āṅgirase kule bhadrā somasya duhitā rūpeṇa paramā matā sā ca tīvram tapaḥ tepe mahābhāgā yaśasvinī utathyam tu mahābhāgam tad kṛte avarayat tadā utathya arthe tu cāru aṅgā param niyamam āsthitā tatas āhūya sā utathyam dadau atra yaśasvinīm tām tu akāmayata śrīmān varuṇaḥ pūrvam eva ha sa ca āgamya vanaprastham yamunāyām jahāra tām parama adbhuta saṃkāśam ṣaṣ sahasra śatahradam prāsādaiḥ apsarobhiḥ ca divyaiḥ kāmaiḥ ca śobhitam tatra devaḥ tayā sārdham reme rājñ jaleśvaraḥ provāca gaccha brūhi tvam varuṇam paruṣam vacaḥ mad vākyāt muñca mama bhāryām kasmāt vā hṛtavān asi somena dattā bhāryā mama tvayā ca apahṛtā adya vai mama eṣā su priyā bhāryā na enām utsraṣṭum utsahe iti uktaḥ varuṇena atha nāradaḥ prāpya tam munim utathyam abravīt vākyam na ati hṛṣṭa manāḥ iva gale gṛhītvā kṣiptaḥ asmi varuṇena mahā mune nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā kruddhaḥ prājvalat aṅgirāḥ apibat tejasā vāri viṣṭabhya su mahā tapāḥ suhṛdbhiḥ kṣipyamāṇaḥ api na eva amuñcata tām tadā tatas tat iriṇam jātam samudraḥ ca apasarpitaḥ tasmāt deśāt nadīm ca eva provāca asau dvijottamaḥ tasmin saṃcūrṇite deśe bhadrām ādāya vāripaḥ adadāt śaraṇam gatvā bhāryām āṅgirasāya vai pratigṛhya tu tām bhāryām utathyaḥ su manāḥ bhavat tatas sa labdhvā tām bhāryām varuṇam prāha dharma vid aspṛśyaḥ apāna yogyaḥ ca kṣipram eva bhaviṣyati utathyaḥ su mahā tejāḥ yat tat śṛṇu narādhipa muktaḥ tvam āyuḥ śeṣeṇa mā bhaiḥ gaccha jaleśvara mā avamaṃsthāḥ punar mohāt mā tvām ninyuḥ yama kṣayam mayā eṣā tapasā prāptā krośataḥ te jalādhipa eṣa rājan īdṛśaḥ vai utathyaḥ brāhmaṇa ṛṣabhaḥ bravīmi aham brūhi vā tvam utathyāt kṣatriyam varam uvāca iti uktaḥ sa tadā tūṣṇīm abhūt vāyuḥ tatas abravīt śṛṇu rājan agastyasya māhātmyam brāhmaṇasya ha asuraiḥ nirjitāḥ devāḥ nirutsāhāḥ ca te kṛtāḥ yajñāḥ ca eṣām hṛtāḥ sarve pitṛbhyaḥ ca svadhā tathā karma ijyāḥ mānavānām ca dānavaiḥ haihaya ṛṣabha bhraṣṭa aiśvaryāḥ tatas devāḥ ceruḥ pṛthvīm iti śrutiḥ abhivādya ca tam devāḥ dṛṣṭvā ca yaśasā vṛtam idam ūcuḥ mahātmānam vākyam kāle janādhipa dānavaiḥ yudhi bhagnāḥ sma tathā aiśvaryāt ca bhraṃśitāḥ tat asmān naḥ bhayāt tīvrāt trāhi tvam muni puṃgava prajajvāla ca tejasvī kālāgniḥ iva saṃkṣaye tena dīpta aṃśu jālena nirdagdhāḥ dānavāḥ tadā antarikṣāt mahā rāja nyapatanta sahasraśas ubhau lokau parityajya yayuḥ kāṣṭhām sma dakṣiṇām baliḥ tu yajate yajñam aśvamedham mahīm gataḥ ye anye svasthāḥ mahī sthāḥ ca te na dagdhāḥ mahā asurāḥ tatas lokāḥ punar prāptāḥ suraiḥ śāntam ca tat rajaḥ atha enam abruvan devāḥ bhūmiṣṭhān asurān jahi dagdhum tapaḥ hi kṣīyet me dhakṣyāmi iti ca pārthiva evam dagdhāḥ bhagavatā dānavāḥ svena tejasā agastyena tadā rājan tapasā bhāvitātmanā īdṛśaḥ ca api agastyaḥ hi kathitaḥ te mayā anagha bravīmi aham brūhi vā tvam agastyāt kṣatriyam varam iti uktaḥ sa tadā tūṣṇīm abhūt vāyuḥ tatas abravīt śṛṇu rājan vasiṣṭhasya mukhyam karma yaśasvinaḥ vaikhānasa vidhānena gaṅgā tīram samāśritāḥ ādityāḥ satram āsanta saraḥ vai mānasam prati vasiṣṭham manasā gatvā śrutvā tatra asya gocaram yajamānān tu tān dṛṣṭvā vyagrān dīkṣā anukarśitān hantum icchanti śaila ābhāḥ khalinaḥ nāma dānavāḥ adūrāt tu tatas teṣām brahmadatta varam saraḥ hatāḥ hatāḥ vai te tatra jīvanti āplutya dānavāḥ tatas taiḥ arditāḥ devāḥ śaraṇam vāsavam yayuḥ sa ca taiḥ vyathitaḥ śakraḥ vasiṣṭham śaraṇam yayau tatas abhayam dadau tebhyaḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ tathā tān duḥkhitān jānan ānṛśaṃsya paraḥ muniḥ kailāsam prasthitām ca api nadīm gaṅgām mahā tapāḥ saraḥ bhinnam tayā nadyā sarayūḥ sā tatas abhavat evam sa indrāḥ vasiṣṭhena rakṣitāḥ tridivaukasaḥ bravīmi aham brūhi vā tvam vasiṣṭhāt kṣatriyam varam uvāca iti uktaḥ tu arjunaḥ tūṣṇīm abhūt vāyuḥ tam abravīt śṛṇu me haihaya śreṣṭha karma atreḥ su mahātmanaḥ devāḥ nṛpati śārdūla saha eva balibhiḥ tadā asuraiḥ vadhyamānāḥ te kṣīṇa prāṇāḥ divaukasaḥ vayam vadhyāmahe ca api śatrubhiḥ tamasā āvṛte na adhigacchāma śāntim ca bhayāt trāyasva naḥ prabho dṛṣṭvā na ati prabham somam tathā sūryam ca pārthiva vyajayat śatru saṃghān ca devānām svena tejasā atriṇā dahyamānān tān dṛṣṭvā devāḥ mahā asurān udbhāsitaḥ ca savitā devāḥ trātā hata asurāḥ phala bhakṣeṇa rājarṣe paśya karma atriṇā kṛtam tasya api vistareṇa uktam karma atreḥ su mahātmanaḥ bravīmi aham brūhi vā tvam atritaḥ kṣatriyam varam iti uktaḥ tu arjunaḥ tūṣṇīm abhūt vāyuḥ tam abravīt śṛṇu rājan mahat karma cyavanasya mahātmanaḥ aśvinoḥ pratisaṃśrutya cyavanaḥ pākaśāsanam cyavanasya mahā rāja śṛṇu māhātmyam uttamam yaṣṭvā yajñam mahābhāga cyavanaḥ su mahā tapāḥ aśvibhyām saha na icchāmaḥ pātum somam mahā vrata kriyatām mad vacaḥ devāḥ yathā vai samudāhṛtam pibantu anye yathākāmam na aham pātum iha utsahe tatas karma samārabdham hitāya sahasā aśvinoḥ tat tu karma samārabdham dṛṣṭvā indraḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ tathā vajreṇa bhagavant amarṣa ākula locanaḥ tam āpatantam dṛṣṭvā eva cyavanaḥ tapasā anvitaḥ madam mantra āhuti mayam vyādita āsyam mahā muniḥ dvi yojana śatāḥ tasya daṃṣṭrāḥ parama dāruṇāḥ hanuḥ tasya bhavat bhūmau ekaḥ ca asya spṛśat divam jihvā mūle sthitāḥ tasya sarve devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ timeḥ āsyam anuprāptāḥ yathā matsyāḥ mahā arṇave abruvan sahitāḥ śakram praṇama asmai dvijātaye aśvibhyām saha somam ca pibāmaḥ vigam jvara cyavanaḥ kṛtavan tau ca api aśvinau soma pīthinaḥ akṣeṣu mṛgayāyām ca pāne strīṣu ca vīryavān etaiḥ doṣaiḥ naraḥ rājan kṣayam yāti na saṃśayaḥ bravīmi aham brūhi vā tvam cyavanāt kṣatriyam varam uvāca tūṣṇīm āsīt arjunaḥ tu pavanaḥ tu abravīt punar śṛṇu me brāhmaṇeṣu eva mukhyam karma janādhipa tadā iyam cyavanena iha hṛtā teṣām vasuṃdharā śoka ārtāḥ ca mahātmānam brahmānam śaraṇam yayuḥ ūcuḥ mad āsya vyatiṣiktānām asmākam loka pūjita cyavanena hṛtā bhūmiḥ kapaiḥ ca api divam prabho gacchadhvam śaraṇam viprān āśu sa indrāḥ divaukasaḥ te yayuḥ śaraṇam viprān te ūcuḥ kān jayāmahe tatas karma samārabdham brāhmaṇaiḥ kapa nāśanam tat śrutvā preṣitaḥ dūtaḥ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ dhanī kapaiḥ sa ca tān brāhmaṇān āha dhanī kapavacaḥ yathā bhavadbhiḥ sadṛśāḥ sarve kapāḥ kim iha vartate sarve veda vidaḥ prājñāḥ sarve ca kratu yājinaḥ śrīḥ ca eva ramate teṣu dhārayanti śriyam ca te vṛthak dārān na gacchanti vṛthāmāṃsam na bhuñjate dīptam agnim juhvati ca gurūṇām vacane sthitāḥ sarve ca niyata ātmānaḥ bālānām saṃvibhāginaḥ garbhiṇī vatsaka ādiṣu pūrvāhṇeṣu na dīvyanti etaiḥ ca anyaiḥ ca bahubhiḥ guṇaiḥ yuktān katham kapān vijeṣyatha nivartadhvam nivṛttānām śubham hi vaḥ ūcuḥ kapān mayam vijeṣyāmaḥ ye devāḥ te vayam smṛtāḥ tasmāt vadhyāḥ kapā mama dhanin yāhi yathāgatam dhanī gatvā kapān āha na vaḥ viprāḥ priyaṃkarāḥ gṛhītvā astrāṇi atho viprān kapāḥ sarve samādravan samudagra dhvajān dṛṣṭvā kapān sarve dvijātayaḥ vyasṛjan jvalitān agnīn kapānām prāṇa nāśanān brahma sṛṣṭāḥ havyabhujaḥ bhuktvā sanātanāḥ nabhasi iva yathā abhrāṇi vyarājanta narādhipa hatvā vai dānavān devāḥ sarve saṃbhūya saṃyuge te na abhyajānan hi tadā brāhmaṇaiḥ nihatān kapān yathā hatā mahābhāgaiḥ tejasā brāhmaṇaiḥ kapāḥ nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā prītāḥ sarve divaukasaḥ praśaśaṃsuḥ dvijān ca eva brahmāṇam ca yaśasvinam teṣām tejaḥ tathā vīryam devānām vavṛdhe tatas avāpnuvan ca amara tvam triṣu lokeṣu pūjitam pratipūjya mahā bāho yat tat śṛṇu narādhipa jīvāmi aham brāhmaṇa arthe sarvathā satatam prabho brahmaṇe brāhmaṇebhyaḥ ca praṇamāmi ca nityaśas dattātreya prasādāt ca mayā prāptam idam yaśaḥ aho brāhmaṇa karman yathā māruta tattva uvāca brāhmaṇān kṣatra dharmeṇa pālayasva indriyāṇi ca uvāca brāhmaṇān arcase rājan satatam saṃśita vratān kam tu karma udayam dṛṣṭvā tān arcasi narādhipa kām vā brāhmaṇa pūjāyām vyuṣṭim dṛṣṭvā mahāvrata uvāca eṣa te keśavaḥ sarvam ākhyāsyati mahāmatiḥ vyuṣṭim brāhmaṇa pūjāyām dṛṣṭa vyuṣṭiḥ mahā vrataḥ balam śrotre vāc manaḥ cakṣuṣī ca deha nyāsaḥ na ati cirāt mataḥ mama na ca ati tūrṇam savitā adya yāti uktāḥ dharmāḥ ye purāṇe mahāntaḥ brāhmaṇānām kṣatriyāṇām viśām ca paurāṇam ye daṇḍam upāsate ca śeṣam kṛṣṇāt upaśikṣasva pārtha aham hi enam vedmi tattvena kṛṣṇam yaḥ ayam hi yat ca asya balam purāṇam ameya ātmā keśavaḥ kaurava indra saḥ ayam dharmam vakṣyati saṃśayeṣu kṛṣṇaḥ pṛthvīm asṛjat kham divam ca varāhaḥ ayam bhīma balaḥ purāṇaḥ kṛṣṇasya dehāt medinī saṃbabhūva kṛtsnam etat sthāvaram jaṃgamam ca asya ca adhas atha antarikṣam divam ca diśaḥ catasraḥ pradiśaḥ catasraḥ sṛṣṭiḥ tathā eva iyam anuprasūtā sa nirmame viśvam idam purāṇam asya nābhyām puṣkaram saṃprasūtam yatra utpannaḥ svayam eva amita ojāḥ yena ācchinnam tat tamaḥ pārtha ghoram yat tat tiṣṭhati arṇavam tarjayānam balam tu āsīt dvāpare pārtha kṛṣṇaḥ kalau adharmaḥ kṣitim ājagāma sa bhūtānām bhāvanaḥ bhūta bhavyaḥ sa viśvasya asya jagataḥ ca api goptā yadā dharmaḥ glāyati vai surāṇām tadā kṛṣṇaḥ jāyate mānuṣeṣu dharme sthitvā sa tu vai bhāvitātmā parān ca lokān aparān ca yāti tyājyān tyaktvā atha asurāṇām vadhāya kārya akārye kāraṇam ca eva pārtha sa viśva karmā sa ca viśva rūpaḥ sa viśva bhṛt viśva sṛj viśva jit ca sa viśvasṛj pārtha sa viśva rūpaḥ tam gandharvāḥ apsarasaḥ ca nityam upatiṣṭhante vibudhānām śatāni tam rākṣasāḥ ca parisaṃvahante rāyaspoṣaḥ sa vijigīṣuḥ ekaḥ sa paurāṇīm brahma guhām praviṣṭaḥ mahī satram bhārata agre dadarśa sa ca eva gām uddadhāra agrya karmā vikṣobhya daityān uragān dānavān ca tam ghoṣa arthe gīrbhiḥ indrāḥ stuvanti sa ca api īśaḥ bhārata ekaḥ paśūnām tasya antarikṣam pṛthivī divam ca sarvam vaśe tiṣṭhati śāśvatasya sa kumbharetāḥ sasṛje purāṇam yatra utpannam ṛṣim āhuḥ vasiṣṭham sa mātariśvā vibhuḥ aśva vājī sa raśmimān savitā ca ādidevaḥ tena asurāḥ vijitāḥ sarve eva tasya vikrāntaiḥ vijitāni iha trīṇi sa devānām mānuṣāṇām pitṝṇām tam eva āhuḥ yajña vidām vitānam mahā tejāḥ sarva gaḥ sarva siṃhaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ lokān dhārayate tathā ekaḥ hiraṇmayaḥ sapta gūḍhaḥ sa saṃvid caturbāhuḥ padmagaḥ padmanābhaḥ aśnan an aśnan ca tathā eva dhīraḥ kṛṣṇam sadā pārtha kartāram ehi saḥ ekadā kakṣa gataḥ mahātmā tṛptaḥ vibhuḥ khāṇḍave dhūmaketuḥ saḥ eva aśvaḥ śvetam aśvam prayacchat saḥ eva aśvān atha sarvān cakāra evam ramyān asṛjat parvatān ca hṛṣīkeśaḥ amita dīpta agni tejāḥ tam ṛk sahasraiḥ puruṣam purāṇam durvāsāḥ vai tena na anyena śakyaḥ gṛhe rājan vāsayitum mahā ojāḥ tam eva āhuḥ ṛṣim ekam purāṇam sa viśva kṛt vidadhāti ātma bhāvān vedān ca yaḥ vedayate adhidevaḥ vidhīn ca yaḥ ca āśrayate purāṇān jyotīṃṣi śuklāni ca sarva loke trayaḥ lokāḥ lokapālāḥ trayaḥ ca saṃvatsaraḥ saḥ ṛtuḥ saḥ ardha māsaḥ saḥ ahorātraḥ sa kalā vai sa kāṣṭhāḥ mātrāḥ muhūrtāḥ ca lavāḥ kṣaṇāḥ ca viṣvaksene sarvam etat pratīhi candra ādityau graha nakṣatra tārāḥ sarvāṇi darśāni atha paurṇamāsyaḥ rudra ādityāḥ vasavaḥ atha aśvinaḥ ca sādhyāḥ viśvāḥ marutām ṣaṭ gaṇāḥ ca prajāpatiḥ deva mātā aditiḥ ca sarve kṛṣṇāt ṛṣayaḥ ca eva sapta vāyuḥ bhūtvā vikṣipate ca viśvam agniḥ bhūtvā dahate viśva rūpaḥ āpaḥ bhūtvā majjayate ca sarvam brahmā bhūtvā sṛjate viśva saṃghān jyotiḥ bhū paramaḥ asau purastāt prakāśayan prabhayā viśva rūpaḥ apaḥ sṛṣṭvā hi ātmabhūḥ ātmayoniḥ purā akarot sarvam eva atha viśvam ṛtūn utpātān vividhāni adbhutāni meghān vidyut sarvam airāvatam ca ṛtūn māsān vividham kārya jātam vidyut saṃghaiḥ āpatantaḥ ca meghāḥ sarvam kṛṣṇāt sthāvaram jaṅgamam ca viśva ākhyātāt viṣṇum enam pratīhi viśvāvāsam nirguṇam vāsudevam saṃkarṣaṇam jīva bhūtam vadanti sa pañcadhā pañca jana upapannam saṃcodayan viśvam idam sisṛkṣuḥ sṛṣṭvā viśvam viśvayoniḥ mahātmā tatra atiṣṭhat viśvarūpaḥ hi yogāt tatas bhūmim vyadadhāt pañca bījām dyauḥ pṛthivyām dhāsyati bhūri vāri tatas devān asurān mānuṣān ca lokān ṛṣīn ca atha pitṝn prajāḥ ca samāsena vividhān prāṇi lokān sarvān sadā bhūtapatiḥ sisṛkṣuḥ śubha aśubham sthāvaram jaṅgamam ca mṛtyuḥ ca eva prāṇinām antakāle sākṣāt kṛṣṇaḥ śāśvataḥ dharma vāhaḥ yat praśastam ca lokeṣu puṇyam yat ca śubha aśubham etādṛśa keśavaḥ ayam svayambhuḥ nārāyaṇaḥ paramaḥ ca avyayaḥ ca madhyam ca asya jagataḥ tasthivasaḥ ca sarveṣām bhūtānām prabhavaḥ ca apyayaḥ ca tādṛśaḥ keśavaḥ devaḥ bhūyas nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ ādiḥ antaḥ ca madhyam ca deśāt kālāt hariḥ jagatām tasthivasām ca eva bhūtānām prabhava apyayaḥ vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ pitāmaha vacaḥ śrutvā rājan te prapitāmahaḥ praṇamya puṇḍarīkākṣam idam vacanam abravīt uvāca brūhi brāhmaṇa pūjāyām vyuṣṭim tvam madhusūdana uvāca śṛṇuṣva avahitaḥ rājan dvijānām bharata ṛṣabha dvāravatyām samāsīnam purā mām kuru nandana kim phalam brāhmaṇeṣu asti pūjāyām madhusūdana sadā dvijātīn saṃpūjya kim phalam tatra mānada etat brūhi pitar sarvam su mahān saṃśayaḥ atra mama pratyabruvam mahā rāja yat tat śṛṇu samāhitaḥ vyuṣṭim brāhmaṇa pūjāyām raukmiṇeya nibodha mama trivarge ca apavarge ca yaśaḥ śrī roga śāntiṣu devatā pitṛ pūjāsu saṃtoṣyāḥ eva naḥ dvijāḥ ete hi soma rājānaḥ īśvarāḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ brāhmaṇa pramukham saukhyam na me atra asti vicāraṇā brāhmaṇa pramukham vīryam āyuḥ kīrtiḥ yaśaḥ balam lokāḥ loka īśvarāḥ ca eva sarve brāhmaṇa pūrvakāḥ anyān api sṛjeyuḥ ca lokān loka īśvarān tathā avasat mad gṛhe tāta brāhmaṇaḥ hari piṅgalaḥ cīra vāsāḥ bilva daṇḍī dīrgha śmaśru nakha ādimān dīrghebhyaḥ ca manuṣyebhyaḥ pramāṇāt adhikaḥ bhuvi sa sma saṃcarate lokān ye divyāḥ ye ca mānuṣāḥ imāḥ gāthāḥ gāyamānaḥ catvareṣu sabhāsu ca durvāsasam vāsayet kaḥ brāhmaṇam satkṛtam gṛhe roṣaṇam sarva bhūtānām sūkṣme api apakṛte kṛte paribhāṣām ca me śrutvā kaḥ nu dadyāt pratiśrayam yaḥ mām kaḥ cit vāsayeta na sa mām kopayet iha sa sma bhuṅkte sahasrāṇām bahūnām annam ekadā na ca asya vayasā tulyaḥ pṛthivyām abhavat tadā saḥ mad āvasatham gatvā śayyāḥ ca āstaraṇāni ca kanyāḥ ca alaṃkṛtāḥ dagdhvā tatas vyapagataḥ svayam atha mām abravīt bhūyas sa muniḥ saṃśita vrataḥ sarvāṇi eva anna pānāni bhakṣyāḥ ca uccāvacāḥ tathā a vimṛś eva ca tatas kṛtavan asmi tat tathā tena ucchiṣṭena gātrāṇi śiraḥ ca eva abhyamṛkṣayam sa dadarśa tadā abhyāśe mātaram te śubha ānanām muniḥ pāyasa digdha aṅgīm rathe tūrṇam ayojayat pratodena ātudat bālām rukmiṇīm mama paśyataḥ na ca me stokam api āsīt duḥkham īrṣyā kṛtam tadā tatas sa rājamārgeṇa mahatā niryayau bahis tat dṛṣṭvā mahat āścaryam dāśārhāḥ jāta manyavaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ eva jāyeran na anyaḥ varṇaḥ katham cana kaḥ hi enam ratham āsthāya jīvet anyaḥ pumān iha āśīviṣa viṣam tīkṣṇam tatas tīkṣṇataram viṣam brahma āśīviṣa dagdhasya na asti kaḥ cit cikitsakaḥ tām na amarṣayata śrīmān tatas tūrṇam acodayat padātiḥ utpathena eva prādhāvat dakṣiṇā mukhaḥ jitaḥ krodhaḥ tvayā kṛṣṇa prakṛtyā eva mahā bhuja prītaḥ asmi te govinda vṛṇu kāmān yathā īpsitān yāvat eva manuṣyāṇām anne bhāvaḥ bhaviṣyati yathā eva anne tathā teṣām tvayi bhāvaḥ bhaviṣyati yāvat ca puṇyā lokeṣu tvayi kīrtiḥ bhaviṣyati triṣu lokeṣu tāvat ca vaiśiṣṭyam pratipatsyase sarvam tathā eva draṣṭāsi viśiṣṭam vā janārdana atas mṛtyu bhayam na asti yāvat icchā te acyuta iti uktaḥ aham śarīram svam apaśyam śrī samāyutam rukmiṇī ca abravīt prī sarva strīṇām vara yaśaḥ kīrti ca anuttamām loke samavāp śobhana na tvām jarā vā rogaḥ vā vaivarṇyam ca api bhāmini sprakṣyanti puṇya gandhā ca kṛṣṇam ārādhayiṣyasi ṣoḍaśānām sahasrāṇām vadhūnām keśavasya ha variṣṭhā saha lokyā ca keśavasya bhaviṣyasi tasmin antarhite ca aham upāṃśu vratam ādiśam yat kim cit brāhmaṇaḥ brūyāt sarvam kuryām iti prabho tatas parama hṛṣṭa ātmā prāviśam gṛham eva ca praviṣṭa mātraḥ ca gṛhe sarvam paśyāmi tat navam tatas aham vismayam prāptaḥ sarva dṛṣṭvā navam dṛḍham apūjayam ca manasā raukmiṇeya dvijam tadā māhātmyam dvijamukhyasya sarvam ākhyātavan tadā pūjayasva mahābhāgān vāgbhiḥ dānaiḥ ca nityadā evam vyuṣṭim aham prāptaḥ brāhmaṇānām prasāda jām yat ca mām āha bhīṣmaḥ ayam tat satyam bharata ṛṣabha uvāca durvāsasaḥ prasādāt te yat tadā madhusūdana avāptam iha vijñānam tat me vyākhyātum arhasi mahābhāgyam ca yat tasya nāmāni ca mahātmanaḥ uvāca yat avāptam mahā rāja śreyaḥ yat ca arjitam yaśaḥ prayataḥ prātar utthāya yat adhīye viśām pate prāñjaliḥ śatarudrīyam tat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu śivaḥ sarva gataḥ rudraḥ sraṣṭā yaḥ tam śṛṇuṣva mama śaṃkaraḥ tu asṛjat tāta prajāḥ sthāvara jaṅgamāḥ na asti kim cit param bhūtam mahādevāt viśām pate iha triṣu api lokeṣu bhūtānām prabhavaḥ hi saḥ visaṃjñāḥ hata bhūyiṣṭhāḥ vepanti ca patanti ca śrutvā vidīryet hṛdayam devānām api saṃyuge yān ca ghoreṇa rūpeṇa paśyet kruddhaḥ pinākadhṛk tad kṣaṇāt eva kuryāt sa bhasma vahni śikhā yathā na surāḥ na asurāḥ loke na gandharvāḥ na pannagāḥ dhanuṣā bāṇam utsṛjya sa ghoṣam vinanāda ca te na śarma kutas śāntim viṣādam lebhire surāḥ tena jyā tala ghoṣeṇa sarve lokāḥ samākulāḥ babhūvuḥ avaśāḥ pārtha viṣeduḥ ca sura asurāḥ andhena tamasā lokāḥ prāvṛtāḥ na cakāśire pranaṣṭā jyotiṣām bhās ca saha sūryeṇa bhārata bhṛśam bhītāḥ tatas śāntim cakruḥ svastyayanāni ca ṛṣayaḥ sarva bhūtānām ātmanaḥ ca hita eṣiṇaḥ pūṣāṇam ca abhidudrāva para vapuṣā anvitaḥ puroḍāśam bhakṣayataḥ daśanān vai vyaśātayat tatas praṇemuḥ devāḥ te vepamānāḥ sma śaṃkaram punar ca saṃdadhe rudraḥ dīptam su niśitam śaram rudrasya vikramam dṛṣṭvā bhītāḥ devāḥ saha ṛṣibhiḥ tatas prasādayām ās śarva te vibudha uttama jepuḥ ca śatarudrīyam devāḥ kṛtvā añjalim tatas saṃstūyamānaḥ tridaśaiḥ prasasāda maheśvaraḥ rudrasya bhāgam yajñe ca viśiṣṭam te tu akalpayan bhayena tridaśāḥ rājan śaraṇam ca prapedire yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tripurāṇi mahā bāho jitavan sa maheśvaraḥ vāsudevaḥ ācakṣva me yathātattvam sarvajña madhusūdana śṛṇu me gadataḥ tāta yathā dagdham puratrayam asurāṇām purāṇi āsan trīṇi vīryavatām divi āyasam rājatam ca eva sauvarṇam aparam tathā atha sarve amarāḥ rudram jagmuḥ śaraṇam arditāḥ tatas ūcuḥ mahātmānaḥ devāḥ sarve samāgatāḥ rudram tam raudra karmāṇi sarva astra kuśalam prabhum sa tathā uktaḥ tathā iti uktvā viṣṇum kṛtvā śara uttamam śalyam agnim tathā kṛtvā puṅkham vaivasvatam yamam vedān kṛtvā dhanuḥ sarvān jyām ca sāvitrim uttamām devān ratha varam kṛtvā viniyujya ca sarvaśas śareṇa āditya varṇena kālāgni sama tejasā te asurāḥ sa purāḥ tatra dagdhāḥ rudreṇa bhārata tam ca eva aṅka gatam dṛṣṭvā bālam pañcaśikham punar umā jijñāsamānā vai kaḥ ayam iti abravīt tadā asūyataḥ ca śakrasya vajreṇa prahariṣyataḥ ayam śreṣṭhaḥ iti jñātvā vavande tam umāpatim tatas prasādayām āsuḥ umām rudram ca te surāḥ sa ca api brāhmaṇaḥ bhūtvā durvāsāḥ nāma vīryavān dvāravatyām mama gṛhe ciram kālam upāvasat tān udāra tayā ca aham akṣamam tasya duḥsaham sa candramāḥ sa ca īśānaḥ sa sūryaḥ varuṇaḥ ca saḥ sa kālaḥ saḥ antakaḥ mṛtyuḥ sa tamaḥ rātri ahāni ca māsa ardha māsāḥ ṛtavaḥ saṃdhye saṃvatsaraḥ ca saḥ sa dhātā sa vidhātā ca viśva karmā sa sarva vid nakṣatrāṇi diśaḥ ca eva pradiśaḥ atha grahāḥ tathā viśvamūrtiḥ ameya ātmā bhagavant amita dyutiḥ īdṛśaḥ sa mahādevaḥ bhūyas ca bhagavant atas na hi śakyāḥ guṇāḥ vaktum api varṣa śataiḥ api uvāca yudhiṣṭhira mahā bāho mahā bhāgyam mahātmanaḥ vadanti agnim mahādevam tathā sthāṇum maheśvaram eka akṣam tryambakam ca eva viśvarūpam śivam tathā dve tanū tasya devasya veda jñāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ viduḥ ghorām anyām śivām anyām te tanū bahudhā punar śivā saumyā ca yā tasya dharmaḥ tu apaḥ atha candramāḥ īśvara tvāt mahā tvāt ca maheśvaraḥ iti smṛtaḥ devānām su mahān yat ca yat ca asya viṣayaḥ mahān yat ca viśvam mahat pāti mahādevaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ śivam icchan manuṣyāṇām tasmāt eṣa śivaḥ smṛtaḥ sthira liṅgaḥ ca yat nityam tasmāt sthāṇuḥ iti smṛ yat asya bahudhā rūpam bhūtam bhavyam bhavat tathā sthāvaram jaṅgamam ca eva bahurūpaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ dhūmram rūpam ca yat tasya dhūrjaṭi iti atas ucyate viśve devāḥ ca yat tasmin viśvarūpaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ ayuta akṣaḥ vā sarvata ukṣi mayaḥ api vā cakṣuṣaḥ prabhavaḥ tejaḥ na asti antaḥ atha asya cakṣuṣām teṣām adhipatiḥ yat ca tasmāt paśupatiḥ smṛtaḥ bhakta anugrahaṇa arthāya gūḍhaliṅgaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ vigraham pūjayet yaḥ vai liṅgam vā api mahātmanaḥ liṅgam pūjayitā nityam mahatīm śriyam aśnute ṛṣayaḥ ca api devāḥ ca gandharva apsarasaḥ tathā sukham dadāti prī ātman bhaktānām bhakta vatsalaḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ ca eva śaṃkaraḥ eṣaḥ eva śmaśāneṣu devaḥ vasati nityaśas yajante tam janāḥ tatra vīrasthāna niṣeviṇam viṣama sthaḥ śarīreṣu sa mṛtyuḥ prāṇinām iha sa ca vāyuḥ śarīreṣu prāṇaḥ apānaḥ śarīriṇām tasya ghorāṇi rūpāṇi dīptāni ca bahūni ca nāmadheyāni vedeṣu bahūni asya yathārthataḥ vyāsāt anantaram yat ca api upasthānam mahātmanaḥ pradātā sarva lokānām viśvam ca api ucyate mahat jyeṣṭha bhūtam vadanti enam brāhmaṇāḥ ṛṣayaḥ apare prathamaḥ hi eṣa devānām mukhāt agniḥ ajāyata grahaiḥ bahuvidhaiḥ prāṇān saṃruddhān utsṛjati api sa mocayati puṇya ātmā śaraṇyaḥ śaraṇa āgatān āyuḥ ārogyam aiśvaryam vittam kāmān ca puṣkalān sa dadāti manuṣyebhyaḥ saḥ eva ākṣipate punar aiśvaryāt ca eva kāmānām īśvaraḥ punar ucyate maheśvaraḥ ca lokānām mahatām īśvaraḥ ca saḥ uvāca bhīṣmam śāṃtanavam bhūyas paryapṛcchat yudhiṣṭhiraḥ pratyakṣam āgamaḥ vā iti kim tayoḥ kāraṇam bhavet uvāca śṛṇu vakṣyāmi te prājña samyak tvam anupṛcchasi dṛṣṭam śrutam anantam hi yatra saṃśaya darśanam pratyakṣam kāraṇam dṛṣṭam hetukāḥ prājña māninaḥ tat ayuktam vyavasyanti bālāḥ paṇḍita māninaḥ śakyam dīrghena kālena yuktena atandritena ca prāṇayātrām anekām ca kalpayānena bhārata hetūnām antam āsādya vipulam jñānam uttamam uvāca pratyakṣam lokatas siddham lokāḥ ca āgama pūrvakāḥ śiṣṭa ācāraḥ bahuvidhaḥ brūhi tat me pitāmaha uvāca adharmāḥ dharma rūpeṇa tṛṇaiḥ kūpāḥ iva āvṛtāḥ tatas taiḥ bhidyate vṛttam śṛṇu ca eva yudhiṣṭhira avṛttyā ye ca bhindanti śruta tyāga parāyaṇāḥ dharma vidveṣiṇaḥ mandāḥ iti uktaḥ teṣu saṃśayaḥ atṛpyantaḥ tu sādhūnām ye eva āgama buddhayaḥ param iti eva saṃtuṣṭāḥ tān upāssva ca pṛccha ca kāma arthau pṛṣṭhatas kṛtvā lobha moha anusāriṇau na teṣām bhidyate vṛttam yajña svādhyāya karmabhiḥ mūlācāraḥ tu sādhūnām yajña svādhyāya vṛttāt ācāraḥ kāraṇam ca eva dharmaḥ ca eva trayam punar uvāca apāre mārgamāṇasya param tīram a paśyataḥ vedāḥ pratyakṣam ācāraḥ pramāṇam tat trayam yadi uvāca yadi evam manyase rājan tridhā dharma vicāraṇā uktaḥ mārgaḥ trayāṇām ca tat tathā eva samācara sadā eva bharata śreṣṭha mā te bhūt atra saṃśayaḥ andhaḥ jaḍaḥ iva āśaṅkaḥ yat bravīmi tat ācara brāhmaṇeṣu ca vṛttiḥ yā pitṛpaitāmaha ucitā tām anvehi mahā bāho svargasya ete hi deśikāḥ pramāṇam apramāṇam vai yaḥ kuryāt abudhaḥ naraḥ eteṣu eva tu ime lokāḥ kṛtsnāḥ iti nibodha tān uvāca bravītu bhagavat etat kva te gacchanti tādṛśāḥ uvāca dharme eva ratiḥ teṣām ācārya upāsanāt bhavet manuṣyāḥ yadi vā devāḥ śarīram upatāpya vai prathamam brahmaṇaḥ putram dharmam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ dharmiṇaḥ paryupāsante phalam pakvam iva āśayaḥ uvāca asatām kīdṛśam rūpam sādhavaḥ kim ca kurvate bravītu me bhavān etat santaḥ asantaḥ ca kīdṛśāḥ uvāca durācārāḥ ca durdharṣāḥ durmukhāḥ ca api asādhavaḥ sādhavaḥ śīla saṃpannāḥ śiṣṭa ācārasya lakṣaṇam satya ārjava parāyaṇāḥ eteṣām dharma śīlānām rājamārge gavām madhye goṣṭha madhye ca dharmiṇaḥ na upasevanti rāja indra sargam mūtra purīṣayoḥ pañcānām aśanam dattvā śeṣam aśnanti sādhavaḥ na jalpanti ca bhuñjānāḥ na nidrānti ārdra pāṇayaḥ citra bhānum anaḍvāham devam goṣṭham catuṣpatham brāhmaṇam dhārmikam caityam te kurvanti pradakṣiṇam vṛddhānām bhāra taptānām strīṇām bāla āturasya ca brāhmaṇānām gavām rājñām panthānam dadate ca te atithīnām ca sarveṣām preṣyāṇām sva janasya ca sāmānyam bhojanam kuryāt svayam na agrya aśanam vrajet muni śāpāt dvijaḥ kaḥ cit vyāghra tām samupāgataḥ bahulām bhakṣaṇa rucim āsvādya śapathena tu vimucya pīta vatsām tām dṛṣṭvā smṛtvā purātanam jagāma lokān amalān sā sva rāṣṭram tathā punar tasmāt satya ārjava rataḥ rājā rāṣṭram samānavam tathā śaraṇa kāmānām goptā syāt svāgata pradaḥ sāyam prātar manuṣyāṇām aśanam deva nirmitam na antarā bhojanam dṛṣṭam upavāsa vidhiḥ hi saḥ homa kāle yathā vahniḥ kālam eva pratīkṣate ṛtu kāle tathā nārī ṛtum eva pratīkṣate amṛtam brāhmaṇāḥ gāvaḥ iti etat trayam ekatas yajuṣā saṃskṛtam māṃsam upabhuñjan na duṣyati pṛṣṭha māṃsam vṛthāmāṃsam putra māṃsam ca tat samam karma vai saphalam kṛtvā gurūṇām pratipādayet gurūn abhyarcya vardhante āyuṣā yaśasā śriyā vṛddhān na ativadet jātu na ca saṃpreṣayet api na āsīnaḥ syāt sthiteṣu evam āyuḥ asya na riṣyate na nagnām īkṣate nārīm na vidvān puruṣān api maithunam satatam guptam āhāram ca samācaret tīrthānām guravaḥ tīrtham śucīnām hṛdayam śuci darśanānām param jñānam saṃtoṣaḥ paramam sukham sāyam prātar ca vṛddhānām śṛṇuyāt puṣkalāḥ giraḥ śrutam āpnoti hi naraḥ satatam vṛddha sevayā dāna āgāre gavām ca eva brāhmaṇānām ca saṃnidhau svādhyāye bhojane ca eva dakṣiṇam pāṇim uddharet yacchet vāc manasī nityam indriyāṇām ca vibhramam saṃskṛtam pāyasam nityam yavāgūm kṛsaram haviḥ aṣṭakāḥ pitṛ daivatyāḥ vṛddhānām abhipūjanam śmaśrukarmaṇi maṅgalyam kṣutānām abhinandanam vyādhitānām ca sarveṣām āyuṣaḥ pratinandanam avarāṇām samānānām śiṣyāṇām ca samācar pāpam ācakṣate nityam hṛdayam pāpa karmiṇām jñāna pūrvam vinaśyanti gūhamānāḥ mahājane jñāna pūrvam kṛtam karma chādayante hi asādhavaḥ na mām manuṣyāḥ paśyanti na mām paśyanti devatāḥ pāpena abhihataḥ pāpaḥ pāpam eva abhijāyate yathā vārddhuṣikaḥ vṛddhim dehabhede pratīkṣate prāyaścitta hatam pāpam tathā sadyas praṇaśyati tasmāt pāpam na gūheta gūhamānam vivardhate kṛtvā tu sādhuṣu ākhyeyam te tat praśamayanti uta āśayā saṃcitam dravyam yat kāle na upabhujyate mānasam sarva bhūtānām dharmam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ tasmāt sarvāṇi bhūtāni dharmam eva samāsate nidhim nidadhyāt pāratryam yātrā artham dāna śabditam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ mānasāni iha tīrthāni praśaṃsanti mahā ṛṣayaḥ bhīṣmaḥ śṛṇu tīrthāni gadataḥ mānasāni iha mānada yeṣu samyak naraḥ snātvā prayāti paramām gatim satyam tīrtham kṣamā tīrtham satyam indriya nigrahaḥ dānam tīrtham damaḥ tīrtham saṃtoṣaḥ tīrtham uttamam brahmacaryam param tīrtham tīrtham ca priya vādi tā jñānam tīrtham tapaḥ tīrtham dhṛtiḥ tīrtham udāhṛtam tīrthānām api yat tīrtham viśuddhiḥ manasaḥ parā yaḥ lubdhaḥ piśunaḥ krūraḥ dāmbhikaḥ viṣaya ātmakaḥ sarva tīrtheṣu api snātaḥ pāpaḥ malinaḥ eva saḥ cittam antargatam duṣṭam tīrtha snānaiḥ na śudhyati śataśas api jale dhautam surā bhāṇḍam iva aśuci tatra tasya kurukṣetram naimiṣam puṣkaram gayā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ yaḥ snātaḥ mānase tīrthe sa yāti paramām gatim pāpasya kim adhiṣṭhānam kā prasūtiḥ ca bhārata bhīṣmaḥ kim ca asya kāraṇam proktam tat me brūhi pitāmaha atra te saṃśayaḥ mā bhūt lobhaḥ pāpasya kāraṇam lobhāt mohaḥ ca māyā ca mānāt mātsaryam eva ca nityam gambhīra toyābhiḥ āpagābhiḥ iva arṇavaḥ sarva bhūteṣu aviśvāsaḥ sarva bhūteṣu anirdayaḥ su mahānti api śāstrāṇi dhārayantaḥ bahuśrutāḥ chettāraḥ saṃśayānām ca lobha grastāḥ pratyānti adhas lobha kṣaye kṣayam yānti sarva pāpāni dehinām yadi icchasi mahā rāja śāśvatīm gatim ātmanaḥ uvāca na abhāgadheyaḥ prāpnoti dhanam su balavān api bhāgadheya anvitaḥ tu arthān kṛśaḥ bālaḥ ca vindati kṛta yatna aphalāḥ ca eva dṛśyante śataśas narāḥ ayatnena edhamānāḥ ca dṛśyante bahavaḥ janāḥ yadā prayatnam kṛtavān dṛśyate hi aphalaḥ naraḥ mārgan naya śataiḥ arthān a mārgan ca aparaḥ sukhī akāryam asakṛt kṛtvā dṛśyante hi adhanāḥ narāḥ dhana yuktāḥ tu adharma sthāḥ dṛśyante ca apare janāḥ adhītya nītim yasmāt ca nīti yuktaḥ na dṛśyate anabhijñaḥ ca sācivyam gamitaḥ kena hetunā yadi vidyām upāśritya naraḥ sukham avāpnuyāt na vidvān vidyayā hīnam vṛtti artham upasaṃśrayet yathā pipāsām jayati puruṣaḥ prāpya vai jalam dṛṣṭa arthaḥ vidyayā api evam avidyām prajahet naraḥ na aprāpta kālaḥ mriyate viddhaḥ śara śataiḥ api tṛṇa agreṇa api saṃspṛṣṭaḥ prāpta kālaḥ na jīvati uvāca īhamānaḥ samārambhān yadi na āsādayet dhanam dānena bhogī bhavati medhāvī vṛddha sevayā ahiṃsayā ca dīrgha āyuḥ iti prāhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ tasmāt dadyāt na yāceta pūjayet dhārmikān api su ābhāṣī priya kṛt śuddhaḥ sarva sattva avihiṃsakaḥ yadā pramāṇa prabhavaḥ svabhāvaḥ ca sukha asukhe maśa kīṭa pipīlānām sthiraḥ bhava yudhiṣṭhira uvāca tatra āśvasīta satkṛtvā a satkṛtvā na viśvaset buddhim āviśya bhūtānām dharma artheṣu pravartate tadā āśvasīta dharma ātma adṛḍha buddhiḥ na viśvaset etāvat mātram etat hi bhūtānām prājña lakṣaṇam yathā hi upasthita aiśvaryāḥ pūjayante narāḥ narān evam eva ātmanā ātmānam pūjayanti iha dhārmikāḥ bhāva śuddhiḥ tu tapasā devatānām ca pūjayā tasmāt viśuddham ātmānam jānīyāt dharma cāriṇam trayāṇām api lokānām āloka karaṇaḥ bhavet yudhiṣṭhiraḥ pitāmaha mahā bāho sarva dharma bhṛtām vara bhīṣmaḥ nānā janapada ākīrṇe yajña vāṭa vibhūṣite tatra sā nagarī ramyā yamunā tīram āśritā ardhacandra pratīkāśā vidvas jana vibhūṣitā indra yaṣṭi dhvaja ākīrṇā gopībhiḥ upaśobhitā bahu dvija samākīrṇā nānā paṇya upaśobhitā su pramāṇā su ramyā ca svāti nakṣatra nirmitā prākāra aṭṭa pratolībhiḥ durjayā parikhādibhiḥ āmrātaka kapitthaiḥ ca rājavṛkṣaiḥ ca śobhitā devatāyatanaiḥ divyaiḥ kadala khaṇḍa maṇḍitā haṃsa mālā pratīkāśaiḥ dīpyate dhavalaiḥ gṛhaiḥ karavīraiḥ karṇikāraiḥ pāṭalā aśoka campakaiḥ mallikā kunda jātībhiḥ kubja āhlāda kuraṇṭakaiḥ suvarṇa śveta yūthībhiḥ kiṃkirāta utpala ādibhiḥ puṃnāga vṛkṣa bakulaiḥ udyānaiḥ upaśobhitā saṃpūrṇā dhana dhānyaiḥ ca go dhanaiḥ upaśobhitā veda adhyayana ghoṣaiḥ ca pavitrīkṛta maṅgalā vedi śṛṅgāṭakaiḥ ramyaiḥ trika catvara śobhitā rāvaṇasya iva ratna āḍhyā laṅkā ca eva mahā purī kṣatra dharme rataḥ śrīmān prajāpati samaḥ kṣitau tena sā nagarī ramyā rāja siṃhena pālitā nitya utsava pramuditā śaṅkha vāditra nāditā su saṃgīta vidagdhaiḥ ca prekṣaṇīyaiḥ samākulā antarāpaṇa vīthibhiḥ suvibhaktaiḥ catuṣpathaiḥ dīrghikā kūpa vāpībhiḥ taḍāgaiḥ upaśobhitā sabhā prapā samākīrṇā vivāha makha saṃkulā purī candravatī nāma dṛṣṭā te yadi vā śrutā tasyām puryām purā vṛttam tattvam śṛṇu yudhiṣṭhira hṛṣṭa puṣṭā su saṃtuṣṭā bahulā nāma viśrutā go dhanasya ca sā mukhyā haṃsa varṇā ghaṭa sravā dīrgha ghoṇā vibhakta aṅgā śreṣṭha loma tanu tvacā vistīrṇa jaghanā divyā pīna śroṇi payodharā sarva lakṣaṇa saṃpannā sarva avayava sundarā nīla kaṇṭhā śubha grīvā ghaṇṭālī madhura svarā sāndram su puṣpitam surabhi acchinnam carate tṛṇam mṛga siṃha samākīrṇe bahu śvāpada sevite vallī vṛkṣa ādi gahane śivā śata ninādite dvīpī śoṇita māṃsa āśī mahā daṃṣṭraḥ mahā balaḥ tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭraḥ nakha āyudhaḥ tasya yūtha paribhraṣṭā bahulā tṛṇa tṛṣṇayā abhidravan ca tām vyāghraḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt vyāghrasya vacanam śrutvā niṣṭhuram loma harṣaṇam sutam rūpa anvitam bālam candra rūpa sama prabham rudantī karuṇam sā tu nirāśā putra darśane dṛṣṭvā tu bahulām vyāghraḥ krandamānām su duḥkhitām na rudantyāḥ vā hasantyāḥ vā tathā te jīvitam bhavet kautukam me adya saṃjātam aśeṣam kathayasva naḥ vyāghrasya vacanam śrutvā bahulā vākyam abravīt tvām samālokya lokasya paritrāṇam na vidyate jīvita artham na śocāmi prāptavyam maraṇam mayā tasmāt tat na aham eva ekam vyāghra śocāmi jīvitam kim tu sneha vaśāt vyāghra duḥkhena ruditam mayā asti me hṛdi saṃtāpaḥ tam ca tvam śrotum arhasi agre vayasi vartantī prasūtā aham mṛgādhipa iṣṭaḥ prathama jātaḥ tu sutaḥ ca mama bālakaḥ kṣīram pibati me vatsaḥ tṛṇam na adya api jighrati sutam tam anuśocāmi katham jīviṣyate sutaḥ tasya icchāmi stanam dātum putra sneha vaśa anugā sakhīnām arpayitvā ca saṃdiśya ca hita ahitam punar pratyāgamiṣyāmi yatheṣṭam bhakṣayiṣyasi śīghra aham āgamiṣyāmi mahā vyāghra tava antikam bahulāyāḥ vacaḥ śrutvā mṛgendraḥ punar abravīt kim te putreṇa kartavyam maraṇam kim na paśyasi tvam punar kṛpayā āviṣṭā putra putra iti bhāṣase na mantrāḥ na tapaḥ dānam na mātā na pitā sutaḥ śaknuvanti paritrātum āgatām mad samīpatas vṛṣabhaiḥ nāditam ramyam bāla vatsa vibhūṣitam bhūṣaṇam deva lokasya svarga tulyam na saṃśayaḥ pavitram tat pavitrāṇām maṅgalānām ca maṅgalam yat tīrtham sarva tīrthānām ramyāṇām ramyam uttamam samasta guṇa saṃkīrṇam īśvara āyatanam mahat yatra vatsāḥ ca huṃkāram karuṇam mātṛ kāṅkṣayā yat gopaiḥ pālitam śūraiḥ bāhu yuddha viśāradaiḥ pragīta nṛtya saṃlāpam valgu tā āsphoṭa nāditam saraḥ vat bhrājate goṣṭham śrīmadbhiḥ iva paṅkajaiḥ tat śrīniketanam ramyam mātaram bhrātaram sutam dṛṣṭvā sakhī janam bhūyas katham pratyāgamiṣyasi na nirāśāni bhūtāni vāc mātreṇa karomi aham prathamam dṛṣṭavat sā aham mṛgendra śṛṇu mama vacaḥ dṛṣṭvā sakhī janam bālam gopān ca paricārakān gopī janam samāgamya jananīm ca viśeṣataḥ vyāghraḥ śapathaiḥ āgamiṣyāmi manyase yadi muñca mām śapathāḥ kīdṛśāḥ bhadre ye tvayā parinoditāḥ śapathaiḥ āgamiṣyāmi satyam brūyām na saṃśayaḥ mā dadasva iti yaḥ brūyāt guru agni brāhmaṇeṣu ca madhu māṃse ca yat pāpam lākṣā vikrayaṇe tathā asaṃtoṣī ca yaḥ vipraḥ nityam bhavati yācakaḥ matsarī gotra bhāvena bhūtānām guṇa nāśakaḥ kaumāram ca api bhartāram yā nārī na anumanyate ye saktāḥ guru dāreṣu svāmi dāreṣu ye narāḥ brāhmaṇaḥ vṛṣalīm gatvā na tu tīrthāni sevate brāhmaṇaḥ kṛta saṃskāraḥ śūdra prekṣaṇa kārakaḥ anṛtam dhana saṃbaddhe kūṭasākṣyam vadanti ye yat pāpam brahmahatyāyām mātā pitṛ vadhena ca yat pāpam lubdhakānām ca mlecchānām gara dāyinām pādena spṛśate gāḥ ca śirobhiḥ na namanti ye goṣu avajñām prakurvanti śapante tāḍayanti ca sakṛt dattvā tu yaḥ kanyām dvitīyāya prayacchati kathāyām kriyamāṇāyām antarāyam karoti yaḥ dvi bhāryaḥ puruṣaḥ yaḥ tu ekām snehena paśyati ekākī mṛṣṭam aśnāti yaḥ kaḥ cit puruṣa adhamaḥ yaḥ trīn hale balīvardān viṣamam vāhayeta yaḥ tena pāpena lipye aham yadi na āyām tava antikam iti etaiḥ pātakaiḥ ghoraiḥ āgamiṣyāmi aham punar loke asmin nāstikāḥ ke cid mūrkhāḥ paṇḍita māninaḥ bhrāmayanti ca te buddhim cakra ārūḍhaḥ iva īkṣaṇam prāyas kṛtārthaḥ lokaḥ ayam manyate na upakāriṇam vatsaḥ kṣīra kṣayam dṛṣṭvā parityajati mātaram ṛṣi deva asura gaṇaiḥ śapathāḥ kārya siddhaye kṛtāḥ parasparam pūrvam tat na manyāmahe katham tena evam darśitam pūrvam yathā iṣṭam kuru sāṃpratam mātaram bhrātaram dṛṣṭvā sakhīḥ sva jana bāndhavān bhīṣmaḥ satyam eva agratas kṛtvā śīghram āgamanam kuru evam sā pratyayam kṛtvā bahulā satya vādinī anujñātā mṛgendreṇa prayātā putra vatsalā aśru pūrṇa mukhī dīnā vepamānā su duḥkhitā kurarī niḥśvasantī iva patitā śoka sāgare kariṇī iva hi nāgena gṛhītā salilāśaye aśakta ātma paritrāṇe vilapantī muhur muhur sā tu gopa kulam gatvā bahulā hṛta vikramā śrutvā ātma vatsam krośantam paryadhāvata tad mukhī upāsarpata tam vatsam bāṣpa paryākula īkṣaṇā sa prāptām mātaram vatsaḥ śaṅkitaḥ paripṛcchati udvignā ca api te dṛṣṭiḥ bhīta bhītā ca dṛśyate āgatā ca tava snehāt kuru tṛptim yathā īpsitām apaścimam idam vatsa durlabham mātṛ darśanam eka aham atha mām pītvā pratyūṣe kasya pāsyasi kāmarūpasya vyāghrasya dātavyam jīvitam mayā bahulāyāḥ vacaḥ śrutvā vatsaḥ vacanam abravīt ślāghyam mama api maraṇam tvayā saha na saṃśayaḥ ekākinā api martavyam mayā avaśyam tvayā vinā yadi mām sahitam mātar vane vyāghraḥ haniṣyati yā gatiḥ mātṛ bhaktānām dhruvam sā me bhaviṣyati tasmāt avaśyam yāsyāmi tvayā saha na saṃśayaḥ atha mātar ca tiṣṭha tvam śapathāḥ santu te mama na asti mātṛ samaḥ bandhuḥ bālānām kṣīra pāyinām na asti mātṛ samaḥ nāthaḥ na asti mātṛ samā gatiḥ na asti mātṛ samaḥ snehaḥ na asti mātṛ samam sukham na ca ayam anya jīvānām mṛtyuḥ syāt anya mṛtyunā apaścimam imam putra mātuḥ saṃdeśam uttamam anutiṣṭhasva mad vākyam tatra śuśrūṣaṇam param pramādāt sarva bhūtāni vinaśyanti na saṃśayaḥ lobhāt vināśaḥ sarveṣām iha loke paratra ca samudram aṭavīm yuddham viśantaḥ lobha mohitāḥ sarpebhyaḥ śvāpadebhyaḥ ca mleccha cora ādi saṃkaṭe tiryañcām pāpa jātīnām ekatra vasatām api nadīnām nakhinām ca eva śṛṅgiṇām śastra pāṇīnām viśvāsaḥ na eva kartavyaḥ strīṇām veśyā janasya ca viśvāsāt bhayam utpannam mūlāni api nikṛntati gāvaḥ paśyanti gandhena vedaiḥ paśyanti brāhmaṇāḥ cāraiḥ paśyanti rājānaḥ cakṣurbhyām itare janāḥ yathā hi pathikaḥ kaḥ cit chāyām āśritya viśramet vatsa antar śokam utsṛjya mad vākyam anupālaya śokena mahatā āviṣṭā bāṣpa vyākula locanā viniḥśvasantī mārgī iva vyāghrāṇām vaśam āgatā mahā paṅka vinirmagnā tiṣṭhantī eva atra sīdati nā asti putra samā prītiḥ nā asti putra samā gatiḥ anṛtam vadate lokaḥ candanam kila śītalam putra gātra pariṣvaṅgaḥ candanāt api śītalaḥ digambaram gata vrīḍam jaṭilam dhūli dhūsaram kim candanena pīyūṣa bindunā kim kim indunā putra gātra pariṣvaṅga pātram gātram bhavet yadi iti putra guṇān uktvā nirīkṣya ca muhur muhur sva mātaram sakhīḥ gopān kramāt tān anupṛcchati yūthasya agre carantīm mām āsasāda mṛgādhipaḥ muktā aham tena śapathaiḥ kulam dṛṣṭvā āgamiṣyasi sā aham bhavantam saṃdraṣṭum mātaram sva kulam sutam mātar kṣamasva tat sarvam bāla tve yat kṛtam mayā ajñānāt jñānataḥ vā api yat uktam kva cit apriyam tat kṣamadhvam mahābhāgāḥ paścāt yat ca kṛtam mayā sarvāḥ sarva guṇa upetāḥ sarva lokasya mātaraḥ sarvāḥ sarva pradāḥ nityam rakṣadhvam mama bālakam anātham abalam dīnam sīdantam mama putrakam mātṛ śoka abhisaṃtaptam bhaginyaḥ pālayiṣyatha bhaginīnām ayam putraḥ sāṃpratam ca viśeṣataḥ bālaḥ abalābhiḥ sarvābhiḥ poṣyaḥ pālyaḥ ca putra vat para putra ātma putreṣu yāsām cittam samam bhavet tāḥ dhanyāḥ tāḥ kṛtārthāḥ ca tāḥ striyaḥ tāḥ ca mātaraḥ modante deva lokeṣu tāḥ gāvaḥ tāḥ ca yoṣitaḥ yāḥ pālayanti anāthān ca para putrān ātma putra vat rakṣadhvam ca mahābhāgāḥ yāsyāmi satya saṃśrayāt śrutvā etat bahulā vākyam mātā sakhyaḥ ca vihvalāḥ viṣādam paramam jagmuḥ idam ūcuḥ su vismitāḥ praveṣṭum udyatā bhīmam bahulā satya vākyataḥ atra gāthāḥ purā gītāḥ ṛṣibhiḥ tattva darśibhiḥ uktvā anṛtam bhavet yatra prāṇinām prāṇa rakṣaṇam anṛtam tatra vai satyam satyam ca eva anṛtam bhavet kāminīṣu vivāheṣu gavām kārye tathā eva ca pareṣām prāṇa rakṣā artham vadāmi eva anṛtam vacaḥ bhuṅkte ca ekaḥ sukham duḥkham mātar satyam vadāmi aham udadhiḥ satya vākyena maryādām na vilaṅghati viṣṇave pṛthivīm dattvā baliḥ pātālam āśritaḥ svarga apavarga narakāḥ sarve vāci pratiṣṭhitāḥ yaḥ tām lopayate vācam aśeṣam tena lopitam kim tena na kṛtam pāpam coreṇa ātma apahāriṇā yāsyāmi narakam ghoram vilopya ātmānam ātmanā snātvā pāpa vinirmuktaḥ prayāti paramām gatim satyam sādhu tapaḥ śrutam ca paramam kleśa ādibhiḥ varjitam svādhīnam ca su durlabham ca jagataḥ sādhāraṇam bhūṣaṇam sādhūnām nikaṣam satām kula dhanam sarva āśramāṇām balam mā tvam parama satyena prāṇān tyajasi dustyajān brūmaḥ kim atra kalyāṇi yā tvam dharma dhuraṃdharā adhiyogam ca paśyāmaḥ tyāgāt asmāt sutena te na hi kalyāṇa cittānām āpadaḥ santi kutra cit dṛṣṭvā gopāñjanam sarvam parikramya ca gokulam bahulā prasthitā devān vṛkṣān ca āpṛcchya tān punar kṣitim ca jalam agnim ca vāyum kha arka niśākaram daśa digdevatām adrīn nakṣatrāṇi grahān tathā karuṇā hita cittānām na syāt para janaḥ yatas tasmāt karuṇayā bālam anātham pālayiṣyatha ye saṃśritāḥ vane siddhāḥ sarvāḥ ca vana devatāḥ campaka aśoka puṃnāga sarala arjuna kiṃśukāḥ śṛṇvantu pādapāḥ sarve saṃdeśam mama viklavam bālam ekākinam dīnam carantam viṣame vane mātā pitṛ vinirmuktam anātham dīnam āturam vicarantam imām bhūmim krandamānam su duḥkhitam mātṛ śoka abhibhūtasya kṣudh pipāsā āturasya ca nyastasya ekākinaḥ śūnyam jagat sarvam prapaśyataḥ caramāṇasya kartavyam sa anukrośasya rakṣaṇam evam saṃdiśya bahulā putra sneha vaśam gatā śoka agninā ati saṃtaptā chinna āśā putra darśane gatvā tu sā punar tatra yatra asau piśita aśanaḥ āste visphūrjita mukhaḥ tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭraḥ bhayānakaḥ vyāghram dṛṣṭvā tu sā dhenuḥ idam vacanam abravīt āgatā aham mahābhāga satya dharma vyavasthayā kuru tṛptim yathākāmam mama māṃsena sāṃpratam tarpayasva sva bhūtāni pañca asya śoṇitena me vyāghraḥ tvayā uktam bahule pūrvam satyāt pratyāgatā punar tena naḥ kautukam jātam prāptā āgacchet katham punar anyathā mām samāsādya jīvantī yāsyase katham tat ca naḥ kautukam pūrṇam dṛṣṭam satyam gavām mayā satye pratiṣṭhitāḥ lokāḥ dharmaḥ satye pratiṣṭhitaḥ satye pratiṣṭhitam jñānam sarvam satye pratiṣṭhitam satyena ṛṣayaḥ siddhāḥ sarvam satye pratiṣṭhitam dhanyaḥ sa rāṣṭraḥ sa tṛṇaḥ prāṇi vṛkṣa samanvitaḥ cacāra bahulāḥ yatra diṣṭyā pāpa vināśinī te dhanyāḥ te kṛtārthāḥ ca taiḥ eva sukṛtam kṛtam taiḥ prāptam janmanaḥ sāram ye pibanti gavām payaḥ mṛgendraḥ pratyayam gatvā vismayam paramam gataḥ pratyādeśaḥ ayam asmākam sarvaiḥ devaiḥ pradarśitaḥ tat kariṣyāmi aham karma yena mokṣyāmi kilbiṣāt mayā jīva sahasrāṇi bhakṣitāni hatāni ca gatim kām nu gamiṣyāmi dṛṣṭvā go satyam īdṛśam aham pāpī durācāraḥ nṛśaṃsaḥ jīva ghātakaḥ kān lokān hi gamiṣyāmi kṛtvā karma su dāruṇam gamiṣye puṇya tīrthāni kariṣye kāya śodhanam patiṣye girim āsādya viśe vā api hutāśanam bahule yat mayā kāryam tapaḥ pāpa viśuddhaye tat ādeśaya saṃkṣepāt na kālaḥ vistarasya me tapaḥ kṛte praśaṃsanti tretāyām yajña karma ca abhayam sarva bhūtānām na asti dānam atas param cara acarāṇām bhūtānām abhayam yaḥ prayacchati na asti ahiṃsā param dānam na asti ahiṃsā paraḥ damaḥ yogavṛkṣasya yā chāyā tāpa traya vināśinī duḥkha traya arka saṃtaptaḥ chāyām yogataroḥ śritaḥ iti evam paramam śreyaḥ kīrtitam te samāsatas vyāghraḥ jñātam ca etat tvayā sarvam kevalam mām hi pṛcchasi aham devaiḥ purā sarvaiḥ vyāghra rūpeṇa pātitaḥ tatra prāṇi vadhe ghore aśeṣam mama vismṛtam tvad saṃparka upadeśena saṃjātam smaraṇam punar mukta śāpaḥ ca saṃjātaḥ prasādāt tava dhenuke prāṇāyāmaiḥ svakam deham parityajya divam gataḥ vimāne haṃsa saṃyukte mahatā apsaraḥ gaṇaiḥ vimāna saṃsthitam dṛṣṭvā vismayam paramam gataḥ bahulā hṛṣṭa tuṣṭa aṅgī gokulam punar āgatā āgatya ca yathāvṛttam vyāghra saṃvādam uttamam sakhībhyaḥ kathayām āsa putrasya ca viśeṣataḥ bahulā putra saṃyuktā su prītā su nirākulā vicacāra aṭavīm sarvām aśeṣa bhaya varjitā yatheṣṭa ceṣṭam abhavat gokulam tad prabhāvataḥ sa rāṣṭra bhṛtya rājānam sa antaḥpura paricchadam sarvān gopān ca tān dṛṣṭvā gopī go maṇḍalāni ca mahā vimānaiḥ śrīmadbhiḥ asaṃkhyaiḥ sarvatas vṛtam prāpya svargam kramāt ūrdhvam aśeṣaiḥ sahitā punar upari upari lokānām gatvā golokam āsthitā tatra saṃbhoga saṃkīrṇe asaṃkhyātaiḥ pura uttamaiḥ bhīṣmaḥ krīḍate sahitā sarvaiḥ yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam iti etat satya vākyasya māhābhāgyam udāhṛtam yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api svarga lokam sa gacchati bahulā vyāghra saṃvādam yaḥ paṭhet satatam dvijaḥ śṛṇuyāt ekacittaḥ ca sa vyāghraiḥ na abhibhūyate viyuktā yā sutaiḥ nārī naraḥ vā api paṭhet sadā yaḥ paṭhet prātar utthāya caturdaśī aṣṭamīṣu ca satām puṇya kṛtām lokān gacchate na atra saṃśayaḥ gavām goṣṭhe ca paṭhatām go vṛddhiḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ kṣetra madhye ca paṭhatām sasya vṛddhiḥ prajāyate gṛha madhye ca paṭhatām bālānām śānti vardhanam bhavet graha abhibhūtānām rakṣām etām ca yaḥ paṭhet durgeṣu paṭhatām nityam aṭavī āyataneṣu ca duḥsvapna ariṣṭa durmitram śrutvā idam saṃpraṇaśyati kumārī ca sadā śṛṇvan vīram patim avāpnuyāt nārī vā puruṣaḥ vā api durbhagaḥ subhagaḥ bhavet gavām parvasu bhaktyā ca māhātmyam puratas paṭhet śūdraḥ aham na adhikāraḥ me cāturāśramya sevane viśeṣeṇa ca vakṣyāmi cāturvarṇyasya liṅgataḥ pañcabhūta śarīrāṇām sarveṣām sadṛśa ātmanām sarveṣām tulya dehānām sarveṣām sadṛśa ātmanām kālaḥ dharmeṇa saṃyuktaḥ śeṣaḥ eva su saṃgrahaḥ evam sati na doṣaḥ asti bhūtānām dharma sevane pālaya tvam prajāḥ sarvāḥ śānta ātmā ca anuśāsitaḥ dvaipāyanaḥ tu ayam cakṣuḥ kṛṣṇaḥ te astu parāyaṇam iti uktvā upāsana arthāya virarāma mahāmatiḥ uvāca śara talpa gatam bhīṣmam pāṇḍavaḥ atha kuru udvahaḥ uvāca vipāpmā ca bhavet kena kim vā kalmaṣa nāśanam tasmai śuśrūṣamāṇāya bhūyas śāṃtanavaḥ tadā deva vaṃśam yathānyāyam ācaṣṭa puruṣa ṛṣabha uvāca ayam daivata vaṃśaḥ vai ṛṣi vaṃśa samanvitaḥ dvi saṃdhyam paṭhitaḥ putra kalmaṣa apaharaḥ paraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ sarva śānti karam japyam dāridrya ātura duḥkhinām tuṣṭi puṣṭi pradam nityam pitāmaha vadasva mama bhīṣmaḥ ayam śastaḥ mahā japyaḥ deva rāja ṛṣi saṃyutaḥ buddhi pūrvam abuddhiḥ vā rātrau yaḥ ca api saṃdhyayoḥ pitāmaha jagannāthaḥ sāvitrī brahmaṇaḥ satī veda bhūḥ atha kartā ca viṣṇuḥ nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ viṣṇoḥ nābhi saraḥ jātaḥ brahmā bhuvana pāvanaḥ umāpatiḥ virūpākṣaḥ skandaḥ senāpatiḥ tathā śakraḥ śacīpatiḥ devaḥ yamaḥ dhūmorṇayā saha varuṇaḥ saha gauryā ca saha ṛddhyā dhaneśvaraḥ saumyā gauḥ surabhiḥ devī viśravāḥ ca mahān ṛṣiḥ ṣaṣ kālaḥ sāgaraḥ gaṅgā sravantyaḥ atha marut gaṇāḥ vālakhilyāḥ tapaḥsiddhāḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ tathā nāradaḥ parvataḥ ca eva viśvāvasuḥ hahā huhūḥ tumbaruḥ citrasenaḥ ca deva dūtaḥ ca viśrutaḥ deva kanyāḥ mahābhāgāḥ divyāḥ ca apsarasām gaṇāḥ urvaśī menakā rambhā miśrakeśī alambuṣā viśvāciḥ ca ghṛtācī ca pañcacūḍā tilottamā ādityāḥ vasavaḥ rudrāḥ sa aśvinaḥ pitaraḥ api ca dharmaḥ satyam tapaḥ dīkṣā vyavasāyaḥ pitāmahaḥ śarvaryaḥ divasāḥ ca eva mārīcaḥ kaśyapaḥ tathā śukraḥ bṛhaspatiḥ bhaumaḥ budhaḥ rāhuḥ śanaiścaraḥ nakṣatrāṇi ṛtavaḥ ca eva māsāḥ saṃdhyāḥ sa vatsarāḥ vainateyāḥ samudrāḥ ca kadru jāḥ pannagāḥ tathā anantaḥ nāga rājaḥ ca vāsukiḥ takṣakaḥ tathā śatadrūḥ ca vipāśā ca candrabhāgā sarasvatī gaṅgā mahānadī ca eva kapilā narmadā tathā kampunā ca viśalyā ca karatoyā ambuvāhinī sarayūḥ gaṇḍakī ca eva lohityaḥ ca mahā nadaḥ tāmrāruṇā vetravatī parṇāśā gautamī tathā godāvarī ca veṇṇā ca kṛṣṇaveṇā tathā adrijā dṛṣadvatī ca kāverī vaṃkṣuḥ mandākinī tathā prayāgam ca prabhāsam ca puṇyam naimiṣam eva ca puṇya tīrthaiḥ ca kalilam kurukṣetram prakīrtitam sindhūttamam tapodānam jambūmārgam atha api ca hiraṇvatī vitastā ca tathā eva ikṣumatī nadī bhūmi bhāgāḥ tathā puṇyāḥ gaṅgādvāram atha api ca ṛṣikulyāḥ tathā medhyā nadī citrapathā tathā kauśikī yamunā sītā tathā carmaṇvatī nadī carmaṇvatī nadī puṇyā kauśikī yamunā tathā nadī bhīmarathā ca eva bāhudā ca mahā nadī mahendravāṇī tridivā nīlikā ca sarasvatī nandā ca aparanandā ca tathā tīrtham mahāhradam gayā atha phalgutīrtham ca dharmāraṇyam suraiḥ vṛtam puṇyam triloka vikhyātam sarva pāpa haram śivam etāḥ pāpa hara sarvāḥ devanadyaḥ prakīrtitāḥ vindhyaḥ dhātu vicitra aṅgaḥ tīrthavān auṣadha anvitaḥ śṛṅgavant mandaraḥ nīlaḥ niṣadhaḥ darduraḥ tathā citrakūṭaḥ añjana ābhaḥ ca parvataḥ gandhamādanaḥ puṇyaḥ somagiriḥ ca eva tathā eva anye mahīdharāḥ diśaḥ ca vidiśaḥ ca eva kṣitiḥ sarve mahīruhāḥ viśvedevāḥ nabhaḥ ca eva nakṣatrāṇi grahāḥ tathā pāntu vaḥ satatam devāḥ kīrtitā a kīrtitā mayā devatā anantaram viprān tapaḥ siddhān tapaḥ dhikān kīrtitān kīrtayiṣyāmi sarva pāpa pramocanān yavakrītaḥ atha raibhyaḥ ca kakṣīvant auśijaḥ tathā bhṛgvaṅgirāḥ tathā kaṇvaḥ medhātithiḥ atha prabhuḥ barhī ca guṇa saṃpannaḥ prāñcam diśam upāśritāḥ bhadrām diśam mahābhāgāḥ ulmucuḥ pramucuḥ tathā mumucuḥ ca mahābhāgaḥ svastyātreyaḥ ca vīryavān mitrāvaruṇayoḥ putraḥ tathā agastyaḥ pratāpavān dṛḍhāyuḥ ca ūrdhvabāhuḥ ca viśrutau ṛṣi sattamau paścimām diśam āśritya ye edhante nibodha tān uṣadguḥ saha sodaryaiḥ parivyādhaḥ ca vīryavān ṛṣiḥ dīrghatamāḥ ca eva gautamaḥ kaśyapaḥ tathā atreḥ putraḥ ca dharma ātmā tathā sārasvataḥ prabhuḥ uttarām diśam āśritya ye edhante nibodha tān atriḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ śaktiḥ ca pārāśaryaḥ ca vīryavān ṛcīka pautraḥ rāmaḥ ca ṛṣiḥ auddālakiḥ tathā ṛṣiḥ ugraśravāḥ ca eva bhārgavaḥ cyavanaḥ tathā ādyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ rājan sarva pāpa pramocanaḥ nṛgaḥ yayātiḥ nahuṣaḥ yaduḥ pūruḥ ca vīryavān dhundhumāraḥ dilīpaḥ ca sagaraḥ ca pratāpavān kṛśāśvaḥ yauvanāśvaḥ ca citrāśvaḥ satyavant tathā duḥṣantaḥ bharataḥ ca eva cakravartī mahā yaśāḥ yavanaḥ janakaḥ ca eva tathā dṛḍharathaḥ nṛpaḥ rājā rathaṃtaraḥ ca eva bhārgavaḥ cyavanaḥ tathā rāmaḥ rākṣasa hā vīraḥ śaśabinduḥ bhagīrathaḥ udarkaḥ ca eva māndhātā tathā eva uḍaḥ mahodayaḥ karaṃdhamaḥ nara śreṣṭhaḥ kadhmoraḥ ca nara adhipaḥ dakṣaḥ ambarīṣaḥ kukuraḥ ravataḥ ca mahā yaśāḥ kuruḥ saṃvaraṇaḥ ca eva māndhātā satya vikramaḥ mucukundaḥ ca rājarṣiḥ mitrabhānuḥ priyaṃkaraḥ ādi rājaḥ pṛthuḥ vainyo trasadasyuḥ tathā rājā śvetaḥ rāja ṛṣi sattamaḥ mahābhiṣaḥ ca vikhyātaḥ nimi rājaḥ tathā aṣṭakaḥ āyuḥ kṣupaḥ ca rājarṣiḥ kakṣeyuḥ ca nara adhipaḥ śibiḥ auśīnaraḥ ca eva gayaḥ ca eva nara adhipaḥ pṛthuḥ tathā uparicaraḥ kekayaḥ ca mahā yaśāḥ pratardanaḥ divodāsaḥ saudāsaḥ kosala īśvaraḥ ailaḥ nalaḥ ca rājarṣiḥ manuḥ ca eva prajāpatiḥ havidhraḥ ca pṛṣadhraḥ ca pratīpaḥ śaṃtanuḥ tathā pṛṣadhruḥ ca pratīpaḥ ca śaṃtanuḥ ca tathā nṛpaḥ havidhraḥ ca ajaḥ ca eva rantidevaḥ purūravāḥ ajaḥ prācīnabarhīḥ ca tathā ikṣvākuḥ mahā yaśāḥ rambhodbhavaḥ ca rājarṣiḥ māndhātā rāja sattamaḥ kakṣasenaḥ ca rājarṣiḥ ye ca anye na anukīrtitāḥ devāḥ devarṣayaḥ ca eva stutāḥ rājarṣayaḥ tathā puṣṭim āyuḥ yaśaḥ svargam vidhāsyanti mama īśvarāḥ mā vighnam mā ca me pāpam mā ca me paripanthinaḥ avikārāya śuddhāya nityāya paramātmane sadā eka rūpa rūpāya viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave uvāca śara talpa gate bhīṣme kauravāṇām dhuraṃdhare śayāne vīra śayane pāṇḍavaiḥ samupasthite yudhiṣṭhiraḥ mahā prājñaḥ mama pūrva pitāmahaḥ dharmāṇām āgamam śrutvā viditvā dharma saṃśayān dānānām ca vidhim śrutvā chinna dharma artha saṃśayaḥ uvāca abhūt muhūrtam stimitam sarvam tat rāja maṇḍalam tūṣṇīṃbhūte tadā bhīṣme paṭe citram iva arpitam muhūrtam iva ca dhyātvā vyāsaḥ satyavatī sutaḥ nṛpam śayānam gāṅgeyam idam āha vacaḥ tadā rājan prakṛtim āpannaḥ kururājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ sahitaḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ sarvaiḥ pārthivaiḥ ca anuyāyibhiḥ upāste tvām nara vyāghra saha kṛṣṇena dhīmatā yudhiṣṭhiram saha amātyam anujajñe nadī sutaḥ uvāca ca enam madhuram tatas śāṃtanavaḥ nṛpaḥ yayātiḥ iva rāja indra śraddhā dama puraḥsaraḥ kṣatra dharma rataḥ pārtha pitṝn devān ca tarpaya rañjayasva prajāḥ sarvāḥ prakṛtīḥ parisāntvaya anu tvām tāta jīvantu mitrāṇi suhṛdaḥ tathā caitya sthāne sthitam vṛkṣam phalavantam iva dvijāḥ dhṛtarāṣṭram puraskṛtya gāndhārīm ca pativratām saha taiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ sarvaiḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ keśavena ca praviveśa kuru śreṣṭha puram vāraṇasāhvayam uvāca tatas kuntī sutaḥ rājā paura jānapadam janam pūjayitvā yathānyāyam anujajñe gṛhān prati sāntvayām āsa nārīḥ ca hata vīrāḥ hata īśvarāḥ vipulaiḥ artha dānaiḥ ca tadā pāṇḍu sutaḥ nṛpaḥ saḥ abhiṣiktaḥ mahā prājñaḥ prāpya rājyam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ avasthāpya nara śreṣṭhaḥ sarvāḥ sva prakṛtīḥ tadā pratigṛhya āśiṣaḥ mukhyāḥ tadā dharma bhṛtām varaḥ uṣitvā śarvarīḥ śrīmān pañcāśat nagara uttame tatas ca puṇḍarīkākṣam āha dharma bhṛtām varaḥ bhagavan yoga yuktaḥ asi tūṣṇīm dhyāyasi śatru han brūhi mām puruṣa śreṣṭhaḥ ājñāpyaḥ bhavatā hi aham dhyā puṇḍarīkākṣa śreyas mad parama hita bhagavant śara talpa gataḥ bhīṣmaḥ śāmyan iva hutāśanaḥ mām dhyāti puruṣa vyāghraḥ tatas mama tad gatam manaḥ dṛṣṭvā nivṛttam ādityam pravṛttam ca uttarāyaṇam ghṛtam mālyam ca gandhān ca kṣaumāṇi ca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ candana agaru mukhyāni tathā kāla agarūṇi ca prasthāpya pūrvam kaunteyaḥ bhīṣma saṃsādhanāya vai mālyāni ca mahārhāni ratnāni vividhāni ca dhṛtarāṣṭram puraskṛtya gāndhārīm ca yaśasvinīm mātaram ca pṛthām dhīmān bhrātṝn ca puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ bhrātṝn ca eva puraskṛtya mātaram ca pṛthām api mahatā rāja bhogyena paribarheṇa saṃvṛtaḥ stūyamānaḥ mahā rāja bhīṣmasya agnīn anuvrajan āsasāda kurukṣetre tatas śāṃtanavam nṛpam upāsyamānam vyāsena pārāśaryeṇa dhīmatā hata śiṣṭaiḥ nṛpaiḥ ca anyaiḥ nānā deśa samāgataiḥ rakṣibhiḥ ca mahātmānam rakṣyamāṇam samantataḥ śayānam vīra śayane dadarśa nṛpatiḥ tatas dhyāyantam paramātmānam kṛṣṇa dharmam sanātanam tatas rathāt avārohat bhrātṛbhiḥ saha dharmarāj dvaipāyana ādīn viprān ca taiḥ ca pratyabhinanditaḥ mādhavena mahā rājaḥ kṛṣṇena akliṣṭa karmaṇā āsādya śara talpa stham ṛṣibhiḥ parivāritam abravīt bharata śreṣṭham dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha kauravya śayānam nimnagā sutam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ aham nṛpate namaḥ te jāhnavī suta śṛṇoṣi ced mahā bāho brūhi kim karavāṇi te ācāryāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ca eva ṛtvijaḥ bhrātaraḥ ca me putraḥ ca te mahā tejāḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ janeśvaraḥ upasthitaḥ saha amātyaḥ vāsudevaḥ ca vīryavān hata śiṣṭāḥ ca rājānaḥ sarve ca kurujāṅgalāḥ tān paśya kuru śārdūla samunmīlaya locane evam uktaḥ tu gāṅgeyaḥ kuntī putreṇa dhīmatā dadarśa bhāratān sarvān sthitān saṃparivārya tam diṣṭyā prāptaḥ asi kaunteya saha amātyaḥ yudhiṣṭhira parivṛttaḥ hi bhagavān sahasrāṃśuḥ divākaraḥ aṣṭa pañcāśatam rātryaḥ śayānasya adya me gatāḥ śareṣu niśita agreṣu yathā varṣa śatam tathā māghaḥ ayam samanuprāptaḥ māsaḥ puṇyaḥ yudhiṣṭhira tri bhāga śeṣaḥ pakṣaḥ ayam śuklaḥ bhavitum arhati dhṛtarāṣṭram atha āmantrya kāle vacanam abravīt rājan vidita dharmaḥ asi su nirṇīta artha saṃśayaḥ bahu śrutāḥ hi te viprāḥ bahavaḥ paryupāsitāḥ veda śāstrāṇi sarvāṇi dharmān ca manuja īśvara vedān ca caturaḥ sa aṅgān nikhilena avabudhyase śrutam deva rahasyam te kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāt api yathā pāṇḍoḥ sutāḥ rājan tathā eva te dharmataḥ tān pālaya sthitaḥ dharme guru śuśrūṣaṇe ratān ānṛśaṃsya param hi enam jānāmi guru vatsalam tava putrāḥ durātmānaḥ krodha lobha parāyaṇāḥ īrṣyā abhibhūtāḥ durvṛttāḥ tān na śocitum arhasi uvāca etāvat uktvā vacanam dhṛtarāṣṭram manīṣiṇam vāsudevam mahā bāhum abhyabhāṣata kauravaḥ vāsudevaḥ hiraṇya ātmā puruṣaḥ savitā virāj jīva bhūtaḥ anurūpaḥ tvam parama ātmā sanātanaḥ trāyasva puṇḍarīkākṣa puruṣottama nityaśas anujānīhi mām kṛṣṇa vaikuṇṭha puruṣottama rakṣyāḥ ca te pāṇḍaveyāḥ bhavān hi eṣām parāyaṇam duryodhanam durācāram kṣatriya anta karam raṇe vāsudevena tīrthena putra saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ suhṛdbhiḥ sahitaḥ rājan bhuṅkṣva rājyam akaṇṭakam saṃdhānasya paraḥ kālaḥ tava iti ca punar punar na ca me tat vacaḥ mūḍhaḥ kṛtavan sa su manda dhīḥ ghātayitvā iha pṛthivīm tatas sa nidhanam gataḥ tvām ca jānāmi aham vīra purāṇam ṛṣi sattamam nareṇa sahitam devam badaryām su cira uṣitam tathā mad nāradaḥ prāha vyāsaḥ ca su mahā tapāḥ nara nārāyaṇau etau saṃbhūtau manujeṣu iti sa mām tvam anujānīhi kṛṣṇa mokṣye kalevaram tvayā aham samanujñātaḥ gaccheyam paramām gatim uvāca anujānāmi bhīṣma tvām vasūn āpnuhi pārthiva na te asti vṛjinam kim cit mayā dṛṣṭam mahā dyute pitṛ bhaktaḥ asi rājarṣe mārkaṇḍeyaḥ iva aparaḥ uvāca evam uktaḥ tu gāṅgeyaḥ pāṇḍavān idam abravīt dhṛtarāṣṭra mukhān ca api sarvān sa suhṛdaḥ tathā prāṇān utsraṣṭum icchāmi tat mā anujñātum arhatha ānṛśaṃsya paraiḥ bhāvyam sadā eva niyata ātmabhiḥ brahmaṇyaiḥ dharma śīlaiḥ ca ca bhārata dhanam bahuvidham rājan dattvā nityam dvijātiṣu punar eva abravīt dhīmān yudhiṣṭhiram idam vacaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ca eva te nityam prājñāḥ ca eva viśeṣataḥ ācāryāḥ ṛtvijaḥ ca eva pūjanīyāḥ narādhipa uvāca evam uktvā kurūn sarvān bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ tadā tūṣṇīm babhūva kauravyaḥ sa muhūrtam ariṃdama dhārayām āsa ca ātmānam dhāraṇāsu yathākramam tasya ūrdhvam agaman prāṇāḥ saṃniruddhāḥ mahātmanaḥ idam āścaryam āsīt ca madhye teṣām mahātmanām yat yat muñcati gātrāṇām sa śaṃtanu sutaḥ tadā kṣaṇena prekṣatām teṣām viśalyaḥ saḥ abhavat tadā tam dṛṣṭvā vismitāḥ sarve vāsudeva purogamāḥ deva dundubhi nādaḥ ca puṣpa varṣaiḥ saha abhavat siddhāḥ brahmarṣayaḥ ca eva sādhu sādhu iti harṣitāḥ niḥsṛtya ākāśam āviśya kṣaṇena antaradhīyata evam sa nṛpa śārdūla nṛpaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ tadā tatas tu ādāya dārūṇi gandhān ca vividhān bahūn candanānām ca khaṇḍāni mahārghāṇi bahūni ca citām cakruḥ mahātmānaḥ pāṇḍavāḥ viduraḥ tathā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tu gāṅgeyam viduraḥ ca mahāmatiḥ uṣṇīṣe paryagṛhṇītām mādrī putrau ubhau tadā yudhiṣṭhireṇa sahitau dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ tu pādataḥ tālavṛntāni upādāya paryavījan samantataḥ yājakāḥ juhuvuḥ ca agnim jaguḥ sāmāni sāmagāḥ tatas candana kāṣṭhaiḥ ca tathā kāleyakaiḥ api samavacchādya gāṅgeyam prajvālya ca hutāśanam apasavyam akurvanta dhṛtarāṣṭra mukhāḥ nṛpāḥ saṃskṛtya ca kuru śreṣṭham gāṅgeyam kuru sattamāḥ jagmuḥ bhāgīrathī tīram ṛṣi juṣṭam kuru udvahāḥ kṛṣṇena bharata strībhiḥ ye ca paurāḥ samāgatāḥ vidhivat kṣatriya śreṣṭhāḥ sa ca sarvaḥ janaḥ tadā utthāya salilāt tasmāt rudatī śoka lālasā nibodhata yathāvṛttam ucyamānam mayā anaghāḥ rāja vṛttena saṃpannaḥ prajñayā abhijanena ca satkartā kuru vṛddhānām pitṛ bhaktaḥ dṛḍha vrataḥ jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa purā yaḥ na parājitaḥ divyaiḥ astraiḥ mahā vīryaḥ sa hataḥ adya śikhaṇḍinā aśmasāra mayam nūnam hṛdayam mama pārthivāḥ sametam pārthivam kṣatram kāśi puryām svayaṃvare hatam śikhaṇḍinā śrutvā yat na dīryati me manaḥ pīḍitaḥ na ati yatnena nihataḥ sa śikhaṇḍinā evaṃvidham bahu tadā vilapantīm mahānadīm āśvāsayām āsa tadā sāmnā dāmodaraḥ vibhuḥ samāśvasihi bhadre tvam mā śucaḥ śubha darśane gataḥ sa paramām siddhim te putraḥ na saṃśayaḥ vasuḥ eṣa mahā tejāḥ śāpa doṣeṇa śobhane saḥ eṣa kṣatra dharmeṇa yudhyamānaḥ raṇa ajire dhanaṃjayena nihataḥ na eṣa nunnaḥ śikhaṇḍinā bhīṣmam hi kuru śārdūlam udyata iṣum mahā raṇe na śaktaḥ saṃyuge hantum sākṣāt api śatakratuḥ na śaktāḥ syuḥ nihantum hi raṇe tam sarva devatāḥ iti uktā sā tu kṛṣṇena vyāsena ca saridvarā tyaktvā śokam mahā rāja svam vāri avatatāra ha satkṛtya te tām saritam tatas kṛṣṇa mukhāḥ nṛpāḥ anujñātāḥ tayā sarve nyavartanta janādhipāḥ sarve te dīna manasaḥ śocamānāḥ punar punar hasti aśva ratha yānaiḥ ca saṃprāptāḥ hastināpuram iti etat bahu vistāram ānuśāsanikam śubham yatra uktāḥ sarva dharmāḥ ca parvaṇi asmin trayodaśe śrutvā yān svastha tām āpa dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bhīṣmāt bhāgīrathī putrāt sarva saṃdeha hāriṇaḥ adhyāyānām śatam ca atra ṣaṭcatvāriṃśat eva tu nava śloka sahasrāṇi śatāni aṣṭau tathā eva ca vyāsena udāra matinā dṛṣṭaḥ granthaḥ mahātmanā ānuśāsanikam parva śrutvā bhakti samanvitaḥ nārāyaṇam pūjayitvā bhaktyā paramayā tatas bhīṣma uddeśena kartavyam brāhmaṇānām ca tarpaṇam vyāsa rūpī hariḥ sākṣāt paśyatām iti kīrtayet dadyāt dhenu hiraṇya ādi vācakāya viśeṣataḥ sarva kāmān avāpnoti dīrgham āyuḥ ca vindati
